# Foreword by James Clear — Ultralearning

### _(Prastavana — James Clear Dwara)_

---

> _"In theory, there is no difference between theory and practice. But in practice, there is."_
> _(Siddhant mein, siddhant aur abhyas mein koi farq nahi hota. Lekin vyavahar mein, hota hai.)_

---

Scott Young ke saath mera rishta 2013 ke madhya mein shuru hua tha. 10 July ko, maine unhein ek email bheja aur poocha ki kya woh agle mahine ek call set up karna chahenge. Hum kuch hi din pehle ek conference mein mile the, aur main umeed kar raha tha ki woh baatcheet ko jaari rakhne ke liye taiyar honge.

“Shayad,” unhone jawab diya. “Main tab Spain mein hunga, aur mere aane wale project ka language-learning ka focus shayad prathmikta (precedence) le le.”

Yeh woh jawab nahi tha jiski main umeed kar raha tha, lekin yeh wajib (reasonable) lag raha tha. International travel karte waqt calls manage karna pechida (tricky) ho sakta hai, aur main samajhta tha agar woh unke wapas lautne tak wait karna chahte hon. Halanki, mujhe jaldi hi pata chal gaya ki woh jald hi wapas nahi laut rahe commercial plane se, aur yeh koi samay ka badlav nahi tha aur na hi koi kharab (spotty) internet connection tha jo hamari baatcheet ko postpone karne wala tha.

Nahi, Scott se sampark banana mushkil hone wala tha kyunki woh poore ek saal tak koi English nahi bolne ka plan bana rahe the.

Is tarah Scott Young aur unke ultralearning ke prati samarpan (commitment) se mera parichay shuru hua. Agle baarah mahinon mein, main Scott ke saath ruka-ruka (sporadic) emails ka len-den karta raha jab unhone Spain, Brazil, China, aur Korea ka travel kiya, aur raaste mein unhone unme se har ek bhasha mein baatcheet karne ke kabil (conversational) banna jaari rakha. Woh apne vaade ke pakke the: agle summer 2014 tak hum niyamit roop se catch up karne ke liye waqt nahi nikaal paaye aur har kuch mahino mein ek doosre se chat karna shuru kiya.

Main Scott ke saath apni calls ke liye hamesha excited rehta tha—mukhya roop se swarthi (selfish) kaaranon se. Ek writer ke roop mein mera ek mukhya (core) interest is science mein hai ki achhi habits kaise banayein aur buri habits ko kaise todein. Scott jaisa koi insaan, jisne itni saaf taur par apni khud ki habits par maharat (mastered) haasil kar li thi, exactly usi tarah ka insaan tha jo mujhe ek ya do cheezein sikha sakta tha. Aur theek (precisely) wahi hua. Mujhe mushkil se (scarcely) hi yaad hai ki maine Scott ke saath koi call khatam ki ho aur pichle ghante ke dauran kuch seekha na ho.

Iska matlab yeh nahi hai ki unki samajh (insight) ne mujhe hairan kiya. Scott pahle se hi mere dhyan mein the jab hum 2013 mein us conference mein mile the. Ek saal pahle unhone poore MIT undergraduate computer science ke paathyakram (curriculum) ko seekh kar aur ek saal se kam samay mein saare final tests pass karke internet ki duniya mein tezi se oonchaiyon par (catapulted) pahunche the—char saal ke classes ka kaam baarah mahinon se kam mein. Maine unke experience ko summarize karne wala TEDx Talk dekha tha, aur conference mein unhein khojna (tracking him down) shuru karne se pehle maine learning aur self-improvement par unke kuch articles padhe the.

Kisi mahatvakankshi (ambitious) project ko haath mein lene ka idea—jaise ek saal mein MIT ka undergraduate curriculum padhna ya har teen mahine mein ek nayi bhasha seekhna—bahut se logon ke liye preranadayak (inspirational) hota hai. Mujhe nishchit roop se yeh sahasik (bold) projects aakarshak (fascinating) lage. Lekin Scott ke projects ke baare mein kuch aur bhi tha jisne mere dil ko gehrai se chhooa (resonated): unke paas action ki taraf ek jhukaav (bias) tha.

Yeh kuch aisa hai jise maine hamesha Scott ke approach ke baare mein saraaha hai aur kuch aisa jo mujhe vishwas hai ki aap is book ke ek reader ke roop mein sarahenge. Woh sirf knowledge ko grahan karne (soaking up) par focus nahi karte. Woh us knowledge ko use mein lane ke liye vachanbaddh hain. Learning ko ek tivrata (intensity) aur action ke prati samarpan ke saath approach karna Scott ki process ki ek mukhya nishani (hallmark) hai. Yeh approach mujhse baat karta hai, aashik roop se, kyunki main apni life aur career mein isi tarah ke patterns dekhta hoon. Mere kuch sabse arthpurna (meaningful) experiences khud ke dwara nirdeshit (self-directed) tivra learning ka nateeja rahe hain.

Halanki main us samay _ultralearning_ shabd nahi jaanta tha, mera pahla ultralearning project photography tha. Late 2009 mein, main kuch mahinon ke liye Scotland move kar gaya. Yeh pehli baar tha jab main videsh mein reh raha tha, aur Scottish Highlands ke khoobsurat nazaaron (scenery) ko dekhte hue, maine socha ki mujhe ek achha camera kharidna chahiye. Halanki, jis cheez ki maine umeed nahi ki thi, woh yeh thi ki mujhe photos lene ki process se pyaar ho jayega. Jo follow hua woh meri life ke sabse ranatmak (creative) periods mein se ek tha.

Maine photography ko kai tarah ke methods se seekha. Maine famous photographers ke portfolios ka adhyayan kiya. Maine locations ko dhoondha (scouted) aur aakarshak (compelling) nazariyon (perspectives) ki talaash ki. Lekin, sabse badhkar, maine ek simple method se seekha: maine us pahle saal mein 100,000 se zyaada photos khinchin. Maine kabhi kisi photography class mein daakhila nahi liya. Maine behtar photographer kaise banein is par books nahi padhin. Maine bas unthak prayog (relentless experimentation) ka vaada kiya. Yeh "karke seekhna" (learning by doing) approach is kitab ke mere favorite chapters mein se ek aur Scott ke ultralearning ke teesre niyam ko sakaar (embodies) karta hai: pratyakshata (directness).

Directness us cheez ko directly karne dwara seekhne ka abhyas hai jise aap seekhna chahte hain. Basically, yeh nishkriya (passive) learning ke bajaye sakriya abhyas (active practice) ke zariye improvement hai. "Kuch naya seekhna" aur "kuch naya practice karna" phrases ek jaise lag sakte hain, lekin yeh do methods gehre roop se alag (profoundly different) results paida kar sakte hain. Passive learning gyan (knowledge) banati hai. Active practice hunar (skill) banati hai.

Yeh ek aisa point hai jise Scott chapter 6 mein mazeed poori tarah se saaf karte hain: directness se skill development hota hai. Aap bench press technique par sabse best instructions ko research kar sakte hain, lekin taqat banane ka akela tarika weights uthane ki practice karna hai. Aap saari bestselling sales books padh sakte hain, lekin actually customers paane ka akela tarika sales calls karne ki practice karna hai. Learning bahut useful ho sakti hai, beshak, lekin khatra yeh hai ki naye facts ko grahan karne ka kaam naye skill ko behtar banane ki process se alag ho sakta hai. Aap kisi industry ke baare mein har ek fact jaan sakte hain aur phir bhi asli duniya ke anubhav ki kami ho sakti hai kyunki aapne us kala (craft) ki practice nahi ki hai.

Scott naye skills ko actually seekhne ki kathinai ko samajhte hain. Main unki na keval unki writing ki quality ke liye izzat karta hoon balki is simple fact ke liye bhi ki woh apne hi ideas par amal karne wale (practitioner) hain. Main is baare mein jitna kahoon kam hai ki yeh kitna important hai: unka isme khud ka fayda-nuksaan shamil (skin in the game) hai. Kai ideas paper par brilliant lagte hain lekin real world mein fail ho jaate hain. Jaisa ki kahavat hai, _"In theory, there is no difference between theory and practice. But in practice, there is."_

Jahan tak meri photography ki koshish (quest) ka sawaal hai, mere direct practice ke samarpan ko fayda pahunchane (pay off) karne mein zyaada waqt nahi laga. Camera kharidne ke kuch mahino baad, maine Norway ka travel kiya aur aurora borealis ki ek image capture karne ke liye Arctic Circle ke ooper sahasik safar (ventured) kiya. Uske kuch hi samay baad, Northern Lights ki us image ki wajah se mujhe _Travel Photographer of the Year_ ke liye ek finalist ke roop mein chuna gaya. Yeh ek hairan karne wala nateeja (outcome) tha, lekin is baat ka ek pramaan (testament) bhi tha ki aap learning ke ek chhote lekin tivra period ke dauran kitna progress kar sakte hain.

Maine kabhi photographer ke roop mein career aage nahi badhaya. Yeh ek ultralearning project tha jo maine fun aur apne santoosh ke liye kiya tha. Lekin kuch saal baad, theek usi samay jab main pehli baar Scott se mila tha, maine ek mazeed upyogi (utilitarian) nateejay ko dimaag mein rakh kar tivra learning ka ek aur period shuru kiya: main ek entrepreneur banna chahta tha, aur maine socha ki writing ek aisa raasta hoga jo mujhe wahan tak pahuncha sakta hai.

Ek baar phir, maine ek aisa kshetra (domain) select kiya tha jahan mere paas na ke barabar formal experience tha. Mere family mein koi entrepreneurs nahi the, aur maine college ki sirf ek single English class li thi. Lekin jaise hi maine _Ultralearning_ ko padha, main yeh dekhkar hairan (startled) reh gaya ki Scott ne, lagbhag step-by-step tareeqe se, us process ko explain kiya jise maine ek anjaan entrepreneur se bestselling author banne ke liye follow kiya tha.

- **Principle #1: Metalearning** — Maine doosre popular bloggers aur authors ko jaanchne (examining) se shuru kiya. Unke methods ne mujhe ek map banane mein madad ki ki mujhe ek safal writer banne ke liye kya karne ki zarurat thi.
- **Principle #2: Focus** — Main lagbhag shuruat se hi full-time writer ke roop mein chala gaya. Un kuch freelance projects ke alava jo maine bills pay karne ke liye haath mein liye the, mera bhaari hissa (vast majority) waqt padhne aur likhne mein beet-ta tha.
- **Principle #3: Directness** — Maine likhna likh kar hi seekha. Maine har Monday aur Thursday ko ek naya article likhne ka apne liye ek schedule set kiya. Pehle do saalon mein, maine 150 se zyaada essays taiyar kiye.
- **Principle #4: Drill** — Maine systematically articles likhne ke har ek aspect ko toda—headline, introductory sentence, badlav (transitions), storytelling, aur bahut kuch—aur har ek segment ke examples se bhari spreadsheets taiyar kin. Phir main bade task ke har ek chhote aspect ko perform karne ki apni ability ko test aur refine karne mein lag gaya.
- **Principle #6: Feedback** — Maine personally apne pehle das hazar subscribers mein se lagbhag sabhi ko hello kehne aur meri writing par feedback maangne ke liye email kiya. Yeh bade paimane par nahi badha (scale), lekin isne mujhe shuruat mein bahut kuch sikhaya.
- . . . aur isi tarah aage bhi.

Mera point yeh hai ki Scott ka method kaam karta hai. Is kitab mein unhone jo techniques batayi hain, unhein follow karke, main ek writing career banane, ek safal business create karne, aur, aakhirkar, ek _New York Times_ bestselling book likhne mein kabil raha. Jab maine _Atomic Habits_ release ki, toh yeh ultralearning ki process ke saalon ki mehnat ka parinaam (culmination) tha.

Mujhe lagta hai ki ek bestselling book likhne ya ek saal mein char bhashayein seekhne ke baare mein stories sunna aur yeh sochna aasan hai ki, "Yeh doosre logon ke liye hai." Main disagree karta hoon. Kuch keemti seekhna aur ise tezi se karna kisi geniuses ke chhote daire tak seemit (confined) nahi rehna chahiye. Yeh ek aisi process hai jise koi bhi apna (embrace) sakta hai. Yeh bas itna hai ki zyaadatar log ise kabhi nahi karte kyunki unke paas kabhi koi playbook nahi thi jo unhein dikhaye ki kaise karna hai. Ab tak.

Ultralearning ko pursue karne ke achhe kaaran hain—chahe aap personal interest ke liye koi project kar rahe hon ya professional interests ke liye.

Pahle, deep learning life mein maqsad (purpose) ka ek ehsaas karati hai. Skills develop karna arthpurna hai. Kisi cheez mein achha hona achha feel karwata hai. Ultralearning apne aap ko yeh prove karne ka ek raasta hai ki aapke paas improve karne aur apni life ka sabse behtar upyog karne ki ability hai. Yeh aapko confidence kou badhati hai ki aap ambitious cheezon ko poora (accomplish) kar sakte hain.

Doosre, deep learning se hi aapko asadharn (outsized) returns milte hain. Simple truth yeh hai ki zyaadatar log aapke interest ke area ka kabhi tivra study nahi karenge. Aisa karna—chahe yeh sirf kuch mahino ke liye hi kyun na ho—aapko sabse alag dikhne (stand out) mein madad karega. Aur ek baar jab aap stand out karte hain, toh aap ek behtar job paa sakte hain, ek higher salary ya zyaada free time ke liye negotiate kar sakte hain, zyaada interesting logon ke saath network kar sakte hain, aur apni personal aur professional life ko behtar (level up) kar sakte hain. Ultralearning aapko leverage develop karne mein madad karti hai jise aap kahin aur use kar sakte hain.

Finally, deep learning possible hai. Famous entrepreneur aur investor, Paul Graham ne ek baar note kiya tha, _"Kai fields mein ek saal ka focused kaam plus bahut zyaada parwah karna hi kaafi hoga."_ Isi tarah, mujhe lagta hai ki zyaadatar log hairan honge ki woh ek saal (ya kuch mahino) ki focused learning se kya haasil kar sakte hain. Intense self-directed learning ki process un skills ko banana (fashion) kar sakti hai jinhe aapne kabhi nahi socha tha ki aap develop kar sakte hain. Ultralearning aapko aapki kshamta (potential) fulfill karne mein madad kar sakti hai, aur yeh shayad isko pursue karne ka sabse behtar kaaran hai.

Sachi baat yeh hai ki, meri writing aur photography ki koshishon ki safalta ke bavajood, yeh projects bina soche-samjhe/astar-vyastar (haphazard) the. Maine unhein intensely kiya lekin bina kisi guidance ya direction ke. Maine bahut si galtiyan kin. Kaash jab main shuruat kar raha tha toh mere paas yeh kitab hoti. Main sirf kalpana kar sakta hoon ki maine kitna wasted time aur energy bacha liya hota.

_Ultralearning_ ek aakarshak aur preranadayak padhai hai. Scott ne kisi bhi cheez ko tezi se seekhne ke liye amal mein lane yogya (actionable) strategies ka ek sone ki khadaan (gold mine) taiyar kiya hai. Unki mehnat ab aapka fayda hai. Main umeed karta hoon ki aap is kitab ko utna hi enjoy karenge jitna maine kiya, aur, sabse important, main umeed karta hoon ki aap in ideas ka use apni life mein kuch ambitious aur exciting poora karne ke liye karenge. Un stories aur strategies ke saath jo Scott is kitab mein share karte hain, aapke paas knowledge hogi. Ab jo bacha hai woh hai action lena.

—James Clear

---

# Chapter 1 — Can You Get an MIT Education Without Going to MIT?

### _(Kya Aap MIT Gaye Bina Wahan Ki Education Haasil Kar Sakte Hain?)_

---

> _"In many fields a year of focused work plus caring a lot would be enough."_
> _(Kai kshetron mein ek saal ka kendrit kaam plus bahut zyaada parwah karna hi kaafi hoga.)_

---

Bas kuch hi ghante bache the. Maine khud ko khidki se baahar jhaankte hue pakda jab subah ki shuruati roshni mere samne ki buildings par chamak (glittered) rahi thi. Yeh ek sardi ki thandak bhari (crisp) fall (sharat ritu) ka din tha, ek aise city ke liye hairatangez roop se sunny (dhoop wala) jo apni baarish ke liye famous hai. Achhe kapde pehne mard briefcases liye hue the aur fashionable auraten meri eleventh-story (gyarahvin-manzil) ke nazaare (vantage point) ke neeche chote-chote miniature dogs ko le ja rahi thi. Buses weekend se pehle aakhiri baar anichhit (reluctant) commuters (aane-jaane walon) ko town ke andar khinch rahi thi. City shayad apni neend (slumber) se jaag raha tha, lekin main dawn (bhor/subah-savere) se pehle se hi jaga hua tha.

"Abhi daydreaming (khayali pulao pakane) ka samay nahi hai," maine apne aap ko yaad dilaya aur apna dhayan apne samne notebook par likhe aadhe-adhure math ke problems par wapas shift kiya. “Show that for any finite part of the unit sphere . . .” problem shuru hua. Yeh class Massachusetts Institute of Technology ke liye _Multivariate Calculus_ thi. Final exam jald hi shuru hone wala tha, aur mere paas prepare karne ke liye bahut kam samay bacha tha. Curl kya tha, phir se... ? Maine apni aankhein close kin aur apne head mein problem ki ek picture banane ki koshish ki.

Wahan ek sphere (gola) hai. Main woh jaanta hoon. Maine apni mind’s eye (man ki aankh) mein ek bright red ball ki kalpana (conjured) ki, jo khaali space mein float kar rahi hai. Ab n̂ kya था? n̂ ka matlab normal hai, maine apne aap ko yaad dilaya, yaani ek arrow jo surface se seedhe upar ki taraf point karta hai. Meri red ball furry (baal-daar) ho gayi, jisme hairlike vectors saare ends par seedhe khade the. Lekin curl ke baare mein kya? Meri imagination ek vishal sea mein pulsate (dhadakti) karti tiny arrows ki waves ki taraf mudi. Curl ne eddies (bhanwar) ko mark kiya, jo chote loops mein chaaron taraf swirl (ghoom) rahe the. Maine static-charged hairdo (baal khade rehne wale hairstyle) wali apni furry, red ball ke baare mein phir socha. Mere fuzzy (baal-daar) sphere mein koi whorls (ghumaav) nahi the, isliye koi curl nahi hona chahiye, maine tarka (reasoned) lagaya. Lekin main ise prove kaise karoon? Maine kuch equations neeche scratch down (likhi) kin.

Behtar hoga ise double-check kar loon. Meri mental pictures saaf thin, lekin mera symbol manipulation (chinhon ka her-pher) bahut zyaada laparwah (sloppier) tha. Zyaada waqt nahi bacha tha, aur preparation ka har ek second keemti tha. Mujhe samay khatam hone se pehle jitne ho sake utne problems ke beech grind through (mehnat se nikalna) karne ki zarurat thi.

Yeh ek MIT student ke liye kuch bhi unusual (asadharn) nahi tha. Pechida equations, amurt (abstract) concepts, aur mushkil proofs sabhi math aur science mein duniya ki sabse pratisthit (prestigious) educations mein se ek ka normal hissa hain. Sivaye iske ki main ek MIT student nahi tha. In fact, main kabhi Massachusetts gaya bhi nahi tha. Yeh sab mere bedroom mein ho raha تھا, pachees sau miles door Vancouver, Canada mein. Aur halanki ek MIT student aam taur par ek semester ke dauran multivariate calculus ke poore hisse ko cover karta hai, maine sirf paanch din pehle shuru kiya تھا.

## The MIT Challenge

_(MIT Challenge)_

Maine kabhi MIT mein padhai nahi ki hai. Iske bajaye, mere college ke din University of Manitoba mein business padhte hue beete the, jo ek middle-ranked Canadian school tha jise main actually afford kar sakta था. Bachelor of commerce ke saath graduate karne ke baad, mujhe aisa feel hua jaise maine galat major (mukhya vishay) chuna tha. Main ek entrepreneur banna chahta تھا aur isliye business padha tha, yeh sochte hue ki apna khud ka boss banne ka yeh sabse behtar raasta (route) hoga. Char saal baad, maine discover kiya ki ek business major bade corporations, gray suits, aur standard operating procedures (manak sanchalan prakriyaon) ki duniya mein enter karne walon ke liye largely (mukhya roop se) ek finishing school (shishtachar sikhane wala school) tha.

Computer science, iske ulat (contrast), ek aisa major tha jahan aap actually cheezon ko banana seekhte the. Programs, websites, algorithms, aur artificial intelligence wahi the jinhone mujhe pehli jagah entrepreneurship mein interest jagaya tha, aur main struggles kar raha tha yeh faisla karne mein ki is baare mein kya kiya jaye.

Main wapas school ja sakta hoon, maine socha. Phir se enroll (daakhila) loon. Ek doosri degree ke liye kaam karte hue aur char saal bitaoon. Lekin student loans lena aur college ki amlashahi (bureaucracy) aur rules ko repeat karne ke liye apni life ka aadha decade (dashak) chhod dena bahut zyaada appealing (aakarshak) nahi laga. Jo main chahta tha use seekhne ka koi behtar raasta hona hi chahiye tha.

Uss samay ke aas-paas, main MIT mein padhai jaane wali aur online post ki gayi ek class se takraya (stumbled across). Isme fully recorded lectures, assignments, aur quizzes the; yahan tak ki asli class mein use kiye gaye actual exams solution keys ke saath provide kiye gaye the. Maine class lene ki koshish karne ka faisla kiya. Mere surprise ke liye, maine paaya ki yeh class un zyaadatar classes se kahin behtar thi jinhein university mein attend karne ke liye maine hazaron dollars pay kiye the. Lectures polished (saaf-suthre) the, professor engaging (dilchasp) the, aur material fascinating tha. Mazeed dig further (gehrai mein dhoondhne) par, main dekh sakta tha ki yeh akeli class nahi thi jise MIT free mein offer kar raha tha. MIT ne saikdon different classes se material upload kiya tha. Maine socha ki kya yeh meri problem ka solution ho sakta hai. Agar koi bhi free mein ek MIT class ka content seekh sakta hai, toh kya ek poori degree ka content seekhna possible hoga?

Is tarah ek project mein lagbhag cheh mahine ki intense research shuru hui jise maine _The MIT Challenge_ naam diya. Maine computer science undergrads ke liye actual MIT curriculum ko dekha. Maine us list ko un resources ke saath match aur compare kiya jo MIT online offer karta tha. Unfortunately (durbhagya se), yeh kehna aasan tha aur karna bahut mushkil. MIT ka OpenCourseWare, jo class material upload karne ke liye use kiya jaane wala platform tha, uska maqsad kabhi bhi school attend karne ka ek vikalp (substitute) banna nahi tha. Kuch classes simply offer hi nahi ki gayi thin aur unhein swap out (badalna) karne ki zarurat thi. Doosri classes mein itna scant (kam/adhura) material tha ki maine socha kya unhein complete karna possible bhi hoga.

_Computation Structures_, jo zaroori courses mein se ek tha, jo sikhata tha ki circuits aur transistors ka use karke shuruat se computer kaise banaya jaye, usme koi recorded lectures ya assigned textbook nahi thi. Class content ko seekhne ke liye, mujhe lecture ke saath chalne ke liye bani ek slideshow par likhe abstract symbols ko decode/samajhna (decipher) karna hoga. Missing materials aur aspasht (ambiguous) evaluation criteria (moolyankan manandand) ka matlab tha ki har ek class ko exactly ek MIT student ki tarah karna out of the question (bematlab/asamhav) tha. Halanki, ek simpler approach kaam kar sakti hai: bas final exams ko pass karne ki koshish karo.

Final exams par yeh focus baad mein un classes ke liye programming projects ko shamil karne tak badh gaya jinke paas woh the. In do criteria ne ek MIT degree ka skeleton (dhancha) banaya, jisme zyaada tar knowledge aur skills cover the jinhein main seekhna chahta था, bina kisi dikhaawe (frills) ke. Koi mandatory (anivarya) attendance policy nahi. Assignments par koi due dates nahi. Final exams jab bhi main ready hota tab liye ja sakte the aur agar main kisi mein fail ho jata toh ek alternate exam ke saath retake (phir se dena) kiye ja sakte the. Sudden jo shuruat mein ek nuksaan (disadvantage) lag raha tha—MIT tak physical access na hona—ek fayda (advantage) ban gaya. Main cost, samay aur simaon (constraints) ke ek chhote hisse (fraction) mein ek MIT student ki education ka anuman (approximate) laga sakta था.

Is possibility ko mazeed explore karte hue, maine nayi approach ka use karke ek test class bhi ki. Prescheduled lectures mein dikhne ke bajaye, maine class ke liye downloaded videos ko normal speed se dugni raftaar par dekha. Har ek assignment ko meticulous tareeqe se karne aur apne results jaan'ne ke liye hafton wait karne ke bajaye, main ek baar mein ek question karke material par apna test le sakta tha, apni galtiyon se jaldi seekhte hue. In aur doosre methods ka use karke, maine paaya ki main ek hafte jitne kam samay mein ek class se nikal (scrape through) sakta hoon. Kuch quick calculations karke aur error (galti) ke liye kuch room add karte hue, maine faisla kiya ki baki bachi unpredictable thirty-two classes se ek saal se kam mein nipatna possible ho sakta hai.

Halanki yeh ek personal quest (khoj) ke roop mein shuru hua tha, main dekhne laga tha ki mere chhote project se pare bade prabhav (implications) the. Technology ne learning ko pehle se kahin zyaada aasan bana diya hai, phir bhi tuition costs explode (tezi se badh) rahi hain. Ek char saal ki degree ek decent job ka ek aashwasan (assurance) hua karti thi. Ab yeh mushkil se door mein ek kadam (foot in the door) rakhne jaisa hai. Sabse behtar careers sophisticated (jatil/uchh-stariya) skills ki demand karte hain jinpar aap shayad hi chance se takrayenge. Na keval programmers balki managers, entrepreneurs, designers, doctors, aur lagbhag har ek doosra profession required knowledge aur skills ko rapidly accelerate (tezi se badhana) kar raha hai, aur kai log keep up (sath chalne) mein struggle kar rahe hain. Mere mind ke pichle hisse mein, mujhe na keval computer science mein interest tha balki yeh dekhne mein bhi tha ki kya kaam aur life mein required skills par maharat haasil (master) karne ka koi naya raasta ho sakta hai.

Jaise hi mera dhayan ek baar phir meri khidki ke baahar develop ho rahe scene par gaya, maine socha ki yeh sab kaise shuru hua tha. Maine socha ki agar lagbhag teen saal pehle ek doosre continent par ek tivra, sharab na peene wale (teetotaling) Irishman ke saath ek akasmat mulaqat (chance encounter) na hui hoti, toh main apne is ajeeb chote experiment ki koshish bilkul nahi kar raha hota.

## Fluent in Three Months?

_(Teen Mahine Mein Faraatedar?)_

"Meri problem French logon se nahi hai—bas Parisians se hai," Benny Lewis ne Paris ke heart (bichon-beech) mein ek Italian restaurant mein mujhse apna gussa nikaala (vented). Lewis vegetarian the, steak tartare aur foie gras ke liye famous country mein accommodate (tal-mel bithana) karna hamesha aasan nahi hota. _Penne arrabbiata_ ki ek plate khate hue, jo ek favorite unhone Italy mein ek youth hostel mein kaam karne ke dauran pick kiya tha, Lewis fluent French mein bol rahe the, is baat ki parwah kiye bina ki kya koi locals unki complaints (shikayaton) ko sun raha hai. Unki na-khushi (discontent) Paris mein ek engineering firm mein ek stagiaire (trainee) ke roop mein kaam karne wale ek khhasakar udas (dreary) saal se paid hui thi. Unhone France ke sabse bade city mein badnam job demands aur social life ke saath adjust karna mushkil paaya tha. Phir bhi, unhone socha, shayad unhein zyaada aashlochnatmak (critical) nahi hona chahiye. Akhirkar, yeh wahi experience tha jisne unhein ek engineer ke roop mein apni life chhodne aur languages seekhte hue duniya bhar mein travel karne ke liye prerit kiya tha.

Mera parichay Lewis se personal frustration (niraasha) ke ek moment ke dauran hua tha. Main ek student exchange program ke hisse ke roop mein France mein reh raha tha. Main saal ka ant bina kisi mehnat ke (effortless) French bolne ki high hopes ke saath ghar se nikla tha, lekin cheezein us tarah se banti hui nahi dikh rahi thin. Mere zyaadatar doston ne mujhse English mein baat ki, jisme French dost bhi shamil the, aur aisa feel hona shuru ho raha tha jaise ek saal kaafi nahi hoga.

Maine is sthiti (state of affairs) ke baare mein apne ghar ke ek dost se shikayat ki; usne mujhe ek aise bande ke baare mein bataya jiske baare mein usne suna tha jo country to country travel karta tha, apne aap ko teen mahine mein ek bhasha seekhne ka challenge deta tha. "Bakwaas (Bullshit)," maine jalan (envy) ke ek ishaare se zyaada ke saath kaha. Yahan main immersion (bhasha ke maahol mein doobna) ke mahino baad logon se chat karne ke liye struggle kar raha tha, aur yeh banda sirf teen mahine baad aisa karne ke liye apne aap ko challenge de raha تھا. Apne shakk (skepticism) ke bavajood, main jaanta tha ki mujhe Lewis se milne ki zarurat hai yeh dekhne ke liye ki kya woh learning languages ke baare mein kuch aisa samajhte hain jo main nahi jaanta tha. Ek email aur ek train ride ke baad, aur Lewis aur main face-to-face mil rahe the.

"Hamesha ek challenge rakho," Lewis ne mujhe bataya jab unhone apni life advice jaari rakhi, ab lunch ke baad central Paris ke ek tour par mera marghdarshan (guiding) karte hue: Paris ke baare mein Lewis ke pehle ke feelings ab naram (soften) hone lage the, aur jaise hi hum Notre Dame se Louvre tak chale, unka mood city mein unke dino ke baare mein atit ki yaadon mein dooba (nostalgic) ho gaya. Unke strong opinions aur passions, jaisa main baad mein seekhunga, na keval unhein ambitious challenges lene ke liye fuel (prerit) karte the balki unhein trouble mein bhi daal sakte the. Unhein ek baar Brazilian federal police ne tab hiraasat mein liya (detained) tha jab ek immigration officer ne unhein baahar doston se Portuguese mein uspar kasam khate (cursing) hue sun liya tha jab usne unke visa extension ko deny (mana) kar diya tha. Irony (vengya) yeh tha ki unka visa isliye deny kiya gaya kyunki us officer ko vishwas nahi tha ki itne chhote stay se unki Portuguese itni achhi ho sakti hai, aur use unpar secretly apne tourist visa ke terms ke baare mein bina bataye Brazil mein immigrate (palaayan) karne ki koshish karne ka shak tha.

Jaise hi hum chalna jaari rakhte hain, ab Eiffel Tower ke samne grounds par, Lewis ne apna approach explain kiya: Pehle hi din bolna shuru karo. Strangers se baat karne se mat daro. Shuruat karne ke liye ek phrasebook ka use karo; formal study ko baad ke liye save karo. Vocabulary ko yaad karne ke liye visual mnemonics (smaran-sahayak nishaniyon) ka use karo. Jis cheez ne mujhe hit kiya woh methods nahi the balki woh nidarrta (boldness) thi jiske saath unhone unhein apply kiya tha. Jabki main darr-darr ke kuch French pick up karne ki koshish kar raha tha, galat cheezein kehne aur apni insufficient (aparyapt) vocabulary se sharminda (embarrassed) hone ke baare mein chintit tha, Lewis nidarr (fearless) the, seedhe conversations mein dive karte hue aur apne liye seemingly (dekhne mein) impossible challenges set karte hue.

Us approach ne unki achhi madad ki thi. Woh pehle se hi Spanish, Italian, Gaelic, French, Portuguese, Esperanto, aur English mein faraatedar (fluent) the aur haal hi mein Czech Republic mein teen mahine rehne ke dauran ek conversational level tak pahunch gaye the. Lekin yeh unka sabse naya challenge tha jise woh plan kar rahe the jisne mujhe sabse zyaada utsuk kiya (intrigued): engineering ki tarah just teen mahine baad German mein fluency.

Yeh, strictly speaking (sahi mayne mein), Lewis ka German ke saath pehli baar nahi था. Unhone high school mein paanch saal tak German classes li thin aur pehle do baar briefly Germany visit kiya tha. Halanki, school mein ek bhasha seekhne mein samay bitane waale kai students ki tarah, woh abhi bhi ise bol nahi sakte the. Unhone embarrassment ke saath admit (swikar) kiya, "Agar main chahta toh German mein breakfast ka order bhi nahi de sakta tha." Phir bhi, ek decade (dashak) se pehle li gayi classes se bani anupyogi knowledge (unused knowledge) shayad unke challenge ko shuruat se (scratch) shuru karne ke mukable aasan bana degi. Kam hui difficulty ko compensate (barabar) karne ke liye, Lewis ne daanv badhane (raise the stakes) ka faisla kiya.

Normally, woh apne aap ko teen mahine baad ek bhasha mein B2 level ke barabar pahunche ka challenge dete the. B2 level—A1, A2, B1 se shuru hone wale cheh levels mein se chautha—use Common European Framework of Reference for Languages (CEFR) dwara upper intermediate (uchh-madhyamik) ke roop mein describe kiya jata hai, jo speaker ko "fluency aur spontaneity (sahajta) ki ek aisi degree ke saath interact karne ki izazat deta hai jo native speakers ke saath niyamit interaction ko dono pakshon ke liye bina kisi tanav (strain) ke kabil banata hai." Halanki, apne German challenge ke liye, Lewis ne offer kiye gaye sabse highest exam level par jaane ka faisla kiya: C2.

Yeh level bhasha par ek poori maharat (complete mastery) ko represent karta hai. Ek C2 level tak pahunche ke liye, learner ko "suni ya padhi gayi lagbhag har ek cheez ko ease (aasaani) ke saath samajhna" chahiye aur "apne aap ko spontaneously, bahut fluently aur precisely (sateek tareeqe se) express karna chahiye, yahan tak ki sabse jatil (complex) situations mein bhi matlab ke finer shades (baareek farq) ko alag karte hue." Goethe-Institut, jo exam ko sanchalit (administers) karta hai, is benchmark (manak) tak pahunche ke liye kam se kam 750 hours ki instruction ki salah deta hai, jisme classroom ke baahar ka vyapak abhyas (extensive practice) shamil nahi hai.

Kuch mahino baad, maine Lewis se unke project ke baare mein wapas suna. Woh ek baal barabar (hair) se C2 exam pass karne ke apne goal se chhook gaye the. Unhone apne exam ke paanch mein se char criteria pass kar liye the lekin listening comprehension (sun kar samajhne wala) section mein fail ho gaye the. "Maine radio sunne mein bahut zyaada waqt bita diya," unhone khud ko fatkaara (chastised). "Mujhe mazeed active listening practice karni chahiye thi." Teen mahine ke intense practice mein fluency unse bach nikli (eluded) thi, halanki woh hairatangez roop se paas pahunch gaye the. Is Irish bahubhashi (polyglot) ke saath meri pehli mulaqat ke saat saal baad, unhone aadha dozen se zyaada doosre countries mein apne teen-month challenge ka attempt karna jaari rakkha hai, apne bhashayi sangrah (linguistic repertoire) mein kuch Arabic, Hungarian, Mandarin Chinese, Thai, American Sign Language, aur yahan tak ki Klingon (ijaad ki gayi Star Trek bhasha) ko add kiya hai.

Jis cheez ko maine us samay realize nahi kiya tha lekin ab samajhta hoon woh yeh thi ki Lewis ke accomplishments (uplabdhiyan) aisi koi rare (durlabh) nahi thin. Akeli bhashayi carnamo (linguistic feats) ke space mein, main aise hyperpolyglots se mila hoon jo forty-plus bhashayein bolte hain, adventurer-anthropologists (sahasik-manavvigyanik) jo exposure ke kuch ghante baad pehle se anjaan bhashayein bolna shuru kar sakte hain, aur Lewis ki tarah kai doosre travelers, jo tourist visa se tourist visa par hop karte hain, nayi bhashon par maharat haasil karte hue. Maine yeh bhi dekha ki avishwasniya results (incredible results) ke saath aakramak swa-shiksha (aggressive self-education) ka yeh phenomenon (prapanch/tathya) akeli bhashon tak seemit nahi tha.

## How Roger Craig Gamed Jeopardy!

_(Roger Craig Ne Jeopardy! Ko Kaise Game Diya)_

“What is The Bridge on the River Kwai?” Roger Craig ne jaldi se (hastily) apne screen par question scratch down (likha). Film ke title ke aakhiri word ki legibility (padhne yogya) par pehle fumbling (ladkhadane) ke bavajood, Craig sahi the. Unhone $77,000 jeete the—jo us samay Jeopardy! ke history mein sabse highest single-day winnings thi. Craig ki victory koi fluke (tuka) nahi thi. Unhone phir se records tode, lagbhag do lakh dollars ikhatha (amassing) kiye, jo abhi tak ka sabse highest five-game winning streak (lagataar jeet) tha.

Aisa carnama apne aap mein remarkable hota, lekin jo cheez isse bhi zyaada incredible thi woh yeh thi ki unhone ise kaise kiya. Us moment par reflect (vichar) karte hue, Craig kehte hain, "Mera pehla thought yeh nahi tha 'Wow, maine abhi satattar hazar dollars jeet liye.' Yeh tha 'Whoa, meri site ne sach mein kaam kiya.'"

Aap ek aise test ke liye kaise study karte hain jo koi bhi question pooch sakta hai? Yeh mukhya problem thi jiska Craig ne compete karne ki preparation karte waqt samna kiya. Jeopardy! home audiences ko aisi trivia questions se chakkar mein dalne (stumping) ke liye famous hai jo Danish kings se lekar Damocles tak kisi bhi cheez ke baare mein pooch sakti hain. Is tarah Jeopardy! ke bade champions dimaagi know-it-alls (sab-jaanne-waale) hote hain jinhone kisi bhi topic par answers ugalne (spit out) ke liye required factual knowledge ki vishal library ko ikhatha karne mein ek lifetime bitaya hota hai. Jeopardy! ke liye study karna ek impossible task jaisa feel ho sakta hai, kyunki aapko lagbhag har ek conceivable (sochne yogya) subject ka study karna hoga. Halanki, Craig ka solution knowledge ko acquire (haasil) karne ki process par hi phir se vichar karna tha. Aisa karne ke liye, unhone ek website banayi.

"Har koi jo kisi game mein succeed hona chahta hai woh game ki practice karne wala hai," Craig tark karte hain (contends). "Aap haphazardly practice kar sakte hain, ya aap efficiently (kushalata se) practice kar sakte hain."

Records todne ke liye required wide-ranging trivia ko amassing karne ke liye, unhone is baare mein nishthurta se vishleshnatmak (ruthlessly analytical) hone ka faisla kiya ki unhone knowledge kaise acquire ki. Peshe se ek computer scientist (computer vigyanik), unhone ever aired (abhi tak prasharit) har ek Jeopardy! game se daso hazar questions aur answers ko download karke shuruat karne ka faisla kiya. Unhone mahino tak apne free time mein unpar apna test liya, aur phir, jaise hi yeh saaf ho gaya ki woh television par jaane wale hain, unhone full-time aakramak roop se questions par quizzing (khud se sawaal-javaab) karna shuru kar diya. Phir unhone questions ko different topics, jaise art history, fashion, aur science mein vargikrit (categorize) karne ke liye text-mining software apply kiya. Unhone apni strengths aur weaknesses ko map karne ke liye data visualization ka use kiya. Text-mining software ne different topics ko separate kiya, jinhein unhone different circles ke roop mein visualize kiya. Unke graph par kisi bhi diye gaye circle ki position dikhati thi ki woh us topic mein kitne achhe the—higher ka matlab tha ki woh us topic ke baare mein zyaada jaante the. Circle ka size indicate karta tha ki woh topic kitna frequent (baar-baar aane wala) tha. Bade circles zyaada common the aur isliye mazeed study ke liye behtar choices the.

Show ke andar variety aur randomness (anischitta) ke neeche, unhone hidden patterns ko uncover (ujagar) karna shuru kiya. Show mein kuch clues “Daily Doubles” hote hain, jo ek pratiyogi (contestant) ko apna score double karne, ya sab kuch lose karne ki izazat dete hain. Yeh behad keemti clues randomly placed lag sakte hain, lekin poore Jeopardy! ke archives unke fingertips par hone ki wajah se, Craig ne paaya ki unki position trends ko follow karti thi. Koi bhi categories ke beech hop (kood kar) karke aur high-point clues par focus karke keemti Doubles ko hunt out (dhoondh) sakta tha, single category ke andar tab tak tike rehne ke show ke paramparagat approach (conventional approach) ko todte hue jab tak ki woh complete na ho jaye.

Craig ne poochay gaye questions ke types ke andar bhi trends paaye. Halanki Jeopardy! sochne yogya roop se kisi bhi topic par questions pooch sakta tha, game ka format home audience ko entertain karne ke liye design kiya gaya hai, competitors ko challenge karne ke liye nahi. Is tarka ko follow karte hue, Craig ne paaya ki woh kisi category ke andar sabse behtar jaani jaane wali trivia ka study karke nikal sakte hain, bajaye kisi particular direction mein gehra dig (khodne) karne ke. Agar koi subject specialized (vishingt) tha, toh woh jaante the ki answers sabse behtar jaane gaye examples ki taraf geared (mude) honge. Archival questions par apni khud ki weakness ka vishleshan (analyzing) karke, woh dekh sakte the ki unhein competitive hone ke liye kaun se topics ka mazeed study karne ki zarurat hai. For example, unhone paaya ki woh fashion par weak the aur unhone us topic ko mazeed gehrai se study karne par focus kiya.

Kya study karna hai yeh figure out karne ke liye analytics ka use karna sirf pehla step tha. Wahan se, Craig ne apni efficiency ko maximize karne ke liye spaced-repetition software ka istemal kiya. Spaced-repetition software ek advanced flash card algorithm hai jise pehli baar 1980s mein Polish researcher Piotr Woźniak dwara develop kiya gaya tha. Woźniak ka algorithm material ko yaad rakhne ke liye aapko use kab review karne ki zarurat hai iske samay ko anukoolit (optimally time) karne ke liye design kiya gaya تھا. Facts ke ek bade database ko dekhte hue, zyaadatar log jo pehle seekhte hain use bhool jayenge, use tikane ke liye baar-baar apne aap ko yaad dilane ki zarurat hoti hai. Algorithm har ek fact ko review karne ke liye optimal samay calculate karke is problem ko theek karta hai taaki aap same jankari ko overdrilling (zarurat se zyaada abhyas) karke energy waste na karein, lekin isliye bhi taaki aap jo pehle seekh chuke hain use bhoolein nahi. Is tool ne Craig ko un hazaron facts ko efficiently memorize (yaad) karne ki izazat di jinqi unhein apni baad ki victory ke liye zarurat hone wali thi.

Halanki show per day sirf ek episode air karta hai, Jeopardy! ek baar mein paanch episodes tape karta hai. Craig lagataar paanch games jeetne ke baad apne hotel room mein wapas aa rahe the, aur woh soo nahi sake. Unhone kaha, "Aap game ko simulate kar sakte hain, lekin aap paanch ghante mein do lakh dollars jeetne aur ek game show par single-day record set karne ko simulate nahi kar sakte jis par aap tab se jaana chahte the jab aap baarah saal ke the." Aprathagat takshon (unorthodox tactics) aur aakramak vishleshan (aggressive analysis) ko combine karke, unhone game show ko game de diya tha aur jeet gaye the.

Roger Craig akele insaan nahi the jinhe maine paaya tha jinki kismat (fortunes) aakramak swa-shiksha (aggressive self-education) ke nateejay mein badal gayi thi. Main us samay yeh nahi jaanta tha, lekin 2011 mein, jis saal mera MIT Challenge shuru hone wala tha, Eric Barone apni khud ki ek dhun (obsession) shuru kar rahe the. Halanki, mere mukable, unki koshishon ka vistar (extend) lagbhag paanch saal tak hone wala tha aur unhein kai poori tarah se different skills par maharat haasil karne ki zarurat thi.

## From Minimum Wage to Millionaire

_(Minimum Wage Se Millionaire Tak)_

Eric Barone ne abhi University of Washington Tacoma se computer science mein degree ke saath graduate kiya tha jab unhone socha, _Abhi mera chance hai._ Unhone faisla kiya tha ki woh apne khud ke video games banana chahte hain aur abhi, isse pehle ki woh ek salaried programming job mein comfortable hon, unke paas is baare mein kuch karne ka opportunity tha. Unke paas pehle se hi unki inspiration thi. Woh apne game ko _Harvest Moon_ ke prati ek samman (homage) dena chahte the, jo games ki ek charming Japanese series thi jisme player ko ek safal farm (kheti) banana hota hai: crops ugana, animals paalna, countryside ko explore karna, aur doosre villagers ke saath relationships banana. "Mujhe us game se pyaar tha," unhone us title ke saath apne childhood experience ke baare mein kaha. "Lekin yeh isse kahin behtar ho sakta tha." Woh jaante the ki agar unhone apne khud ke vision ko follow through (poora) nahi kiya, toh woh improved version kabhi ek reality nahi ban payega.

Ek commercially safal video game develop karna aasan nahi hai. AAA game companies hundreds of millions of dollars ka budget rakhti hain aur apne top titles par hazaron logon ko employ karti hain. Required talent bhi similarly broad (vyapak) hota hai. Game development ke liye programming, visual art, musical composition, story writing, game design, aur develop kiye gaye game ke genre aur style ke aadhar par daso aur skills ki zarurat hoti hai. Required skills ki choudai (breadth) game development ko choti teams ke liye doosre art forms jaise music, writing, ya visual arts ke mukable bahut zyaada harder banati hai. Yahan tak ki highly talented independent game developers ko aam taur par required saari skills ko span (sametne) karne ke liye kuch logon ke saath collaborate (sath milkar kaam) karna padta hai. Halanki, Eric Barone ne poori tarah se akele apne game par kaam karne ka faisla kiya.

Akele kaam karne ka faisla unke apne vision ke prati ek personal commitment aur ek unthak aatmavishwas (indefatigable self-confidence) se aaya tha ki woh game ko khatam kar sakte hain. "Main apne khud ke vision par complete control rakhna pasand karta hoon," unhone explain kiya, yeh kehte hue ki design ke mamle mein "un logon ko dhoondhna impossible ho sakta tha jo same page par (ek jaisi soch wale) hon." Halanki, us choice ka matlab tha ki unhein game programming, music composition, pixel art, sound design, aur story writing mein kushal (proficient) banna hoga. Sirf ek game design project se kahin zyaada, Barone ki is yatra (odyssey) mein game design ke hi har ek aspect par maharat haasil karna shamil hoga.

Pixel art Barone ki sabse badi weakness thi. Art ka yeh style video games ke pehle ke daur ki yaad dilata hai (harkens back) jab slow computers par graphics ko render karna mushkil hota tha. Pixel art fluid lines ya photorealistic textures ke saath nahi kiya jata hai. Iske bajaye, computer graphics banane wale colored dots, yaani pixels ko ek baar mein ek karke rakhne dwara ek compelling image banayi jaani chahiye—ek mehnat-bhara (painstaking) aur mushkil kaam. Ek pixel artist ko colored squares ke grid se movement, emotion, aur life ko convey karna hota hai. Barone ko doodle aur draw karna pasand tha, lekin usne unhein is difficulty ke liye prepare nahi kiya tha. Unhein yeh skill "poori tarah se shuruat se (scratch)" seekhni thi. Apne art skills ko ek commercial level tak laana aasan nahi tha. "Maine zyaadatar artwork ko teen se paanch baar dobara kiya hoga," unhone kaha. "Character portraits ke liye, maine unhein kam se kam das baar kiya."

Barone ki strategy simple lekin effective thi. Unhone un graphics par directly kaam karke practice ki jinhein woh apne game mein use karna chahte the. Unhone apne khud ke kaam ka aalochnatmak moolyankan (critiqued) kiya aur iski comparison us art se ki jise woh admire karte the. "Maine ise scientifically todne ki koshish ki," unhone explain kiya. "Main apne aap se poochta tha, 'Mujhe yeh kyun pasand hai? Mujhe woh kyun pasand nahi hai?'" jab doosre artists ke kaam ko dekhte the. Unhone pixel art theory ke baare mein padh kar aur un tutorials ko dhoondh kar apni practice ko purna kiya (supplemented) jo unke knowledge ke gaps ko fill kar sakte the. Jab unhein apne art mein koi difficulty aati, toh woh use tod dete: "Maine poocha, 'Main kis goal tak pahunchna chahta hoon?' aur phir 'Main wahan kaise pahunch sakta hoon?'" game par apne kaam ke kisi point par, unhein feel hua ki unke colors bahut zyaada dull (fike) aur boring the. "Main chahta tha ki colors pop (chamkein) karein," unhone kaha. Isliye unhone color theory par research ki aur doosre artists ka tivra study kiya yeh dekhne ke liye ki unhone cheezon ko visually interesting banane ke liye colors ka use kaise kiya.

Pixel art sirf ek single aspect tha jise Barone ko seekhna tha. Unhone apne game ke liye saari music bhi compose ki, apni high expectations ko poora karne ke liye ise ek se zyaada baar scratch se redoing (dobara) kiya. Game mechanics ke poore sections develop kiye gaye aur scrap (phenk) diye gaye jab woh unke kade manandando (rigorous standards) ko poora karne mein fail ho gaye. Directly practice karne aur cheezon ko redoing karne ki is process ne unhein game design ke sabse aspects mein steadily behtar banane ki izazat di. Halanki isne game ko complete karne mein lagne wale samay ko lamba kar diya, isne unke finished product ko specialized artists, programmers, aur composers ki ek army dwara banaye gaye games ke saath compete karne ke kabil bhi banaya.

Poore paanch saal ke development process ke dauran, Barone ne ek computer programmer ke roop mein employment dhoondhne se parhez kiya. "Main kisi substantial (badi/thos) cheez mein involve nahi hona chahta تھا," unhone kaha. "Mere paas samay nahi hota, aur main game development ko apna sabse behtar shot dena chahta tha." Iske bajaye, unhone ek theater usher (darshak-prabandhak) ke roop mein kaam kiya, minimum wage (nyuntam mazdoori) kamate hue taaki woh bhatak (distracted) na jayein. Unki job se unki mamuli kamayi (meager earnings) ne, unki girlfriend ke support ke saath milkar, Barone ko gujara karne ki izazat di jab unhone apne passion par focus kiya.

Us passion aur maharat ke prati samarpan (dedication to mastery) ne fayda pahunchaya (paid off). Barone ne February 2016 mein _Stardew Valley_ release ki. Game quickly ek surprise hit ban gaya, computer game platform Steam par offer kiye jaane wale kai bade-studio titles se zyaada bikte hue. Multiple platforms par, Barone ka anuman hai ki iske release ke pehle saal ke andar, _Stardew Valley_ ki 3 million se zyaada copies bik chuki thin. Mahinon mein, woh minimum wage kamane wale ek anjaan designer se ek millionaire ban gaye jinhein game development ke andar _Forbes’ “30 Under 30”_ stars mein se ek ke roop mein naamit kiya gya. Skills par maharat haasil karne ke unke samarpan ne us safalata mein koi chhota part nahi nibhaya. _Destructoid_ ne, Stardew Valley ke apne review mein, artwork ko "hairatangez roop se aakarshak aur khoobsurat (incredibly endearing and beautiful)" describe kiya. Barone ke apne vision ke prati commitment aur aakramak swa-shiksha ne unhein shandaar fayda pahunchaya tha.

## The MIT Challenge and Beyond

_(MIT Challenge Aur Usse Pare)_

Apne tang (cramped) apartment mein wapas, main apne calculus exam ko grade kar raha था. Yeh tough tha, lekin aisa lag raha tha jaise main pass ho gaya hoon. Mujhe raahat mili, lekin yeh relax karne ka samay nahi tha. Agle Monday, main ek naye course ke saath phir se sab kuch shuru kar raha hunga, aur mere paas abhi bhi lagbhag ek saal baki tha.

Jaise-jaise calendar badla, waise-waise meri strategies bhi badlin. Maine keval kuch dino mein ek single class karne ki koshish se badalkar ek mahina parallel (saath-saath) mein teen se char classes karne mein bitana shuru kiya. Mujhe umeed thi ki yeh learning ko ek lambe samay par phaila dega aur cramming (ratta maarne) ke kuch negative effects ko kam karega. Jaise-jaise maine mazeed progress ki, main thoda slow bhi hua. Meri pehli kuch classes aakramak jaldi (aggressive haste) ke saath ki gayi thin taaki main apni self-imposed deadline ko poora karne ke liye schedule par reh sakoon. Yeh lagne ke baad ki main khatam kar sakta hoon, main per week sixty hours study karne se shift hokar thirty-five to forty study karne mein kabil raha. Finally, September 2012 mein, mere shuru karne ke baarah mahinon se kam samay baad, maine final class khatam ki.

Project ko complete karna mere liye aankhein kholne wala (eye-opening) tha. Saalon tak, maine socha tha ki cheezon ko gehrai se seekhne ka akela tarika school se nikalna (push through school) tha. Is project ko khatam karne ne mujhe na keval yeh sikhaya ki yeh dharana (assumption) false thi balki yeh alternate path mazeed fun aur exciting ho sakta hai. University mein, maine aksar stifled (ghuta hua) feel kiya tha, boring lectures ke dauran jaagne ki koshish karte hue, busywork assignments ke beech ghiste hue, apne aap ko sirf grade paane ke liye aisi cheezon ko seekhne par majboor karte hue jisme mujhe koi interest nahi tha. Kyunki yeh project mera apna vision aur design tha, yeh shayad hi kabhi painful feel hua, bhale hi yeh aksar challenging tha. Subjects complete kiye jaane wale baasi kaamon (stale chores) ke bajaye zinda aur exciting feel hote the. Pehli baar kabhi, maine feel kiya ki main sahi plan aur effort ke saath jo kuch bhi chahta hoon seekh sakta hoon. Possibilities endless thin, aur mera mind pahle se hi kuch naya seekhne ki taraf ghoom raha था.

Phir mujhe ek dost se ek message mila: "Tumhe pata hai, tum Reddit ke front page par ho." Internet ne mera project dhoondh liya tha, aur yeh kaafi charcha (discussion) generate kar raha tha. Kuch ko idea pasand aaya lekin unhein iski upyogita par shakk tha: "Yeh sad hai ki employers ise real degree ki tarah treat nahi karenge, bhale hi uske paas ek graduate ke barabar (ya usse zyaada) knowledge kyun na ho." Ek user ne, jisne ek software company ke liye R&D ka head hone ka claim kiya tha, disagree kiya: "Yeh is tarah ka insaan hai jise main chahta hoon. Mujhe sach mein koi parwah nahi hai ki aapke paas degree hai ya nahi." Behes chidh (raged) gayi. Kya maine actually ise kiya tha ya nahi? Kya main iske baad ek programmer ke roop mein job paa sakunga? Ek saal mein aisa karne ki koshish kyun ki? Kya main crazy (paagal) tha?

Attention ke shuruati ubaal (surge) ne doosri requests ko janam diya. Microsoft ke ek employee ne mujhe ek job interview ke liye set up karna chaha. Ek naye startup ne mujhe apni team mein join karne ke liye poocha. China ke ek publishing house ne mujhe bechaare Chinese students ke saath kuch studying tips share karne ke liye ek book deal offer ki. Halanki, woh un kaaranon mein se nahi the jinqi wajah se maine project kiya tha. Main online ek writer ke roop mein kaam karke pehle se hi khush تھا, jisne mere poore project ke dauran mujhe financially support kiya tha aur baad mein bhi aisa karna jaari rakhega. Project ke liye mera goal job paana nahi tha balki yeh dekhna tha ki kya possible hai. Apne pehle bade project ko khatam karne ke bas kuch hi mahino baad, naye projects ke liye ideas pehle se hi mere head ke andar bulbula rahe (bubbling up) the.

Maine Benny Lewis ke baare mein socha, intense self-education ki is ajeeb duniya mein mera pehla example. Unki advice ko follow karte hue, main aakhirkar French ke ek intermediate level tak pahunch gaya tha. Yeh hard work tha, aur mujhe garv (proud) tha ki main French seekhne ke liye English speakers ke ek bubble se ghire hone ki apni shuruati difficulty ke khilaf push karne mein kabil raha tha taaki gujara karne jitni French seekh sakoon. Halanki, apne MIT experience ko khatam karne ke baad, mujhmein ek naya confidence inject (bhara) hua tha jo mere paas France mein nahi tha. Kya ho agar main woh galti na karoon jo maine pichli baar ki थी? Kya ho agar, English bolne wale doston ka ek group banane aur meri French kaafi achhi hone par us bubble se baahar nikalne ke liye struggle karne ke bajaye, main Benny Lewis ki nakal (emulated) karoon aur pehle hi din se directly immersion mein dive kar jaoon? Main kitna behtar ho sakta hoon, agar mere MIT Challenge ki tarah, main kuch bhi peeche na chhodoon aur naye language ko jitna ho sake utna intensely aur effectively seekhne ke chaaron taraf sab kuch anukulit (optimize) karoon?

Jaisa ki kismat ko manzoor tha (As luck would have it), us samay ke aas-paas mera roommate grad school wapas jaane ka plan bana raha tha aur pehle travel karne ke liye kuch samay off chahta था. Hum dono saving kar rahe the, aur agar hum apne resources ko ek saath pool (ikhatha) karein aur apne trip ko plan karne ke tarike mein kifayati (frugal) hon, toh humne socha ki hum kuch exciting karne mein kabil ho sakte hain. Maine use France mein apne experiences ke baare mein bataya, dono French seekhne ke aur secretly yeh vishwas karne ke ki bahut kuch mazeed possible tha. Maine use us social bubble ke baare mein bataya jo tab bana tha jab main bhasha bole bina arrived (pahuncha) hua tha aur baad mein usse break out karna kitna mushkil raha tha. Kya ho agar, sirf yeh umeed karne ke bajaye ki aap kaafi practice karenge, aap apne aap ko koi escape route (bach nikalne ka raasta) hi na dein? Kya ho agar aap plane se utarne ke pehle hi moment se sirf wahi bhasha bolne ka commitment karein jise aap seekhne ki koshish kar rahe hain? Mera dost skeptical (shakk-mizaj) tha. Usne mujhe apne apartment ke doosri taraf se ek saal tak MIT classes study karte hue dekha tha. Mera mansik santulan (sanity) abhi bhi ek open question tha, lekin woh apni khud ki ability mein utna confident nahi tha. Woh sure nahi tha ki woh aisa kar sakta hai, halanki woh isko ek shot dene ke liye taiyar tha, jab tak ki mujhe usse succeed hone ki koi expectations na hon.

Woh project, jise mere dost aur maine “The Year Without English” title diya tha, simple tha. Hum char countries jayenge, teen-teen mahine ke liye. Har country mein plan straightforward (seedha) tha: pehle din se koi English nahi bolna, na ek doosre ke saath aur na hi kisi ke saath jisse hum milenge. Wahan se hum dekhenge ki hamare tourist visas khatam hone aur hame ek naye destination ki taraf dhakel diye jaane se pehle hum kitna seekh sakte hain.

Hamara pehla stop Valencia, Spain था. Hum abhi airport par land hi hue the jab humne apne pehle obstacle (badha) ka samna kiya. Do attractive British girls hamare paas aayin, directions maangte hue. Humne ek doosre ko dekha aur awkwardly us thodi si Spanish ko ugal diya (sputtered out) jise hum jaante the, yeh dikhava karte hue ki hum koi English nahi bolte. Woh hame nahi samjhin aur unhone humse phir se poocha, ab ek na-khush (exasperated) tone mein. Hum kuch aur Spanish par ladkhadaye aur, yeh vishwas karte hue ki hum English nahi bol sakte, woh frustration mein door chali gain. Pehle se hi, aisa laga, English na bolne ke unintended (anjaane) parinaam ho rahe the. Us ashubh shuruat (inauspicious beginning) ke bavajood, hamari Spanish ability meri umeed se bhi zyaada tezi se badhi. Spain mein do mahine baad, hum Spanish mein interact kar rahe the usse pare jo maine France ke partial immersion ke ek poore saal mein haasil kiya tha. Hum subah apne tutor ke paas jaate, ghar par thoda study karte, aur baki ka din doston ke saath hanging out karne, restaurants mein chatting karne, aur Spanish sun ko sokhne (soaking up) mein bitate. Mera dost, apne pehle ke doubts ke bavajood, cheezon ko seekhne ke is naye approach ka ek prashansak (convert) ban gaya tha. Halanki woh grammar aur vocabulary ko mere jitne aakramak roop se study karne ki parwah nahi karta tha, hamare stay ke ant tak, woh bhi Spain mein life mein seamless roop se samahit (integrating) ho raha تھا. Method hamari umeed se kahin behtar kaam kiya, aur ab hum vishvasi (believers) the.

Humne trip jaari rakkha, Portuguese seekhne ke liye Brazil gaye, Mandarin seekhne ke liye China, aur Korean seekhne ke liye South Korea gaye. Asia Spain ya Brazil ke mukable kahin zyaada harder task sabit hua. Apni preparation mein, humne assume kiya tha ki woh bhashayein European bhashon se sirf thodi si zyaada difficult hongi, halanki yeh pata chala ki woh kahin zyaada harder thin. Nateejatan, hamara no-English rule crack (tootne) laga tha, halanki humne ise jitna ho saka utna apply kiya. Bhale hi hamari Mandarin aur Korean ek chhote stay ke baad ability ke same level tak nahi pahunchi, phir bhi yeh dost banane, travel karne, aur different topics par logon ke saath converse (baatcheet) karne ke liye kaafi tha. Apne saal ke ant mein, hum confidently keh sakte the ki hum char nayi bhashayein bolte the.

Academic computer science aur language-learning ke adventures ke liye same approach ko kaam karte hue dekh kar, main slowly convince (vashibhoot) ho raha tha ki ise bahut kuch par apply kiya ja sakta hai. Mujhe bachpan mein drawing karna pasand tha, lekin zyaadatar logon ki koshishon ki tarah, mere dwara draw kiye gaye koi bhi faces awkward aur artificial (nakli) dikhte the. Maine hamesha un logon ko admire kiya tha jo quickly ek likeness (shakal) sketch kar sakte the, chahe woh street-side caricaturists (vyang-chitrkar) hon ya professional portrait painters. Maine socha ki kya MIT classes aur languages seekhne ka same approach art par bhi apply ho sakta hai.

Maine faces draw karne ki apni ability ko bhatar banane ke liye ek mahina bitane ka faisla kiya. Meri mukhya difficulty, maine realize kiya, facial features ko properly place karne mein thi. For instance, faces draw karte waqt ek common mistake eyes ko head par bahut zyaada upar rakhna hai. Zyaadatar log sochte hain ki woh head ke top do-tihaai (two-thirds) hisse mein baithti hain. Truth yeh hai ki, woh more typically head ke top aur chin ke beech aadhe raaste par hoti hain. In aur doosre biases (puvagrahon) ko door karne ke liye, maine pictures par based sketches banaye. Phir main apne phone se sketch ki ek photo leta aur original image ko apni drawing ke upar overlay (upar rakhna) kar deta. Photo ko semitransparent (ardh-paradarshi) banane ne mujhe turant dekhne ki izazat di ki kya head bahut zyaada narrow (tang) ya wide (chouda) tha, lips bahut low ya bahut high the ya maine eyes ko sahi spot par rakha tha ya nahi. Maine aisa saikdon baar kiya, unhi rapid feedback (turant pratikriya) strategies ka use karte hue jinhone MIT classes ke saath meri achhi madad ki thi. Is aur doosre strategies ko apply karte hue, main ek chhote samay ke dauran portraits draw karne mein bahut behtar hone mein kabil raha.

## Uncovering the Ultralearners

_(Ultralearners Ko Ujagar Karna)_

Satah (surface) par, Benny Lewis ke bhashayi adventures, Roger Craig ki trivia mastery, aur Eric Barone ki game development odyssey jaise projects kaafi different hain. Halanki, woh ek mazeed samanya prapanch (general phenomenon) ke instances (udaharan) ko represent karte hain jise main _ultralearning_ kehta hoon. Jaise-jaise maine mazeed gehra dig kiya, mujhe aur stories milin. Halanki woh is baat ke specifics mein differ (alag) the ki kya seekha gaya tha aur kyun, unhone charam, swa-shiksha ke projects (extreme, self-directed learning projects) ko pursue karne ka ek common thread share kiya aur unhein successfully complete karne ke liye similar tactics apply kiye.

Steve Pavlina ek ultralearner hain. Apne university schedule ko optimize karke, unhone ek triple course load liya aur teen semesters mein computer science ki degree complete ki. Pavlina ka challenge MIT courses ke saath mere apne experiment se bahut pehle ka tha aur yeh un pehli inspirations mein se ek tha jisne mujhe dikhaya ki learning time ko compress (chhota) karna possible ho sakta hai. Halanki, free online classes ke fayde ke bina kiya gaya, Pavlina ne California State University, Northridge mein attend kiya, aur computer science aur mathematics mein actual degrees ke saath graduate hue.

Diana Jaunzeikare ne computational linguistics mein ek PhD ko replicate (nakal) karne ke liye ek ultralearning project shuru kiya. Carnegie Mellon University ke doctoral program ko benchmark (manak) banate hue, woh na keval classes lena chahti thin balki original research (mool anusandhan) bhi sanchalit karna chahti thin. Unka project isliye shuru hua tha kyunki ek real doctorate paane ke liye wapas academia mein jaane ka matlab hota Google mein apni us job ko chhodna jise woh pyaar karti thin. Apne se pehle ke kai doosre ultralearners ki tarah, Jaunzeikare ka project education mein ek gap ko fill karne ki ek koshish thi jab formal alternatives unke lifestyle ke saath fit nahi baithte the.

Online communities dwara facilitated (sahulat paaye), kai ultralearners gupt roop se (anonymously) operate karte hain, unke efforts keval unverify karne yogya forum postings dwara hi dekhne yogya hote hain. Chinese-forums.com par ek aisa hi poster, jo keval username _Tamu_ se jata hai, usne shuruat se Chinese padhne ki apni process ko vyapak roop se document kiya. Char mahinon mein “har hafte 70–80+ ghante” devote (samarpit) karte hue, unhone apne aap ko HSK 5, China ke second highest Mandarin proficiency exam ko pass karne ka challenge diya.

Doosre ultralearners exams aur degrees ke paramparagat dhanchon (conventional structures) ko poori tarah se tyag (shed) dete hain. Trent Fowler ne, early 2016 mein shuru karte hue, engineering aur mathematics mein kushal banna ke liye ek saal lambi koshish shuru ki. Unhone ise _The STEMpunk Project_ title diya, jo science, technology, engineering, aur mathematics ke STEM fields jise woh cover karna chahte the aur retrofuturistic steampunk aesthetic (sundaryabodhi style) par ek khel tha. Fowler ne apne project ko modules mein split (toda) kiya. Har ek module ek particular topic ko cover karta tha, jisme computation, robotics, artificial intelligence, aur engineering shamil the, lekin formal classes ki nakal karne ke bajaye hands-on projects dwara driven (chalit) tha.

Mera samna jis bhi ultralearner se hua woh unique tha. Kuch, Tamu ki tarah, kade, self-imposed deadlines ko poora karne ke liye kashtdayak (punishing), full-time schedules ko prefer karte the. Doosre, Jaunzeikare ki tarah, full-time jobs aur kaam ki zimmedariyon (work obligations) ko maintain karte hue side mein apne projects ko manage karte the. Kuch ka maqsad standardized exams ke recognizable benchmarks, formal curricula, aur competitions jeetna tha. Doosron ne aise projects design kiye jo comparison ko chunauti dete the. Kuch specialized the, exclusively bhashon ya programming par focus karte the. Doosre ek sachche polymath (bahushrut/bahu-gyani) banna chahte the, skills ka ek highly varied set pick karte hue.

Unki vishestaon (idiosyncrasies) ke bavajood, ultralearners ke paas bahut saare shared traits (sanjha lakshan) the. Woh aam taur par akele kaam karte the, aksar apne efforts ko announce karne ke liye ek blog entry se zyaada ke bina mahino aur saalon tak parishram (toiling) karte the. Unke interests dhun (obsession) ki taraf jhukte the. Woh apni strategies ko optimize karne ke baare mein aggressive the, _interleaving practice_, _leech thresholds_, ya _keyword mnemonics_ jaise gudh (esoteric) concepts ke gun-dosh (merits) par tivra behes karte the. Sabse badhkar, woh learning ke baare mein care karte the. Seekhne ke unke motivation ne unhein intense projects se nipatne ke liye push kiya, bhale hi yeh aksar credentials (yogyata praman) ya conformity (anuroopta) ke balidan par aaya ho.

Jin ultralearners se main mila woh aksar ek doosre se anjaan (unaware) the. Is kitab ko likhne mein, main un common principles (samanya niyamon) ko ek saath lana chahta tha jinhein maine unke unique projects mein aur apne khud ke projects mein observe kiya tha. Main saari upri differences (superficial differences) aur ajeeb idiosyncrasies ko strip away (hatana) karna chahta tha aur dekhna chahta tha ki kaun si learning advice bachti hai. Main unke extreme examples se kuch aisa samanyakaran (generalize) bhi karna chahta tha jise ek ordinary student ya professional useful paa sake. Bhale hi aap mere dwara describe kiye gaye projects jitni extreme kisi cheez se nipatne ke liye ready na hon, phir bhi aisi jagah hain jahan aap ultralearners ke experience ke aadhar par aur cognitive science (bhavnatmak vigyan) ki research dwara backed (samarthit) apne approach ko adjust kar sakte hain.

Halanki ultralearners logon ka ek extreme group hain, cheezon ke prati yeh approach normal professionals aur students ke liye potential (kshamta) rakhta hai. Kya ho agar aap ek naye role, project, ya yahan tak ki profession mein transition (badlav) karne ke liye skills ko tezi se seekhne ke liye ek project create kar sakein? Kya ho agar aap apne kaam ke liye ek important skill par maharat haasil kar sakein, jaisa Eric Barone ne kiya? Kya ho agar aap Roger Craig ki tarah topics ki ek wide variety ke baare mein knowledgeable ho sakein? Kya ho agar aap ek nayi bhasha seekh sakein, ek university degree program ko simulate kar sakein, ya kisi aisi cheez mein achhe ho sakein jo abhi aapko impossible lagti hai?

Ultralearning aasan nahi hai. Yeh hard aur frustrating hai aur iske liye un limits se baahar stretch (khinchna) karne ki zarurat hoti hai jahan aap comfortable feel karte hain. Halanki, jo cheezein aap accomplish kar sakte hain woh ise effort ke layak banati hain. Aaiye ek moment yeh dekhne ki koshish mein bitayein ki exactly ultralearning kya hai aur yeh learning aur education ke sabse common approaches se kaise differ (alag) karti hai. Phir hum dekh sakte hain ki woh kaun se principles hain jo saari learning ke aadhar (underlie) hain, yeh dekhne ke liye ki ultralearners tezi se seekhne ke liye unka fayda kaise uthaate (exploit) hain.

---

# Chapter 2 — Why Ultralearning Matters

### _(Ultralearning Kyun Zaruri Hai)_

---

> _"In many fields a year of focused work plus caring a lot would be enough."_
> _(Kai kshetron mein ek saal ka kendrit kaam plus bahut zyaada parwah karna hi kaafi hoga.)_

---

Exactly ultralearning kya hai? Jabki tivra swa-shikshakon (intense autodidacts) ke is bahumukhi (eclectic) group se mera parichay asadharn learning carnamo ke examples dekhne se shuru hua tha, aage badhne ke liye hamein kuch mazeed sateek (concise) chahiye. Yahan ek asampurna paribhasha (imperfect definition) hai:

> **Ultralearning:** Skills aur knowledge haasil karne ki ek aisi strategy jo dono hai—khud ke dwara nirdeshit (self-directed) aur tivra (intense).

Pehle, ultralearning ek strategy hai. Ek strategy kisi diye gaye problem ka akela solution nahi hoti, lekin yeh ek achha solution ho sakti hai. Strategies kisi khhas situation ke liye behtar sui-suited hoti hain aur doosriyon ke liye nahi, isliye unka use karna ek choice hai, koi aadesh (commandment) nahi.

Doosre, ultralearning khud ke dwara nirdeshit (self-directed) hai. Yeh is baare mein hai ki aap kya seekhna hai aur kyun seekhna hai iske baare mein faisle kaise lete hain. Yeh possible hai ki aap poori tarah se ek self-directed learner hon aur phir bhi yeh faisla karein ki kisi khhas school mein attend karna kisi cheez ko seekhne ka sabse behtar raasta hai. Similarly, aap ek textbook mein bataye gaye steps ko bina soche-samjhe follow karke apne dum par khud ko kuch "teach yourself" (sikha) sakte hain. Self-direction is baare mein hai ki project ke liye driver’s seat par kaun baitha hai, is baare mein nahi ki yeh jagah kahan hai.

Finally, ultralearning tivra (intense) hai. Jin bhi ultralearners se main mila unhone learning mein apni kushalata (effectiveness) ko maximize karne ke liye asadharn steps uthaye. Ek nayi bhasha jise aapne abhi practice karna shuru kiya hai use nidarrta se bolne ka attempt karna, systematically daso hazar trivia questions par quizzing (drilling) karna, aur art par baar-baar tab tak kaam (iterating) karna jab tak ki yeh perfect na ho jaye, ek hard dimaagi kaam hai. Yeh aisa feel ho sakta hai jaise aapka mind apni limit par ho. Iska ulta learning ko fun ya suvidha ke liye anukulit (optimized) karna hai: kisi language-learning app ko chuna kyunki yeh entertaining hai, television par trivia show ke reruns (dobara prasharan) ko nishkriya roop se (passively) dekhna taaki aap bewakoof feel na karein, ya serious practice ke bajaye upri taur par haath aazmana (dabbling). Ek intense method pravah (flow) ki ek pleasurable state bhi paida kar sakta hai, jisme challenge ka experience aapke focus ko sokh leta hai aur aap samay ka track kho dete hain. Halanki, ultralearning ke saath, cheezon ko gehrai se aur effectively seekhna hamesha mukhya prathmikta (priority) hoti hai.

Yeh paribhasha un examples ko cover karti hai jinpar maine abhi tak discuss kiya hai, lekin kuch mayno mein yeh asantoshjanak roop se vyapak (unsatisfyingly broad) hai. Jin ultralearners se main mila hoon unke paas is minimal definition ke mukable kahin zyaada overlapping (sanjha) qualities hain. Yahi wajah hai ki book ke second part mein main un gehre niyamon (principles) par discuss karunga jo ultralearning mein samanya hain aur kaise woh kuch impressive achievements ko kabil bana sakte hain. Usse pehle, halanki, main explain karna chahta hoon ki mujhe kyun lagta hai ki ultralearning matter karti hai—kyunki bhale hi ultralearning ke examples ajeeb (eccentric) lag sakte hain, learning ke is approach ke fayde gehre aur vyavaharik (practical) hain.

## The Case for Ultralearning

_(Ultralearning Ke Paksh Mein Tark)_

Yeh obvious hai ki ultralearning aasan nahi hai. Aapko apne busy schedule se samay alag rakhna hoga taaki aap kisi aisi cheez ko pursue kar sakein jo aapko mansik, bhavnatmak aur shayad sharirik roop se bhi thaka (strain) degi. Aapko mazeed comfortable options mein retreat (peeche hatne) ke bajaye niraashaon (frustrations) ka directly samna karne par majboor hona padega. Is difficulty ko dekhte hue, mujhe lagta hai ki yeh saaf taur par bayan (articulate) karna important hai ki ultralearning ek aisi cheez kyun hai jispar aapko gombhirta se vichar (seriously consider) karna chahiye.

Pahla kaaran aapke kaam (work) ke liye hai. Aap pehle se hi rozi-rooti kamane ke liye kaam karne mein apna zyaada tar energy kharch (expend) karte hain. Iske comparison mein, ultralearning ek chhota investment hai, bhale hi aap ise temporary roop se ek full-time commitment banane tak kyun na chale jayein. Halanki, hard skills ko tezi se seekhna job par saalon ke ausat darje ke prayas (mediocre striving) ke mukable ek bada impact daal sakta hai. Chahe aap careers badalna chahte hon, naye challenges lena chahte hon, ya apni progress ko tez (accelerate) karna chahte hon, ultralearning ek powerful tool hai.

Doosra kaaran aapki personal life ke liye hai. Hum mein se kitne logon ke sapne ek instrument bajane, ek foreign bhasha bolne, ek chef, writer, ya photographer banne ke hote hain? Aapki happiness ke sabse gehre moments aasan cheezon ko karne se nahi aate; woh aapke potential ko realize karne aur apne baare mein apni hi seemit dharanaon (limiting beliefs) par vijay paane se aate hain. Ultralearning un cheezon par maharat haasil karne ka ek raasta offer karti hai jo aapko gehra santoosh (satisfaction) aur aatmavishwas (self-confidence) dengi.

Halanki ultralearning ke peeche ka motivation timeless (sada-bahaar) hai, aaiye shuruat yeh dekhne se karein ki hard cheezon ko jaldi seekhne ki kala par maharat haasil karne mein invest karna aapke future ke liye kyun aur bhi important hone wala hai.

## Economics: Average Is Over

_(Arthshastra: Ausat Ka Samay Khatam)_

Economist Tyler Cowen ke lafzon mein, “Average is over.” Apni isi title ki book mein, Cowen tark karte hain ki zyaada computerization, automation, outsourcing (baari srot se kaam karwana), aur kshetrikaran (regionalization) ki wajah se, hum tezi se ek aisi duniya mein reh rahe hain jisme top performers baaki sab ke mukable bahut zyaada behtar karte hain.

Is asar ko chalane wali cheez woh hai jise “skill polarization” (hunar ka dhruvikaran) ke roop mein jaana jata hai. Yeh achhi tarah se jaana jata hai ki United States mein pichle kai dashakon mein aamdani ki asamanta (income inequality) badh rahi hai. Halanki, yeh description ek mazeed baareek picture ko nazarandaz karta hai. MIT ke economist David Autor ne dikhaya hai ki poore board par inequality badhne ke bajaye, actually do different effects hain: inequality top par badh rahi hai aur bottom par kam (lowering) ho rahi hai. Yeh Cowen ke ausat ke khatam hone ke thesis se match karta hai, jisme income spectrum ka middle part bottom mein compress (sikud) raha hai aur top par stretch (phail) raha hai.

Autor ne is effect ko create karne mein technology ke role ko identify kiya hai. Computerization aur automation technologies ke advance ka matlab yeh raha hai ki kai medium-skilled jobs—clerks, travel agents, bookkeepers, aur factory workers—ko nayi technologies ke saath replace kar diya gaya hai. Unki jagah naye jobs paida hue hain, lekin woh jobs aksar do types mein se ek hote hain: ya toh woh high-skilled jobs hote hain, jaise engineers, programmers, managers, aur designers, ya woh lower-skilled jobs hote hain jaise retail workers, cleaners, ya customer service agents.

Computers aur robots ke kaaran paida hue trends ko globalization aur regionalization mazeed badtar (exacerbating) kar rahe hain. Jaise hi medium-skilled technical work developing nations ke workers ko outsource kiya jata hai, unmein se kai jobs ghar par gayab ho rahe hain. Lower-skilled jobs, jinhein aksar face-to-face contact ya sanskritik ya bhashayi kshamtayon ke roop mein social knowledge ki zarurat hoti hai, unke bane rehne ki sambhavna hai. Higher-skilled work management aur market ke saath taal-mel (coordination) ke faydon ke kaaran samundar paar bheje jaane ke prati mazeed pratirodhi (resistant) hota hai. Apple ke us tagline ke baare mein sochein jo uske saare iPhones par hota hai: _“Designed in California. Made in China.”_ Design aur management rukte hain; manufacturing chali jaati hai. Regionalization is effect ka ek mazeed vistar (extension) hai, jisme kuch high-performing companies aur cities economy par asadharn (outsized) impacts daalte hain. Hong Kong, New York, aur San Francisco jaise superstar cities ka economy par dominating asar hota hai kyunki firms aur talent nikatata (proximity) ka fayda uthane ke liye ek saath ikhatha (cluster) hote hain.

Yeh ek aisi picture paint karta hai jo ya toh bleak (nirashajanak) ho sakti hai ya hopeful (umeed-bhari), is par depend karte hue ki aapka ispar kya response hai. Bleak, kyunki iska matlab hai ki ek safal, middle-class lifestyle jeene ke liye kya zaruri hai is baare mein hamari sanskriti mein samahit zyaadatar dharanaon ka tezi se ksharan (eroding) ho raha hai. Medium-skilled jobs ke gayab hone ke saath, succeed hone ke liye ek basic education paana aur har din hard work karna hi kaafi nahi hai. Iske bajaye, aapko higher-skilled category mein move karne ki zarurat hai, jahan learning constant hai, ya aapko bottom par lower-skilled category mein dhakel diya jayega.

Is pareshan karne wali (unsettling) picture ke neeche, halanki, umeed bhi hai. Kyunki agar aap naye skills ko jaldi aur effectively seekhne ke personal tools par maharat haasil kar sakte hain, toh aap is naye environment mein mazeed successfully compete kar sakte hain. Economic landscape badal raha hai yeh shayad ek aisa choice nahi hai jispar hum mein se kisi ka control ho, lekin hum jin hard skills ki hamein thrive (fale-phoole) karne ke liye zarurat hai unhein aakramak roop se seekh kar ispar apna response taiyar (engineer) kar sakte hain.

## Education: Tuition Is Too High

_(Shiksha: Tuition Fee Bahut Zyada Hai)_

High-skilled work ki tez hoti demand ne college education ki demand ko badha diya hai. Sivaye iske ki sabhi ke liye shiksha mein vistar karne ke bajaye, college ek crushing (kuchalne wala) bojh ban gaya hai, jisme aasmaan chhooti tuition costs ne dashakon ke debt (karz) ko graduates ke liye ek new normal bana diya hai. Tuition inflation ki rate se kahin zyaada tezi se badhi hai, jiska matlab hai ki jab tak aap us education ko ek bade salary increase mein translate karne ke liye achhi tarah se taiyar (well poised) nahi hain, tab tak yeh is kharch ke layak nahi ho sakti.

Kai sabse behtar schools aur institutions un core vocational (vyavsayik) skills ko sikhane mein fail ho jaate hain jinqi naye high-skilled jobs mein succeed hone ke liye zarurat hoti hai. Halanki higher education paramparagat roop se ek aisi jagah rahi hai jahan minds ko shape kiya jata tha aur characters develop kiye jaate the, woh oonche goals naye graduates ke samne khade basic financial realities ke saath tezi se sampark se baahar (out of touch) lagte hain. Isliye, un logon ke liye bhi jo college jaate hain, jo school mein seekha gaya tha aur jo succeed hone ke liye required hai, unke beech bahut zyaada skill gaps hote hain. Ultralearning un gaps mein se kuch ko fill kar sakti hai jab wapas school jana ek affordable option na hon.

Rapidly changing fields ka matlab yeh bhi hai ki professionals ko relevant (prasangik) bane rehne ke liye constantly naye skills aur abilities seekhne ki zarurat hai. Jabki wapas school jana kuch ke liye ek option hai, yeh kai logon ki reach se baahar hai. Kiske paas apni life ko saalon tak hold par rakhne ki ability hai jab woh aisi classes ke beech se nikalte (wade through) hain jo aakhirkar un situations ko cover karein ya na karein jinse unhein actually deal karne ki zarurat hai? Ultralearning, kyunki yeh khud learners dwara directed hoti hai, schedules aur situations ki ek mazeed vyapak variety mein fit baith sakti hai, bina kisi waste ke exactly wahi target karte hue jise aapko seekhne ki zarurat hai.

Ultimately, isse koi farq nahi padta ki ultralearning higher education ka ek suitable replacement hai ya nahi. Kai professions mein, degree ka hona na keval achha hai, balki legally required hai. Doctors, lawyers, aur engineers sabhi ko kaam shuru karne ke liye bhi formal credentials (yogyata praman) ki zarurat hoti hai. Halanki, wahi professionals school chhodne par seekhna band nahi karte, aur is tarah khud ko naye subjects aur skills sikhane ki ability essential bani rehti hai.

## Technology: New Frontiers in Learning

_(Technology: Seekhne Ki Nayi Seemayein)_

Technology insaniyat ke vices (buraiyon) aur virtues (gunon) dono ko badha-chadhakar dikhati (exaggerates) hai. Hamari buraiyan isliye badtar ho gayi hain kyunki ab woh downloadable, portable, aur socially transmissible (phailne yogya) hain. Apne aap ko bhatkane (distract) ya dhoke mein rakhne (delude) ki ability pehle kabhi itni zyaada nahi rahi, aur nateejatan hum privacy aur politics dono ke crises ka samna kar rahe hain. Bhale hi woh dangers real hain, unke peeche ek opportunity bhi create hui hai.
