Un logon ke liye jo technology ka wisely use karna jaante hain, khud ko kuch naya sikhane ke liye history ka yeh sabse aasan samay hai. Alexandrian Library mein jitni jankari thi usse bhi vishal jankari kisi bhi device aur internet connection wale ke liye freely accessible hai. Harvard, MIT, aur Yale jaise top universities apne sabse best courses online free mein publish kar rahi hain. Forums aur discussion platforms ka matlab hai ki aap ghar chhode bina hi groups mein learn kar sakte hain.

In naye advantages mein software add kiya gaya hai jo seekhne ke act ko hi tez karta hai. Kisi nayi bhasha, jaise Chinese seekhne par vichar karein. Ek aadha dashak pehle, learners ko bhaari-bhkam paper dictionaries se consult karna padta tha, jisne padhna seekhne ko ek nightmare bana diya tha. Aaj ke learner ke paas vocabulary ko yaad karne ke liye spaced-repetition systems hain, document readers hain jo ek button ke tap se translate karte hain, vishal (voluminous) podcast libraries hain jo practice ke liye endless opportunities offer karti hain, aur translation apps hain jo immersion ke badlav ko aasan (smooth) banati hain. Technology mein yeh rapid change dikhata hai ki purane subjects ko seekhne ke kai sabse behtar tareeqon ka ijaad kiya jana ya unhein kade tareeqe se apply kiya jana abhi baki hai. Learning possibilities ka space immense (vishal) hai, jo bas ambitious autodidacts ke iska fayda uthane (exploit) ke naye tareeqe nikaalne ka wait kar raha hai.

Ultralearning ke liye nayi technology ki zarurat nahi hoti, halanki. Jaisa ki main aane wale chapters mein discuss karunga, is abhyas (practice) ka ek lamba history hai, aur kai sabse famous minds ko iske kisi version ko apply karne wale ke roop mein describe kiya ja sakta hai. Halanki, technology innovation ke liye ek incredible opportunity offer karti hai. Cheezon ko seekhne ke abhi bhi kai tareeqe hain jinhein hamein poori tarah se explore karna baki hai. Shayad sahi technical innovation ke saath kuch learning tasks ko kahin zyaada aasan ya obsolete (gair-zaruri/lupt) bhi banaya ja sake. Aakramak aur efficiency-minded ultralearners unmein maharat haasil karne wale pehle log honge.

## Accelerate, Transition, and Rescue Your Career with Ultralearning

_(Ultralearning Ke Saath Apne Career Ko Tez Karein, Badlein Aur Bachayein)_

Economy mein skill polarization, aasmaan chhooti tuition, aur nayi technology ke prati trends sabhi global hain. Lekin ek individual ke liye actually ultralearning kaisi dikhti hai? Mera vishwas hai ki teen mukhya cases hain jisme hard skills ko tezi se haasil karne ki yeh strategy apply ho sakti hai: aapke paas jo career hai use tez (accelerate) karna, ek naye career mein transition karna, aur ek competitive duniya mein ek chhupa hua advantage (fayda) viksit karna.

Yeh dekhne liye ki ultralearning aapke pehle se majood career ko kaise tez kar sakti hai, Colby Durant par vichar karein. College se graduate karne ke baad, unhone ek web development firm mein kaam shuru kiya lekin mazeed tezi se progress karna chahti thin. Unhone copywriting seekhne ke liye ek ultralearning project haath mein liya. Initiative lene aur apne boss ko dikhane ke baad ki woh kya kar sakti hain, woh ek promotion paane mein kabil rahin. Ek keemti skill ko chun kar aur tezi se kushalata (proficiency) viksit karne par focus karke, aap apne normal career progression ko tez kar sakte hain.

Learning aksar us career mein transition karne ka sabse bada obstacle (badha) hoti hai jise aap paana chahte hain. Vishal Maini, for instance, tech duniya mein apne marketing role mein comfortable the. Lekin unka sapna artificial intelligence research ke saath mazeed closely involve hone ka tha. Unfortunately, yeh ek gehra technical skill set tha jise unhone haasil nahi kiya tha. Ek saavdhaan cheh mahine ke ultralearning project ke zariye, halanki, woh itne strong skills develop karne mein kabil rahe ki woh fields switch kar sakein aur us field mein kaam pa sakein jisme woh chahte the.

Finally, ek ultralearning project un doosre skills aur assets ko badha (augment) sakta hai jinhein aapne apne kaam mein viksit (cultivate) kiya hai. Diana Fehsenfeld ne apne native New Zealand mein saalon tak ek librarian ke roop mein kaam kiya. Government cutbacks aur apni field ke rapid technologization ka samna karte hue, woh chintit thin ki unka professional experience keep up karne ke liye kaafi nahi ho sakta hai. Nateejatan, unhone do ultralearning projects kiye, ek statistics aur programming language R seekhne ke liye aur doosra data visualization par. Un skills ki unki industry mein demand thi, aur unhein ek librarian ke roop mein apne background mein add karne ne unhein bleak prospects (nirashajanak sambhavnaon) se indispensable (apariharya/behad zaruri) banne ke tools diye.

## Beyond Business: The Call to Ultralearning

_(Business Se Pare: Ultralearning Ki Pukaar)_

Ultralearning ek badalti duniya se nipatne ke liye ek potent (prabhavshali) skill hai. Hard cheezon ko jaldi seekhne ki ability tezi se keemti hone wali hai, aur is tarah yeh is layak hai ki aap ise jis had tak ho sake develop karein, bhale hi iske liye pehle kuch investment ki zarurat ho.

Professional success, halanki, shayad hi kabhi woh cheez thi jo mere dwara mile ultralearners ko motivate karti thi—un logon ko shamil karte hue jinhone aakhirkar apne naye skills se sabse zyaada paise kamaye. Iske bajaye yeh ek compelling vision tha ki woh kya karna chahte hain, ek gehri jigyasa (curiosity), ya yahan tak ki challenge hi tha jo unhein aage badhata tha. Eric Barone ne ek millionaire banne ke liye paanch saal tak tanhai (solitude) mein apne passion ko pursue nahi kiya balki isliye kiya kyunki woh ek aisi cheez create karne ka santoosh chahte the jo unke vision se perfectly match karti ho. Roger Craig prize money jeetne ke liye Jeopardy! par nahi jaana chahte the balki us show par compete karne ke liye apne aap ko push karna chahte the jise woh bachpan se pyaar karte the. Benny Lewis ne ek technical translator, ya baad mein ek popular blogger banne ke liye bhashayein nahi seekhin, balki isliye seekhin kyunki unhein travel karna aur raaste mein milne wale logon ke saath interact karna pasand tha. Sabse behtar ultralearners woh hote hain jo kisi skill ko seekhne ke practical kaaranon ko ek aisi inspiration ke saath blend (milate) hain jo kisi aisi cheez se aati hai jo unhein excite karti hai.

Ultralearning ka ek added benefit hai jo un skills se bhi pare nikal jata hai jinhein koi isse seekhta hai. Hard cheezon ko karna, khhasakar aisi cheezein jisme kuch naya seekhna shamil ho, aapke aatm-bodh (self-conception) ko khinchta (stretches) hai. Yeh aapko confidence deta hai ki aap aisi cheezein karne ke kabil ho sakte hain jinhein aap pehle nahi kar sakte the. Meri MIT Challenge ke baad mera feeling na keval math aur computer science mein ek gehra interest tha balki possibility mein ek vistar (expansion) tha: _Agar main yeh kar sakta hoon, toh main aur kya kar sakta hoon jise try karne se main pehle hichkichata tha?_ Learning, iske core mein, horizons (क्षितिज/dayre) ka ek vistar hai, aisi cheezon ko dekhna jo pehle invisible thin aur apne andar aisi kshamtayon (capabilities) ko pehchanna jinka aapko pata nahi tha ki woh exist karti hain. Main is possible ke vistar ke mukable mere dwara describe kiye gaye ultralearners ke tivra aur samarpit prayason (intense and devoted efforts) ko pursue karne ka koi isse bada justification (auchitya) nahi dekhta. Agar aap ise safal banane ke liye sahi approach apnayein toh aap kya seekh sakte hain? Aap kaun ban sakte hain?

## What About Talent? The Terence Tao Problem

_(Talent Ke Baare Mein Kya? Terence Tao Ki Problem)_

Terence Tao smart hain. Do saal ki umra tak, unhone khud ko padhna sikha diya tha. Saat saal ki umra mein, woh high school math classes le rahe the. Satrah saal tak, unhone apni master’s thesis complete kar li thi. Iska title _“Convolution Operators Generated by Right-Monogenic and Harmonic Kernels”_ تھا. Uske baad, unhone Princeton se PhD haasil ki, coveted Fields Medal (jise kuch log “mathematics ka Nobel Prize” kehte hain) jeeta, aur unhein aaj ke samay mein zinda sabse behtar mathematical minds mein se ek maana jata hai. Jabki kai mathematicians extreme specialists hote hain—rare orchids (durlabh phool) jo mathematical tree ki ek khhas branch par hi thrive karne ke liye adapted hote hain—Tao phenominally diverse (adbhut roop se bahumukhi) hain. Woh niyamit roop se mathematicians ke saath collaborate karte hain aur door ke fields mein important contributions dete hain. Is vishishtata (virtuosity) ne ek colleague ko unki ability ki comparison _"ek leading English-language novelist dwara sudden definitive Russian novel produce karne"_ se karne par majboor kiya.

Kahin zyaada, unke carnamo ka koi obvious explanation nahi dikhta. Woh akaal-praudh (precocious/samay se pehle viksit) the, nishchit roop se, lekin mathematics mein unki safalata aakramak roop se haavi hone wale parents (overbearing parents) dwara unhein study karne ke liye push karne se nahi aayi thi. Unka childhood apne do younger brothers ke saath khelne, family ke Scrabble board aur mah-jongg tiles ke saath games ijaad karne, aur fantasy terrain ke kaalpnik maps draw karne se bhara tha. Normal kid stuff. Na hi unke paas koi khhas innovative studying method lagta hai. Jaisa ki _New York Times_ mein unke profile mein note kiya gaya hai, woh apni intelligence par itna float (coasted) karte rahe ki, apni PhD tak pahunchna par, woh “apni usual test-prep strategy: last-minute cramming (aakhiri waqt ka ratta)” par wapas gir gaye. Halanki woh approach ek baar apni field ke pinnacle (shikhara) par pahunchne par ladkhada (faltered) gayi, yeh fact ki woh itne lambe samay tak classes ke beech se aasaani se nikal gaye (breezed through), kisi unique strategy ke bajaye ek powerful mind ki taraf point karta hai. Genius ek aisa shabd hai jo bahut zyaada casually feka jata hai, lekin Tao ke case mein yeh label nishchit roop se chipak (sticks) jata hai.

Terence Tao aur doosre naturally gifted learners ultralearning ke sarvabhumikta (universality) ke liye ek mukhya challenge present karte hain. Agar Tao jaise log bina aggressive ya inventive studying methods ke itna kuch accomplish kar sakte hain, toh hamein doosre impressive learners ke habits aur methods ki jaanch karne ki takleef kyun uthani chahiye? Bhale hi Lewis, Barone, ya Craig ke carname Tao ke brilliance ke level tak na pahunche, shayad unki uplabdhiyan bhi kisi aisi chhupi hui intellectual ability ke kaaran hon jiski normal logon mein kami hoti hai. Agar aisa hota, toh ultralearning examine karne ke liye kuch interesting ho sakti hai lekin aisi cheez nahi jise aap actually replicate (nakal/dohra) kar sakein.

## Putting Talent Aside

_(Talent Ko Ek Taraf Rakhna)_

Natural talent kya role play karta hai? Jab intelligence aur janmjaat gunon (innate gifts) ka saya hamare upar mandra raha ho toh hum kisi ki safalata ke kaaranon ki jaanch kaise kar sakte hain? Tao jise stories un mere mortals (sadharan maranbhoomi ke insaanon) ke liye kya mean karti hain jo bas apni learn karne ke kshamtata (capacity) ko improve karna chahte hain?

Psychologist K. Anders Ericsson tark karte hain ki khhas tarah ke practice expert-level performer banne ke liye required zyaadatar attributes ko badal sakte hain, sivaye height aur body size ke janmjaat lakshanon (innate traits) ke. Doosre researchers hamari natures ke parivartansheelta (malleability) ke baare mein kam optimistic hain. Kai tark karte hain ki hamari intelligence ka ek substantial (bada) proportion, shayad zyaadatar, genetically derived (anuvanshik roop se haasil) hota hai. Agar intelligence mukhya roop se genes se aati hai, toh ultralearners dwara ek mazeed effective method ya strategy ke use ke bajaye ultralearning ko explain karne ke liye iska use kyun na kiya jaye? Mathematics mein Tao ki safalata kisi normal human beings dwara aasaani se replicable cheez ke roop mein nahi dikhti, toh yeh assume kyun karein ki koi bhi ultralearners kisi alag hain?

Main un do extremes ke beech ek madhya position leta hoon. Main socha hoon ki natural talents exist karte hain aur woh bina kisi shakk ke un results ko influence karte hain jinhein hum dekhte hain (khaaskar extreme levels par, jaise Tao ke case mein). Mera yeh bhi vishwas hai ki strategy aur method bhi matter karte hain. Is poori book mein, main aisi science ko cover karunga jo dikhati hai ki aap kaise seekhte hain isme badlav karna aapki kushalata (effectiveness) par kaise impact daal sakta hai. Har ek principle kuch aisa hai jo, agar appropriately apply kiya jaye, toh aapko ek behtar learner banayega, bhale hi aapka starting point dull (manda) ho ya brilliant.

Is kitab ke liye stories batane mein mera approach, isliye, yeh determine karne ka nahi hoga ki kisi ki intellectual success ka akela kaaran kya hai. Na keval yeh impossible hai, balki yeh khhasakar useful bhi nahi hai. Iske bajaye, main aap kaise seekhte hain ise improve karne ke liye aap jo sabse practical aur useful cheezein kar sakte hain unhein prithak (isolate) aur pradarshit (illustrate) karne ke liye stories aur anecdotes ka use karne ja raha hoon. Mere dwara zikr kiye gaye ultralearners ko un exemplars (namunon) ke roop mein kaam karna chahiye jinhein aap yeh dekhne ke liye use kar sakte hain ki ek niyan vyavahar (practice) mein kaise apply hota hai, is baat ki guarantee ke roop mein nahi ki aap identical effort ke saath ek identical result haasil kar sakte hain.

## Finding Time for Ultralearning

_(Ultralearning Ke Liye Samay Nikalna)_

Ek aur shakk (doubt) jo abhi tak padhne par aapke mind mein bana hoga woh yeh pooch raha hai ki aap in intensive learning projects ko karne ke liye samay kaise nikaalenge. Aap chintit ho sakte hain ki yeh advice aap par apply nahi hogi kyunki aapke paas pehle se hi kaam, school, ya family commitments hain jo aapko full-time learning mein jhonkne se rokti hain.

Vyavahar (practice) mein, halanki, yeh aam taur par koi problem nahi hai. Teen mukhya tareeqe hain jinse aap ultralearning ke ideas ko apply kar sakte hain, bhale hi aapko apni life mein doosre commitments aur challenges ko manage karna pade: naye part-time projects, learning sabbaticals (shiksha ki chhutti), aur pehle se majood learning prayason (learning efforts) ki phir se kalpana karna.

Pahla tarika ultralearning ko part-time pursue karna hai. Learning success ke sabse dramatic examples aam taur par woh hote hain jahan ultralearner ne project mein impressive matra mein samay lagaya. Ek project par week mein fifty hours spend karna week mein five hours spend karne ke mukable zyaada accomplish karega, bhale hi efficiency same ho, aur is tarah sabse captivatting (akarshak) stories mein aam taur par veertapurna schedules (heroic schedules) shamil hote hain. Halanki yeh achhi storytelling ke liye hota hai, jab aapke apne ultralearning projects ko pursue karne ki baat aati hai toh yeh actually gair-zaruri (unnecessary) hai. Ultralearning strategy ka core tivrata (intensity) aur kushalata ko prathmikta dene ki ek ichha hai. Chahe yeh ek full-time schedule par ho ya per week sirf ek-do ghante par, yeh poori tarah se aap par depend karta hai. Jaisa ki main chapter 10 mein discuss karunga, ek phaila hua schedule (spread-out schedule) long-term memory ke mamle mein mazeed efficient bhi ho sakta hai. Jab bhi aap is book mein kisi intensive schedule ke baare mein padhein, to be jhijhak ise apni situation ke mutabik adapt karein, unhi ruthlessly efficient tactics ko apply karte hue ek mazeed aaramdayak raftaar (leisurely pace) apnayein.

Doosra tarika kaam aur school ke beech ke gaps ke dauran ultralearning ko pursue karna hai. Jin logon ka maine interview liya unmein se kai ne apne projects temporary unemployment (berozgari), career transitions, semesters off, ya sabbaticals ke dauran kiye. Halanki inke liye plan karna utna reliable nahi hai, learning ka ek burst aapke liye perfect ho sakta hai agar aap jaante hain ki aapke paas is tarah ka samay nikalne wala hai. Meri MIT Challenge ko pursue karne ka ek motivation wahi tha jab maine kiya: Main abhi-abhi graduate hua tha, isliye apni majooda student life ko ek aur saal badhana ise char saal ke liye aage dhakhelne se zyaada aasan tha. Agar mujhe aaj wahi same project karna hota, toh main ise ek lambe samay ke dauran, kuch evenings aur weekends par karta, kyunki mera kaam aaj us samay ke mukable kam flexible hai jab school se working life mein transition ka moment tha.

Teesra tarika ultralearning principles ko us samay aur energy mein samahit (integrate) karna hai jise aap pehle se hi learning ke liye devot (samarpit) karte hain. Us aakhiri business book ke baare mein sochein jise aapne padha tha ya us samay ke baare mein jab aapne Spanish, pottery (mitti ke bartan), ya programming pick karne ki koshish ki thi. Us naye software ke baare mein kya jise aapko kaam ke liye seekhne ki zarurat thi? Un professional development hours ke baare mein kya jinhein aapko apni certification maintain karne ke liye log karne ki zarurat hai? Ultralearning ko ek additional activity hone ki zarurat nahi hai; yeh us samay ko suchit (inform) kar sakti hai jise aap pehle se hi learning mein spend karte hain. Aap us learning aur studies ko kaise align kar sakte hain jinhein aapko pehle se hi kushalata ko maximize karne ke niyamon ke saath karne ki zarurat hai?

Jaise talent wale section mein tha, extreme examples ko unhi principles ko apply karne se khud ko rokne (dissuade) mat dene dein. Jo kuch bhi main aapke saath share karunga use customize ya integrate kiya ja sakta hai jo pehle se exist karta hai. Jo matter karta hai woh hai intensity, pahel (initiative), aur effective learning ke prati commitment, aapki nirdeshika (timetable) ke specifics nahi.

## The Value of Ultralearning

_(Ultralearning Ki Keemat)_

Hard skills ko effectively aur efficiently haasil karne ki ability behad keemti (immensely valuable) hai. Na keval yeh, balki economics, education, aur technology ke majooda trends is skill wale aur iske bina wale logon ke beech ke farq ko mazeed badhane (exacerbate) wale hain. Is discussion mein, halanki, maine shayad sabse important question ko nazarandaz kiya hai: Ultralearning keemti ho sakti hai, lekin kya yeh seekhne yogya (learnable) hai? Kya ultralearning sirf asadharn personalities wale logon ka ek description hai, ya yeh kisi aisi cheez ko represent karti hai jo koi aisa insaan jo pehle ultralearner nahi tha actually ban sakta hai?

---

# Chapter 3 — How to Become an Ultralearner

### _(Ek Ultralearner Kaise Banen)_

---

> _"In many fields a year of focused work plus caring a lot would be enough."_
> _(Kai kshetron mein ek saal ka kendrit kaam plus bahut zyaada parwah karna hi kaafi hoga.)_

---

“Main ek prayog ka vishay (guinea pig) banna pasand karunga.” Yeh Tristan de Montebello ka ek email tha. Main is aakarshak, aadhe-French aur aadhe-American musician aur entrepreneur se pehli baar saat saal pehle mila tha, lagbhag theek usi samay jab Benny Lewis ke saath meri bhagyashali mulaqat (fateful encounter) hui thi. Bikhre hue blond baalon aur ek chhoti-kati (close-cropped) daadhi ke saath, woh aisa dikhta tha jaise California ke kisi tat (coastline) par surfboard par baitha ho. De Montebello us tarah ka banda tha jise aap turant pasand kar lete the: aatmavishwasi (confident), phir bhi zameen se juda hua (down to earth), uski lagbhag behtar English mein French accent ka sirf ek dhundhla sa ishaara tha. Saalon se, hum sampark mein the: main apne ajeeb learning experiments ke saath; woh duniya bhar mein hop karte hue, ek Parisian startup jo makhsoos (bespoke) cashmere sweaters banata tha uske saath kaam karne se lekar guitarist, khanabadosh (vagabond), aur aakhirkar Los Angeles mein web consultant banne tak, jo un beaches ke bahut paas tha jo uspar bahut suit karte the. Ab usne suna tha ki main learning par ek book likh raha hoon, aur woh interested tha.

Uske email ka context yeh tha ki halanki main daso hazar logon se mila tha aur unke baare mein jankari ikhatha (documented) ki thi jo ajeeb aur dilchasp learning carnamo ko accomplish kar rahe the, woh mulaqatei largely nateejay ke baad (after the fact) hui thin. Woh aise log the jinse main unki safalataon ke baad mila tha ya unke baare mein suna tha, pehle nahi; safalataon ke moolyankan (observations of successes), na ki un prayogon (experiments) ke jo unhein paada karte hain. Nateejatan, yeh batana mushkil tha ki yeh ultralearning cheez kitni sugaam/pahunch mein (accessible) thi. Agar aap kaafi saare kankad (pebbles) ko filter karenge, toh aapko nishchit roop se sone ke kuch kan (flecks of gold) milenge. Kya main bhi ajeeb learning projects ki khoj karte hue (scouring) wahi same cheez kar raha tha? Kaafi logon ko sift through (chhan'ne) par, aapko nishchit roop se kuch aise milenge jo incredible lagte hain. Lekin agar ultralearning mein woh potential tha jiski maine kalpana ki thi, toh kisi project ko try karne se pehle kisi insaan ko dhoondhna aur uske results dekhna achha hoga. Ise test karne ke liye, maine lagbhag ek dozen logon ka ek chhota group ikhatha kiya (mukhya roop se mere blog ke readers) jo is ultralearning cheez ko ek shot dene mein interested the. Unmein se ek de Montebello tha.

## Becoming an Ultralearner

_(Ek Ultralearner Banna)_

“Shayad piano?” de Montebello ne suggest kiya. Halanki woh ultralearning ke concept mein interested tha, unhein koi idea nahi tha ki woh kaun sa skill seekhna chahta hai. Unhone guitar bajaya tha aur ek band ke lead singer rahe the. Unke musical background ke saath, piano bajana seekhna ek relatively safe (tulnatmak roop se surakshit) choice lagta tha. Unhone online guitar lessons sikhane ka ek course bhi banaya tha, isliye ek aur musical instrument seekhna potentially unke business ko expand kar sakta tha. Swarthi (selfishly) roop se, maine unhein apni aaram-dayak seema se baahar (outside his comfort zone) kuch seekhne ki koshish karne ke liye prerit kiya. Ek musician ka ek aur instrument pick karna is baare mein study karne ke liye ek ideal case nahi lagta tha ki kya ultralearning ko vyapak roop se (broadly) apply kiya ja sakta hai. Humne aur ideas chaaron taraf phenke. Ek ya do hafte baad, unhone public speaking (bhashan kala) par faisla kiya. Ek musician ke roop mein unke background ne unhein onstage hone ka experience diya tha, lekin otherwise unke paas bhashan (speeches) dene ka bahut kam experience tha. Public speaking ek useful skill bhi hai, unhone tark diya, isliye isme behtar hona mehnat ke layak hoga bhale hi is prayas se kuch dhyan dene yogya (noteworthy) na nikle.

De Montebello ke paas public speaking mein behtar banne ke liye ek private motivation tha. Unhone apni life mein sirf mutthi bhar (handful) speeches di thin, aur unmein se zyaada tar college mein thin. Unhone mujhse ek example share kiya, jab woh Paris mein ek web design firm mein ek dozen logon ko ek talk dene gaye the: “Main jab bhi us baare mein sochta hoon toh sharm se sikud (cringe) jata hoon.” Unhone explain kiya, “Main bas bata sakta tha ki main connect nahi kar raha tha. Aise kai hisse the jahan main unhein bore kar raha tha. Aise mazaak (jokes) the jahan main hansta tha, kyunki mujhe lagta tha ki yeh funny hai, lekin koi aur nahi hansta tha.” Ek musician hone ke naate, woh hairan the ki “iska kitna kam hissa (how little of it) public speaking mein translate (tabdil) hua.” Phir bhi, yeh ek aisi cheez thi jisme unhone potential value dekhi, agar woh isme behtar ho sakein. “Public speaking ek metaskill hai,” woh feel karte hain. Yeh is tarah ka skill hai jo doosre skills mein assist (madhad) karta hai: “aatmavishwas, storytelling, writing, creativity, interviewing skills, selling skills. Yeh bahut si different cheezon ko chhoota hai.” Ise dimaag mein rakh kar, woh kaam par lag gaye.

## First Steps of a Fledgling Ultralearner

_(Ek Nau-Sikhia Ultralearner Ke Pehle Kadam)_

De Montebello ne apna topic chuna tha, lekin woh sure nahi the ki unhein ise exactly kaise seekhna chahiye. Unhone Toastmasters International ki ek meeting mein attend karne ka faisla kiya, jo public speaking seekhne ki ek sanstha (organization) hai. Us point par, unki kahani mein do baar luck (kismat) ne sath diya. Pehla yeh tha ki unki public speaking project ki sabse pehli meeting mein Michael Gendler majood the. Gendler ek lambe samay se Toastmaster the, aur de Montebello ke charm aur public speaking mein behtar banne ki unthak tivrata (obsessive intensity) ne unhein de Montebello ko unke project ke dauran coach (sikhane) karne mein madad karne ke liye vashibhoot (convinced) kiya. Luck ka doosra khorakh (dose) kuch aisa tha jise de Montebello ne us samay poori tarah se appreciate nahi kiya tha: woh _World Championship of Public Speaking_ mein compete karne ke liye patra (eligible) hone ki deadline se theek das din pehle pahunche the.

World Championship of Public Speaking Toastmasters dwara annually aayojit ki jaane wali ek competition hai jisme members compete karte hain, elimination style (baahar hone wale tarike) mein, individual clubs se shuru karke aur organization ke bade se bade units tak jaate hain, jab tak ki kuch chune hue log final stage tak na pahunch jayein. De Montebello ke paas prepare karne ke liye ek hafte se thoda hi zyaada samay tha. Phir bhi, competition ne unke ultralearning project ke liye ek sambhavit dhancha (potential structure) provide kiya, isliye woh iske liye gaye, aane wale hafte mein chheh mandatory qualifying speeches ko nikaala (cranking out), aakhiri speech ko bilkul aakhiri mauqe par (in the nick of time) khatam karte hue.

De Montebello ne deewanapan ki had tak (obsessively) practice ki, kabhi-kabhi ek hi din mein do baar bolte hue. Unhone har ek speech ka ek video record kiya aur flaws (galtiyon) ke liye iska aakramak roop se vishleshan (analyzed) kiya. Unhone har baar speech dene par feedback maanga, aur unhein iska kaafi hissa mila. Unke coach, Gendler ne unhein unki aaram-dayak seema se bahut baahar push kiya. Ek baar, jab unke samne ek pehle se majood speech ko behtar banane (polishing) aur shuruat se ek brand-new speech create karne ke beech choice thi, toh de Montebello ne poocha ki unhein kya karna chahiye. Gendler ka response tha ki wahi karo jo unke liye sabse zyaada dravna (scariest) ho.

Unke is anvarat prayas (relentless drive) ne de Montebello ko asadharn jagahon par dhakela. Unhone apni sahaj prastuti (spontaneous delivery) par kaam karne ke liye improv (bina tayyari ke natak) ki classes lin. Wahan unhone seekha ki unke head mein jo kuch bhi hai uspar trust karein aur bina kisi hichkichahat (hesitation) ke use deliver karein. Isne unhein apne lafzon par ladkhadane se ya onstage freeze hone ke darr se bachaya. Unhone ek dost se baat ki jo Hollywood director ke roop mein kaam karta hai taaki woh unki delivery par feedback de sake. Director ne de Montebello ko apni speech daso baar different styles mein dene ke liye sikhaya—angry, monotone (ek-hi-sur), screaming, yahan tak ki ek rap ke roop mein—phir wapas jaakar dekho ki unki normal voice se kya different tha. De Montebello ke mutabik, isne unhein us vichitra-paraye (uncanny valley) se baahar nikalne mein madad ki jo tab hota tha jab unki normal speaking delivery halke se aswabhabik (unnatural) feel hoti thi.

Theater ke background wale ek aur dost ne unhein stage presence (stage par majoodgi) par tips diye. Woh de Montebello ko unki speech ke beech le gaya aur dikhaya ki kaise har ek word aur sentence halchal (movement) ko indicate karta hai jise stage par unke move karne ki jagah par translate kiya ja sakta hai. Spotlight ke neeche sankuchit (constricted) khade rehne ke bajaye, de Montebello ab gracefully move kar sakte the aur apne lafzon ke upar apne message ko communicate karne ke liye apni body ka use kar sakte the. Unhone apni speech ek middle school mein bhi di, yeh jaante hue ki seventh graders sabhi mein se sabse nishthur feedback (ruthless feedback) denge. Toastmasters ke comfort se baahar buri tarah flop (bombing terribly) hone ke baad, unhone onstage jaane se pehle apni audience se baat karna seekha: unki bhasha aur emotions ko seekho aur unke saath connect karo. Us tarike se, abhi tak seekhe gaye sabhi cheezon ko apply karte hue, woh chalte-chalte (on the fly) apni speech ko badal sakte the, taaki yeh nishchit roop se ek nayi audience ke saath connect ho sake. Sabse badhkar, Gendler ne unhein relentlessly push kiya. “Mujhe parwah karne par majboor karo (Make me care),” Gendler ne unhein de Montebello ke speeches mein se ek ko sunne ke baad bataya. “Main samajhta hoon ki yeh aapke liye kyun important hai, lekin audience ko aapki parwah nahi hai. Aapko mujhe parwah karne par majboor karna hoga.” Bahumukhi salah (Diverse advice) aur vyapak abhyas (voluminous practice) un lessons ko gehrai se sokh (soak) lenge, jisse de Montebello stage par apni shuruati jhijhak/anadi-pan (awkwardness) ko tezi se paar kar sakein.

Ek mahine baad, de Montebello ne apni area competition jeet li, Toastmasters mein do dashakon ke experience wale ek pratiyogi (competitor) ko harate hue. Unhone apni district aur division competitions bhi jeetin. Finally, public speaking mein pehli baar haath aazmane ke saat mahino se kam samay baad, woh World Championships mein compete karne ja rahe the. “Lagbhag tees hazar log hain jo har saal compete karte hain,” unhone note kiya, yeh add karte hue “Main kaafi confident hoon ki main history mein is had tak pahunche wala sabse tez competitor hoon, kyunki agar maine das din baad shuru kiya hota, toh main compete nahi kar sakta tha.” Woh top ten mein pahunch gaye.

## From Semifinalist to Career Change

_(Semifinalist Se Career Change Tak)_

“Main jaanta tha ki yeh project mere liye bada hone wala hai jab maine ise shuru kiya tha,” de Montebello ne international competition mein apne top ten placement ke mahino baad mujhe bataya. “Lekin yeh literally life changing (zindagi badalne wala) tha. Maine umeed nahi ki thi ki yeh actually meri life badal dega.” World Championship mein final competition tak pahunchna ek lambi yatra thi, lekin yeh uske baad hi tha jab unhone realize karna shuru kiya ki unhone kitna seekha tha. “Main public speaking ke is bahut hi narrow (tang) duniya ke liye seekh raha था. Yeh uske baad hi tha jab maine un saare skills ki gehrai ko realize kiya jinpar maine itna kaam kiya tha: storytelling, confidence, communicating.”

Jin doston ne de Montebello ki safalata ke baare mein suna unhone poochne shuru kiya ki kya woh unki apni speeches par kaam karne mein madad kar sakte hain. Unhone aur Gendler ne doosron ko unki public speaking skills improve karne mein madad karne ka ek opportunity dekha. Demand tivra (intense) thi. Authors jo five-figure (pach-anko ki) speaking fees lete hain, unhone is duo (jodi) ko approach karna shuru kiya yeh dekhne ke liye ki kya unhein ultralearning tarike se apni public speaking improve karna sikhaya ja sakta hai. Jald hi unhone apna pehla client haastal kiya, bees hazar dollars ki keemat par. Gendler aur de Montebello swarthi/bhaade ke (mercenary) nahi the; woh sirf un speakers par focus karna chahte the jinke message par woh sach mein vishwas karte the. Lekin is fact ne ki unhone itne high-status clients ko attract kiya tha, unhein full-time public speaking coaching mein switch karne ke liye convince karne mein nishchit roop se madad ki. Gendler aur de Montebello ne apni consultancy ka naam _UltraSpeaking_ rakhne ka faisla kiya, us strategy ke prati ek samman (nod) ke roop mein jisne is sab ko possible banaya.

De Montebello ki kahani hamari shuruati umeed se kahin zyaada dramatic sabit hui. Unki shuruati umeed yeh thi ki woh kuch mahino tak intensely practice kar sakein, kahin ek achhi speech deliver karein, aur use record kar sakein—ek achha yaasgar (memento) aur ek naya skill—lekin yeh nahi ki woh ek international competitor ke status tak pahunch jayenge aur aakhirkar ek complete career change ka experience karenge. Un doze ya usse zyaada logon mein se jinhein maine ultralearning mein coach karne mein kuch samay bitaya, kisi ne bhi itna dramatic example present nahi kiya. Kuch ne drop out (chhod diya) kar diya. Life beech mein aa gayi (ya shayad yeh zahir kiya ki woh actually utne committed nahi the jitne woh shuruat mein dikhte the). Doosron ke paas aadarsh safalataayein (respectable successes) thin, jinphone medicine, statistics, comic book drawing, military history, aur yoga seekhne mein mahatvapurna suvidhaon/badlav (significant improvements) kiye, bhale hi woh de Montebello ke safalata ke darje (degree) tak na pahunche hon.

Jis cheez ne de Montebello ko alag kiya woh yeh nahi tha ki unhone socha ki woh chheh mahine mein lagbhag zero experience se World Championship ke finalist ban sakte hain. Balki, yeh unki dhoon-bhari kaam karne ki naitikta (obsessive work ethic) thi. Unka goal kisi pehle se taye charam (predetermined extreme) tak pahunchna nahi tha balki yeh dekhna tha ki woh kitna door ja sakte hain. Kabhi-kabhi aap lucky honge aur ek aise raaste par nikal padenge jo aapko kaafi door le jayega. Lekin ultralearning ka failure mode (asafalata ka tarika) bhi aam taur par yeh hota hai ki aap ek skill ko kaafi achhi tarah se seekh jayenge. Un logon ke beech bhi jinke paas is chhote group mein itne dramatic results nahi the jinhein maine coaching dene mein samay bitaya, jinhone apne project ke saath tike rahe unhone aakhirkar ek naya skill seekha jiski unhein parwah thi.

Aap shayad world championships mein compete na karein ya poori tarah se careers switch na karein, lekin jab tak aap process ke saath tike rehte hain, aap nishchit roop se kuch naya seekhenge. De Montebello ka example mere liye jo embody (samet-ta) karta tha woh na keval yeh tha ki aap ek ultralearner ban sakte hain balki yeh bhi ki aisi safalataayein kisi khhas tarah ke genius ya talent ke hone ka apariharya parinaam (inevitable consequences) nahi hain. Agar de Montebello ne iske bajaye piano par focus kiya hota, toh speeches dene ka unka experience shayad Paris ke un dino ka wahi ek awkward example bana rehta.

## Principles of Becoming an Ultralearner

_(Ek Ultralearner Banne Ke Niyam)_

De Montebello ki kahani pradarshit karti hai ki ek ultralearner banne ka faisla karna possible hai. Lekin ultralearning koi sancha-baddh/ek-jaisa (cookie-cutter) method nahi hai. Har project unique hota hai, aur is par maharat haasil karne ke liye required methods bhi waisa hi hote hain. Ultralearning projects ki yeh vilakshanta (uniqueness) un tatvon (elements) mein se ek hai jo un sab ko ek saath baandhta hai. Agar ultralearning ko bottle mein band ya standardize kiya ja sake, toh yeh simply structured education ka ek intense roop hoga. Jo cheez ultralearning ko interesting banati hai wohi cheez ise step-by-step formulas mein ubaalna (boil down) harder bhi banati hai.

Yeh ek mushkil challenge hai, lekin main sabse pehle niyamon (principles) par focus karke isse bach nikalne (sidestep) ki koshish karne ja raha hoon. Principles aapko problems solve karne ki izazat dete hain, yahan tak ki unhein bhi jisse aap pehle kabhi na takraye hon, ek aise tareeqe se jo ek recipe ya mechanical procedure nahi kar sakta. Agar aap sach mein physics ke principles ko samajhte hain, for instance, aap ek naye problem ko simply working backward (peeche se kaam karke) solve kar sakte hain. Principles duniya ko samajhne kabil (make sense) banate hain, aur bhale hi woh hamesha exactly bayan na karein ki aapko kisi khhas challenge ko kaise solve karna chahiye, woh ek vishal marghdarshan (immense guidance) provide kar sakte hain. Ultralearning, mere nazariye se, sabse behtar tab kaam karti hai jab aap ise niyamon ke ek simple set ke zariye dekhte hain, bajaye exact steps ya protocols ko copy aur paste karne ki koshish karne ke.

Ultralearning ke principles is book ke second part ka focus hone wale hain. Har chapter mein, main ek naya principle introduce karunga, plus ultralearning ke examples aur scientific research dono se iska samarthan karne ke liye kuch evidence share karunga. Finally, main un sambhavit tareeqon ko share karunga jisse woh niyan vishisht rannitiyon (specific tactics) ke roop mein khud ko zahir kar sakta hai. Yeh tactics sirf ek chhota namuna (sample) hain. Lekin unhein aapke liye apne khud ke ultralearning challenges ke baare mein ranatmak roop se (creatively) sochne ke liye ek starting point provide karna chahiye.

Wahan nau universal principles hain jo abhi tak describe kiye gaye ultralearning projects ke aadhar (underlie) hain. Har ek safal learning ke ek particular aspect ko embody karta hai, aur main describe karta hoon ki ultralearners apne projects mein kiye gaye choices ke zariye principle ke kushalata (effectiveness) ko kaise maximize karte hain. Woh hain:

1. **METALEARNING: FIRST DRAW A MAP.** _(Pehle Ek Map Banayein.)_ Uss subject ya skill ko seekhna kaise hai yeh seekh kar shuruat karein jisse aap nipatna chahte hain. Discover karein ki achhi research kaise karni hai aur naye skills ko mazeed aasaani se seekhne ke liye apni pichli kshamtayon (competencies) ka upyog kaise karna hai.
2. **FOCUS: SHARPEN YOUR KNIFE.** _(Apni Chhaku Ko Tez Karein.)_ Concentrate (kendrit) karne ki ability ko viksit karein. Samay ke un tukdon (chunks) ko nikaalein jab aap learning par focus kar sakein, aur ise bas karna aasan banayein.
3. **DIRECTNESS: GO STRAIGHT AHEAD.** _(Seedhe Aage Badhein.)_ Uss cheez ko karke seekhein jisme aap behtar banna chahte hain. Ise doosre tasks ke liye trade off (badla-badli) mat karein, sirf isliye kyunki woh mazeed convenient (suvidha-janak) ya comfortable hain.
4. **DRILL: ATTACK YOUR WEAKEST POINT.** _(Apne Sabse Kamzor Point Par Hamla Karein.)_ Apne sabse kamzor points ko behtar banane mein ruthlessly (nishthur) rahein. Jatil (complex) skills ko chote parts mein todein; phir un parts par maharat haasil karein aur unhein wapas ek saath build karein.
5. **RETRIEVAL: TEST TO LEARN.** _(Seekhne Ke Liye Test Karein.)_ Testing sirf knowledge ka moolyankan karne ka ek tarika nahi hai balki ise create karne ka ek tarika hai. Apne aap par tabhi test lein jab aap confident feel na kar rahe hon, aur nishkriya roop se review karne ke bajaye jankari ko active roop se yaad karne (actively recall) ke liye apne aap ko push karein.
6. **FEEDBACK: DON’T DODGE THE PUNCHES.** _(Punches Se Mat Bacho.)_ Feedback karrwa (harsh) aur uncomfortable hota hai. Apne ego (aham) ko beech mein laye bina iska use karna jaanein. Noise (shor) se signal (kaam ki cheez) ko extract karein, taaki aap jaankein ki kis par dhayan dena hai aur kise ignore karna hai.
7. **RETENTION: DON’T FILL A LEAKY BUCKET.** _(Ek Tooti Hui Balti Ko Mat Bharo.)_ Aap kya bhoolte hain aur kyun bhoolte hain ise samajhein. Cheezon ko na keval abhi ke liye balki hamesha ke liye yaad rakhna seekhein.
8. **INTUITION: DIG DEEP BEFORE BUILDING UP.** _(Upar Build Karne Se Pehle Gehra Khodein.)_ Concepts aur skills ke khel aur exploration ke zariye apni antardrishti (intuition) ko viksit karein. Samajhein ki samajh (understanding) kaise kaam karti hai, aur cheezon ko gehrai se jaan'ne se bachne ke liye rote-memorization (ratta maarne) ke saste tricks ka sahara na lein.
9. **EXPERIMENTATION: EXPLORE OUTSIDE YOUR COMFORT ZONE.** _(Apni Aaram-dayak Seema Se Baahar Explore Karein.)_ Yeh saare nau principles sirf starting points hain. Sachchi maharat (True mastery) na keval doosron dwara taye kiye gaye raaste par chalne se aati hai balki un possibilities ko explore karne se aati hai jinki unhone abhi tak kalpana nahi ki hai.

Maine in nau niyamon ko ultralearning projects ke mere moolyankano (observations) ke saath-saath mere apne personal experience ke aadhar par organized kiya, jahan main kar saka, vishal bhavnatmak vigyan ke sahitya (cognitive science literature) ka sandarbh (referencing) dete hue. Maine khud ultralearners se shuruat ki. Agar ek insaan ne kisi cheez ko ek khhas tareeqe se kiya, toh yeh ek interesting example ho sakta hai, lekin yeh us insaan ki ek vishesta (idiosyncrasy) bhi ho sakti hai. Agar kai logon ne ya, isse bhi behtar, mere samne aaye har ek ultralearner ne, ek khhas cheez ko ek khhas tareeqe se kiya, toh yeh is baat ka kahin zyaada strong evidence tha ki main ek samanya niyan (general principle) par chal pada tha. Maine phir un niyamon ko scientific literature ke khilaf check kiya. Kya cognitive science se aisi mechanisms aur findings hain jo mere dwara dekhi gayi tactics ka samarthan karti hain? Isse bhi behtar, kya learning ke ek approach ko doosre se compare karne wale controlled experiments hue hain? Scientific research un kai learning strategies ka samarthan karti hai jinhein mere dwara dekhe gaye ultralearners ne employ kiya tha. Yeh suggest karta hai ki ultralearners, efficiency aur effectiveness par apne nishthur focus ke saath, learning ki kala mein kuch universal niyamon par utar aaye hain.

Principles aur tactics se pare ek mazeed vyapak ultralearning aacharan (ethos) hai. Yeh apni khud ki learning ki zimmedari lene ka ek aacharan hai: yeh decide karna ki aap kya seekhna chahte hain, aap ise kaise seekhna chahte hain, aur jo aapko chahiye use seekhne ke liye apna khud ka plan taiyar karna. Aap hi driver's seat par hain, aur aap hi aakhirkar un results ke liye responsible hain jinhein aap generate karte hain. Agar aap is bhavna ke saath ultralearning ko approach karte hain, toh aapko in niyamon ko lachile marghdarshakon (flexible guidelines) ke roop mein lena chahiye, kade niyamon (rigid rules) ke roop mein nahi. Achhi tarah se seekhna sirf nirdeshon (prescriptions) ke ek set ko follow karne ke baare mein nahi hai. Aapko cheezon ko apne liye try karna hoga, un learning challenges ki nature ke baare mein gehrai se sochna hoga jinka aap samna karte hain, aur unhein overcome karne ke liye solutions ko test karna hoga. Ise dimaag mein rakh kar, aaiye pehle ultralearning niyan ki taraf mudein: metalearning.

---

# Chapter 4 — Principle 1: Metalearning

### _(Niyam 1 — Metalearning: Pehle Ek Map Banayein)_

---

> _"If I have seen further it is by standing on the shoulders of giants."_
> _(Agar maine mazeed door tak dekha hai, toh yeh giants ke kandhon par khade hone ki wajah se hai.)_

---

Dan Everett ek khhachakhhach bhare auditorium ke samne khade hain. Saath saal (early sixties) ki umra ke ek majboot kad-kaathi wale mard, woh slowly aur aatmavishwas ke saath bolte hain, unka muskurata hua chehra kam hote blond baalon aur ek daadhi se ghira hai. Unke paas ek table hai jo tarah-tarah ki cheezon se bhari hai: lakdiyan, patthar, patte, dibbe, phal, aur ek paani ka pitcher (jag). Woh ishara karte hain ki pradarshan (demonstration) shuru hone wala hai.

Right side ke ek door se enter karte hue, dark brown baalon aur olive skin wali ek bhaari-bhakam, adheed umra ki aurat stage ki taraf badhti hai. Everett uske paas jaate hain aur ek aisi bhasha mein kuch kehte hain jise woh nahi samajhti. Woh chaaron taraf dekhti hai, poori tarah se chakraayi hui (confused), aur phir hichkichate hue javab deti hai, “Kuti paoka djalou.” Woh us baat ko dohrane ki koshish karte hain jo usne abhi kahi hai. Shuruat mein thoda ladkhadana (stumbling) hota hai, lekin ek ya do aur koshishon ke baad, woh unke dohrane se santusht lagti hai. Woh blackboard par jaate hain aur likhte hain, “Kuti paoka djalou ➱ ‘Greeting (?).’” Next woh ek chhoti lakdi uthaate hain aur uski taraf point karte hain. Woh aurat correctly guess karti hai ki woh naam jaan'na chahte hain aur javab deti hai, “ŋkindo.” Ek baar phir, Everett blackboard par jaate hain aur likhte hain, “ŋkindo ➱ stick.” Next woh do lakdiyan try karte hain aur unhein same response milta hai, “ŋkindo.” Phir woh lakdi gira dete hain, jispar aurat kehti hai, “ŋkindo paula.” Demonstration aage badhta hai, Everett cheezon ko uthaate hain, actions perform karte hain, aurat ke responses ko sunte hain, aur results ko blackboard par record karte hain. Jald hi woh simple naming tasks se aage badh jaate hain aur mazeed jatil vakyoon (complicated sentences) ke baare mein poochne lagte hain: “Woh paani peeti hai,” “Aap banana khate ho,” aur “Patthar ko dibbe mein rakho.” Har ek naye sawaal/bhav (elicitation) ke saath, woh prayog karte hain, naye sentences banate hain aur uske reaction ko test karte hain yeh dekhne ke liye ki kya woh sahi hain. Ek aadhe ghante ke andar, wahan do se zyaada blackboards nouns, verbs, pronouns, aur dhwanyatmak tippaniyon (phonetic annotations) se bhar jaate hain.

Kisi nayi bhasha mein daso sabd aur phrases seekhna pehle tees minutes ke hisab se ek achha start hai. Jo cheez is carname ko khhasakar impressive banati hai woh yeh hai ki Everett ko koi bhi aisi bhasha bolne ki izazat nahi hai jo unke aur speaker ke beech common ho sake. Woh sirf use sabd aur phrases bolne ke liye prerit (encourage) kar sakte hain aur bhasha ki grammar, pronunciation, aur vocabulary ko figure out karne ke liye unhein dohra sakte hain. Unhein yeh bhi nahi pata ki kaun si bhasha boli ja rahi hai.

Everett ek nayi bhasha ko shuruat se (scratch), bina teachers, translations ya bina yeh jaane ki woh kaun si bhasha seekh rahe hain, aadhe ghante mein kaise bolna shuru kar sakte hain, jabki hum mein se zyaada tar log high school ki Spanish classes ke saalon baad bhi aisa karne mein struggle karte hain? Kaun si cheez Everett ko vocabulary pick karne, grammar aur pronunciation ko decode karne mein aap ya mujhse kahin zyaada tezi se kabil banati hai, un saare additional constraints (badhaon) ke bavajood? Kya woh ek bhashayi genius (linguistic genius) hain, ya kuch aur chal raha hai?

Javab hamara pehla ultralearning niyan hai: metalearning.

## What Is Metalearning?

_(Metalearning Kya Hai?)_

Prefix _meta_ Greek shabd _μετά_ se aata hai, jiska matlab hai "pare" (beyond). Yeh aam taur par tab sanket deta hai jab koi cheez apne hi "baare mein" ho ya abstraction (amurtata) ki ek oonchi layer se deal karti hai. Is case mein metalearning ka matlab hai learning ke baare mein seekhna (learning about learning). Yahan ek example hai: Agar aap Chinese characters seekh rahe hain, toh aap seekhenge ki 🔥 ka matlab "fire" (aag) hai. Yeh normal learning hai. Aap yeh bhi seekh sakte hain ki Chinese characters aksar kisi cheez dwara organized hote hain jise mool-tatva (radicals) kehte hain, jo indicate karte hain ki character kis tarah ki cheez ko describe karta hai. Character 灶, for example jiska matlab "stove" (choolha) hai, uske left-hand side par ek 🔥 hai yeh indicate karne ke liye ki iska aag se kuch rishta hai. Chinese characters ki is vishesta (property) ko seekhna metalearning hai—aapki jinjyasa ke object ke baare mein khud seekhna nahi, is case mein sabd aur phrases, balki is baare mein seekhna ki is subject ke andar knowledge kaise structured aur haasil ki jaati hai; doosre lafzon mein, ise seekhna kaise hai yeh seekhna.

Everett ke case mein, we can see glimpses (jhalak) of the enormous wealth (vishal bhandar) of metalearning jo satah (surface) ke theek neeche chhupi hai. “Well, is baare mein humne kaun si cheezon ko notice kiya?” Everett demonstration khatam hone ke baad audience se poochte hain, “Yeh SVO lagta hai, ek subject-verb-object bhasha, yeh bahut zyaada hairan karne wala (shocking) nahi hai.” Woh jaari rakhte hain, “Nouns par koi plural marking nahi lagti, jab tak ki yeh tones na hon aur maine ise miss na kiya ho. . . . Yahan saaf taur par pitch chal rahi hai; chahe yeh tone ho ya na ho, iska vishleshan kiya jana baki hai.” Is jargon (takniki bhasha) se hum dekh sakte hain ki jab Everett apne saathi se ek sabd ya phrase ugalwate hain, toh woh sirf awaazon ki nakal (parroting) nahi kar rahe hote; woh saalon ke bhasha seekhne ke experience par grounded bhasha kaise kaam karti hai iske baare mein theories aur hypotheses ke saath ek map draw kar rahe hote hain.

Ek linguist (bhasha vigyanik) ke roop mein knowledge ke apne vishal bhandar ke alava, Everett ke paas ek aur trick hai jo unhein ek vishal advantage deti hai. Unhone jo demonstration prastut kiya hai woh unka apna ijaad nahi hai. Ise “monolingual fieldwork” (ek-bhashayi kshetra-kaary) demonstration kaha jata hai, is method ko pehli baar Everett ke teacher Kenneth Pike ne indigenous (asthaniya/adivasi) bhashon ko seekhne ke ek madhyam ke roop mein develop kiya tha. Yeh method objects aur actions ki ek sequence (shrankhla) ko lay out karta hai jise practitioner bhasha ko ek saath jodne (piecing together) ke liye use kar sakta hai. Is method ko Hollywood ka exposure bhi mila jab Louise Banks, ek kaalpnik linguist, ne 2016 ki science fiction movie _Arrival_ mein ek alien bhasha ko decode karne ke liye iska use kiya tha.

Everett ke bhashayi arsenal (hathiyar-ghar) mein in do cheezon ne—bhashayein kaise kaam karti hain iska ek richly detailed map aur ek method jo fluency ka raasta provide karta hai—Everett ko sirf kuch simple sentences seekhne se kahin zyaada accomplish karne ki izazat di hai. Pichle tees saalon mein woh Pirahã mein faraatedar (fluent) banne wale mutthi bhar outsiders mein se ek ban gaye hain, jo planet par sabse unusual aur difficult bhashon mein se ek hai, jo Amazon jungle mein sirf ek door-daas ke kabile (remote tribe) dwara boli jaati hai.

## The Power of Your Metalearning Map

_(Aapke Metalearning Map Ki Taqat)_

Everett ka case naye cheezon ko jaldi aur mazeed effectively seekhne ke liye metalearning ka use karne ki taqat ko khoobsurat roop se pradarshit (illustrates) karta hai. Ek subject kaise kaam karta hai, kis tarah ke skills aur jankari par maharat haasil karni hogi, aur aisa mazeed effectively karne ke liye kaun se methods available hain, yeh dekh paana hi saare ultralearning projects ki safalata ke core mein hai. Metalearning is tarah map banata hai, jo aapko dikhata hai ki bina khoye apne destination tak kaise pahunchna hai.

Yeh dekhne liye ki metalearning kyun itni important hai, ek teesri bhasha seekhte waqt pehle se ek doosri bhasha jaan'ne ke sahayak asaron par ek study par vichar karein. Yeh study Texas mein hui thi, jahan monolingual (ek-bhashayi) English speakers aur bilingual (dwi-bhashayi) Spanish/English speakers ne ek French class mein enroll kiya tha. Baad ke tests ke follow-up ne dikhaya ki bilingual speakers ne nayi bhasha seekhte waqt monolingual students se behtar perform kiya. Apne aap mein, yeh bahut zyaada hairan karne wala nahi hai. French aur Spanish dono Romance bhashayein hain, isliye grammar aur vocabulary ke shared features hain jo English mein majood nahi hain jo sochne yogya roop se ek advantage provide kar sakte hain. Mazeed interesting, halanki, yeh hai ki Spanish/English bilinguals ke beech bhi, jinhone Spanish classes bhi li thin, unhone baad mein French seekhne ki zarurat padne par mazeed behtar kiya. Kaaran yeh lagta hai ki classes lena us cheez ko banane mein assist (madhad) karta hai jise study ke authors bhashatmak jagrukta (metalinguistic awareness) kehte hain, ek aise tareeqe se jo simply kisi bhasha ko informally jaan'ne se nahi hota. Do tarah ke bilingual speakers ke beech ka farq mukhya roop se metalearning par aaya: ek group ke paas bhasha ki content knowledge thi, lekin jis group ne classes li thin unke paas is baare mein bhi knowledge thi ki ek bhasha mein jankari kaise structured hoti hai.

Na hi metalearning ka yeh idea bhashon tak seemit hai. Linguistic examples ko study karna aksar aasan hota hai kyunki metalearning aur regular learning ka ek saaf separation hota hai. Yeh isliye hai kyunki unrelated bhashon ke contents, jaise vocabulary aur grammar, aksar kaafi different hote hain, bhale hi metalearning structure same ho. French vocabulary seekhna aapko Chinese vocabulary seekhne mein bahut zyaada madad nahi karega, lekin French mein vocabulary acquisition (shabd-sangrah haasil karna) kaise kaam karta hai ise samajhna nishchit roop se Chinese seekhne mein bhi madad karega. Jab tak mera dost aur main languages seekhne ke apne saal ke aakhiri country tak pahunche the, khud ko immersion mein jhonkne aur shuruat se ek nayi bhasha seekhne ki process vyavaharik roop se ek routine ban chuki थी. Korean ke words aur grammar bhale hi poori tarah se naye rahe hon, lekin learning ki process pehle se hi achhi tarah chali hui (well trodden) thi. Metalearning saare subjects mein exist karti hai, lekin ise regular learning se independently examine karna aksar harder ho sakta hai.

## How to Draw Your Map

_(Apna Map Kaise Banayein)_

Ab jab aapke paas kuch idea hai ki metalearning kya hai aur tezi se seekhne mein iska kya importance hai, aap apne khud ke learning prayason mein ek edge (fayda) paane ke liye ise kaise apply kar sakte hain? Do mukhya tareeqe hain: short term ke dauran aur long term ke dauran.

**Short term** ke dauran, aap ek learning project ke pehle aur uske dauran apni metalearning ko behtar banane par focus karne ke liye research kar sakte hain. Ultralearning, apni intensity aur self-directed nature ke kaaran, normal schooling prayason ke mukable bahut zyaada higher variance (badlav/antat) ka opportunity rakhti hai. Ek achha ultralearning project, excellent materials aur kya seekhne ki zarurat hai iski awareness ke saath, formal schooling ke mukable jaldi complete hone ka potential rakhta hai. Intensive immersion ke zariye bhasha seekhna lambi classes ko hara (beat) sakta hai. Aakramak raftaar wale coding bootcamps participants ko ek aise level tak pahuncha sakte hain jahan woh normal undergraduate degree walon ke mukable jobs ke liye bahut zyaada tezi se compete kar sakein. Yeh isliye hai kyunki aap apne project ko apne exact needs aur abilities ke mutabik tailor (dhal) sakte hain, school mein apnaye gaye sabhi ke liye ek hi size (one-size-fits-all) wale approach se bachte hue. Halanki, bina soche-samjhe chun'ne aur badtar sthiti mein pahunchna ka danger bhi hota hai. Metalearning research is problem se bachti hai aur aapko un points ko seekhne mein madad karti hai jahan aap yathasthiti (status quo) par ek mahatvapurna advantage haasil karne mein kabil ho sakte hain.

**Long term** ke dauran, aap jitne zyaada ultralearning projects karenge, aapke general metalearning skills ka set utna hi bada hoga. Aap jaankenge ki seekhne ke liye aapki capacity (kshamta) kya hai, aap apne samay ko kaise sabse behtar schedule kar sakte hain aur apni motivation ko manage kar sakte hain, aur aapke paas samanya problems se nipatne ke liye well-tested strategies hongi. Jaise-jaise aap zyaada cheezein seekhenge, aap mazeed aatmavishwas acquire karenge, jo aapko kam niraasha (frustration) ke saath learning ki process ko mazeed enjoy karne ki izazat dega.

Is chapter mein, main agle section ka zyaada tar hissa short-term research strategies ko devot karne ja raha hoon, kyunki unse aapko sabse zyaada fayda milega. Halanki, yeh zor metalearning ke long-term asaron ke importance ko kam nahi karna chahiye. Ultralearning ek skill hai, bilkul bicycle chalane ki tarah. Aapko iska jitna zyaada abhyas milega, aap ise achhi tarah se kaise karna hai iske liye utne hi zyaada skills aur knowledge pick karenge. Yeh long-term advantage nishchit roop se short-term benefits se bada hota hai aur jab doosron mein dekha jata hai toh ise intelligence ya talent samajhne ki galti karna sabse aasan hota hai. Meri umeed hai ki jaise-jaise aapko ultralearning mein mazeed practice milegi, aap tezi se aur mazeed effectively seekhne ke liye unmein se kai skills ko automatically apply karna shuru kar denge.

## Determining Why, What, and How

_(Why, What, Aur How Tay Karna)_

Mujhe kisi vishisht (specific) project ke liye ki jaane wali metalearning research ko teen sawaalon mein todna useful lagta hai: **“Why?,” “What?,” aur “How?”**

- **“Why?”** aapki seekhne ki motivation ko samajhne ko sandarbhit (refers to) karta hai. Agar aap exactly jaante hain ki aap koi skill ya subject kyun seekhna chahte hain, toh aap apna project exactly usi par focus karke bahut saara samay bacha sakte hain jo aapke liye sabse zyaada matter karta hai.
- **“What?”** un knowledge aur abilities ko sandarbhit karta hai jinhein aapko safal hone ke liye acquire karne ki zarurat hogi. Cheezon ko concepts, facts, aur procedures mein todna aapko yeh map karne kabil bana sakta hai ki aap kis tarah ke obstacles ka samna karenge aur unhein kaise sabse behtar overcome karenge.
- **“How?”** un resources, environment, aur methods ko sandarbhit karta hai jinhein aap seekhte waqt use karenge. Yahan saavdhaan choices karna aapki overall kushalata (effectiveness) mein ek bada farq la sakta hai.

In teen sawaalon ko dimaag mein rakh kar, aaiye unmein se har ek par ek nazar daalein aur dekhein ki aap apna map kaise draw kar sakte hain.

## Answering “Why?”

_(“Why?” Ka Javab Dena)_

Pehla sawaal jiska javab dene ki koshish karni hai woh yeh hai ki aap kyun seekh rahe hain aur iska is baat par kya prabhav (implies) padta hai ki aapko project ko kaise approach karna chahiye. Vyavaharik roop se (Practically speaking), aap jo projects haath mein lete hain unke paas do vyapak motivations mein se ek hone wala hai: instrumental (vikalp-moolak/sadhnatmak) aur intrinsic (andharuni/swabhavik).

**Instrumental** learning projects woh hote hain jinhein aap ek different, gair-learning result (non-learning result) haasil karne ke maqsad se seekh rahe hain. Pehle zikr kiye gaye Diana Fehsenfeld ke case par vichar karne, jinhone ek librarian ke roop mein kuch dashakon ke baad paaya ki unki job lupt/gair-zaruri (obsolete) ho rahi thi. Computerized file systems aur budget cuts ka matlab tha ki unhein relevant bane rehne ke liye naye skills seekhne ki zarurat hogi. Unhone kuch research ki aur faisla kiya ki aisa karne ka sabse behtar tarika statistics aur data visualization par ek mazboot pakad haasil karna hoga. Is case mein, woh statistics aur data visualization ke prati apne kisi gehre pyaar ke kaaran nahi seekh rahi thin balki isliye seekh rahi thin kyunki unhein vishwas tha ki aisa karne se unke career ko fayda pahunchega.

**Intrinsic** projects woh hote hain jinhein aap unke apne hi roop mein pursue kar rahe hain. Agar aap hamesha se French bolna chahte the, bhale hi aap sure na hon ki aap iska use kaise karenge, toh yeh ek intrinsic project hai. Intrinsic ka matlab useless (bematlab) nahi hota. French seekhne ke fayde baad mein ho sakte hain jab aap travel karne ka faisla karein ya aapko apne kaam par France ke kisi client ke saath kaam karne ki zarurat ho. Farq yeh hai ki aap subject ko uske apne hi roop mein seekh rahe hain, kisi doosre outcome ke ek madhyam (means) ke roop mein nahi.

Agar aap mukhya roop se instrumental kaaranon se kisi project ko pursue kar rahe hain, toh research ka ek additional step karna aksar ek achha idea hota hai: yeh determine karna ki kya sawaal ke ghere mein majood skill ya topic ko seekhna actually aapko aapka goal haasil karne mein madad karega. Maine aksar aise logon ke stories sune hain jo apne career ki progress se un-happy the jinhone faisla kiya ki graduate school jaana hi javab hai. Agar unke paas sirf ek MBA ya ek MA hota, toh employers unhein mazeed seriously lete, woh sochte hain, aur unke paas woh career hota jiske woh icchuk hain. Isliye woh do saal ke liye school chale jaate hain, daso hazar dollars ka student debt ikhatha kar lete hain, aur discover karte hain ki unke naye bane credentials actually unhein pehle se bahut zyaada behtar job opportunities nahi dilate. Yahan fix yeh hai ki apni research pehle karein. Shuru karne se pehle yeh determine karein ki kya kisi topic ko seekhne ka wahi asar hone ki sambhavna hai jo aap chahte hain.

### Tactic: The Expert Interview Method

_(Ranniti: Expert Interview Method)_

Is tarah ki research karne ka mukhya tarika un logon se baat karna hai jinhone pehle se wahi haasil kar liya hai jise aap haasil karna chahte hain. Maan lijiye aap ek safal architect banna chahte hain aur sochte hain ki design skills par maharat haasil karna sabse behtar step ho sakta hai. Shuru karne se pehle, kuch safal architects se baat karna ek achha idea hoga taaki ek ehsaas (sense) haasil kiya ja sake ki kya woh sochte hain ki aapka project actually aapke intended goal mein madad karega. Bhale hi is method ka use research process ke kai parts ke liye kiya ja sakta hai, maine ise instrumental projects ki janch (vetting) karne ke liye khhasakar keemti paaya hai. Agar koi aisa insaan jinhone pehle se us goal ko accomplish kar liya hai jise aap haasil karna chahte hain, woh nahi sochta ki aapka learning project use paane mein madad karega ya sochta hai ki yeh kisi doosre skill par maharat haasil karne ke mukable kam important hai, toh yeh ek achha sign hai ki aapka motivation aur project aapas mein misaligned (bina mel ke) hain.

Aise logon ko dhoondhna utna hard nahi hai jitna yeh sunne mein lagta hai. Agar aapka goal career se related hai, toh un logon ko dekhein jinke paas woh career hai jise aap chahte hain aur unhein ek email bhejein. Aap unhein apne majooda workplace, conferences, ya seminars mein, ya yahan tak ki Twitter ya LinkedIn jaise social networking websites par paa sakte hain. Agar aapka goal kisi aur cheez se related hai, toh aap online un forums mein khoj sakte hain jo us subject ke liye samarpit (dedicated) hain jise aap seekhna chahte hain. Agar aap programming seekhna chahte hain, apne khud ke apps banane ke goal ke saath, for example, aap programming ya app development ke liye dedicated online forums paa sakte hain. Phir aapko bas un frequent posters (baar-baar post karne walon) ko dekhna hai jinke paas lagta hai ki woh knowledge hai jise aap dhoondh rahe hain aur unhein email karein.

Kisi expert tak pahunchna aur ek meeting set up karna bhi hard nahi hai, lekin yeh ek aisa step hai jisse kai log peeche hat te (shy away from) hain. Kai log, khhasakar hamare beech ke antarmukhi (introverts), salah maangne ke liye kisi stranger tak pahunchna ke idea se peeche hat jaate (recoil) hain. Woh chintit hote hain ki unhein reject kar diya jayega, ignore kiya jayega, ya kisi insaan ka samay lene ke dharstata (presuming) ke liye unpar chillaya bhi jayega. Truth yeh hai ki, halanki, aisa shayad hi kabhi hota hai. Zyaada tar experts salah offer karne ke liye taiyar rehte hain aur is thought se prashansit (flattered) feel karte hain ki koi unke experience se seekhna chahta hai. Key ek simple, to-the-point email likhna hai, yeh explain karte hue ki aap un tak kyun pahunch rahe hain aur pooch rahe hain ki kya woh kuch simple sawaalon ke javab dene ke liye fifteen minutes nikaal sakte hain. Email ko sankshept (concise) aur gair-dhamki-bhara (non-threatening) banayein. Fifteen minutes se zyaada ya lagataar mentorship (marghdarshan) ke liye mat maangien. Bhale hi kuch experts un tareeqon se aapki madad karke khush hon, pehle email mein bahut zyaada maangna achha aacharan (good form) nahi hai.

Kya ho agar woh insaan jiska aap interview lena chahte hain aapke city mein na rehta ho? Us case mein, phone ya online calls bade alternatives hain. Email bhi aakhiri mauqe par (in a pinch) kaam kar sakta hai, lekin maine paaya hai ki text aksar tone ko achhi tarah translate nahi karta, aur aap aksar us tareeqe ko sense karne se chhook jaate hain jo insaan aapke project ke baare mein feel karta hai. Kisi baat ko utsahheen tareeqe se (lukewarmly) "great idea" kehna versus enthusiastically kehna duniya bhar ka farq la sakta hai, phir bhi woh baareek farq (nuance) miss ho jata hai agar aap sirf text ke zariye communicate karte hain.

Bhale hi aapka project intrinsically motivated ho, “Why?” poochna tab bhi bahut useful hai. Zyaada tar learning plans jinqi aap nakal (emulate) karna chun sakte hain, woh curriculum designers ke is idea par based honge ki aapke seekhne ke liye kya important hai. Agar yeh aapke apne goals ke saath perfectly lined up nahi hain, toh aap aakhirkar aisi cheezon ko seekhne mein bahut saara samay bita sakte hain jo aapke liye important nahi hain ya un cheezon ko kam mahatva (underemphasizing) de sakte hain jo matter karti hain. Is tarah ke projects ke liye, apne aap se poochna useful hai ki aap kya seekhne ki koshish kar rahe hain kyunki yeh aapko aapke goals ke saath unke fit hone ke liye different study plans ko evaluate karne mein madad karega.

## Answering “What?”

_(“What?” Ka Javab Dena)_

Ek baar jab aapne is baat par pakad bana li ki aap kyun seekh rahe hain, toh aap dekhna shuru kar sakte hain ki aapke subject mein knowledge kaise structured hai. Aisa karne ka ek achha tarika paper ke ek sheet par teen columns likhna hai jinke headings hon **“Concepts,” “Facts,” aur “Procedures.”** Phir un saari cheezon ko brainstorm karein jinhein aapko seekhne ki zarurat hogi. Isse koi farq nahi padta ki list is stage par perfectly complete ya accurate hai ya nahi. Aap ise baad mein hamesha badal (revise) sakte hain. Aapka goal yahan ek rough pehli baari (first pass) paana hai. Ek baar jab aap seekhna shuru kar dete hain, toh aap list ko adjust kar sakte hain agar aap discover karte hain ki aapke categories kaafi sahi nahi hain.

### Concepts

_(Avadharnayein)_
Pehle column mein, koi bhi aisi cheez likhein jise samajhne ki zarurat hai. Concepts aise ideas hain jinhein aapko lachile tareeqon (flexible ways) mein samajhne ki zarurat hai taaki woh useful ho sakein. Math aur physics, for example, dono aise subjects hain jo mukhya roop se concepts ki taraf jhukte hain. Kuch subjects concept/fact ke batware ko paar karte hain, jaise law, jisme legal principles hote hain jinhein samajhne ki zarurat hoti hai, saath hi details hoti hain jinhein memorize karne ki zarurat hoti hai. In general, agar kisi cheez ko samajhne ki zarurat hai, sirf memorize karne ki nahi, toh main ise facts ke liye doosre column ke bajaye is column mein rakhta hoon.

### Facts

_(Tathya)_
Doosre column mein, koi bhi aisi cheez likhein jise memorize karne ki zarurat hai. Facts aisi koi bhi cheez hain jo agar aap unhein bilkul yaad rakh sakein toh kafi hain. Aapko unhein bahut zyaada gehrai se samajhne ki zarurat nahi hai, jab tak ki aap unhein sahi situations mein recall kar sakein. Languages, for instance, vocabulary, pronunciation, aur thodi kam had tak grammar ke baare mein facts se bhari hoti hain. Yahan tak ki concept-heavy subjects mein bhi aam taur par kuch facts hote hain. Agar aap calculus seekh rahe hain, toh aapko gehrai se samajhne ki zarurat hogi ki derivatives kaise kaam karte hain, lekin kuch trigonometric identities ko memorize karna hi kafi ho sakta hai.

### Procedures

_(Prakriyayein)_
Teesre column mein, koi bhi aisi cheez likhein jise practice karne ki zarurat hai. Procedures aise actions hain jinhein perform karne ki zarurat hoti hai aur inme shayad bahut zyaada conscious thinking (sachet soch) shamil nahi hoti. Bicycle chalana seekhna, for instance, lagbhag poori tarah se procedural hai aur isme mukhya roop se koi facts ya concepts shamil nahi hote. Kai doosre skills mukhya roop se procedural hote hain, jabki doosron ke paas ek procedural component ho sakta hai phir bhi memorize karne ke liye facts aur samajhne ke liye concepts hote hain. Ek bhasha mein nayi vocabulary seekhne ke liye facts ko memorize karne ki zarurat hoti hai, lekin pronunciation ke liye practice ki zarurat hoti hai aur isliye yeh is column mein aati hai.

### Using This Analysis to Draw Your Map

_(Apna Map Draw Karne Ke Liye Is Vishleshan Ka Use Karna)_

Ek baar jab aap apna brainstorm khatam kar lein, toh un concepts, facts, aur procedures ko underline karein jo sabse zyaada challenging hone wale hain. Yeh aapko ek achha idea dega ki mukhya learning bottlenecks (badhayein) kya hone wali hain aur aapko un difficulties ko overcome karne ke liye methods aur resources khojna shuru karwa sakta hai.

Aap recognize kar sakte hain ki medicine seekhne ke liye bahut zyaada memorization ki zarurat hoti hai, isliye aap spaced-repetition software jaise system mein invest kar sakte hain. Agar aap mathematics seekh rahe hain, toh aap recognize kar sakte hain ki khhas concepts ki gehrai se samajh hi pechida spot (tricky spot) hone wala hai aur un concepts ko doosre logon ko explain karne mein samay bitane par vichar karein taaki aap unhein sach mein khud samajh sakein. Yeh jaan'na ki bottlenecks kya honge, aapko apne study samay ko mazeed efficient aur effective banane ke tareeqon ke baare mein sochne mein madad kar sakta hai, saath hi un tools se bachne mein jo aapke goal ke liye shayad bahut zyaada sahayak nahi honge.

Aksar yeh coarse-grained (mota-mota) vishleshan research ke agle phase mein badhne ke liye kafi hota hai. Halanki, mazeed experience ke saath, aap gehra dig kar sakte hain. Aap jin concepts, facts, aur procedures ko seekhne ki koshish kar rahe hain unki kuch khhas features ko dekh sakte hain taaki unhein mazeed effectively master karne ke tareeqe dhoondh sakein.

Jab maine apna portrait-drawing challenge shuru kiya tha, for instance, main jaanta tha ki safalata is baat par highly depend karegii ki main facial features ko kitna accurately size aur place kar sakta hoon. Zyaada tar log realistic faces draw nahi kar sakte kyunki agar woh attributes thode se bhi off hon (jaise chehre ko bahut wide banana ya eyes ko bahut high rakhna), toh woh chehroon ko pehchanne ki hamari sophisticated ability ke samne instantly galat dikhenge. Isliye, mujhe bahut saare sketches karne aur reference photos ko upar rakh kar (overlaying) unki comparison karne ka idea aaya. Us tareeqe se main jaldi se diagnose kar sakta tha ki main kis tarah ki errors kar raha tha bina guess kiye. Agar aap abhi is tarah ki predictions nahi kar sakte aur is tarah ki strategies ke saath nahi aa sakte, toh chinta mat karein. Yeh metalearning ka wahi long-term benefit hai jo mazeed projects karne se aata hai.

## Answering “How?”

_(“How?” Ka Javab Dena)_

Ab jab aapne do sawaalon ke javab de diye hain—aap kyun seekh rahe hain aur aap kya seekh rahe hain—yeh aakhiri sawaal ka javab dene ka samay hai: Aap ise kaise seekhne ja rahe hain?

Main kisi cheez ko kaise seekhenge iska javab dene ke liye do methods ko follow karne ka suggestion deta hoon: **Benchmarking** aur **The Emphasize/Exclude Method**.

### Benchmarking

_(Manak-Nirdharan)_
Kisi bhi learning project ko shuru karne ka tarika un samanya tareeqon (common ways) ko dhoondhna hai jisme log us skill ya subject ko seekhte hain. Yeh aapko ek default strategy ko ek starting point ke roop mein design karne mein madad kar sakta hai.

Agar main kisi aisi cheez ko seekhne ki koshish kar raha hoon jo school mein padhai jaati hai, maan lijiye computer science, neurology, ya history, toh ek cheez jo main karunga woh hai schools mein us subject ko sikhane ke liye use kiye jaane wale paathyakram (curricula) ko dekhna. Yeh ek single class ka syllabus ho sakta hai ya, jaise meri MIT Challenge ke case mein tha, ek poori degree ke liye course list. Jab main cognitive science ke baare mein mazeed jaan'na chahta tha, toh maine un textbooks ki ek list dhoodhi jise University of San Diego ka Cognitive Science doctoral program un incoming students ke liye recommend karta hai jinka cognitive science background nahi hai. Is approach ke liye vichar karne ke liye acche resources universities hain (MIT, Harvard, Yale, aur Stanford acche examples hain lekin akele nahi hain). Aam taur par course lists aur syllabi unke websites par majood students ko dekhne ke liye available hote hain.

Agar main kisi gair-academic subject ya ek professional skill ko seekhne ki koshish kar raha hoon, toh main iske bajaye online un logon ki khoj karunga jinhone pehle us skill ko seekha hai ya us subject par maharat haasil karne ke liye available resources par focus karne ke liye Expert Interview Method ka use karunga. Lagbhag kisi bhi skill ke liye online khoj karne mein bitaya gaya ek ghante courses, articles, aur ise kaise seekhna hai iske liye recommendations lekar aana chahiye. Yahan samay invest karne ke adbhut fayde (incredible benefits) ho sakte hain kyunki aap jin materials ka use karte hain unki quality aapki kushalata (effectiveness) mein orders-of-magnitude (kai guna) farq paida kar her sakti hai. Bhale hi aap turant seekhna shuru karne ke liye utsuk (eagerness) hon, abhi kuch ghante invest karna aapko baad mein daso ya saikdon ghante bacha sakta hai.

### The Emphasize/Exclude Method

_(Zor Dene/Hataane Ka Tarika)_
Ek baar jab aapko ek default curriculum mil jaye, toh aap isme modifications (badlav) karne par vichar kar sakte hain. Mujhe skills ke saath aisa karna mazeed aasan lagta hai jinke paas saaf safalata ke criteria (obserious success criteria) hote hain (maan lijiye drawing, bhashayein, ya music) aur jiske liye aap aam taur par study karne se pehle subject topics ke relative importance par ek guess laga sakte hain. Conceptual subjects ya topics ke liye jahan aap syllabus mein terms ke matlab bhi nahi samajh sakte, behtar hoga ki jab tak aap thoda zyaada seekh na lein tab tak apne benchmark ke mazeed paas tike rahein.

The Emphasize/Exclude Method mein sabse pehle adhyayan ke un kshetron (areas of study) ko dhoondhna shuil hai jo un goals ke saath align hote hain jinhein aapne apni research ke pehle part mein identify kiya tha. Agar aap French seekh rahe hain do hafte ke liye Paris jaane aur shops aur restaurants mein bolne ke idea ke saath, toh main correctly spell karne kabil hone ke bajaye pronunciation par kahin zyaada focus karunga. Agar aap programming solely apna khud ka app banane ke liye seekh rahe hain, toh main computation ke theories ke mukable app development ke andaruni kaamyon (inner workings) par focus karunga.

The Emphasize/Exclude Method ka doosra hissa aapke benchmarked curriculum ke un tatvon (elements) ko chhodna (omit) ya delay karna hai jo aapke goals ke saath align nahi hote. For example, Mandarin Chinese seekhne ke liye ek samanya recommendation, jise prasiddh linguist aur Sinologist Victor Mair jaise logon dwara samarthit (advocated) kiya gaya hai, characters ko padhne ki koshish karne se pehle bolna seekhne par focus karna hai. Yeh akela raasta available nahi hai, lekin agar aapka mukhya goal bolna hai, toh fluency ka yeh raasta mazeed effective ho sakta hai.

## How Much Planning Should You Do?

_(Aapko Kitni Planning Karni Chahiye?)_

Ek sawaal jiska aap samna kar sakte hain woh yeh hai ki research karna kab rokna hai aur bas shuru kaise karna hai. Swa-shiksha (self-directed learning) par sahitya, jaisa ki aam taur par abhyas kiya jata hai, pradarshit karta hai ki zyaada tar log sambhavit learning goals, methods, aur resources ki ek poori janch (thorough investigation) karne mein fail ho jaate hain. Iske bajaye woh learning ke jis bhi method ko chunte hain woh unke environment mein naturally saamne aata hai. Yeh saaf taur par jo abhyas kiya jata hai aur sabse behtar sambhavit method ka use karke jo efficiency possible hai uske beech ek gap chhodta hai. Halanki, research karna bhatkaane/taalne (procrastinating) ka ek tarika bhi ho सकता hai, khhasakar agar learning ka method uncomfortable ho. Bas thodi si mazeed research karna phir learning ke kaam se bachne ki ek strategy ban jata hai. Aapke approach mein hamesha kuch anischitta (uncertainty) rahegi, isliye aparyapt research (insufficient research) aur analysis paralysis (sochte hi rehna par action na lena) ke beech sahi sweet spot dhoondhna important hai. Aap jaante hain ki aap kab procrastinate kar rahe hain, isliye bas shuru karein.

### The 10 Percent Rule

_(Das Pratishat Ka Niyam)_
Ek achha rule of thumb yeh hai ki aapko shuru karne se pehle research mein apne total expected learning time ka lagbhag **10 percent** invest karna chahiye. Agar aap cheh mahine seekhne mein spend karne ki umeed karte hain, per week lagbhag char ghante, toh yeh lagbhag ek sau ghante ke barabar hoga, jo suggest karta hai ki aapko apni research karne mein lagbhag das ghante, ya do hafte spend karne chahiye. Yeh percentage thoda kam ho jayega jaise-jaise aapka project bade paimane par (scales up) jayega, isliye agar aap pach sau ya ek hazar ghante learning karne ka plan banate hain, toh mujhe nahi lagta ki yeh nishchit roop se pachas ya sau ghante ki research ki demand karta hai, balki shayad aapke samay ke 5 percent ke paas. Yahan goal har ek learning possibility ko thakana nahi hai balki simply yeh sure karna hai ki aap alternatives ke baare mein soche bina pehle possible resource ya method se chipak (latched onto) nahi gaye hain.

Apni MIT Challenge shuru karne se pehle, maine saare course materials ke beech se nikalne (combing through) mein part-time lagbhag cheh mahine bitaaye. Ek achha idea shuru karne se pehle learning ke samanya tareeqon, popular resources, aur tools ke saath-saath unki strengths aur weaknesses ke baare mein aware hona hai. Lambe projects derailed (patri se utarne) aur delayed hone ke mazeed opportunities provide karte hain, isliye shuruat mein sahi research karna baad mein badi matra mein samay aasaani se bacha sakta hai.

### Diminishing Returns and Marginal Benefit Calculation

_(Ghatt-te Pratiphal Aur Simant Fayde Ka Hisab)_
Metalearning research koi aisi onetime activity nahi hai jo aap sirf apne project ko shuru karne se pehle karte hain. Jaise-jaise aap zyaada seekhte hain, aapko research karna jaari rakhna chahiye. Aksar obstacles aur opportunities aapke shuru karne se pehle saaf nahi hote, isliye phir se moolyankan karna (reassessing) learning process ka ek zaroori step hai. Meri portrait-drawing challenge ke dauran, for instance, maine lagbhag aadhe raaste mein discover kiya ki mujhe apne sketch-and-compare method se ghatt-te pratiphal (diminishing returns) mil rahe the. Maine realize kiya ki mujhe drawing ke liye ek behtar technique ki zarurat thi jisme higher accuracy ho. Isne mujhe research ke ek doosre round karne par dhakela, jo mujhe Vitruvian Studio dwara padhaye jaane wale ek course tak le gaya, jisne ek mazeed systematic method ko detail se bataya jisne meri accuracy ko bahut badha diya. Maine apni original research mein ise notice nahi kiya tha kyunki main apni khud se develop kiye gaye technique ki kami (deficiency) se aware nahi tha.

Sawaal ka ek mazeed sophisticated (jatil/samajhdaari bhara) javab ki kab aur kaise research karni hai, regular learning se metalearning research ke simant faydon (marginal benefits) ki comparison karna hoga. Aisa karne ka ek tarika mazeed research karne mein kuch ghante spend karna hai—mazeed experts ka interview lena, mazeed resources ke liye online search karna, naye sambhavit techniques ke liye search karna—aur phir apne chune gaye raaste par mazeed learning karne mein kuch ghante spend karna. Dono par kuch samay spend karne ke baad, do gatividhiyon (activities) ke relative value ka ek quick assessment karein. Agar aapko aisa feel hota hai jaise metalearning research ne learning par spend kiye gaye ghante ke mukable zyaada contribute kiya, toh aap lagbhag ek aise point par hain jahan mazeed research karna abhi bhi beneficial hai. Agar aapne feel kiya ki extra research bahut zyaada sahayak nahi thi, toh aap pehle se majood plan par tike rehne mein mazeed behtar hain. Is tarah ka vishleshan ek cheez par depend karta hai jise _Law of Diminishing Returns_ ke roop mein jaana jata hai. Yeh bayan karta hai ki aap kisi gatividhi mein jitna zyaada samay invest karte hain (jaise mazeed research), fayde utne hi kamzor aur kamzor hote jayenge jaise-jaise aap ideal approach ke mazeed paas pahunchete hain. Agar aap research karte rehte hain, toh aakhirkar yeh simply mazeed learning karne ke mukable kam keemti hoga, isliye us point par aap safely learning par focus kar sakte hain. Vyavahar (practice) mein, research ka return lumpy (asaman) aur variable hota hai. Aap kuch ghante spend kar sakte hain aur kuch nahi paa sakte, phir aap apni progress ko tez karne ke liye perfect resource par stumble (takra) sakte hain.
