Jaise-jaise aap mazeed projects khatam karte hain, is point ko sahaj roop se (intuitively) judge karna aasan ho jata hai, lekin Law of Diminishing Returns aur 10 Percent Rule is baare mein achha anuman (good approximations) provide kar sakte hain ki kitni research karni hai aur kab.

## Long-Term Prospects for Metalearning

_(Metalearning Ke Long-Term Sambhavnayein)_

Abhi tak humne sirf short-term benefits ke baare mein baat ki hai. Halanki, metalearning ke asli fayde short term nahi balki long term hain. Woh kisi vishisht project mein nahi rehte balki ek learner ke roop mein aapki overall strengths ko influence karte hain.

Aap jo bhi project karte hain woh aapki general metalearning ko behtar banayega. Har project ke paas aapko naye learning methods, resources ikhatha karne ke naye tareeqe, behtar samay prabandhan (time management), aur apni motivation ko manage karne ke liye improved skills sikhane ka opportunity hota hai. Ek project mein safalata aapko apne agle project ko nidarrta ke saath aur bina kisi aatm-shakk (self-doubt) aur procrastination ke execute karne ka confidence degi. Ultimately, yeh asar kisi vishisht project ko karne ke asar se kahin bada hota hai. Unfortunately, yeh kuch aisa bhi hai jise kisi tactic ya tool mein ubaala (boiled down) nahi ja sakta. Long-term metalearning bas kuch aisi cheez hai jise aap experience ke saath acquire karte hain.

Ultralearning ke fayde hamesha pehle project se saaf nahi hote kyunki woh pehla project tab hota hai jab aap apni metalearning ability ke sabse lowest level par hote hain. Aap jo bhi project complete karte hain woh aapko agle se nipatne ke liye naye tools dega, ek achhi shrankhla (virtuorous cycle) shuru karte hue. Is book ke liye jin kai ultralearners ka maine interview liya unhone mujhe ek jaise kahani batayi: ki unhein individual projects mein apni accomplishments par garv tha lekin asli fayda yeh raha tha ki woh ab hard cheezon ko seekhne ki process ko samajhte the. Isne unhein doosre ambitious goals ko pursue karne ka confidence diya jinhon par unhone pehle vichar bhi nahi kiya hota. Yeh confidence aur ability hi ultralearning ke ultimate goals hain, bhale hi unhein shuruat se dekhna aksar hard hota hai. Yeh fayde, halanki, sirf kaam mein lagne (putting in the work) se hi haasil kiye ja sakte hain. Sabse behtar research, resources, aur strategies bematlab hain jab tak ki aap seekhne ke liye ek kendrit prayas (concentrated efforts) ke saath follow up nahi karte. Yeh hamein agle ultralearning niyan tak le jata hai: focus.

---

# Chapter 5 — Principle 2: Focus

### _(Niyam 2 — Focus: Apni Chhaku Ko Tez Karein)_

---

> _"Now I will have less distraction."_
> _(Ab mujhe bhatkaane wali cheezein [distraction] kam milengi.)_
> — Leonhard Euler, mathematician, apni right eye ki roshni khone par

---

Agar scientific shresthata (greatness) ke liye koi sabse asambhavit ummedwar (unlikely candidate) ho sakta tha, toh woh Mary Somerville thin. Woh eighteenth century mein ek gareeb Scottish family mein paida hui thin, jab higher education ko ek lady ke liye sahi nahi maana jata tha. Unki mother ne unhein padhne se nahi roka, lekin poore samaj (society at large) ne ise pasand nahi kiya. Unki ek aunt ne, unka yeh behaviour dekh kar, unki mother se comment kiya, “Mujhe hairani hai ki tum Mary ko padhne mein apna samay barbaad karne deti ho, woh usse zyaada kabhi nahi seeti jitna ki ek mard seeta.” Jab unhein briefly school attend karne ka ek opportunity mila, toh unki mother ko us kharch par afsos hua. Somerville ne explain kiya, “woh santusht (contented) hotin agar maine sirf achhi tarah likhna aur hisab-kitab rakhna seekha hota, jo ki ek aurat se jaan'ne ki umeed ki jaati thi.” Ek aurat ke roop mein, unhein isse bhi bade obstacles ka samna karna pada, jahan ghar ke kaamon aur expectations ko kisi bhi tarah ke swa-shiksha (self-education) par prathmikta (precedence) di jaati thi. “Ek mard business ka bahana (plea) banakar hamesha apne samay par control rakh sakta hai, ek aurat ko aise kisi excuse ki izazat nahi hoti,” unhone dukh jataya. Unke pehle husband, Samuel Greig, auraton mein learning ke sakht khilaf the.

Phir bhi un obstacles ke bavajood, Somerville ki uplabdhiyan (accomplishments) vishal thin. Unhone mathematics mein awards jeete, kai bhashon ko faraatedar (fluency) seekha, aur painting karna aur piano bajana jaanti thin. 1835 mein, woh, German astronomer Caroline Herschel ke saath, _Royal Astronomical Society_ mein chuni jaane wali pehli auraten thin. Jo uplabdhi aakhirkar unhein shohrat (fame) tak le gayi woh Pierre-Simon Laplace ke _Traité de mécanique céleste_ ke pehle do volumes ka unka translation aur vistar (expansion) tha, jo gravitation ke theory aur advanced mathematics par ek vishal paanch-volume ka kaam tha, jise Isaac Newton dwara _Principia Mathematica_ likhne ke baad se sabse badi intellectual uplabdhi ke roop mein saraaha gya. Laplace ne khud comment kiya ki duniya mein Somerville hi akeli aurat thin jo unke kaam ko samajhti thin.

Somerville ki sthiti aur unki uplabdhiyon ke beech ke is vishal farq (vast discrepancy) ka sabse aasan explanation genius hoga. Yeh bina kisi shakk ke sach hai ki unke paas ek incredibly sharp mind tha. Unki daughter ne ek baar comment kiya ki jab unhein padhaya ja raha tha, toh unki mother be-sabr (impatient) ho sakti thin. “Mujhe achhi tarah yaad hai unka patla safed haath be-sabri se kitab ya slate ki taraf point karta tha—‘Kya tum ise nahi dekhti? Isme koi difficulty nahi hai, yeh poori tarah saaf hai.’” Halanki, unki life ke unke descriptions ko gehrai se padhne par, yeh dikhne wala genius kai asurakshaon (insecurities) se ghira tha. Unhone “bad memory” (kharab yaadashth) hone ka claim kiya, bachpan mein nayi cheezon ko seekhne ke struggles ko bayan kiya, aur yahan tak ki ek point par “apne aap ko ek foreign bhasha bolna seekhne ke liye bahut zyaada boodha (too old)” socha tha. Chahe woh ek shisht namrata (polite modesty) thi ya genuine roop se aparyaptata ki bhavnaayein (feelings of inadequacy), hum nahi jaan sakte, lekin yeh kam se kam is idea mein darar (cracks) zaroor daalta hai ki unhone ek atoot aatmavishwas (unshakable confidence) aur talent ki jagah se learning ko approach kiya.

Mazeed gehrai se dekhne (peering deeper) par, Somerville ki ek doosri picture saamne aati hai. Unke paas ek teez dimaag (keen intellect) tha, haan, lekin jo cheez unke paas isse bhi badi matra mein thi woh thi focus karne ki ek asadharn kshamta (exceptional ability to focus). Ek kishor (adolescent) ke roop mein, jab unhein bed par bhej diya jata tha aur padhne ke liye candle dene se mana kar diya jata tha, toh woh mathematics mein Euclid ke kaamon par dimaag mein hi grind through karti thin. Apne bachhe ko breastfeed karne ke dauran bhi, ek parichit (acquaintance) ne unhein botany padhne ke liye encourage kiya, isliye unhone har subah “us science ke adhyayan ke liye ek ghante” devote kiye. Yahan tak ki apni sabse badi uplabdhi, Laplace ke _Traité de mécanique céleste_ ke translation aur expansion ke dauran bhi, unhein bacchon ko paalna, cooking, aur cleaning ke ghar ke saare kaamon ko nibhaana padta تھا. “Mujhe hamesha ghar par hona maana jata tha,” woh explain karti hain, “aur mere dost aur acquaintances mujhse milne ke maqsad se apne raaste se itna door aate the, unhein receive na karna nishthur (unkind) aur gair-udaar (ungenerous) hota. Nevertheless (phir bhi), main kabhi-kabhi annoyed ho jaati thi jab ek mushkil problem ke beech mein koi enter karta aur kehta, ‘Main aapke saath kuch ghante bitane aaya hoon.’ Halanki, maine aadat (habit) se ek subject ko chhodna aur use turant wapas resume (phir se shuru) karna seekh liya, jaise kisi kitab mein ek mark (bookmark) lagana jise main padh rahi hoon.”

Bade intellectual uplabdhiyon ke kshetra (realm) mein jaldi aur gehrai se focus karne ki ability lagbhag har jagah majood (ubiquitous) hai. Albert Einstein ne relativity ke general theory ke apne formulation ke dauran itni intensely focus kiya ki unhein stomach problems develop ho gaye thin. Mathematician Paul Erdős focus karne ki apni capacity ko badhane ke liye amphetamines ke heavy user the. Jab ek dost ne unse shart lagayi (bet) ki woh unhein chhod nahi sakte, bhale hi ek chhote samay ke liye, toh woh aisa karne mein kabil rahe. Baad mein, halanki, unhone shikayat ki ki akela nateeja yeh raha tha ki unki is bina-focus wali absence mein mathematics poore roop se ek mahina peeche chala gaya tha. Tivra focus ke in itihaas-pustakon (annals) mein, koi aksar tanhaa geniuses (solitary geniuses) ki ek picture conjures up (sochta) hai jo bina kisi bhatkaav (distraction) ke mehnat kar rahe hain, duniya ke chintao se mukt. Halanki yeh remarkable hai, main us tarah ke focus mein zyaada interested hoon jo Somerville ke paas lagta tha. Koi unke jaise environment mein, lagaatar distractions, kam social support, aur continuous obligations ke saath, kaise itna lamba focus manage kar sakta hai na keval subjects ki ek impressive choudai (breadth) ko seekhne ke liye, balki itni gehrai tak ki French mathematician Siméon Poisson ne ek baar remark kiya ki “France mein bees mard bhi nahi the jo [unki] kitab padh sakein”?

Somerville focus karne mein itni behtar kaise banin? Adarsh se kam sthitiyon (less-than-ideal conditions) mein mushkil dimaagi kaam poora karne mein hum unki strategies se kya bator (glean) sakte hain? Focus ke saath jo struggles logon ko aam taur par aate hain woh teen vyapak varieties mein aate hain: shuru karna (starting), bane rehna (sustaining), aur apne focus ki quality ko anukulit (optimizing) karna. Ultralearners in teen problems se nipatne ke liye solutions nikaalne mein relentless (bina thake lage rehne wale) hote hain, jo achhi tarah se focus karne aur gehrai se seekhne ki ability ka aadhar (basis) banate hain.

## Problem 1: Failing to Start Focusing (aka Procrastinating)

_(Problem 1: Focus Shuru Karne Mein Asafal Hona — Yaani Kaam Talna)_

Pehli problem jo kai logon ko hoti hai woh hai focus shuru karna. Iska sabse saaf pradarshan tab hota hai jab aap procrastinate (kaam talna) karte hain: us cheez ko karne ke bajaye jo aapko karni chahiye, aap kisi doosre kaam par lag jaate hain ya susti (slack off) dikhaate hain. Kuch logon ke liye, procrastination unki lives ki ek constant state hoti hai, ek task se doosri taraf tab tak bhaagte hue jab tak ki deadlines unhein focus karne par majboor na kar dein aur phir samay par kaam poora karne ke liye struggle karna pade. Doosre log procrastination ke mazeed tivra roopon (acute forms) se struggle karte hain jo khhas tarah ke tasks ke saath khud ko zahir karte hain. Main is doosri tarah ke insaan jaisa zyaada tha, jahan khhas tarah ki gatividhiyan (activities) thin jinpar main poora din procrastinate karne mein bita deta tha. Bhale hi mujhe apne blog ke liye essays likhne mein koi problems nahi thin, lekin jab mujhe is book ke liye research karni thi, toh maine apne kadam ghaseete (dragged my feet). Similarly, mujhe MIT classes ke videos dekhne aur baithne mein koi problem nahi thi, lekin maine hamesha pehle problem sets se kaafi darr (trepidation) ke saath nipta. Agar main jis intense schedule par tha woh na hota, toh maine aisa karne se bachne ke liye bahut lambe samay tak excuses dhoondhe hote. In fact, is chapter ko likhna un tasks mein se ek tha jisme maine bahut zyaada procrastinate kiya.

Hum procrastinate kyun karte hain? Simple javab yeh hai ki kisi level par ek tivra ichha (craving) hoti hai jo aapko kuch aur karne par dhakelti hai, us task ko karne ke prati ek na-pasandi (aversion) hoti hai, ya dono. Mere case mein, maine is chapter ko likhne par procrastinate kiya kyunki mere paas bahut saare ideas the aur main unsure tha ki shuru kahan se karoon. Meri chinta (anxiety) yeh thi ki paper par kuch committed karne se, is baat ka ek achha chance tha ki main aakhirkar ise kharab tareeqe se likh baithunga. Bewakoofana hai, main jaanta hoon. Lekin procrastinate karne ke zyaada tar motives bewakoofana hi hote hain jab aap unhein lafzon mein bayan karte hain, phir bhi woh aapki life par rule karne se nahi rukte. Jo mujhe procrastination ko overcome karne ke pehle step par lata hai: **jab aap procrastinate kar rahe hon toh ise recognize (pehchan'ne) karein.**

Bahut zyaada procrastination anjaane (unconscious) mein hota hai. Aap procrastinate kar rahe hote hain, lekin aap ise is tareeqe se andaruni roop se sweekar (internalize) nahi karte. Iske bajaye aap “ek behad zaroori break le rahe hain” ya “fun kar rahe hain, kyunki life hamesha sirf kaam ke baare mein nahi ho sakti.” Problem un beliefs mein nahi hai. Problem tab hai jab unka use actual behaviour ko chhupane (cover up) ke liye kiya jata hai—aap us cheez ko nahi karna chahte jis par aapko focus karne ki zarurat hai, ya toh isliye kyunki aap use karne ke directly khilaf (averse) hain ya isliye kyunki koi aisi cheez hai jise aap mazeed karna chahte hain. Yeh recognize karna ki aap procrastinate kar rahe hain, isse bachne ka pehla step hai.

Har baar jab aap procrastinate karein toh ek mental habit banayein; yeh recognize karne ki koshish karein ki aap us task ko na karne ki koi desire feel kar rahe hain ya kuch aur karne ki ek stronger desire feel kar rahe hain. Aap shayad apne aap se yeh bhi poochna chahein ki us moment par kaun si feeling mazeed powerful hai—kya problem yeh zyaada hai ki aapke paas kisi different activity ko karne ki ek strong tivra ichha (urge) hai (e.g., kuch khana, apna phone check karna, ek jhapki [nap] lena) ya aapke paas us cheez se bachne ki ek strong urge hai jise aapko karna chahiye kyunki aap kalpana karte hain ki yeh uncomfortable, painful, ya frustrating hoga? Yeh awareness progress karne ke liye zaroori hai, isliye agar aapko aisa feel hota hai jaise procrastination aapki ek weakness hai, toh problem ko fix karne ki koshish karne se pehle is awareness ko build karne ko apni pehli priority banayein.

Ek baar jab aap procrastinate karne ki apni tendency ko aasaani se aur automatically recognize kar sakein, jab yeh ho, toh aap impulse (is veg) ka virodh karne ke liye steps utha sakte hain. Ek tarika “crutches” (baisakhiyon) ya dimaagi tools ki ek shrankhla (series) ke roop mein sochna hai jo aapko procrastinate karne ki aapki tendency ke kuch sabse badtar hisson se nikalne mein madad kar sakein. Jaise-jaise aap us project par action lene mein behtar hote jaate hain jispar aap kaam kar rahe hain, in crutches ko badla ja sakta hai ya poori tarah se hataya ja sakta hai jab procrastination ab koi problem na rahe.

Pehli baisakhi (crutch) yeh recognize karne se aati hai ki kisi task mein jo kuch bhi unpleasant hota hai (agar aap iske khilaf averse hain) ya kisi alternative task ke baare mein jo pleasant hota hai (agar aap bhatkaav [distraction] ki taraf khinche hain) woh ek impulse hai jo actually utna lamba nahi tikta. Agar aap actually kaam karna shuru kar dete hain ya kisi potent distractor (mazboot bhatkaane wali cheez) ko ignore karte hain, toh aam taur par sirf kuch minutes lagte hain jab tak ki chinta ghulna (dissolve) shuru na ho jaye, yahan tak ki kaafi unpleasant tasks ke liye bhi. Isliye, ek achhi pehli crutch apne aap ko break lene se pehle maximum unpleasantness ke bas un thode minutes ko paar karne ke liye convince karna hai. Apne aap se yeh kehna ki aapko rukne aur kuch aur karne se pehle task par sirf paanch minutes spend karne ki zarurat hai, aksar aapko shuru karwane ke liye kafi hota hai. Akhirkar, lagbhag koi bhi kisi bhi cheez ke paanch minutes bardaasht (endure) kar sakta hai, chahe yeh kitna bhi boring, frustrating, ya difficult kyun na ho. Halanki, ek baar jab aap shuru kar dete hain, toh aap bina break liye lambe samay tak jaari rakh sakte hain.

Jaise-jaise aap progress karte hain, aapki pehli crutch raaste mein aana shuru ho sakti hai. Aap apne aap ko shuru karte hue paa sakte hain lekin phir, kyunki task unpleasant hai aur focus hard hai, productive hone ke liye paanch-minute ke rule ka bahut zyaada baar fayda uthaate hain. Agar aisa hai aur aapki problem get started hone mein asamarth hone se badalkar bahut zyaada baar breaks lene par shift ho gayi hai, toh aap thodi mazeed harder cheez try kar sakte hain, maan lijiye **Pomodoro Technique**: twenty-five minutes ka focus jiske baad ek five-minute ka break. Apne dimaag mein rakhein ki jab aap pehle ki kisi problem se mukhya roop se badhit (impeded) hon toh ek harder goal par switch na karna essential hai. Agar aap abhi bhi kaam shuru nahi kar sakte, yahan tak ki five-minute rule ke saath bhi, toh mazeed harder aur demanding crutches par switch karna ulta asar (backfire) kar sakta hai.

Kuch cases mein, niraasha (frustration) ka moment shuruat mein nahi aa sakta, lekin phir bhi yeh nirdharit karne yogya (predictable) hota hai. Jab main flash cards ke zariye Chinese characters seekh raha تھا, for instance, main hamesha haar maan'ne (give up) ka ek urge feel karta tha jab bhi mujhe apne cards mein se kisi ek ka javab yaad nahi aata tha. Main jaanta tha ki yeh feeling temporary thi, halanki, isliye maine apne liye ek rule add kiya: main kevel tabhi chhod (quit) sakta hoon jab maine sabse haal hi ke card ko correctly yaad kiya ho. Vyavahar (practice) mein, cards quick the, isliye isme aam taur par persistence (dradhta) ke sirf ek extra twenty ya thirty seconds lagte the; halanki, nateejatan flash cards karne ke liye mera sabr (patience) tezi se upar chala gya.

Aakhirkar, agar aapke project par kaam karna extreme procrastination se pareshan nahi hai, toh aap ek calendar ka use karne par switch karna chahenge jis par aap project par kaam karne ke liye pehle se apne din ke vishisht ghante (specific hours) nikaal lete hain. Yeh approach aapko apne seemit samay (limited time) ka sabse behtar upyog karne kabil banati hai. Halanki, yeh tabhi kaam karta hai agar aap actually ise follow karte hain. Agar aap apne aap ko chunked hours ke saath ek daily schedule set karte hue paate hain aur phir frequently doosra kuch karne ke liye ise ignore karte hain, toh shuruat par wapas jayein aur five-minute rule aur phir Pomodoro Technique ke saath dobara build up karne ki koshish karein.

Aakhirkar, aap Mary Somerville ke focus ke level tak pahunch sakte hain, ek aisa focus jise woh pal-pal ke aadhar (moment-to-moment basis) par activate kar sakti thin, yeh faisla karte hue ki kya unke paas nikaalne ke liye samay tha. Focus karne ki unki zabardast kshamta (formidable capacity) ke bavajood, aisa lagta hai ki Somerville bhi vishisht subjects ke adhyayan ke liye deliberately samay block karti thin. Isliye yeh ek sachet aadat (conscious habit) thi, na ki merely sahaj adhyayan (spontaneous studying), jisne unki kai safalataon ko kabil banaya. Apne liye, main paata hoon ki kuch learning activities intrinsically itni interesting hoti hain ki main bina kisi pressure ke unpar lambe samay tak focus kar sakta hoon. Mujhe MIT Challenge ke dauran lectures dekhne mein aam taur par koi problem nahi thi, for instance. Halanki, doosre tasks ke liye mujhe procrastinate karne ki apni desire ko paar karne ke liye five-minute rule ki zarurat thi. Agar mujhe apni files ko scan aur upload karna hota, toh woh aakhirkar unhein tackle karne se pehle aksar ek dher (pile) mein ikhatha ho jaati thin. Agar aapko ek stage peeche hatna (back up) pade toh kabhi bura feel mat karein; aap apni aversions ya bhatkaav ki tendency ko control nahi kar sakte, lekin practice ke saath aap unke impact ko kam kar sakte hain.

## Problem 2: Failing to Sustain Focus (aka Getting Distracted)

_(Problem 2: Focus Barkarar Rakhne Mein Asafal Hona — Yaani Bhatakna)_

Doosri problem jiska samna log aam taur par karte hain woh hai focus ko barkarar rakhne (sustain) mein asamarthta. Yeh tab ho sakta hai jab aap kisi cheez ko study ya practice karne ke liye baithe hon, lekin phir aapka phone buzz karta hai aur aap door dekhte hain, ek dost hello kehne ke liye door par knock karta hai, ya aap ek khayali pulao (daydream) mein ghoom jaate hain aur sirf yeh realize karte hain ki aap pichle fifteen minutes se same paragraph ko ghoor rahe hain. Focus shuru karne ke challenge ki tarah, focus barkarar rakhna important hai agar aap hard cheezon ko seekhne mein progress karna chahte hain. Isse pehle ki main focus barkarar rakhne ke tareeqon ke baare mein baat karoon, halanki, main ek sawaal uthana chahta hoon ki kis tarah ka focus sustain karne ke liye sabse behtar hai.

**Flow**, ek concept jiske pravartak (pioneered) psychologist Mihály Csíkszentmihályi hain, use aksar is model ke roop mein use kiya jata hai ki ideal focus kaisa dikhta hai. Yeh dimaag ki woh state hai jise aap “zone mein hone” (in the zone) se joaddte hain. Aap bhatkane wale vicharon (distracting thoughts) se interrupt hona band ho jaate hain, aur aapka mind haath mein majood task mein poori tarah se absorbed (leeng) ho jata hai. Flow woh enjoyable state hai jo boredom (bore hone) aur niraasha (frustration) ke theek beech slide karti hai, jab ek task na toh bahut hard hota hai aur na hi bahut aasan. Is gulabi picture (rosy picture) ke, halanki, kuch aashlochnak (detractors) hain. Psychologist K. Anders Ericsson, jo deliberate practice ke peeche ke researcher hain, tark karte hain ki flow ke paas aisi characteristics hain jo “spasht goals aur feedback aur galti sudharne ke opportunities (error correction) ke moolyankan ke liye deliberate practice ki demands ke saath asangat (inconsistent) hain. Hence (Isliye), kushal performers domain-related gatividhiyon ke hisse ke roop mein flow ke experiences ka anand le sakte hain aur unhein dhoondh sakte hain, lekin aise experiences deliberate practice ke dauran paida nahi honge.” Ultralearning, performance-driven learning par apne similar focus ke saath, flow ke liye unsuitable dikhegi, theek usi tareeqe se jaise Ericsson ne originally deliberate practice ke liye tark diya tha.

Mera apna thought yeh hai ki ultralearning ke dauran ek flow state impossible nahi hai. Learning se judi kai cognitive (dimaagi) gatividhiyan difficulty ki us range mein hoti hain jo flow ko possible ya even likely banati hain. Halanki, main Ericsson se bhi sahmat hoon ki learning mein aksar aisi situations mein enter karna shamil hota hai jahan difficulty flow ko impossible bana deti hai. Additionally (Iske alava), aatm-bodh (self-consciousness) jo flow mein absent hota hai use ultralearning aur deliberate practice dono mein present hone ki zarurat ho sakti hai, kyunki aapko consciously apne approach ko adjust karne ki zarurat hoti hai. Apni abilities ki limit par ek programming problem par kaam karna, apne aap ko ek aise style mein likhne par push karna jo aapke liye unfamiliar (anjaan) ho, ya nayi bhasha bolte waqt apne accent ko minimize karne ki koshish karna, har ek aisa task hai jo aapke dwara ikhatha kiye gaye automatic patterns ke khilaf jata hai. Prakriti (natural) ke prati yeh pratirodh (resistance) flow ko haasil karna harder bana sakta hai, bhale hi yeh ultimately aapke learning goal ko accomplish karne ke liye beneficial ho.

Meri advice? **Flow ke baare mein chinta mat karein.** Kuch learning tasks mein, aap ise aasaani se haasil kar lenge. Maine MIT Challenge ke dauran practice problems karne, bhashayein seekhte waqt vocabulary drill karne, ya drawing karte waqt aksar aisa feel kiya jaise main ek flow state mein hoon. Saath hi, agar flow automatically nahi aata hai toh guilty feel mat karein. Aapka goal apni learning ko badhana (enhance) hai, aur isme aksar un sessions ke beech se nikalna shamil hota hai jo flow ke liye ideal maane jaane wale sessions se zyaada frustrating hote hain. Yaad rakhein, bhale hi aapki learning intense ho, baad mein aapka us skill ka use waisa nahi hoga. Abhi learning ke beech se nikalne mein kiye gaye investments aage chalkar kushal abhyas (skillful practice) ko ek kahin zyaada enjoyable activity bana denge.

Aapko kaise focus karna chahiye ispar vichar karne ke baad, aaiye duration (avadhi) par vichar karein. Aapko kab tak study karni chahiye? Jabki yeh problem yeh maan kar chalti hai ki aap bhatak rahe hain aur focus karna usse bahut pehle chhod rahe hain jitna aapko chahiye, focus par sahitya (literature) yeh suggest nahi karta ki learning ke nazariye se focus ke lagataar lambe periods optimal hote hain. Researchers aam taur par paate hain ki log jo seekhte hain use zyaada retain (tikaye) rakhte hain jab practice ko different studying periods mein toda jata hai mukable iske jab ise ek saath thosa (crammed) jata hai. Similarly, interleaving ka phenomenon suggest karta hai ki focus ke ek thos block ke andar bhi, yaad rakhi jaane wali skill ya knowledge ke different aspects ke beech alternate (adla-badli) karna samajhdari lag sakta hai. Isliye, agar aapke paas study karne ke liye kai ghante hain, toh aap ek par exclusively focus karne ke bajaye kuch topics ko cover karne mein mazeed behtar hain. Aisa karne ke trade-offs hain, halanki, isliye agar aapka study samay mazeed fractured (tukdon mein) ho jata hai, toh seekhna lagbhag difficult ho sakta hai.

Jis cheez ki zarurat hai woh hai ek sahi balance (taal-mel). Ise haasil karne liye, pachas minutes se ek ghante ka samay kai learning tasks ke liye ek achhi length hai. Agar aapka schedule per week sirf ek baar kai ghante jaise mazeed concentrated chunks of time ki izazat deta hai, toh aap har ghante ke ant mein kai minutes ka break lena chahenge aur apne samay ko us subject ke different aspects par split karna chahenge jise aap seekhna chahte hain. Beshak, yeh merely efficiency guidelines hain; aapko aakhirkar wahi dhoondhna hoga jo aapke liye sabse behtar kaam karta hai, na keval is baat par vichar karte hue ki retention ke maqsad se kya optimal hai balki is par bhi ki aapke schedule, personality, aur work flow mein kya fit baithta hai. Kuch logon ke liye, twenty minutes jitna kam samay unki lives mein sabse behtar fit baith sakta hai; doosre seekhne mein poora din spend karna prefer kar sakte hain.

Maan lijiye aapne seekhne ke liye samay ka ek aisa chunk dhoondh liya hai jo aapke liye utna hi optimal hai jitna yeh ho sakta hai, aap us samay ke dauran apne focus ko kaise sustain kar sakte hain? Maine paaya hai ki teen different sources hain jo focus ke break down hone aur distraction ke paida hone ka kaaran bante hain. Agar aap concentrate karne ke liye struggle kar rahe hain, toh ek-ek karke in teenon ko dekhein.

### Distraction Source 1: Your Environment

_(Bhatkaav Ka Srot 1: Aapka Environment)_
Bhatkaav ka pehla srot aapka environment hai. Kya aapne apna phone turned off kiya hai? Kya aap internet access kar rahe hain, television dekh rahe hain, ya games khel rahe hain? Kya wahan bhatkane wale noises aur sounds hain? Kya aap kaam karne ke liye prepared hain, ya aapko pens, ek kitab, ya ek lamp dhoondhne ke liye rukne ki zarurat pad sakti hai? Yeh focus barkarar rakhne ki problem ka ek srot hai, lekin yeh ek aisa aspect bhi hai jise log frequently ignore karte hain unhi kaaranon se jinse woh ignore karte hain ki woh procrastinate kar rahe hain. Kai log apne aap se kehte hain ki woh music sunte hue behtar focus karte hain, let’s say, lekin reality yeh ho sakti hai ki woh kisi diye gaye task par kaam nahi karna chahte, isliye music ek low-level, amusing distraction provide karta hai. Yeh kisi ko condemn (ninda) karne ke liye nahi hai jo ek perfect environment mein kaam nahi karta. Main nishchit roop se nahi karta. Balki, aware rahein ki aap kis environment mein sabse behtar kaam karte hain, aur ise test karein. Kya aap actually background mein television on hone par zyaada kaam poora karte hain, ya aapko bas television sunna pasand hai aur feel hota hai ki yeh kaam ko mazeed bardaasht karne kabil (bearable) banata hai? Agar yeh baad wali baat hai, toh aap shayad apne aap ko multitasking se bachne aur greater productivity ka anand lene ki training de sakte hain. Multitasking fun jaisa feel ho sakta hai, lekin yeh ultralearning ke liye unsuitable hai, jisme haath mein majood task par apna poora mind concentrate karne ki zarurat hoti hai. Apne aap ko is burai se mukt karna behtar hai bajaye asafal learning (ineffective learning) ki buri aadat ko strengthen karne ke.

### Distraction Source 2: Your Task

_(Bhatkaav Ka Srot 2: Aapka Task)_
Doosra srot woh task hai jise aap seekhne ki koshish kar rahe hain. Khhas tarah ki gatividhiyon par, unqi nature ke kaaran, doosron ke mukable focus karna harder hota hai. Mujhe video dekhne ke mukable padhne (reading) par focus karna harder lagta hai, bhale hi content same ho. Jab bhi aapke paas learning ke liye different tools ka use karne ke beech ek choice ho, toh aap is faisala ko karte waqt is baat par vichar karna chahenge ki kis par focus karna mazeed aasan hai. Materials ki yeh choice doosre vicharon ko peeche nahi chhodni chahiye—main kisi aise tool ko nahi chununga jo bahut kam direct ho (Niyam 3) ya koi feedback offer na karta ho (Niyam 6), simply mazeed focus ke maqsad se. Fortunately, yeh principles aam taur par aligned hote hain, aur yeh actually thode kam effective methods hote hain jo cognitively kam demanding hote hain aur isliye unpar focus barkarar rakhna harder hota hai. Kabhi-kabhi aap jo kar rahe hain use subtly modify kar sakte hain taaki greater focus kabil ho sake. Agar mujhe mushkil reading karni hai, toh main aksar apne liye hard concepts ko reexplain karne wale notes scratch down karne ka ek prayas karunga. Main aisa mukhya roop se isliye karta hoon kyunki, jab main likh raha hota hoon, toh mere reading hypnosis (padhne ke sammohan) ki state mein enter karne ki sambhavna kam hoti hai jahan main padhne ke act ki nakal (pantomiming) kar raha hota hoon jabki mera mind actually kahin aur hota hai. Mazeed intense strategies, chahe problems solve karna ho, kuch banana ho, ya ideas ko zor se likhna aur explain karna ho, unhein aapke mind ke background mein karna harder hota hai, isliye bhatkaav ke andar ghusne ke mazeed kam opportunities hote hain.

### Distraction Source 3: Your Mind

_(Bhatkaav Ka Srot 3: Aapka Apna Mind)_
Teesra srot aapka mind khud hai. Negative emotions, restless (bechaini), aur daydreaming focus karne ke kuch sabse bade obstacles ho sakte hain. Is problem ke do sides hain. Pehle, yeh obvious hai ki ek saaf, shaant mind (clear, calm mind) lagbhag saari learning problems par focus karne ke liye sabse behtar hai. Gusse, chintao, niraashaon, ya udaasi se bhare mind ke saath study karna harder hoga. Iska matlab hai ki agar aap apni life mein problems se struggle kar rahe hain, toh aapko achhi tarah seekhne mein harder samay lagega, aur aap pehle unse nipatne (dealing) par dekhna chahenge. Ek toxic relationship mein hona, kisi doosre task ke baare mein anxiety hona jisme aap procrastinate kar rahe hain, ya simply yeh jaan'na ki aap life ke galat raaste par ja rahe hain aapki motivation ke saath interfere kar sakta hai, isliye aksar sabse behtar yeh hota hai ki in issues ko ignore na kiya jaye.

Halanki, kabhi-kabhi aap apne emotions ke baare mein kuch nahi kar sakte, aur feelings bina aapke kuch karne ki zarurat ke sahaj roop se (spontaneously) paid hoti hain. Kisi future event ke baare mein ek random chinta bubble up ho sakti hai, let’s say, lekin aap jaante hain ki aapko usse nipatne ke liye us activity ko nahi rokna chahiye jispar aap abhi kaam kar rahe hain. Yahan solution feeling ko acknowledge (sweekar) karna hai, iske baare mein aware hona hai, aur gently apne focus ko wapas apne task par adjust karna hai aur feeling ko guzarne (pass) dena hai.

Negative feelings ko guzarne dena, beshak, kehna bahut aasan hai aur karna bahut mushkil. Emotions mind ko hijack kar sakte hain aur aapke project par awareness lautane ki process ko ek Sisyphean task (bina nateejay ki unthak mehnat) jaisa feel karwa sakte hain. Agar main kisi cheez ke baare mein sach mein anxious hoon, for instance, toh main aisa feel kar sakta hoon jaise main apna dhayan ek task par lauta raha hoon, sirf fifteen seconds baad iske door koodne ke liye, ek ghante ya usse zyaada samay tak baar-baar repeat hote hue. Aise moments mein, recognize karein ki apne task ko poori tarah se abandon (chhodne) ke level par emotion par react na karke, aap future mein iski intensity ko kam kar denge. Aap future ki situations mein is tarah kaam jaari rakhne ke apne commitment ko bhi strengthen karenge, isliye woh mazeed aasan ho jayenge.

Mindfulness researcher aur psychiatrist Susan Smalley aur UCLA ke Mindful Awareness Research Center ki meditation teacher Diana Winston tark karti hain ki jab hum kisi behaviour mein engage hote hain, toh hamara typical reaction bhatkane wale vicharon ko suppress (dabane) karne ki koshish karna hota hai. Agar iske bajaye aap “ise paida hone dena, note karna, aur ise release karna ya jaane dena seekhte hain,” toh yeh us behaviour ko kam kar sakta hai jisse aap bachne ki koshish kar rahe hain. Agar kabhi aisa feel ho jaise kaam jaari rakhna bematlab (pointless) hai kyunki aap ek negative emotion se itne bhatke (distracted) hain ki aap possibly kaam nahi kar sakte, toh yaad rakhein ki is task par persist karne ki aapki ability ka long-term strengthening useful hoga, isliye samay barbaad nahi jata bhale hi aap is particular learning session mein bahut kuch accomplish na karein.

## Problem 3: Failing to Create the Right Kind of Focus

_(Problem 3: Sahi Tarah Ka Focus Create Karne Mein Asafal Hona)_

Teesri problem, doosri do ke mukable mazeed baareek (subtler), aapke dhayan ki quality aur direction se talluk rakhti hai. Maan lijiye aapne procrastination aur distraction ki problems ko itna lamba pakadne (wrangle down) mein manage kar liya hai ki aap apne task par focus kar sakein, aapko ise kaise karna chahiye? Aapki learning ko maximize karne ke liye alertness ka optimal darja (optimal degree of alertness) kya hai?

Yahan do different variables, **arousal (uttajnah/satarkata)** aur **task complexity (kaam ki jatilata)** ko aapko apna dhayan kaise apply karna chahiye is sawaal se jodne wali kuch interesting research hai. Arousal (samanya, sexual nahi) aapki energy ya alertness ki overall feeling hai. Jab aap sleepy hote hain, toh aapke paas low arousal hoti hai; jab aap exercise kar rahe hote hain, toh aapke paas high arousal hoti hai. Yeh sharirik prapanch (bodily phenomenon) sympathetic nervous system ke activation ke kaaran hota hai, aur isme sharir mein asaron ki ek range shamil hoti hai jo aksar ek saath hoti hain, jisme faster heart rate, increased blood pressure, pupil dilation (putliyon ka phailna), aur sweating shamil hain. Mentally, arousal dhayan (attention) ko bhi influence karti hai. High arousal keen alertness ki ek feeling create karti hai, jise aksar focus ki ek kaafi narrow range (tang daire) dwara characterized kiya jata hai, lekin ek aisi range jo thodi bhangur (brittle/jaldi tootne wali) bhi ho sakti hai.

Yeh relatively simple tasks par focus karne ke liye ya un tasks ke liye bahut achha ho sakta hai jinhein ek chhote target ki taraf intense concentration ki zarurat hoti hai. Athletes ko ek target par dart phenkne ya basketball ko properly shoot karne ke liye is tarah ke concentration ki zarurat hoti hai, jahan task kaafi simple hota hai lekin execute karne ke liye concentration ki zarurat hoti hai. Bahut zyaada arousal, halanki, aur focus suffer karne lagta hai. Jittery (ghabrhat) feel hona aur focus ko kisi particular spot par hold rakhne mein harder samay lagna aasan ho jata hai. Jo bhi bahut zyaada coffee pee chuka hai aur jittery feel karta hai woh jaanta hai ki yeh aapke kaam par kaise impact daal sakta hai.

Mazeed complex tasks, jaise math problems solve karna ya essays likhna, ek mazeed relaxed tarah ke focus se benefit leti hain. Yahan focus ka space aksar bada aur mazeed diffuse (bikhra hua/vyapak) hota hai. Iske advantages hote hain jab, aap jis problem ka samna kar rahe hain use solve karne ke liye, aapko kai different inputs ya ideas par vichar karna hota hai. Ek complex math problem solve karne ya ek love sonnet (prem-geet) likhne ke liye is dimaagi khamoshi (mental quietness) ki zarurat hone ki sambhavna hai. Kisi khhasakar creative task ko karte waqt, agar aap stuck (atakh) jaate hain, toh aapko bilkul focus na karne se benefit mil sakta hai. Problem se ek break lena focus ke space ko itna widen (chouda) kar sakta hai ki jo possibilities pehle aapki consciousness mein nahi thin woh conjoin (jud) sakein aur aap nayi discoveries kar sakein. Yeh aaram ke dauran ya sote waqt hone wale “Eureka!” moments ka ek scientific explanation hai, bajaye kaam par hone ke. Phir bhi, isse pehle ki aap yeh sochna shuru karein ki alas (sloth) hi creativity ki key hai, yeh saaf hai ki is tarah ka approach aksar tabhi kaam karta hai jab koi kisi problem par itne lambe samay se focus kar raha ho ki ideas ka avashesh (residue) uske mind mein bana rahe. Bilkul kaam na karne se creative genius ki taraf jaane ki sambhavna nahi hai, lekin ek break lena ek hard problem mein taaza nazariya (fresh perspective) phoonkne mein madad kar sakta hai.

Task complexity aur arousal ke beech ka rishta interesting hai kyunki baad wali ko badla (modify) kiya ja sakta hai. Ek experiment mein, sleep-deprived (neend se vanchit) aur well-rested (achhi tarah aaram kiye hue) subjects ne ek cognitive task par kaam kiya. Hairan karne wali baat nahi thi ki sleepy subjects ne utna achha nahi kiya. Mazeed interesting, halanki, yeh tha ki sleepy subjects ne tab behtar kiya jab background mein ek loud noise bajaya gaya, jabki well-rested subjects ne badtar kiya. Researchers dwara nikala gaya nateeja (conclusion) yeh tha ki noise ne arousal levels ko badha diya, jisne low-arousal sleepy subjects ko benefit pahunchaya, lekin isne well-rested walon ke liye arousal ko bahut zyaada badha diya, jisse unki performance mein giravat (decline) aayi.

Iska matlab hai ki aap ideal level of focus ko sustain karne ke liye apne arousal levels ko optimize karne par vichar karna chahenge. Complex tasks kam arousal se benefit le sakte hain, isliye ghar par ek quiet room mein kaam karna math problems ke liye sahi idea ho sakta hai. Simpler tasks ek mazeed noisier environment se benefit le sakte hain, maan lijiye kisi coffee shop mein kaam karna. Yeh laboratory experiment dikhata hai ki aapko self-testing ke zariye focus karne ki apni kshamta ke liye kya sabse behtar kaam karta hai yeh dhoondhna chahiye. Aap paa sakte hain ki aap noisy coffee place mein bhi complex tasks par behtar kaam kar sakte hain, ya aap paa sakte hain ki simple tasks ke liye bhi aapko library mein quiet room ki zarurat hai.

## Improving Your Ability to Focus

_(Focus Karne Ki Apni Ability Ko Behtar Banana)_

Focus ko un logon ke domain (kshetra) tak seemit (exclusive) hone ki zarurat nahi hai jinke schedule par endless hours aur free time ke bade daire (swaths) hon. Jaisa ki Somerville ke case mein tha, focus karne ki ability un logon ke liye aur bhi important hai jinki lives samay ke aise bade commitments ko impossible banati hain. Practice ke saath aap focus karne ki apni ability ko improve kar sakte hain. Main is baare mein agnostic (sanshayvadi) hoon ki kya focus ko aam taur par ek ability ke roop mein train kiya ja sakta hai. Sirf isliye kyunki aap ek cheez ke baare mein disciplined hain aapko automatically har doosri cheez ke baare mein disciplined nahi banata. Halanki, jo cheez samanyatayein (generalize) rakhti hai woh yeh hai ki ek procedure hai jise aap focus karne mein behtar banne ke liye follow kar sakte hain.

Meri advice yeh hai: **recognize karein ki aap kahan hain, aur chhhote se shuru karein.** Agar aap us tarah ke insaan hain jo ek minute ke liye bhi sthir (still) nahi baith sakta, toh aadhe minute ke liye sthir baithne ki koshish karein. Adha minute jald hi ek minute ban jata hai, phir do. Samay ke saath, kisi khhas subject ko seekhne mein aap jo niraashayein feel karte hain woh genuine interest mein badal (transmuted) sakti hain. Bhatkaav mein engage hone ka impulse har baar kamzor hoga jab aap iska virodh (resist) karenge. Patience aur persistence ke saath, aapke kuch minutes badi cheezon ko accomplish karne ke liye kaafi bade ho sakte hain, theek waise hi jaise Somerville ne lagbhag do sau saal pehle kiya tha.

Ab jab humne discuss kar liya hai ki hard cheezon ko seekhna shuru kaise karna hai, aaiye unhein seekhne ke sahi tareeqe par discuss karne ke liye aage badhein. Agla niyan, **directness (pratyakshata)**, pehla niyan hai jo explain karta hai ki seekhte waqt aapko kis tarah ki cheezein karni chahiye aur, isse bhi important, jinse aapko bachna chahiye agar aap jo seekhte hain useuse use karne kabil banna chahte hain.

---

# Chapter 6 — Principle 3: Directness

### _(Niyam 3 — Directness: Seedhe Aage Badhein)_

---

> _"He who can go to the fountain does not go to the water jar."_
> _(Jo insaan jharne tak ja sakta hai, woh paani ke ghadhe ke paas nahi jata.)_
> — Leonardo da Vinci

---

India mein bade hone ke baad, Vatsal Jaiswal ek architect banne ka sapna lekar Canada move kar gaye. Ab, char saal baad, ek nayi-nayi mili degree ke sath aur Great Depression (bhaari mandi) ke baad ke sabse kharab job market mein enter karte hue, woh sapna bahut door lagne laga tha.

Architecture mein apna ek kadam jamana (foothold) mushkil ho sakta hai, bhale hi economic samay achha ho. Lekin 2007 ke market crash se bas kuch hi saal baad, yeh lagbhag impossible tha. Firms experienced architects ko bhi kaam se nikaal (laying off) rahi thin. Agar koi hire kar bhi raha tha, toh woh school se abhi-abhi nikle kisi kid par chance nahi le rahe the. Unki graduating class mein se, lagbhag kisi ko bhi abhi tak architecture ki job nahi mili thi. Zyaada tar ne haar maan li thi, field se baahar jobs le rahe the, mazeed education ke liye wapas ja rahe the, ya economic toofano ke shant hone tak parents ke sath move kar rahe the.

Ek aur rejection. Jaiswal ek aur architecture firm ke offices se nikalte hain, us ek-bedroom apartment ke apne chote se hisse (sliver) ki taraf wapas chalte hue jise woh do roommates ke sath share karte hain. Bina kisi reply ke saikdon résumés submit karne ke baad, woh ek mazeed aakramak ranniti (aggressive tactic) par badh gaye hain jisme woh directly ek firm ke offices mein jaate hain, jo bhi charge mein ho usse baat karne ki guzarish (pleading) karte hain. Phir bhi, hafton tak darwazo par knock karne aur daso bina-bulaye office visits (unsolicited office visits) karne ke baad, koi job offer nazar mein nahi hai. Unhein ek bhi interview ke liye call back tak nahi aaya hai.

Phir bhi, Jaiswal ko shak (suspected) tha ki unke is struggle ke liye sirf recession (mandi) ko dosh nahi diya ja sakta. Unhone jin jagahon par apply kiya tha, wahan se woh jo thoda-boht feedback nikaal (pry out) sake, usse unhein ehsaas hua ki companies unhein ek useful employee ke roop mein nahi dekhti thin. Unhone school mein architecture padha tha, lekin unka program mukhya roop se design aur theory par focused tha. Unhein un creative design projects mein train kiya gaya tha jo building codes (nirman niyamo), construction costs, aur pechida software ki reality se alag (isolated) the. Kyunki unke school projects ka portfolio un detailed technical documents se mel nahi khata tha jinpar architects kaam karte the, unhein laga ki unhein hire karne mein ek lamba training period shamil hoga, kuch aisa jise abhi bahut kam firms afford kar sakti thin.

Jaiswal ko ek plan nikaalna tha. Mazeed résumé submissions aur office walk-ins kaam nahi karne wale the. Unhein ek naye portfolio ki zarurat thi jo yeh prove kar sake ki unke paas exactly wahi skills hain jo firms chahti thin. Unhein unhein dikhane ki zarurat thi ki, ek bojh (burden) banne ke bajaye, woh turant (straightaway) kaam par lag sakte hain aur pehle hi din se ek keemti team member ban sakte hain.

Aisa karne ke liye, unhein is baare mein mazeed jaan'ne ki zarurat thi ki architects actually buildings ke plans kaise draw karte hain—na ki sirf badi theories aur designs, jo unhone school mein seekhe the, balki unke drawings karne ke tareeqon ke chote details, different materials ko represent karne ke liye woh kaun se codes use karte the, aur drawings kya dikhati thin aur kya chhodti thin. Aisa karne ke liye, unhein ek bade-form ke print shop par job mili, us tarah ki shop jo paper ke un bade sheets par printing karti hai jinhein architectural blueprints ke liye pasand (favored) kiya jata hai. Kam kamayi (low paying) aur kam hunar (low skilled) wali, ek print shop mein job Jaiswal ka end goal nahi thi. Phir bhi, jab woh apna naya portfolio taiyar kar rahe the, toh yeh unhein financially gujara karne (scrape by) mein madad kar sakti thi. Isse bhi behtar, print store ne unhein un blueprints se daily exposure diya jinhein firms use kar rahi thin. Usne unhein is baare mein unginat details grahan karne (absorb) ki izazat di ki drawings ko kaise ek sath joda jata tha.

Next, Jaiswal ko apne technical skills ko upgrade karne ki zarurat thi. Apne walk-in visits se, woh aware the ki jin firms mein woh apply kar rahe the, unmein se kai ek complex design software use kar rahi thin jise _Revit_ kehte hain. Agar woh iske ins and outs (baareekiyon) par maharat haasil kar sakein, unhone socha, toh woh us technology-heavy entry-level position mein immediately useful ho sakte hain jise woh chahte the. Raat mein, unhone online tutorials ke beech se nikalna (pushed through) shuru kiya aur khud ko software sikhaya.

Finally, woh ek naya portfolio construct (banane) ke liye ready the. Apne naye Revit knowledge ko architectural drawings ke us knowledge ke sath combine karte hue jo unhone print shop par kaam karne ke dauran haasil kiya tha, unhone ek naya portfolio banaya. University ke tarah-tarah ke projects ke bajaye, unhone apne khud ke design ki ek single building par focus kiya: uthe hue aangan (raised courtyards) aur ek modern aesthetic ke sath ek teen-tower wali residential structure. Is project ne software ke sath unke skills ko mazeed aage dhakela, unhein online tutorials ke basics aur print shop ke exposure se pare naye methods aur ideas seekhne par majboor kiya. Aakhirkar, kuch mahino ke kaam ke baad, woh ready the.

Naya portfolio haath mein liye, Jaiswal ne ise phir se submit kiya, is baar sirf do architecture firms ko. Unke surprise ke liye, un dono ne immediately unhein job offer kar di.

## The Importance of Being Direct

_(Direct Hone Ka Mahatva)_

Jaiswal ki kahani ultralearning ke teesre niyan ko perfect roop se pradarshit (illustrates) karti hai: **directness**. Yeh dekh kar ki architecture actually kaise kiya ja raha tha aur un skills ka ek set seekh kar jo us job position se closely related tha jise woh perform karna chahte the, woh un-impressive portfolios wale haal hi ke graduates ke daire (swaths) ko kaatne mein kabil rahe.

Directness learning ke us situation ya context se closely jude hone ka idea hai jisme aap iska use karna chahte hain. Jaiswal ke case mein, jab woh itna architectural skill haasil karna chahte the ki firms unhein hire kar lein, toh unhone un firms dwara use kiye jaane wale software ka use karke ek portfolio banane aur un firms dwara abhyas kiye jaane wale style mein design karne ka vikalp chuna. Swa-shiksha (self-education) ke kai raaste hain, lekin unmein se zyaada tar bahut zyaada direct nahi hote. Jaiswal ke ulat, ek aur architect jisse maine baat ki, uska maqsad design theories ke apne knowledge ko gehra karke apni employability (rozgar ke kabil hona) ko behtar banana tha. Bhale hi yeh interesting aur fun raha ho, yeh un actual skills se alag (disconnected) tha jinhein woh entry-level kaam mein use kar raha hota.

Theek jaise Jaiswal ne apne university portfolio ke sath kaam paane ke liye struggle kiya, hum mein se kai log career aur personal uplabdhiyon ke un types ke liye skills ka galat portfolio build kar rahe hain jinhein hum create karna chahte hain. Hum ek bhasha bolna chahte hain lekin actual logon ke sath converse (baatcheet) karne ke bajaye, mukhya roop se fun apps par khel kar seekhne ki koshish karte hain. Hum collaborative, professional programs par kaam karna chahte hain lekin mukhya roop se akele mein scripts code karte hain. Hum bade speaker banna chahte hain, isliye hum bhashan dene ki practice karne ke bajaye, communication par ek kitab kharid lete hain. In saare cases mein problem same hai: directly us cheez ko seekhna jise hum chahte hain bahut zyaada uncomfortable, boring, ya frustrating feel hota hai, isliye hum kisi kitab, lecture, ya app se santusht (settle) ho jaate hain, yeh umeed karte hue ki yeh aakhirkar hamein asli cheez mein behtar bana dega.

Directness zyaada tar ultralearning projects ki ek mukhya nishani (hallmark) hai. Roger Craig ne Jeopardy! ke liye apni testing pichle shows ke actual questions par ki. Eric Barone ne apne video game ke liye art banakar video game art seekha. Benny Lewis pehle hi din se kuch aage-baahar bhashan (back-and-forth dialog) ka attempt karne ki ek policy ko follow karke bhashon ko jaldi bolna seekhte hain. In approaches mein jo cheez sanjha (share) hai woh yeh hai ki learning activities hamesha us context ke sath ek connection ke sath ki jaati hain jisme seekhe gaye skills ko aakhirkar use kiya jayega.

Iska ulta woh approach hai jise paramparagat classroom-style learning (traditional classroom-style learning) mein bahut zyaada pasand kiya jata hai: facts, concepts, aur skills ka ek aisi tareeqe se adhyayan karna jo is baat se door ho ki un cheezon ko aakhirkar kaise apply kiya jayega: formulas par maharat haasil karna isse pehle ki aap us problem ko samajhein jise woh solve karne ki koshish kar rahe hain; kisi bhasha ki vocabulary ko memorize karna kyunki yeh ek list par likhi hai, isliye nahi kyunki aap iska use karna chahte hain; highly idealized (aadarsh banayi gayi) problems ko solve karna jinhein aap graduation ke baad kabhi nahi dekhenge.

Learning ke indirect approaches, halanki, traditional education tak seemit nahi hain. Kai self-directed learners indirect learning ke jaal (trap) mein gir jaate hain. _Duolingo_ par vichar karein, jo currently sabse popular language-learning applications mein se ek hai. Satah (surface) par, is app ke baare mein pasand karne ke liye bahut kuch hai. Yeh colorful aur fun hai aur aapko progress ka ek mazboot ehsaas deti hai. Lekin mujhe shak hai ki progress ka woh zyaada tar ehsaas ek bhram (illusion) hai, kam se kam agar aapka goal aakhirkar bhasha bolne kabil (speak the language) hona hai. Yeh samajhne liye ki kyun, is baat par vichar karein ki Duolingo aapko practice karne ke liye kaise encourage karta hai. Yeh English words aur sentences provide karta hai aur phir aapko unhein translate karne ke liye ek word bank se words chun'ne ke liye kehta hai. Problem yeh hai ki yeh bhasha bolne jaisa bilkul nahi hai! Real life mein, aap shayad ek English sentence ko us bhasha mein translate karne ki koshish se shuru kar sakte hain jise aap seekhna chahte hain. Halanki, real speaking situations apne aap ko ek multiple choice ke roop mein prastut nahi karti hain. Iske bajaye, aapko memory se actual words nikaalne (dredge up) padte hain ya alternative words dhoondhne padte hain agar aapne unmein se koi ek nahi seekha hai jise aap use karna chahte hain.

Yeh, cognitively speaking (dimaagi roop se), ek behad limited word bank se matching translations chun'ne ke mukable kaafi different task hai, aur isse kahin zyaada difficult bhi hai. Benny Lewis ka shuruat se bolne ka method bhale hi hard ho, lekin yeh us task mein perfectly transfer hota hai jisme woh aakhirkar behtar banna chahte hain: conversations karna.

MIT Challenge ke dauran, maine recognize kiya ki aakhirkar classes ko pass karne kabil hone ke liye sabse important resource recorded lectures tak access hona nahi tha, yeh problem sets tak access hona tha. Phir bhi, is project ke baad ke saalon mein, jab mujhse students dwara madad maangi jaati hai, toh woh aksar kuch classes se lecture videos ke na hone ki ninda (decry) karte hain, incomplete ya aparyapt (insufficient) problem sets ke baare mein shayad hi kabhi shikayat karte hain. Yeh mujhe sochne par majboor karta hai ki zyaada tar students ek lecture mein baithne aur sunne ko hi mukhya tarika dekhte hain jisse woh material seekhte hain, un problems ko karne ko jo final exam ke kaafi similar dikhti hain, unke knowledge par ek upri janch (superficial check) ke roop mein dekhte hain. Bhale hi pehle material ko cover karna practice shuru karne ke liye aksar essential hota hai, directness ka niyan yeh bayan (asserts) karta hai ki actually us cheez ko karne ke dauran hi jisme aap behtar banna chahte hain, learning ka ek bada hissa hota hai. Is rule ke exceptions unke pehle dikhne ke mukable mazeed rare (durlabh) hain, aur isliye directness ek dashak se zyaada samay se education ke paksh mein ek karrwa problem (thorny problem) bani hui hai.

Directly seekhne ka sabse aasan tarika simply us cheez ko karne mein bahut saara samay bitana hai jisme aap behtar banna chahte hain. Agar aap ek bhasha seekhna chahte hain, toh ise bolein, jaise Benny Lewis karte hain. Agar aap video games banane par maharat haasil karna chahte hain, toh unhein banayein, jaise Eric Barone karte hain. Agar aap kisi test ko pass karna chahte hain, toh un problems ko solve karne ka abhyas karein jinqi uspar dikhne ki sambhavna hai, jaise maine apni khud ki MIT Challenge mein kiya tha. Karke seekhne (learning by doing) ka yeh style saare projects ke liye kaam nahi karega. “Real” situation kam aane wali, difficult, ya create karne ke liye impossible bhi ho sakti hai, aur is tarah ek different environment mein seekhna apariharya (unavoidable) hai. Roger Craig show par saikdon baar hokar Jeopardy! ki practice nahi kar sakte the. Woh jaante the ki unhein ek different environment mein seekhna hoga aur jab aisa karne ka samay aaye toh us knowledge ko show par transfer karne ki taiyari karni hogi. Aisi situations mein, directness koi sab-kuch-ya-kuch-nahi (all-or-nothing) feature nahi hai balki kuch aisi cheez hai jise aap apni performance ko behtar banane liye gradually badha sakte hain. Craig ka actual past Jeopardy! questions se seekh kar shuruat karne ka approach kahin zyaada effective tha mukable iske agar unhone random topics se trivia seekhna shuru kiya hota.

Jaiswal architectural skills seekhte waqt similarly limited the, kyunki jin jagahon par woh kaam karna chahte the woh unhein hire nahi karengi. Halanki, unhone unhi ke dwara use kiye jaane wale same software par train karke aur ek aisa portfolio design karke iske chaaron taraf kaam kiya jo unhi types ke drawings aur renderings par based tha jinhein actual practice mein kiya jata tha. Directness ka dochar challenge (twin challenge) yeh hai ki kabhi-kabhi exactly woh situation available nahi hoti jisme aap skill ka use karna chahte hain aasan practice ke liye. Bhale hi aap karke seekhne mein seedhe ja sakein, yeh approach passive roop se lecture videos dekhne ya kisi fun app ke sath khelne ke mukable aksar mazeed intense aur uncomfortable hota hai. Agar aap directness par dhayan nahi dete hain, isliye, ghatiya learning strategies (lousy learning strategies) mein slip ho jana bahut aasan hai.

Jaiswal ki kahani ke bade takeaways mein se ek unke swa-shiksha project ki safalata nahi balki unki formal education ka failure ho sakta hai. Akhirkar, unki difficulties tab shuru huin jab unhone university mein architecture ka intensely char saal adhyayan pehle hi kar liya tha. Kyun, phir, graduation ke baad ek chota project unki rozgar ke kabil hone (employability) mein itna bada farq paida karega? Uska javab dene liye, main educational psychology mein sabse mazeed ziddi aur pareshan karne wali problems mein se ek ki taraf mudna chahta hoon: **transfer ki problem**.

## Transfer: Education’s Dirty Secret

_(Transfer: Education Ka Ek Ganda Secret)_

Transfer ko “education ka Holy Grail (sabse keemti khoj)” kaha gaya hai. Yeh tab hota hai jab aap ek context mein kuch seekhte hain, maan lijiye ek classroom mein, aur doosre context mein iska use karne kabil hote hain, maan lijiye real life mein. Bhale hi yeh technical sunne mein lage, transfer sach mein kuch aisi cheez ko embody karta hai jiski hum lagbhag saari learning prayason se umeed karte hain—ki hum ek situation mein padhi jaane wali kisi cheez ka use karne aur use ek nayi situation par apply karne kabil honge. Isse kam kisi bhi cheez ko learning ke roop mein describe karna hard hai.

Unfortunately, transfer ek aisi cheez bhi hai jo, ek dashak se zyaada ki intense mehnat aur research ke bavajood, formal education mein hone mein largely fail rahi hai. Psychologist Robert Haskell ne learning mein transfer par vishal sahitya (vast literature) ke apne excellent coverage mein kaha hai, “Learning ke transfer ke mahatva ke bavajood, pichle nau dashakon ke research findings saaf dikhate hain ki व्यक्तियों (individuals) ke roop mein, aur educational institutions ke roop mein, hum kisi bhi mahatvapurna level (significant level) par learning ka transfer haasil karne mein fail rahe hain.” Unhone baad mein add kiya, “Bina kisi atishayokti (exaggeration) ke, yeh ek education scandal hai.”

Sthiti isse bhi zyaada pareshan karne wali hai jitni yeh sunne mein lagti hai. Haskell ne point out kiya, “Hum umeed karte hain ki learning ka transfer hoga, for example, introductory psychology ke ek high school course se college-level ke introduction to psychology course mein. Yeh saalon se jaana jata hai, halanki, ki jo students high school psychology course lekar college mein enter karte hain woh un students se behtar nahi karte jinhone high school mein psychology nahi li thi. Kuch students jinhone high school mein psychology course liya tha woh college course mein aur bhi badtar karte hain.” Ek aur study mein, college graduates se economic issues ke baare mein questions pooche gaye aur un logon ke beech performance mein koi farq nahi paaya gaya jinhone economics class li thi aur jinhone nahi li thi.

Multiple examples provide karna transfer mein thodi madad karta lagta hai, phir bhi cognitive science researcher Michelene Chi ne note kiya ki “example solutions ke role par abhi tak ke lagbhag saare anubhavatmak kaam (empirical work) mein, ek student jinhone examples ka study kiya hai woh aksar un problems ko solve nahi kar sakta jo example solution se thodi si hat (deviate slightly) jaati hain.” Apni kitab _The Unschooled Mind: How Children Think and How Schools Should Teach_ mein, vikasatmak manovigyanik (developmental psychologist) Howard Gardner ne un evidences ke dher ki taraf point kiya jo dikhate hain ki yahan tak ki “jo students college-level physics courses mein honors grades haasil karte hain woh aksar un basic problems aur questions ko solve karne mein asamarth hote hain jinka samna usse thode alag roop mein hota hai jisme unhein formally instruct aur test kiya gaya tha.” Na hi transfer ka yeh failure schools tak seemit raha hai. Corporate training bhi suffer karti hai, jisme purane Times Mirror Training Group ke chairman John H. Zenger likhte hain “Researchers jinhone kade tareeqe se training ko evaluate kiya hai unhone kaha hai ki training ke baad pradarshit karne yogya badlav (demonstrable changes) dhoondhna hard hai.”

General transfer ke failure ka recognition utna hi lamba history rakhta hai jitna is problem ka study khud. Problem par pehla hamla 1901 mein psychologists Edward Thorndike aur Robert Woodworth se aaya tha, unke seminal paper _“The Influence of Improvement in One Mental Function upon the Efficiency of Other Functions”_ ke sath. Isme, unhone us samay education ke dominant theory par hamla kiya, jise so-called **formal discipline theory** kehte hain. Yeh theory suggest karti thi ki brain ek muscle ke samroop (analogous) tha, jisme memory, attention, aur reasoning ki kaafi general capacities thin, aur un muscles ko train karne se, chahe content kuch bhi ho, general improvement ho sakta hai. Universal instruction mein Latin aur geometry ke peeche yeh predominant theory thi, is idea par ki yeh students ko behtar sochne mein madad karegi. Thorndike is idea ko khandan (refute) karne kabil rahe yeh dikhakar ki transfer karne ki ability zyaada tar logon ke assume karne ke mukable kahin zyaada narrow (tang) thi.

Bhale hi Latin padhna pasand se gir gaya ho, kai educational pundits formal discipline theory ke naye roopon (new incarnations) ko revive kar rahe hain yeh suggest karke ki har koi apni general intelligence ko behtar banane liye programming ya critical thinking seekhe. Kai popular “brain-training” games bhi mind ke is view ko subscribe karte hain, yeh assume karte hui ki cognitive tasks ke ek set par gehra training everyday reasoning tak phaila dega. Faisla aane ke baad se ek sau saal se zyaada samay ho gaya hai, phir bhi ek general transfer procedure ka aakarshan (allure) abhi bhi kai logon ko Holy Grail ki talaash karwa raha hai.

Is sab ke bavajood, sthiti umeed ke bina nahi hai. Halanki empirical work aur educational institutions aksar mahatvapurna transfer pradarshit karne mein fail rahe hain, aisa nahi hai ki transfer exist nahi karta. Wilbert McKeachie ne, transfer ke history ka moolyankan karte hue, note kiya ki “Transfer virodhabhas (paradoxical) hai. Jab hum ise chahte hain, hum ise nahi paate. Phir bhi yeh har waqt hota hai.” Jab bhi aap kisi analogy (upma) ka use karte hain, yeh kehte hue ki koi cheez kisi doosri cheez jaisi hai, aap knowledge transfer kar rahe hote hain. Agar aap jaante hain ki ice skate kaise karna hai aur baad mein Rollerblade karna seekhte hain, aap skills transfer kar rahe hote hain. Jaisa ki Haskell ne point out kiya, agar transfer sach mein impossible hota, toh hum function karne mein asamarth hote.

Toh badlav (disconnect) ko kya explain karta hai? Educational institutions mahatvapurna transfer pradarshit karne liye kyun struggle kar rahe hain, agar transfer kuch aisi cheez hai jiski hum sab ko duniya mein function karne ke liye zarurat hai? Haskell suggest karte hain ki ek mukhya kaaran yeh hai ki transfer tab harder hota hai jab hamari knowledge mazeed limited hoti hai. Jaise-jaise hum kisi area mein mazeed knowledge aur skill develop karte hain, woh mazeed flexible aur un narrow contexts ke baahar apply karne kabil aasan ho jaate hain jisme unhein seekha gaya tha. Halanki, main transfer problem ke ek explanation ke roop mein apna khud ka hypothesis add karna chahta hoon: **zyaada tar formal learning behad niraashajanak roop se (woefully) indirect hai.**

## Overcoming the Problem of Transfer with Directness

_(Directness Ke Sath Transfer Ki Problem Par Vijay Paana)_

Directness transfer ki problem ko do tareeqon se solve karti hai. Pehla aur sabse saaf yeh hai ki agar aap us area se ek direct connection ke sath seekhte hain jisme aap aakhirkar skill ko apply karna chahte hain, toh far transfer (door ke transfer) ki zarurat tezi se kam ho jaati hai. Pichle ek sau saal ke research ko dekhte hue jo prastavit solutions ke sath transfer ki difficulties ko dikhata hai jo lasting results provide karne mein fail rahe hain, kisi bhi student ko is dharana ko gombhirta se lena chahiye ki bahut zyaada different contexts aur situations ke beech seekhi gayi cheez ko transfer karna vishwasghati (treacherous) hoga. Agar hamari learning, jaisa Haskell suggest karte hain, “kisi jagah ya subject matter se welded (judi)” hai, toh yeh bahut zyaada behtar hai ki woh situations unke paas hon jinhein hum actually use karna chahte hain.

Doosra, mera vishwas hai ki directness nayi situations mein transfer ke sath madad kar sakti hai, far transfer ki zarurat ko rokne mein iske mazeed saaf role se pare. Kai real-life situations doosri real-life situations ke sath kai baareek details share karti hain jinhein woh classroom ya textbook ke abstract environment ke sath kabhi share nahi karti hain. Kuch naya seekhna shayad hi kabhi mukhya roop se majood aasaani se bayan aur codified knowledge par depend karta hai balki is baareek details ke unginat details par ki woh knowledge reality ke sath kaise interact karti hai. Ek real context mein seekh kar, koi un chhupi hui details aur skills ko bhi seekhta hai jinki ek classroom ke artificial environment ke mukable ek nayi real-life situation mein transfer hone ki sambhavna kahin zyaada hoti hai.

Ek personal example ka use karte hue, no-English project mein mujhe jo sabse important skills mile unmein se ek meri phone par ek dictionary ya translation app ka quickly use karne kabil hona tha, taaki main midconversation (baatcheet ke beech) mein apne bhashayi knowledge ke gaps ko fill kar sakoon. Halanki, exactly is tarah ka practical skill language-learning curriculum mein shayad hi kabhi cover kiya jata hai. Jabki yeh ek trivial (mamuli) example hai, real-life situations mein aise hazaron skills aur knowledge ke pieces shamil hote hain jinqi zarurat hoti hai agar aap academically seekhe gaye subjects ko real world mein apply karne ja rahe hain.

Ultimately, yeh researchers ke liye taye karna hoga ki kya education ka Holy Grail kabhi dhoondha jayega ya nahi. Is beech, learners ke roop mein, hamein sweekar karna chahiye ki shuruati learning prayas aksar un situations se ziddipurvak chipak (stick stubbornly) jaate hain jisme hum unhein seekhte hain. Jo programmer ek class se kisi algorithm ke baare mein seekhti hai use apne code mein iska use kab karna hai yeh recognize karne mein trouble ho sakti hai. Jo leader ek business kitab se ek naya management philosophy seekhti hai woh apne employees ke sath kaam karne ke usi approach par wapas ja sakti hai jise woh hamesha use karti aayi hai.

Mera favorite example, halanki, tab ka hona chahiye jab doston ke ek group ne mujhe ek casino mein unhein join karne ke liye invite kiya. Maine unse poocha ki kya unki studies unhein kabhi gambling enjoy karne se rokti hain, aur unhone bas mujhe khaali roop se (blankly) dekha. Maine socha ki yeh funny tha kyunki woh students actuaries (bima-sankhyaki ke vidwan) the. Classroom mein statistics study karne mein bitaye gaye unke saalon ne unhein convince kiya hona chahiye tha ki aap house (casino) ko beat karne ki umeed nahi rakh sakte, phir bhi woh connection unpar saaf hota hua lagta nahi tha. Jab hum nayi cheezein seekhte hain, isliye, hamein hamesha unhein directly un contexts se baandhne ka prayas karna chahiye jisme hum unhein use karna chahte hain. Ek real situation ke kernel se baahar knowledge build karna kisi cheez ko seekhne aur yeh umeed karne ki traditional strategy se kahin behtar hai ki hum ise kisi anishchit future samay mein ek real context mein shift karne kabil honge.

## How Ultralearners Avoid the Problem of Transfer and Learn Directly

_(Ultralearners Transfer Ki Problem Se Kaise Bachte Hain Aur Directly Seekhte Hain)_

Transfer ki problem aur directly seekhne ke mahatva ko dekhte hue, aaiye un tareeqon mein se kuch ko dekhein jinse ise different ultralearning projects mein manage kiya jata hai. Directly hone ka sabse aasan tarika karke seekhna (learn by doing) hai. Jab bhi possible ho, agar aap apne learning samay ka ek achha hissa bas us cheez ko karne mein spend kar sakte hain jisme aap behtar banna chahte hain, toh directness ki problem lagbhag chali jayegi. Agar yeh possible nahi hai, toh aapko apne skills ko test karne ke liye ek artificial project ya environment create karne ki zarurat ho sakti hai. Jo cheez yahan sabse zyaada matter karti hai woh yeh hai ki aap jis skill par maharat haasil karne ki koshish kar rahe hain uske cognitive features aur jis tareeqe se aap iska abhyas karte hain woh substantially similar hon. Phir se vichar karein Craig ke Jeopardy! games ke simulation par purane tests se questions karke. Yeh fact ki woh actual past questions use kar rahe the isse kahin zyaada important hai ki kya unka program show ke display par majood signature blue background color se mel khata tha ya nahi. Yeh isliye hai kyunki background color ne aisi koi jankari provide nahi ki jo questions par unke responses ko badal deti. Unka abhyas kiya ja raha skill isse bahut zyaada badla nahi tha. Iske ulat, agar unhone kisi different game se trivia questions liye hote (maan lijiye board game _Trivial Pursuit_) toh isme farq ho sakta tha ki questions aam taur par kaise pooche jaate hain, woh kis topics se liye jaate hain, ya difficulty level kya hai. Badtar, agar unhone trivia seekhne liye random Wikipedia articles padhne mein apna saara samay bitaya hota, toh woh cryptic Jeopardy!-style clues par based answers recall karne ke fundamental skill ka abhyas bilkul nahi kar rahe hote.

Doosre cases mein, jise aap haasil karne ki koshish kar rahe hain woh shayad ek practical skill na ho. Jin kai ultralearners se mera samna hua woh apne end goal ke roop mein, kisi subject ko khhasakar achhi tarah se samajhna chahte the, jaise Vishal Maini machine learning aur artificial intelligence ke sath. Yahan tak ki meri apni MIT Challenge computer science ki ek gehri samajh haasil karne par based thi, bajaye ek app ya video game banane ke ek mazeed practical goal ke. Bhale hi yeh ek aisa case lage jahan directness ab matter nahi karti, yeh sach mein sach nahi hai. Yeh simply hai ki aap in ideas ko jahan apply karna chahte hain woh jagah kam saaf aur concrete hai. Maini ke case mein, woh machine learning ke baare mein intelligently sochne aur baat karne kabil hona chahte the, itna ki ek aisi company mein non-technical role paa sakein jo un methods ka upyog karti ho. Uska matlab tha ki apne ideas ko articulately communicate karne kabil hona, concepts ko saaf taur par samajhna, aur unpar dono knowledgeable practitioners aur laypeople (aam logon) ke sath discuss karne kabil hona important tha. Yahi wajah hai ki machine learning ke basics ko explain karne wala ek minicourse banane ka unka goal itna fit baithta tha. Unki learning directly usse judi thi jahan woh skill apply karna chahte the: ise doosron tak communicate karna.

Halanki transfer par research ke findings kaafi bleak hain, umeed ki ek kiran hai, jo yeh hai ki kisi subject ka mazeed gehra knowledge haasil karna use future transfer ke liye mazeed flexible banayega. Jahan hamari knowledge ki structures shuruat mein brittle hoti hain, un environments aur contexts se welded hoti hain jisme hum unhein seekhte hain, mazeed mehnat aur samay ke sath woh flexible ho sakti hain aur unhein mazeed vyapak roop se apply kiya ja sakta hai. Yeh Robert Haskell ka nateeja hai, aur bhale hi yeh naye learners ke liye problem ka ek short-term solution provide nahi karta, yeh un logon ke liye ek raasta zoor suggest karta hai jo kisi subject par kaam karna tab tak jaari rakhna chahte hain jab tak ki woh ispar maharat haasil na kar lein. Kai ultralearners jinhone fields ke ek chote subset mein specialize kiya hai woh transfer ke masters hain; bina kisi shakk ke yeh largely unke knowledge ki gehrai ke kaaran hai, jo transfer ko accomplish karne kabil aasan banati hai. Dan Everett, jinhein pehle niyan, metalearning par chapter ki opening mein feature kiya gaya تھا, iska ek prime example hain. Unki bhashayi gehrai unhein kisi aise insaan ke mukable relatively aasaani se nayi bhashayein seekhne kabil banati hai jinhone sirf ek second bhasha seekhi hai ya bhashon ko sirf academically seekha hai.

## How to Learn Directly

_(Directly Kaise Seekhein)_

Indirect learning ke forms ke sath is achhi tarah se documented difficulty ko dekhte hue, woh abhi bhi schools aur saari asafal swa-shiksha prayason dono mein default kyun hain? Javab yeh hai ki directly seekhna hard hai. Yeh ek kitab padhne ya ek lecture ke dauran baithne ke mukable aksar mazeed frustrating, challenging, aur intense hota hai. Lekin yahi difficulty kisi bhi hone wale ultralearner ke liye competitive advantage ka ek potent srot (powerful source) create karti hai. Agar aap in difficulties ke bavajood directness ka upyog karne wali tactics apply karne ke liye taiyar hain, toh aap aakhirkar kahin zyaada effectively seekhenge.

Aaiye un tactics mein se kuch ko examine karein jinhein ultralearners is principle ko maximize karne aur mazeed typical schooling ki aparyaptataon (inadequacies) ka fayda uthane ke liye use karte hain.

### Tactic 1: Project-Based Learning

_(Ranniti 1: Project-Based Learning)_
Kai ultralearners required skills seekhne ke liye classes ke bajaye projects ka vikalp chunte hain. Tark simple hai: agar aap kisi cheez ko produce karne ke chaaron taraf apni learning ko organize karte hain, toh aap guarantee ke sath kam se kam us cheez ko produce karna seekh jaate hain. Agar aap classes lete hain, toh aap notes lene aur padhne mein bahut saara samay bita sakte hain lekin apna goal haasil nahi kar paate.

Apna khud ka computer game create karke program karna seekhna project-based learning ka ek perfect example hai. Engineering, design, art, musical composition, carpentry, writing, aur kai doosre skills naturally apne aap ko un projects ke liye lend karte hain jo ant mein kuch produce karte hain. Halanki, ek intellectual topic bhi ek project ka aadhar ho sakta hai. Ek ultralearner jiska maine interview kiya, uska project abhi bhi chal raha hai, woh military history seekhna chahta tha. Uska project, is case mein, ek thesis paper produce karne ki taraf kaam karna تھا. Chunki unka end goal subject ke baare mein knowledgeably converse karne kabil hona tha, ek original paper produce karne ka project bina kuch create kiye simply bahut saari books padhne ki koshish karne ke mukable learning ko mazeed directly apply karta tha.

### Tactic 2: Immersive Learning

_(Ranniti 2: Immersive Learning)_
Immersion target environment se apne aap ko gherne (surrounding) ki process hai jisme skill ka abhyas kiya jata hai. Iska advantage yeh hai ki isme abhyas ki un matraon (amounts of practice) ki zarurat hoti hai jo typical se bahut zyaada hon, sath hi yeh aapko un situations ki ek fuller range se expose karta hai jisme skill apply hoti hai.

Bhasha seekhna iska canonical example hai jahan immersion kaam karta hai. Apne aap ko ek aise environment mein jhonk (immersing) kar jahan ek bhasha boli jaati hai, na keval aap guarantee dete hain ki aap aakhirkar bhasha ka abhyas usse kahin zyaada karenge jitna aap otherwise karte (kyunki aapke paas koi choice nahi hai), balki aap un situations ki ek mazeed vyapak diversity ka bhi samna karte hain jinhein naye words aur phrases seekhne ki zarurat hoti hai. Halanki, language learning akeli jagah nahi hai jahan aap mazeed seekhne ke liye immersion apply kar sakte hain. Un logon ki communities mein join hona jo active roop se learning mein engaged hain, ek similar impact daal sakta hai, kyunki yeh naye ideas aur challenges ke lagaatar exposure ko encourage karta hai. For example, novice programmers naye coding challenges se apne aap ko expose karne ke liye open-source projects join kar sakte hain.

### Tactic 3: The Flight Simulator Method

_(Ranniti 3: Flight Simulator Method)_
Immersion aur projects bade hain, lekin kai skills ke liye skill ka actually directly abhyas karne ka koi tarika nahi hai. Plane urrane (piloting) ya surgery perform karne jaise skills ke liye, training mein pehle se hi mahatvapurna samay invest karne se pehle unhein ek real situation mein practice karna legally kabil bhi nahi hai. Aap ise kaise overcome kar sakte hain?

Yeh note karna important hai ki transfer ke liye jo matter karta hai woh learning environment ka har ek possible feature nahi hai, jaise seekhte waqt aap kis room mein hain ya aapne kaun se kapde pehne hain. Balki, yeh cognitive features hain—situations jahan aapko is baare mein decisions lene ki zarurat hoti hai ki kya karna hai aur us knowledge ko cue karna hota hai jise aapne apne head mein store kiya hai. Yeh suggest karta hai ki jab direct practice impossible ho, toh environment ka ek simulation us darje (degree) tak kaam karega jahan tak yeh sawaal ke ghere mein majood task ke cognitive elements ke prati vafadar (faithful) rehta hai.

Plane urrane ke liye, iska matlab hai ki flight simulator par practice karna learning ke liye utna hi achha ho sakta hai jitna ek actual plane urrana agar yeh ek pilot ko lene waale discriminations (bhed-bhav) aur decisions par sufficiently call karta hai. Behtar graphics aur sounds important nahi hain, jab tak ki woh liye ja rahe decisions ki nature ko ya pilots ko milne wale cues ko na badlein ki kab khhas skills ya knowledge ka use karna hai.

Learning ke liye different methods ko evaluate karte waqt, jo direct approach ko significantly simulate karte hain woh kahin zyaada behtar transfer honge. Isliye, agar aap France ke apne trip se pehle French seekhne ka sabse behtar tarika evaluate karne ki koshish kar rahe hain, toh aapko flash cards ke beech se nikalne ke mukable Skype tutoring karne se mazeed (bhale hi perfect na ho) transfer milega.

### Tactic 4: The Overkill Approach

_(Ranniti 4: Overkill Approach)_
Directness ko badhane ke liye jo aakhiri method maine dhoondha hai woh challenge ko badhana hai, taaki required skill level poori tarah se us goal ke andar samahit (contained) ho jo set kiya gaya hai. Tristan de Montebello ne, jab World Championship of Public Speaking mein compete karne ki taiyari kar rahe the, middle schools mein bolne par push kiya, apne talk ke early versions dete hue. Unka ehsaas tha ki Toastmasters clubs mein unhein jo feedback mila woh unqi speech mein kya kaam kiya aur kya nahi ispar gehra katne (cut deep) ke liye bahut zyaada soft ya badhai-bhara (congratulatory) ho sakta hai. Middle school students, iske ulat, nishthur (merciless) honge. Agar unhone jo mazaak kaha woh funny nahi tha ya unki delivery boring ya cheesy thi, toh woh unke chehroon se immediately bata sakte the ki kispar dobara kaam karne ki zarurat hai. Overkill approach apne aap ko ek aise environment mein dalna hai jahan demands tezi se high hone wali hain, isliye aapke kisi important lessons ya feedback ko miss karne ki sambhavna kam hoti hai.

Is tarah ke environment mein jana intense feel ho sakta hai. Aap aisa feel kar sakte hain jaise aap ek aisi bhasha bolna shuru karne ke liye “ready nahi hain” jise aapne mushkil se seekha hai. Aap stage par khade hone aur ek aisi speech deliver karne se darr sakte hain jise aapne perfectly memorize nahi kiya hai. Aap directly apna khud ka application program karne mein dive nahi karna chahte aur un videos ko dekhne se chipakna prefer karte hain jahan koi aur coding kar raha hai. Lekin yeh fears aksar sirf temporary hote hain. Agar aap is method ko shuru karne ke liye kaafi motivation haasil kar sakte hain, toh ise long term jaari rakhna aksar kahin zyaada aasan hota hai. Mere language learning project mein har naye country mein pehla hafta hamesha ek shock hota tha, lekin jald hi poori tarah se nayi bhasha ke andar jeena poori tarah se normal ho gaya.

Ek tarika jisse aap kisi project ko overkill kar sakte hain woh hai kisi khhas test, performance, ya challenge ka maqsad rakhna jo us skill level se upar ho jiski aapko strictly zarurat hai. Benny Lewis language exams ka attempt karna pasand karte hain, kyunki woh ek concrete challenge provide karte hain. Apne German project mein, woh sabse highest-level exam ka attempt karna chahte the, kyunki us goal ki awareness unhein study karne par usse kahin zyaada push karegi jitna woh tab karte agar woh comfortable conversations se hi santusht hote. Meri ek aur dost ne apne skills aur talent ko push karne ke ek madhyam ke roop mein apni photography ko pradarshit (exhibit) karne ka faisla kiya. Pehle se yeh taye karna ki aapka kaam publicly dekhne yogya hoga, aapke learning ke approach ko badal deta hai aur aapko desired domain mein performance ki taraf geared karega, bajaye sirf seekhe gaye facts ke boxes ko check karne ke.

## Learn Straight from the Source

_(Seedhe Srot Se Seekhein)_
