Directly seekhna mere dwara samne aaye kai safal ultralearning projects ki mukhya nishaniyon mein se ek hai, khhasakar isliye kyunki yeh education ke us style se kitna different ho sakta hai jiske hum zyaada tar aadi (used to) hain. Jab bhi aap kuch naya seekhte hain, toh apne aap se yeh poochna ek achha habit hai ki knowledge kahan aur kaise khud ko zahir karegi. Agar aap uska javab de sakte hain, toh aap phir pooch sakte hain ki kya aap jo seekh rahe hain use us context se baandhne ke liye kuch kar rahe hain. Agar aap nahi kar rahe hain, toh aapko saavdhani se chalna (tread carefully) hoga, kyunki transfer ki problem apna badsoorat sir utha (rear its ugly head) sakti hai.

Directly seekhne ka act, halanki, us sawaal ke javab ka sirf aadha hissa hai ki aapko achhi tarah seekhne ke liye kya karna chahiye. Us environment mein bahut saara direct practice karna jahan aap aakhirkar apne skills ka use karna chahte hain, ek important start hai. Halanki, skills par jaldi maharat haasil karne ke liye, bulk practice (thok abhyas) hi kaafi nahi hai. Yeh hamein hamare agle ultralearning niyan tak le jata hai: **drill (abhyas/shrankhla)**.

---

# Chapter 7 — Principle 4: Drill

### _(Niyam 4 — Drill: Apne Sabse Kamzor Point Par Hamla Karein)_

---

> _"Take care of the bars and the piece will take care of itself."_
> _(Swar-lipi ki ek-ek bar [bars] ka dhayan rakho, poori dhun [piece] apna dhayan khud rakh legi.)_
> — Philip Johnston, composer

---

Benjamin Franklin ne apni poori life mein jitne bhi roles nibhaye—entrepreneur, inventor, scientist, diplomat, aur United States ke founding father—woh sabse pehle aur mukhya roop se ek writer the. Writing mein hi unhein sabse pehli safalata mili thi. Apne bhai ki printing company ke ek naukar (apprentice) ke roop mein bache hue saalon ke anubandhit shram (indentured labor) se bachne ke liye Boston se bhaagne ke baad, woh Philadelphia gaye. Wahan, penniless (kangal) aur anjaan, unhone ek doosre competitor ke roop mein khud ko establish karne se pehle ek doosri printing company ke liye kaam kiya.

Unki _Poor Richard’s Almanack_ ek international bestseller ban gayi aur isne unhein forty-two ki umra mein retire hone ki izazat di. Halanki, yeh unki life ka baad ka aadha hissa (latter half) tha jab unki writing ke duniya ko badal dene wale parinaam (world-changing consequences) hone wale تھے.

Ek scientist ke roop mein, Franklin math mein kharab the aur brahmand ke bade-bade theories ke mukable practical parinaamon mein mazeed interested the. Halanki, unki gady (prose) “ek na-sikhia (uninitiated) insaan ke sath-sath ek philosopher ke liye bhi equally achhi tarah likhi gayi thi,” English chemist Sir Humphrey Davy ne note kiya, yeh add karte hue ki “unhone apne details ko amusing ke sath-sath spasht (perspicuous) banaya hai.” Unki writing ki taqat aur iske practical parinaamon ne unhein ek international sensation bana diya.

Politics mein, yeh phir se Franklin ka writing talent hi tha jisne unhein allies (saathi) jeetne aur sambhavit virodhiyon (potential antagonists) ko manane mein madad ki. American Revolution se pehle, unhone ek essay likha, jo supposedly Prussia ke King Frederick II dwara likha gaya tha, jiska title tha _“An Edict by the King of Prussia.”_ Isme unhone British-American relations par vyang (satirized) kiya, yeh prastav dekar ki, British Isles ke shuruati settlers German origin ke hone ke kaaran, Prussian king dwara “Britain mein unhi colonies se revenue uthaya jana chahiye (revenue should be raised).”

Baad mein, ek pen ke sath unka hunar unki writing ko Declaration of Independence mein tabdil kar dega, jahan unhone Thomas Jefferson ke lafzon ko edit karke ab ka famous _“We hold these truths to be self-evident”_ banaya.

Writing aur persuasion (manane ki kala) ke aise adbhut hunar ke sath, yeh poochne layak hai ki Franklin ne ise kaise haasil kiya. Fortunately (Khush-kismat-se), un kai doosre bade writers ke ulat, jinke apne skills ko behtar banane (honing) ke prayas mysterious bane hue hain, hamare paas Franklin ke khud ke lafz hain ki unhone ise kaise kiya. Apni _Autobiography_ mein, woh ek young boy ke roop mein practice ke liye apni writing skill ke sections ko alag-alag tukdon mein kaatne ke apne samajhdaari bhare prayason (sophisticated efforts) ko detail se batate hain. Bachpan mein ek dost ke sath auraton ko shiksha dene ke gun-dosh (merits) par ek debate se shuru karte hue (Franklin paksh mein the, unka dost khilaf), unke father ne notice kiya ki unki writing ke aspects mein manane ki kshamta (persuasive ability) ki kami thi. Franklin ne is tarah “improvement par prayas karne ka nishchay (determined to endeavor at improvement)” kiya aur apni writing skill ki practice karne ke liye exercises ki ek series par lag gaye.

Ek aisi exercise jise woh document karte hain, unka ek favorite magazine, _The Spectator_ ko lena, aur wahan dikhne wale articles par notes banana tha. Phir woh un notes ko kuch dino ke liye chhod dete aur unpar wapas aate, memory se original argument ko phir se construct karne ki koshish karte hue. Khatam karne ke baad, unhone “apne Spectator ko original ke sath compare kiya, apni kuch faults ko discover kiya, aur unhein correct kiya.” Yeh realize karne par ki unki vocabulary limited thi, unhone ek aur strategy develop ki. Prose (gady) ko verse (kavita) mein badal kar, woh words ko un synonyms (paryayvachi) ke sath replace kar sakte the jo meter ya rhyme mein match karte hon. Ek essay ke bhashan-kala ke pravah (rhetorical flow) ke apne ehsaas ko behtar banane liye, unhone apne imitation approach ko phir se try kiya, lekin is baar unhone hints ko jumbled up (upar-neeche) kar diya taaki unhein dobara likhte waqt ideas ke sequence ke sahi order ko determine karna pade.

Ek baar jab unhone writing ke kuch mechanics ko establish kar liya, toh woh ek aise style mein likhne ke mazeed difficult task par badh gaye jo convince (manane) kar sake. Ek English grammar kitab padhte waqt, unka samna Socratic method ke idea se hua, yaani directly contradict (khandan) karne ke bajaye janch karne wale sawaalon (probing questions) ke zariye doosre ke ideas ko chunauti dena. Phir woh kaam par lag gaye, saavdhani se “abrupt contradiction aur positive argumentation” se bachte hue, iske bajaye ek “vinamra jigyasu aur shakk karne wale (humble inquirer and doubter)” hone par focus karte hue.

Un shuruati prayason ne results produce kiye. Sixteen saal ki umra mein, woh apne kaam ko publish karwana chahte the. Halanki, is darr se ki unke bade bhai ise haath ke haath reject kar sakte hain, unhone apni likhavat (penmanship) ko chhupaya (disguised) aur Silence Dogood ke pseudonym (kaalpnik naam) ke tehat apna essay submit kiya, yeh dikhaate hue ki woh countryside mein rehne wali ek vidhwa aurat (widowed woman) hain. Unke bhai ne, asli author ko jaane bina, essay ko approve aur publish kar diya, isliye Franklin laute aur unhone mazeed likha. Bhale hi ise bhed-bhav ke bina apni writing par vichar karwane ke liye ek chaal (ruse) ke roop mein shuru kiya gaya tha, Franklin ka doosre characters ko apnaane (adopting) ka abhyas unke baad ke career mein behad keemti (invaluable) sabit hoga. For example, _Poor Richard’s Almanack_ ko ek simple husband aur wife, Richard aur Bridget Saunders ke nazariye se likha gaya tha, aur unke political essays jaise unka _“An Edict by the King of Prussia”_ ne bhi similarly kaalpnik nazariyon (imagined perspectives) ko apnaane ki unki lachilepan (flexibility) ka upyog kiya.

Writing par ek maharat pehle establish kiye bina Franklin ka aaj us ghar-ghar ke naam (household name) banna kalpana karna difficult hai. Chahe yeh business ho, science ho, ya raj-kaaj (statecraft), jo cheez unhein persuasive aur bade banati thi uska badalna na wala core achhi tarah likhne ki unki ability thi. Jis cheez ne Franklin ko alag kiya woh merely unka likha gaya matra ya unka raw talent nahi tha balki unka practice karne ka tareeqa tha. Jis tareeqe se unhone writing ki skill ko alag karne aur iske elements ki akele mein (isolation) practice karne ka faisla kiya, usne unhein ek chhoti umra mein writing par maharat haasil karne aur ise un doosre prayason (pursuits) par apply karne kabil banaya jiske liye woh baad mein famous hue. Aisa saavdhaan vishleshan (careful analysis) aur sachet abhyas (deliberate practice) chauthe ultralearning niyan ka aadhar banate hain: drill.

## The Chemistry of Learning

_(Learning Ki Chemistry)_

Chemistry mein, ek useful concept hai jise begh-nirdharit karne wala kadam (rate-determining step) ke roop mein jaana jata hai. Yeh tab hota hai jab ek reaction multiple steps par hoti hai, jisme ek reaction ke products doosri reaction ke liye reagents (pratikarak) ban jaate hain. Rate-determining step reactions ki is chain ka sabse slowest part hota hai, ek bottleneck (badha) banata hai jo ultimately poori reaction ke hone ke liye required kul samay ko nirdharit (defines) karta hai. Learning, main tark dena chahta hoon, aksar similarly kaam karti hai, jisme learning problem ke khhas aspects ek bottleneck banate hain jo us raftaar ko control karta hai jis par aap overall mazeed kushal (proficient) ban sakte hain.

Mathematics seekhne par vichar karein. Yeh ek complex skill hai jiske kai different parts hain: aapko fundamental concepts ko samajhne kabil hona chahiye, aapko kisi khhas tarah ke problem ko solve karne ke algorithm ko yaad rakhne kabil hona chahiye, aur aapko pata hona chahiye ki yeh kis context mein apply hota hai. Is ability ke aadhar (underlying) mein, halanki, arithmetic aur algebra karne ki ability hai taaki sawaal ke ghere mein majood problems ko solve kiya ja sake. Agar aapka arithmetic kamzor hai ya aapka algebra laparwah (sloppy) hai, toh aapko galat answers milenge bhale hi aapne doosre concepts par maharat haasil kar li ho.

Foreign bhasha seekhte waqt ek aur rate-determining step vocabulary ho sakta hai. Aap jitne sentences successfully bol sakte hain woh is baat par depend karta hai ki aap kitne words jaante hain. Agar aap bahut kam jaante hain, toh aap bahut zyaada baare mein baat nahi kar payenge. Agar aap sudden apne dimaagi database mein saikdon naye words inject karne kabil hote hain, toh aap apni fluency ko drastically expand kar sakte hain bhale hi aapki pronunciation, grammar, ya doosra bhashayi knowledge unchanged rahe.

Drills karne ke peeche yahi strategy hai. Apni learning reaction mein ek rate-determining step ko identify karke, aap ise isolate kar sakte hain aur ispar vishisht roop se (specifically) kaam kar sakte hain. Chunki yeh us skill ke sath aapki overall competence (kshamta) ko govern (control) karta hai, isme improve karke aap usse kahin zyaada tezi se improve karenge jitna aap tab karte jab aap skill ke har ek aspect ki ek sath practice karne ki koshish karte hain. Writing ko rapidly behtar banane ke liye Franklin ki antardrishti (insight) wahi thi: writing ki overall skill ke components ko identify karke, yeh figure out karke ki unki situation mein kaun sa matter karta hai, aur phir apni practice mein unhein highlight (emphasize) karne ke chalaak tareeqon ke sath aakar, woh sirf bahut saara samay likhne mein bitane ke mukable mazeed tezi se behtar ho sakte the.

## Drills and Cognitive Load

_(Drills Aur Cognitive Load [Dimaagi Bojh])_

Learning mein rate-determining steps—jahan ek complex skill ka ek component aapki performance ke overall level ko determine karta hai—drills apply karne ka ek powerful kaaran hain. Halanki, woh akele nahi hain. Bhale hi skill ka koi aisa isolatable aspect na ho jo aapki performance ko peeche khinch raha ho, tab bhi drills apply karna ek achha idea ho sakta hai.

Kaaran yeh hai ki jab aap kisi complex skill ki practice kar rahe hote hain, toh aapke dimaagi resources (attention, memory, effort, etc.) task ke kai different aspects par phhaile hone chahiye. Jab Franklin likh rahe the, toh unhein na keval apne prastut kiye ja rahe argument ke logical content par vichar karna tha balki word choice aur bhashan-kala ke style (rhetorical style) par bhi. Yeh ek learning trap (jaal) create kar sakta hai. Ek aspect mein apni performance ko behtar banane liye, aapko us ek aspect par itna zyaada attention devot karne ki zarurat ho sakti hai ki aapki performance ke doosre parts neeche girne (go down) lagte hain. Agar aap apne aap ko kevel is baat par judge kar sakte hain ki aap overall task mein kitna improve karte hain, toh yeh ek aisi situation ki taraf le ja sakta hai jisme aapki improvement slow ho jaati hai kyunki aap kisi vishisht component mein behtar banne ke dauran overall task mein badtar (getting worse) ho rahe honge.

Drills ek skill ko itna simplify (saral) karke is problem ko resolve karti hain ki aap apne dimaagi resources ko ek single aspect par focus kar sakein. Jab Franklin ne pehle padhe gaye ek essay ke order ko dobara construct karne par focus kiya, toh woh word usage, grammar, aur arguments ke content ke baare mein chinta karne ke zarurat ke bajaye apna saara attention is sawaal par devot kar sakte the ki ideas ka kaun sa sequence ek achhe essay ki taraf le jata hai.

Shatir readers (Astute readers) shayad is principle aur pichle principle ke beech ek khinchtan (tension) notice karenge. Agar direct practice mein us poori skill par kaam karna shamil hai jo us situation ke sabse paas ho jisme ise aakhirkar use kiya jayega, toh drills ek ulte direction mein kheenchna (pull) hain. Ek drill direct practice ko leti hai aur ise alag-alag kaat deti hai, taaki aap sirf ek isolated component ki practice kar rahe hon. Aap is virodhabhas (contradiction) ko kaise resolve kar sakte hain?

## The Direct-Then-Drill Approach

_(Direct-Then-Drill Approach)_

Directly seekhne aur drills karne ke beech ki khinchtan tab resolve ho sakti hai jab hum unhein learning ke ek bade cycle mein alternating stages (badalte hue charano) ke roop mein dekhte hain. Learning ke liye kai academic rannitiyon mein ki jaane wali galti direct context ko ignore karna ya ise door (abstract it away) kar dena hai, is umeed mein ki agar kaafi saare component skills develop ho jayein, toh woh aakhirkar transfer ho jayenge.

Ultralearners, iske ulat, frequently iska upyog karte hain jise main _Direct-Then-Drill Approach_ kahunga.

1. **Pehla step skill ki directly practice karne ki koshish karna hai.** Iska matlab hai yeh figure out karna ki skill kahan aur kaise use ki jayegi aur phir jab practice kar rahe hon toh us situation ko jitna possible ho utna paas match karne ki koshish karna. Ek bhasha ki practice ise actually bol kar karein. Software likh kar programming seekhein. Essays likh kar apne writing skills ko behtar banayein. Yeh shuruati connection aur baad ka feedback loop ensure karta hai ki transfer ki problem paida nahi hogi.
2. **Agla step direct skill ka vishleshan karna aur un components ko isolate karne ki koshish karna hai** jo ya toh aapki performance mein rate-determining steps hain ya aise subskills hain jinhein behtar banana aapko difficult lagta hai kyunki aapko unpar focus karne ke liye saari doosri cheezein ek sath chal rahi hain. Yahan se aap drills develop kar sakte hain aur un components ki alag se practice kar sakte hain jab tak ki aap unmein behtar na ho jayein.
3. **Aakhiri step direct practice par wapas jana aur aapne jo seekha hai use samahit (integrate) karna hai.** Iske do maqsad (purposes) hain. Pehla yeh hai ki well-designed drills mein bhi, transfer ke hiccups (ichkiyaan/badhayein) hone wali hain is fact ke kaaran ki jo pehle ek isolated skill thi use ek naye aur mazeed complex context mein move kiya jana chahiye. Ise un muscles ko jodne ke liye sanyoji utak (connective tissue) banane jaisa sochein jinhein aapne alag se strengthen kiya hai. Is step ka doosra function ek check ke roop mein hai ki kya aapki drill well-designed aur sahi thi ya nahi. Ek drill ko isolate karne ki kai koshishon ka ant asafalata (failure) mein ho sakta hai kyunki drill sach mein us baareek cheez ko nahi kaat-ti jo real practice mein difficult thi. Yeh theek hai; yeh feedback aapko un cheezon ko seekhne mein samay barbaad karne se bachane (minimize wasting time) ke liye important hai jo aapke end goals ke liye bahut zyaada matter nahi karti hain.

Learning process mein aap jitne shuruat (earlier) mein honge, yeh cycle utna hi tez hona chahiye. Direct practice aur drills ke beech cycle karna, bhale hi same learning session ke andar ho, ek achha idea hai jab aap abhi shuruat kar rahe hon. Baad mein, jaise-zaise aap jo karne ki koshish kar rahe hain usme behtar hote jaate hain aur aapki overall performance ko notice karne yogya behtar banane liye bahut zyaada effort required hoti hai, toh drills mein lambe raste (detours) lena mazeed acceptable hai. Jaise-jaise aap maharat (mastery) ke paas pahunchete hain, aapka samay aakhirkar zyaada tar drills par focus ho sakta hai kyunki is baare mein aapka knowledge ki complex skill kaise individual components mein toot-ti hai mazeed refined aur accurate ho jata hai aur kisi individual component ko behtar banana harder aur harder hota jata hai.

## Tactics for Designing Drills

_(Drills Design Karne Ki Rannitiyan)_

Is principle ko apply karte waqt teen mukhya problems hoti hain.

**Pehli problem yeh figure out karna hai ki kab aur kya drill karna hai.** Aapko is par focus karna chahiye ki skill ke kaun se aspects aapki performance mein rate-determining steps ho sakte hain. Skill ka kaun sa aspect, agar aapne isme improve kiya, toh sabse kam effort ke liye aapki abilities mein overall sabse badi improvement ka kaaran banega? Aapke accounting skills is fact se limited ho sakte hain ki aapka Excel knowledge upri (superficial) hai, jo aapko jaanti hui saari cheezon ko practical situations par apply karne se rokta hai. Aapki language abilities galat pronunciation hone ke kaaran peeche kheenchi (held back) ja sakti hain, bhale hi aap sahi words jaante hon.

Un aspects ko bhi dekhein jise aapko ek sath juggle (sambhalna) karne ki zarurat hai. Inmein improve karna harder ho sakta hai kyunki aap unhein behtar banane liye kaafi dimaagi resources devot nahi kar sakte. Ek naya article likhte waqt, aapko research, storytelling, vocabulary, aur kai doosre aspects ko ek sath juggle karna pad sakta hai, jisse sirf ek mein bahut behtar hona hard ho jata hai. Kya drill karna hai yeh determine karna pechida (tricky) lag sakta hai, lekin ise hone ki zarurat nahi hai. Key prayog (experiment) karna hai. Is baare mein ek hypothesis banayein ki kaun si cheez aapko peeche khinch rahi hai, Direct-Then-Drill Approach ka upyog karke kuch drills ke sath ispar hamla karein, aur aap jaldi se feedback paa sakte hain ki kya aap sahi hain.

**Doosri kathinai (difficulty) is principle ke sath improvement produce karne ke liye drill ko design karna hai.** Yeh aksar hard hota hai kyunki bhale hi aap apni performance ke us aspect ko recognize kar lein jisme aap kamzor hain, ek aisi drill design karna pechida ho sakta hai jo us component ko train kare bina us cheez ko artificially hataye jo ise actual application mein difficult banati hai. Franklin ki drills asadharn (uncommon) thin, mera vishwas hai, kyunki zyaada tar log, apni writing ability mein vishhisht kamiyon (specific deficits) ko recognize karte hue bhi, unmein subskills jaise arguments ko persuasively order karna aur ek safal writing style ki nakal karne ke tareeqe dhoondhne ki chaturai (ingenuity) nahi hoti.

**Finally, drills karna hard hai aur aksar uncomfortable hota hai.** Aapki performance ke baare mein sabse badtar cheez ko baahar nikaalna (teasing out) aur akele mein uski practice karne ke liye kaleja (guts) chahiye hota hai. Un cheezon par focus karne mein samay bitana kahin zyaada pleasant hota hai jisme aap pehle se hi achhe hain. Is natural tendency ko dekhte hue, aaiye drills karne ke kuch acche tareeqon ko dekhein taaki aap unhein khud apply karna shuru kar sakein.

### Drill 1: Time Slicing

_(Samay Ka Tukda Karna)_
Ek drill create karne ka sabse aasan tarika actions ke ek lambe sequence ke samay mein ek tukde (slice) ko isolate karna hai. Musicians aksar is tarah ki training karte hain jab woh sangheet ke ek hisse (piece of music) ke sabse hardest parts ko identify karte hain aur har ek ki tab tak practice karte hain jab tak ki yeh perfect na ho jaye, isse pehle ki use poore song ya symphony ke context mein wapas samahit (integrate) kiya jaye. Athletes similarly is process mein engage hote hain jab woh un skills ko drill karte hain jo aam taur par kul khelne ke samay (total playing time) ka ek hissa hoti hain, jaise layups ya penalty shots.

Ek nayi bhasha seekhne ke shuruati phase mein, main aksar deewanapan ki had tak kuch mukhya phrases ko repeat karta hoon, taaki woh jaldi se meri long-term memory mein embed (samahit) ho jayein. Aap jo skill seekh rahe hain uske un parts ko dekhein jinhein samay ke vishisht moments mein decomposed (toda) kiya ja sakta hai jisme difficulty ya mahatva badha hua ho.

### Drill 2: Cognitive Components

_(Dimaagi Ghaatak/Components)_
Kabhi-kabhi aap jis cheez ki practice karna chahenge woh ek badi skill ke samay mein ek tukda nahi balki ek vishisht cognitive component hoga. Ek bhasha bolte waqt, grammar, pronunciation, aur vocabulary har moment par hoti hain, lekin woh different dimaagi aspects banati hain jinhein ek sath manage kiya jana chahiye. Yahan tactic ek aisi tareeqe se sirf ek component ko drill karne ka rasta dhoondhna hai jab, vyavahar (practice) mein, doosron ko same samay par apply kiya jata.

Mandarin Chinese seekhte waqt, main tone drills karta tha jisme different tones wale words ke jodon (pairs) ko pronounce karna aur khud ko bolte hue record karna shamil tha. Usne mujhe different tones jaldi produce karne ka abhyas karne ki izazat di, bina is bhatkaav ke ki words ka matlab kya tha ya grammatically sahi sentences kaise banayein.

### Drill 3: The Copycat

_(Nakalchi)_
Kai creative skills mein drills ke sath ek difficulty yeh hai ki doosron ke kaam ko kiye bina ek aspect ki practice karna aksar impossible hota hai. For instance, jab Franklin arguments ko logically order karne ki apni ability ko behtar banane ki koshish kar rahe the, toh ek poora essay likhe bina aisa karna possible nahi tha. Apni khud ki learning mein is problem ko solve karne ke liye, aap Franklin se ek panna le sakte hain: skill ke jin parts ko aap drill nahi karna chahte unhein copy karke (chahe kisi aur se ya apne pichle kaam se), aap exclusively us component bhaag par focus kar sakte hain jiski aap practice karna chahte hain. Na keval yeh bahut saara samay bachata hai, kyunki aapko sirf us part ko repeat karne ki zarurat hai jise aap drill kar rahe hain, balki yeh aapke dimaagi bojh (cognitive burden) ko bhi kam karta hai, jiska matlab hai ki aap us ek aspect par behtar banne ke liye mazeed focus apply kar sakte hain.

Drawing ki practice karte waqt, maine na keval photos se balki un drawings se draw karna shuru kiya jinhein doosre logon ne kiya tha. Usne mujhe picture ko accurately render karne ki skill par focus karne mein madad ki, is faisale ko saral banate hue ki scene ko kaise frame kiya jaye aur kaun se details shamil kiye jaayein. Lachile ranatmak kaamon (flexible creative works) ke liye, pichle samay mein aapne jo works create kiye hain unhein edit karne ka same asar ho sakta hai, jo aapko ek original composition ke doosri demands par vichar kiye bina apne kaam ke ek aspect ko chunaavatmka roop se (selectively) behtar banane ki izazat deta hai.

### Drill 4: The Magnifying Glass Method

_(Magnifying Glass Method)_
Maan lijiye aapko kuch naya create karne ki zarurat hai aur aap jis part ki practice karna chahte hain use edit ya alag nahi kar sakte. Aap ek drill kaise create kar sakte hain? _The Magnifying Glass Method_ skill ke ek component par usse kahin zyaada samay bitana hai jitna aap otherwise bitate. Yeh aapki overall performance ko kam kar sakta hai ya aapke input samay ko badha sakta hai, lekin yeh aapko apna samay aur dimaagi resources ka ek bada hissa us subskill par spend karne ki izazat dega jisme aap maharat haasil karna chahte hain.

Maine is method ko apply kiya jab maine articles likhte waqt research karne ki apni ability ko behtar banane ki koshish ki, research par pehle ke mukable lagbhag das guna lamba samay bitakar. Bhale hi mujhe article likhne ke saare doosre parts karne the, lekin research par normal se kahin zyaada lamba samay bitakar, main aisa karne ke liye nayi habits aur skills develop kar saka.

### Drill 5: Prerequisite Chaining

_(Prerequisite Chaining)_
Ek strategy jise maine ultralearners se baar-baar dekha hai woh ek aisi skill se shuruat karna hai jiske liye unke paas saare prerequisites (puv-aacharya/sharat) nahi hain. Phir, jab woh kharab perform karte hain (jo ki tay hai), toh woh ek step peeche jaate hain, foundational topics mein se ek ko seekhte hain, aur exercise ko repeat karte hain. Bahut zyaada hard se shuruat karne aur prerequisites ko seekhne ka yeh abhyas jaise unqi zarurat padti hai, frustrating ho sakta hai, lekin yeh un subskills ko seekhne mein bahut saara samay bachata hai jo actually performance ko bahut zyaada nahi chalate (don't drive performance much).

Eric Barone ne, for instance, apne pixel art experiments simply unhein banakar shuru kiye. Jab unhone khhas aspects, jaise colors ke sath struggle kiya, toh woh ek step peeche gaye, color theory seekhi, aur apne kaam ko repeat kiya. Benny Lewis ke paas ek phrase book se bolne ke sath shuruat karne aur bhasha ki grammar jo explain karti hai ki phrases kaise function karte hain use baad mein seekhne ki ek similar habit hai.

## Mindful Drilling

_(Sachet Drilling)_

Kai logon ke liye, drilling ka idea ek galat direction mein kheenchna lag sakta hai. Hum sabne homework karne mein samay bitaya hai jise facts aur procedures ko hamare andar drill karne ke liye design kiya gaya tha jo aakhirkar ek total waste of time sabit hua. Yeh aksar isliye tha kyunki hum uske peeche ke kaaranon ko nahi jaante the jiski hum practice kar rahe the ya yeh kaise ek mazeed vyapak context mein fit baithta tha. Bina context ke problems ko drill karna dimaag ko sunn karne wala (mind-numbing) hota hai. Halanki, ek baar jab aapne identify kar liya ki yeh wahi bottleneck hai jo aapko aage badhne se rok raha hai, toh woh ek naye maqsad (purpose) ke sath bhar jaate hain. Ultralearning mein, jise student dwara nirdeshit kiya jata hai, kisi baari srot se nahi, drills ek nayi roshni le leti hain. Anjaan maqsadon ke liye unhein karne par majboor hone ke bajaye, ab yeh aap par depend karta hai ki aap un vishisht cheezon par learning ko tez karke learning process ko badhane ka rasta dhoondhein jinhein aap sabse difficult paate hain. Is sense mein, traditional learning ke mukable ultralearning mein drills ek bahut hi different flavor le leti hain. Bematlab ki ghisaai (meaningless drudgery) hone se door, carefully designed drills creativity aur imagination ko baahar nikaalti (elicit) hain jab aap ek mazeed complex learning challenge ko vishisht parts mein tod kar solve karne ka prayas karte hain.

Drills karna hard hai, yahi wajah hai ki hum mein se kai log unse bachna chahenge. Jab ki hum drills mein engage hote hain, toh yeh aksar un subjects mein hota hai jahan hum kabil aur comfortable feel karte hain. Drills learner se na keval is baare mein gehrai se sochne ki demand karti hain ki kya seekha ja raha hai balki yeh figure out karne ki bhi ki kya sabse difficult hai aur us weakness par directly hamla karne ki, bajaye iske ki uspar focus kiya jaye jo sabse zyaada fun hai ya jisme pehle se hi maharat haasil ho chuki hai. Iske liye strong motivation aur aakramak roop se seekhne ke sath ek comfort ki zarurat hoti hai.

Franklin ne apni _Autobiography_ mein un unchiyon ke baare mein remark kiya jahan tak woh gaye taaki woh khud ko apni writing drills ke liye dedicate kar sakein: “In exercises aur padhne ke liye mera samay raat mein tha, kaam ke baad ya subah shuru hone se pehle.” Unki life mein writing jo prominent (mukhya) role play karegi uske bavajood, Franklin ko print shop mein apne taskmaster bhai ke tehat lambe ghante kaam karna padta tha, jo unke paas thode se bache aaram ke samay mein lagan se apne craft ko behtar banate the. Eric Barone ne similarly apne pixel art ko daso baar repeat kiya, wapas jaakar prerequisite concepts aur theory par maharat haasil ki jab tak ki unhone ise perfect nahi kar liya.

Drills ki difficulty aur usefulness ek aise pattern ko repeat karti hain jo poore ultralearning niyamon mein dobara saamne aayega: ki **kuch dimaagi roop se kadi (mentally strenuous) cheez kisi aasan cheez ke mukable learning ke liye ek bada benefit provide karti hai.** Kahin bhi yeh pattern isse zyaada saaf nahi hai jitna ki agle niyan, **retrieval (punarprapti/yaad karna)** mein, jahan difficulty khud hi mazeed effective learning ki key ho sakti hai.

---

# Chapter 8 — Principle 5: Retrieval

### _(Niyam 5 — Retrieval: Seekhne Ke Liye Test Karein)_

---

> _"It pays better to wait and recollect by an effort from within, than to look at the book again."_
> _(Kitab ko dobara dekhne ke bajaye, theherna aur andar se ek prayas [effort] karke yaad karna [recollect] kahin zyaada fayda pahunchata hai.)_
> — William James, psychologist

---

1913 ki spring (basant) mein, mathematician G. H. Hardy ko ek aisa letter mila jo unki life ke raaste ko hamesha ke liye nirdharit (define) karne wala tha. India mein Madras ke Port Trust Office mein kaam karne waale ek accounting clerk dwara bheje gaye is letter mein prachay (introduction) ka ek vinamra note tha, sath hi kuch hairan karne wale daave (startling assertions) the. Author ne claim kiya tha ki unhone un problems ke liye theorems (prmey) dhoondh liye hain jinhein us samay ke sabse behtar mathematical minds ne abhi tak solve nahi kiya tha. Kahin zyaada, unhone claim kiya ki unke paas “koi University education nahi” thi aur unhone in results ko apni hi tanhaa janchon (solitary investigations) se nikaala (derived) tha.

Maths mein Hardy ke kad (stature) ke kisi insaan ke liye un shaukiya paaglon (amateur crackpots) se letters milna ek samanya baat thi jo famous problems ke solutions hone ka claim karte the, isliye pehle toh unhone is letter ko bas waisa hi samajh kar kharij (dismissed) kar diya. Phir bhi, letter ke sath attach kiye gaye notes ke kai pages ko palat-te (flipping) hue, equations unke mind se nahi ja rahi thin. Jab unhone ghanton baad bhi apne aap ko unke baare mein sochte hue paaya, toh unhone is letter ko apne colleague John Littlewood ke dhyan mein laya. Jaise hi un dono ne un ajeeb daavon ko prove karne ki koshish mein haath aazmaya (toyed), unhone paaya ki unmein se kuch ko toh woh badi effort ke sath prove karne kabil the, jabki doosre, Hardy ke lafzon mein, “vishwasi karne ke layak na ke barabar (scarcely possible to believe)” rahe. Shayad, Hardy ne socha, yeh kisi paagal ka letter nahi tha balki kuch kaafi different tha.

Likhe gaye formulas itne bizarre (ajeeb) aur anjaan (alien) the ki Hardy ne remark kiya, “Unhein sach hona hi hoga kyunki, agar woh sach nahi hote, toh kisi ke paas unhein ijaad karne ki imagination nahi hoti.” Jis cheez ko unhone us din sirf dhundhla sa samjha (vaguely understood) tha woh yeh thi ki unka abhi-abhi sabse brilliant aur bizarre mathematicians mein se ek se pehla parichay hua tha, Srinivasa Ramanujan.

## Ramanujan’s Genius

_(Ramanujan Ka Genius)_

Hardy ko apna letter likhne se pehle, jisne mathematical history ke raaste ko badal diya, Ramanujan south India ka ek gareeb, mota (pudgy) ladka tha jise equations se ek khhas pyaar tha. Kisi bhi doosri cheez se zyaada, woh math se pyaar karta tha. In fact, math ke prati unke pyaar ne unhein aksar difficulties mein daal diya. Doosre subjects ko padhne ki unki anichha (unwillingness) ne unhein university se fail (flunked) karwa diya. Equations hi thin jinki woh parwah karte the. Apne spare time (khaali samay) mein aur berozgari ke dauran, woh apne family ke ghar ke samane bench par ghanton baithte the, haath mein slate liye, formulas ke sath khelte hue. Kabhi-kabhi woh itni der tak jaagte rehte the ki unki mother ko unke haath mein khana dena padta tha taaki woh kha sakein.

Chunki woh apne daur ke mathematics ke center se hazaron miles door the, Ramanujan ke liye high-quality textbooks tak access hona kaafi bada challenge tha. Ek resource jisse unka samna hua aur jiska unhone vyapak roop se upyog (mined extensively) kiya woh George Shoobridge Carr dwara likhi gayi ek volume thi jise _A Synopsis of Elementary Results in Pure and Applied Mathematics_ kehte hain. Carr khud mathematical genius ka koi ooncha kad (towering figure) nahi the. Woh kitab, jo students ke liye ek guide ke roop mein intended (prastavit) thi, usme different fields ke various theorems ki badi lists thin, aam taur par bina kisi explanation ya proof ke. Halanki, bina proofs ya explanations ke available hone par bhi, Carr ki kitab Ramanujan jaise kisi smart aur dhuni (obsessed) insaan ke haathon mein ek powerful resource ban gayi. Kyunki unhone nirdharit theorems kaise nikaale (derived) gaye hain ise simply copy aur memorize karne ke bajaye, unhein unhein apne dum par figure out karna pada.

Bhale hi us samay ke kai commentators ne, Hardy ko shamil karte hue, tark diya ki Ramanujan ke gareeb parvarish (impoverished upbringing) aur mathematics ke cutting edge tak der se access ne unke genius ko lagbhag na-sudharne yogya nuksaan (irreparable harm) pahunchaya, modern psychological experiments ek alternate perspective offer kar sakte hain, kyunki jab Ramanujan ne mathematical formulas ke prati apne hi ajeeb dhun (quirky obsession) ka upyog karke Carr ke theorems ki vyapak list se deal kiya, toh woh bina soche-samjhe ek gehri samajh build karne ke sabse powerful methods mein se ek ka abhyas kar rahe the.

## The Testing Effect

_(Testing Effect)_

Kalpana karein aap ek student hain jo ek exam ke liye prepare kar rahe hain. Aapke paas teen choices hain ki aap apne seemit study samay (limited studying time) ko kaise aavantit (allocate) karein.

1. **Pehle, aap material ko review kar sakte hain.** Aap apne notes aur kitab ko dekh sakte hain aur har cheez ko study kar sakte hain jab tak ki aap sure na hon ki aap ise yaad rakhenge.
2. **Doosre, aap apna test le sakte hain (self-test).** Aap kitab band rakh sakte hain aur yaad karne ki koshish kar sakte hain ki isme kya tha.
3. **Finally, aap ek concept map create kar sakte hain.** Aap ek diagram mein mukhya concepts ko likh sakte hain, yeh dikhaate hue ki woh kaise organized hain aur doosre items se related hain jinhein aapko study karne ki zarurat hai.

Agar aap sirf ek chun sakte hain, toh final exam mein sabse behtar karne ke liye aapko kaun sa chun'na chahiye?

Yeh essentially vahi sawaal hai jo psychologists Jeffrey Karpicke aur Janell Blunt ne learning strategy ke students ke chunaav par adhyayan karne wali ek study mein poocha tha. Study mein, students ko char groups mein divide kiya gya tha, har ek ko same samay diya gaya tha lekin different study strategies use karne ke liye kaha gaya tha: text ko ek single time review karna, ise baar-baar (repeatedly) review karna, free recall (mukti-smaran), aur concept mapping.

Har group mein, students se aane wale test par apne score ko predict karne ke liye kaha gaya tha. Jinhone repeated reviewing ki unhone predict kiya ki woh sabse behtar score karenge, uske baad single-study aur concept-mapping groups the. Jinhone **free recall** ka abhyas kiya (kitab mein dekhe bina jitna ho sake utna yaad karne ki koshish karna) unhone apni final performance ke liye sabse badtar (worst) predict kiya.

Actual results, halanki, aas-paas bhi nahi the. **Testing yourself**—text ko dekhe bina jankari ko yaad karne ki koshish karna (trying to retrieve information)—ne saaf taur par saari doosri conditions se behtar perform kiya. Text ke content par directly based sawaalon par, jinhone free recall ka abhyas kiya unhone doosre groups ke mukable lagbhag 50 percent zyaada yaad rakha. Students, jinhone is baare mein firsthand experience haasil karne mein saalon bitaye hain ki learning ke liye kya matter karta hai, woh kaise is baare mein itne gumrah (misguided) ho sakte hain ki actually kaun si cheez results produce karti hai?

Koi is baat par tark karne ke liye prerit (tempted) ho sakta hai ki self-testing ka yeh benefit us tareeqe ka ek parinaam (artifact) hai jisse safalata ko naapa jata hai. Directness ka niyan bayan karta hai ki transfer difficult hai. Chunki self-testing aur actual testing sabse zyaada similar hain, shayad yahi similarity is method ko behtar kaam karne kabil banati hai. Agar moolyankan ka method (method of evaluation) different hota, toh yeh shak karna reasonable hota ki review ya concept mapping top par aa sakti hain. Interestingly (Dilchasp baat yeh hai), ek aur experiment mein, Karpicke aur Blunt ne dikhaya ki yeh explanation bhi nahi tha. Is experiment mein final test ek concept map create karna tha. Moolyankan ke kaam (evaluation task) se behad similarity ke bavajood, free recall ne study karne ke liye concept mapping ke upyog se abhi bhi behtar perform kiya.

Ek aur sambhavit explanation ki self-testing kyun kaam karti hai, feedback hai. Jab aap kisi cheez ko nishkriya roop se (passively) review karte hain, toh aapko is baare mein koi feedback nahi milta ki aap kya jaante hain aur kya nahi jaante. Chunki tests aam taur par feedback ke sath aate hain, yeh explain kar sakta hai ki self-testing ka abhyas karne wale students ne concept mappers ya passive reviewers ko kyun haraya. Bhale hi yeh sach hai ki feedback keemti hai, ek baar phir, retrieval simply mazeed feedback haasil karne tak hi seemit (reduce down) nahi hoti. Bataye gaye experiments mein, students ko free recall karne ke liye kaha gaya tha lekin un items par koi feedback provide nahi kiya gaya tha jinhein woh miss kar gaye ya galat kar baithe. Memory se knowledge ko summon up (pukaarne/yaad karne) ka prayas apne aap mein ek powerful learning tool hai, direct practice ya feedback se iske connection se pare.

Learning par yeh naya nazariya dikhata hai ki Carr ki kitab, bina solutions ke proofs ki iski lists ke sath, unhein master karne ke liye sufficiently motivated insaan ke haathon mein, math mein brilliant banne ka ek adbhut tool kaise ban sakti thi. Answers haath mein na hone par, Ramanujan ko problems ke apne khud ke solutions ijaad karne par majboor hona pada, kitab mein ise review karne ke bajaye apne mind se jankari ko yaad (retrieving) karte hue.

## The Paradox of Studying

_(Padhai Ka Virodhabhas)_

Agar retrieval practice—memory se facts aur concepts ko yaad karne ki koshish karna—learning ke liye itni zyaada behtar hai, toh students ise realize kyun nahi karte? Kyun kai log concept mapping ya isse bhi kam effective passive review se chipakna prefer karte hain, jabki simply kitab band karke jitna ho sake utna yaad karne ki koshish karna unhein itni zyaada madad karega?

Karpicke ki research ek sambhavit explanation ki taraf point karti hai: **Human beings ke paas yeh nishchitta se jaan'ne ki ability nahi hoti ki unhone kisi cheez ko kitni achhi tarah seekha hai.** Iske bajaye, hamein apne study ke experience se milne wale clues par nirbhar rehna padta hai taaki humein ek ehsaas mile ki hum kitna achha kar rahe hain. Yeh so-called adhyayan ke moolyankan (judgments of learning - JOLs) aashik roop se is baat par based hote hain ki hum kisi cheez ko kitni faraatedar tareeqe se (fluently) process kar sakte hain. Agar learning ka task aasan aur smooth feel hota hai, toh hamari yeh vishwas karne ki zyaada sambhavna hoti hai ki humne ise seekh liya hai. Agar task ek struggle jaisa feel hota hai, toh hum feel karenge ki humne ise abhi tak nahi seekha hai.

Study karne mein kuch samay bitane ke theek baad, yeh JOLs accurate bhi ho sakte hain. Passive review ki strategy ka upyog karke kisi cheez ko study karne ke minutes baad, students usse behtar perform karte hain jitna woh tab karte agar unhone retrieval ka abhyas kiya hota. Yeh feeling ki aap tab zyaada seekh rahe hain jab aap padh rahe hain bajaye band kitab ke sath yaad karne ki koshish karne ke, galat nahi hai. Problem baad mein aati hai. Dino baad phir se test karein, aur retrieval practice passive review ko ek mile se hara (beats by a mile) deti hai. Jo study karne ke theek baad ke samay mein sahayak tha woh actual learning hone ke liye required long-term memory create nahi karta sabit hota.

Ek aur explanation ki students retrieval ke bajaye low-efficiency review ka vikalp kyun chunte hain yeh hai ki woh feel nahi karte ki woh material ko itni achhi tarah jaante hain ki uspar apna test le sakein. Ek aur experiment mein, Karpicke ne students se learning ke liye ek strategy chunwayi. Inevitably (Taye roop se), jo students kamzor perform kar rahe the unhone pehle material ko review karne ka chunaav kiya, tab tak wait karte hue jab tak ki woh practice testing start karne ke liye “ready” na hon. Agar experimental intervention (prayogatmak hastakshep) ke zariye, halanki, unhein retrieval ka abhyas pehle karne par majboor kiya gaya, toh unhone zyaada seekha. **Aap ready hon ya na hon, retrieval practice behtar kaam karti hai.** Especially agar aap retrieval ko answers dekhne kabil hone ke sath combine karte hain, toh retrieval practice study karne ka usse kahin behtar roop hai jise zyaada tar students apply karte hain.

## Is Difficulty Desirable?

_(Kya Mushkil Hona Vanchhaneeya Hai?)_

Kaun si cheez retrieval ka abhyas karne ko review se itna zyaada behtar banati hai? Ek javab psychologist R. A. Bjork ke vanchhaneeya mushkil (desirable difficulty) ke concept se aata hai. **Mazeed difficult retrieval behtar learning ki taraf le jata hai,** bhasharte ki retrieval ka act khud successfully ho sake. Free recall tests, jisme students ko bina kisi prompting (ishare) ke jitna yaad ho sake utna yaad karne ki zarurat hoti hai, unke nateejatan cued recall tests ke mukable behtar retention hota hai, jisme students ko is baare mein hints diye jaate hain ki unhein kya yaad rakhne ki zarurat hai. Cued recall tests, badle mein, recognition tests se behtar hote hain, jaise multiple-choice answers, jahan sahi answer ko recognize karne ki zarurat hoti hai lekin generate karne ki nahi. Kisi ko kuch seekhne ke immediately baad test dena delay ke sath test dene ke mukable retention ko kam behtar banata hai, itna lamba delay ki answers mind mein na hon jab unhein unki zarurat ho. Difficulty, retrieval ko kaam karwane mein ek obstacle hone se door, iske aisa karne ke kaaran ka hissa ho sakti hai.

Retrieval mein desirable difficulties ka idea ultralearning strategy ke liye ek mazboot paksh (potent case) pesh karta hai. Low-intensity learning strategies mein aam taur par ya toh kam ya aasan retrieval shamil hoti hai. Difficulty ko mazeed upar push karna aur aapke “ready” hone se kaafi pehle khud par test lene ka vikalp chunaav mazeed efficient hai. Koi Benny Lewis ke pehle hi din se ek nayi bhasha bolne ki strategy par wapas soch sakta hai. Bhale hi yeh approach difficulty mein high hai, research suggest karti hai ki yeh classroom study ke mazeed aasan roopon se kyun mazeed useful ho sakta hai. Apne aap ko ek mazeed difficult context mein rakhne ka matlab hai ki har baar jab Lewis ko kisi word ya phrase ko yaad karne ki zarurat hoti hai, toh ise classroom setting mein retrieval ke same act ko karne ke mukable mazeed strongly yaad rakha jayega aur simply words aur phrases ki ek list ko dekhne se toh kahin behtar.

Difficulty undesirable (gair-vanchhaneeya) ho sakti hai agar yeh itni hard ho jaye ki retrieval impossible ho jaye. Abhi-abhi seekhe gaye fact ke pehle test ko delay karne ke kuch benefits hain immediately test karne ke mukable. Halanki, agar aap test ko bahut zyaada delay karte hain, toh jankari poori tarah se bhooli ja sakti hai. Idea, isliye, sahi midpoint dhoondhna hai: itna door taaki jo kuch bhi retrieved kiya jaye use gehrai se yaad rakha jaye, itna door nahi ki aap sab kuch bhool chuke hon. Halanki apne aap par test lene se pehle bahut zyaada wait karne ke disadvantages ho sakte hain, apne aap ko kam clues aur prompts dekar difficulty badhana nishchit roop se sahayak hota hai, bhasharte ki aap baad mein unpar kuch feedback paa sakein.

## Should You Take the Final Exam Before the Class Even Begins?

_(Kya Aapko Class Shuru Hone Se Pehle Hi Final Exam De Dena Chahiye?)_

Tests ko dekhne ka standard tareeqa yeh hai ki woh doosri jagah seekhi gayi jankari ka moolyankan (evaluate) karne ke liye kaam karte hain—reading ya lectures sunne ke zariye. Retrieval ka concept is view ko iske head par palat deta hai, yeh suggest karte hui ki ek test lene ka act na keval learning ka ek srot hai balki iske nateejatan review mein spend kiye gaye same samay ke mukable mazeed learning hoti hai. Halanki, yeh abhi bhi knowledge ke pehle haasil kiye jaane, aur phir baad mein strengthened ya tested hone ke paramparagat idea (conventional idea) ke andar fit baithta hai.

Retrieval research se ek interesting moolyankan, jise **forward-testing effect** ke roop mein jaana jata hai, dikhata hai ki retrieval na keval usme badhottari (enhance) karne mein madad karta hai jo aapne pehle seekha hai balki aapko mazeed behtar seekhne ke liye prepare karne mein bhi madad kar sakta hai. Pehle se studied jankari ka niyamit testing nayi jankari seekhna aasan bana sakta hai. Iska matlab hai ki retrieval future learning ko badhane ke liye kaam karti hai, bhale hi abhi retrieve karne ke liye kuch na ho!

Is forward testing effect ke exist hone ko explain karne ke liye tarah-tarah ki mechanisms prastavit ki gayi hain. Kuch researchers tark karte hain ki yeh ho sakta hai ki us knowledge ko dhoondhne ki koshish karna jise abhi seekha nahi gaya hai—maan lijiye, ek aise problem ko solve karne ki koshish karke jiska answer aapne abhi tak nahi seekha hai—phir bhi un search strategies ko reinforce karne mein madad karta hai jinhein baad mein knowledge ka samna hone par use mein laya jata hai. Yahan ek upma (analogy) yeh hai ki ek aise answer ko retrieve karne ki koshish karna jo abhi aapke mind mein exist nahi karta hai, ek aisi road lay down karne jaisa hai jo ek aisi building ki taraf le jaati hai jo abhi construct nahi hui hai. Destination exist nahi karta, lekin jahan yeh hoga wahan tak pahunche ka raasta, ek baar construct hone par, phir bhi develop ho jata hai. Doosre researchers tark karte hain ki mechanism attention (dhayan) ka ho sakta hai. Ek aisi problem ka samna karke jiska answer aap abhi tak nahi jaante hain, aapka mind automatically apne attentional resources ko un jankariyon ko spot karne ke liye adjust karta hai jo baad mein seekhne par ek solution jaisi dikhti hain. Jo bhi exact mechanism ho, forward-testing effect ki reality implies karti hai ki retrieval ka abhyas karne se na keval aapke “ready” hone se pehle shuru karne se benefit ho sakta hai balki isse pehle bhi jab aapke paas correctly answer dene ki possibility ho.

## What Should Be Retrieved?

_(Kya Yaad Kiya Jana Chahiye?)_

Research saaf hai: agar aapko baad mein kisi cheez ko yaad karne ki zarurat hai, toh aap iska retrieval abhyas karne mein mazeed behtar hain. Halanki, yeh ek important question ko nazarandaz karta hai: Pehli jagah yaad rakhne ke liye aapko kis tarah ki cheezein mein samay invest karna chahiye? Same learning impact paane ke liye retrieval review ke mukable kam samay le sakti hai, lekin kisi cheez ko bilkul na seekhna isse bhi zyaada tez hai. Yeh ek important practical question hai. Kisi ke paas har cheez par maharat haasil karne ka samay nahi hota.

MIT Challenge ke dauran, maine bahut saare different ideas ko cover kiya. Kuch directly us tarah ki programming se relevant the jise main khatam karne par karna chahta था, isliye yeh sure karna meri priority thi ki main un ideas ko retain karoon. Doosre interesting the, lekin chunki mere paas unhein immediately use karne ka koi plan nahi tha, maine technical calculations karne ke bajaye underlying concepts ka retrieval abhyas karne mein mazeed effort lagayi. Ek class jo maine ki thi, for instance, woh _Modal Logic_ thi. Chunki mera logician (tarkshastri) banne ka koi plan nahi hai, main honestly keh sakta hoon, aath saal baad, ki main aaj modal logic mein theorems prove nahi kar sakta. Halanki, main aapko bata sakta hoon ki modal logic kis liye hai aur yeh kab use hoti hai, isliye agar koi aisi situation paida hoti hai jisme us class mein seekhi gayi techniques useful ho sakti hain, toh mujhe ise spot karne mein ek bahut behtar samay milega. Hamesha kuch aisi cheezein hongi jinhein aap master karna chunte hain aur doosri jinhein aap yeh jaan kar apne aap ko santusht karte hain ki agar aapko zarurat ho toh aap unhein dekh sakte hain.

Is sawaal ka javab dene ka ek tarika simply direct practice karna hai. Directness is sawaal se bach nikalti (sidestep) hai aapko un cheezon ko retrieve karne par majboor karke jo skill ka use karne ke dauran aksar saamne aati hain. Agar aap ek bhasha seekh rahe hain aur aapko ek word yaad karne ki zarurat hai, aap iski practice karenge. Agar aapko kabhi kisi word ki zarurat nahi hogi, aap use memorize nahi karenge. Is strategy ka advantage yeh hai ki yeh automatically aapko sabse highest frequency (uchh-avriti) wali cheezon ko seekhne ki taraf le jaati hai. Jo cheezein rarely use hoti hain ya jinhein memorize karne ke bajaye dhoondhna (look up) aasan hota hai unhein retrieve nahi kiya jayega. Yeh wahi cheezein hoti hain jo bahut zyaada matter nahi kartin.

Direct practice par exclusively nirbhar rehne ke sath problem yeh hai ki jo knowledge aapke head mein nahi hai use problems solve karne mein madad ke liye use nahi kiya ja sakta. For instance, ek programmer ek problem ko solve karne ke liye kisi khhas function ka use karne ki zarurat ko realize kar sakti hai lekin bhool jaati hai ki ise code mein kaise likha jaye. Syntax ko look up karne ki zarurat shayad use slow kar sakti hai, lekin woh phir bhi problem ko solve karne kabil hogi. Halanki, agar aapke paas yeh recognize karne ke liye kaafi knowledge stored nahi hai ki aap apni problem ko solve karne ke liye kab kisi function ka use kar sakte hain, toh koi bhi look up karna aapki madad nahi kar sakta.

Vichar karein ki pichle bees saalon mein, ek quick online search se aasaani se accessible knowledge ki matra explode (tezi se badh) hui hai. Lagbhag koi bhi fact ya concept ab smartphone wale kisi bhi insaan ko demand par available hai. Phir bhi is incredible advance ke bavajood, aisa nahi hai ki ek average insaan ek generation pehle ke logon ke mukable hazaron guna zyaada smart hai. Cheezon ko look up karne kabil hona nishchit roop se ek advantage hai, lekin aapke head ke andar ek nirdharit matra mein knowledge (certain amount of knowledge) ke bina, yeh aapko hard problems solve karne mein madad nahi karta.

Akeli direct practice aisi jankariyon ko chhod kar (omitting) jo aapko ek problem solve karne mein madad kar sakti hain lekin aisa karne ke liye strictly zaroori nahi hain, kafi retrieval ko encourage karne mein fail ho sakti hai. Hamari us programmer par vichar karein jiske paas apni problem ko solve karne ke do different tareeqe hain, A aur B. Option A kahin zyaada effective hai, lekin B se bhi kaam chal jayega (get the job done). Ab suppose karein ki woh kevel option B ke baare mein jaanti hai. Woh problem ko solve karne ke liye usi tareeqe ka use karna jaari rakhegi jise woh jaanti hai, bhale hi yeh kam effective ho. Yahan, hamari nau-sikhia programmer (fledgling programmer) kahin kisi blog par option A ke baare mein padh sakti hai. Lekin chunki simply reading repeated retrieval practice ke mukable kahin kam effective hai, chances hain ki woh iske baare mein bhool jayegi jab technique ko apply karne ka samay aayega.

Yeh abstract sunne mein lag sakta hai, lekin main tark karunga ki yeh programmers ke sath kaafi samanya hai, aur aksar ausat darje ke programmers (mediocre programmers) ko bade programmers se alag karne wali cheez unke dwara solve kiye ja sakne wale problems ki range nahi hoti balki yeh hoti hai ki baad wale aksar problems ko solve karne ke daso tareeqe jaante hain aur har situation ke liye sabse behtar chun sakte hain. Is tarah ki choudai (breadth) ke liye ek nirdharit matra mein passive exposure ki zarurat hoti hai, jo badle mein retrieval practice se benefit leta hai.

## How to Practice Retrieval

_(Retrieval Ka Abhyas Kaise Karein)_

Retrieval kaam karti hai, lekin yeh hamesha aasan nahi hoti. Na keval effort khud ek obstacle hai, balki kabhi-kabhi yeh saaf nahi hota ki ise exactly kaise kiya jaye. Passive review bhale hi bahut zyaada efficient na ho, lekin kam se kam yeh straightforward (seedha) hai: aap apni kitab kholte hain aur material ko tab tak dobara padhte hain jab tak ki aap ise retain nahi kar lete. Zyaada tar books aur resources ke ant mein sawaalon ki ek handy list nahi hoti jo aapka test le sake yeh dekhne ke liye ki kya aapko yaad hai ki unmein kya shamil hai. Usme madad karne ke liye, neeche kuch useful methods diye gaye hain jinhein lagbhag kisi bhi subject par retrieval apply karne ke liye use kiya ja sakta hai.

### Tactic 1: Flash Cards

_(Ranniti 1: Flash Cards)_
Flash cards sawaalon aur answers ke beech jude sangathon (paired associations) ko seekhne ka ek hairatangez roop se simple, phir bhi effective tareeqa hain. Dil se khud par test lene ke liye paper flash cards create karne ka purana tareeqa powerful hai, lekin ise largely spaced-repetition systems dwara superseded (badla) kar diya gaya hai, jaisa ki main Niyam 7 mein discuss karunga. Yeh software algorithms daso hazar “cards” ko handle kar sakte hain aur ek review schedule bhi organize kar sakte hain taaki aap unhein manage kar sakein.

Flash cards ka mukhya drawback (kamzori) yeh hai ki woh ek vishisht tarah ke retrieval ke liye sach mein achha kaam karte hain—jab ek vishisht cue aur ek khhas response ke beech ek pairing (joda) ho. Knowledge ke kuch forms ke liye, for example foreign-language vocabulary ko memorize karna, yeh perfectly kaam karta hai. Similarly, maps, anatomical diagrams, definitions, aur equations ko aksar flash cards ke zariye memorize kiya ja sakta hai. Halanki, jab woh situation jisme aapko jankari yaad rakhne ki zarurat hai highly variable (badalne wali) hoti hai, toh is tarah ke abhyas ke drawbacks ho sakte hain. Programmers flash cards ke zariye syntax memorize kar sakte hain, lekin jin concepts ko real programs mein apply karne ki zarurat hoti hai woh aksar us cue-response framework mein fit nahi baithte jinqi flash cards demand karte hain.

### Tactic 2: Free Recall

_(Ranniti 2: Free Recall)_
Retrieval apply karne ke liye ek simple tactic hai, kisi kitab se ek section padhne ya ek lecture ke dauran baithne ke baad, ek khaali piece of paper par sab kuch likhne ki koshish karna jise aap yaad rakh sakte hain. Is tarah ka free recall aksar bahut difficult hota hai, aur aisi kai cheezein hongi jo miss ho jayengi, bhale hi aapne sawaal ke ghere mein majood text ko abhi padhna khatam kiya ho. Halanki, yeh difficulty bhi ek achha kaaran hai ki yeh abhyas kyun sahayak hai. Apne aap ko mukhya points aur arguments ko yaad karne par majboor karke, aap unhein baad mein mazeed behtar yaad rakhne kabil honge.

Is book ke liye research karne ke dauran, for instance, main aksar journal articles ka print out leta tha aur unmein se har ek ke baad unhein kuch khaali sheets of paper ke sath ek binder mein rakh deta تھا. Padhna khatam karne ke baad, main ek quick free recall exercise karta tha taaki yeh sure kar sakoon ki jab likhne ka samay aaye toh main important details ko retain kar sakoon.

### Tactic 3: The Question-Book Method

_(Ranniti 3: Question-Book Method)_
Zyaada tar students mukhya points ko copy karke notes lete hain jaise hi woh unse takrate hain. Halanki, notes lene ki ek aur strategy yeh hai ki aapne jo record kiya hai use baad mein javab diye jaane wale sawaalon ke roop mein rephrase (phir se bayan) karein. Yeh likhne ke bajaye ki Magna Carta par 1215 mein sign kiye gaye the, aap iske bajaye sawaal likh sakte hain “Magna Carta par kab sign kiye gaye the?” is sandarbh (reference) ke sath ki agar aap bhool jayein toh answer kahan dhoondhna hai. Answers ke bajaye sawaalon ke roop mein notes lekar, aap baad mein retrieval ka abhyas karne ke liye material generate karte hain.

Is technique ko apply karne mein maine jo ek galti ki hai woh sawaal poochne ke liye galat tarah ki cheezon par focus karna hai. Maine is method ko computational neuroscience par ek kitab par apply karne ki koshish ki, aur maine aakhirkar apne aap se tarah-tarah ke detailed sawaal pooch liye jaise khhas neuronal circuits ki firing rate kya thi ya kisne ek vishisht theory prastavit ki thi. Yeh intentional nahi tha balki kitab mein majood factual content ko laas-parwahi se sawaalon ke roop mein restate karne ka ek by-product tha. Jo harder aur mazeed useful hai woh ek chapter ya section ke bade idea (big idea) ko ek sawaal ke roop mein restate karna hai. Chunki yeh aksar implicit (antarnihit) hota hai, iske liye kuch gehre thinking ki zarurat hoti hai na ki sirf aapke dwara verbatim (shabdshah) copy kiye gaye notes mein ek question mark add karne ki. Ek rule jo maine iske liye sahayak paaya hai woh hai apne aap ko text ke per section ek sawaal tak limited rakhna, is tarah apne aap ko mukhya point ko acknowledge aur rephrase karne par majboor karna bajaye ek aise detail par zoom in karne ke jo baad mein largely irrelevant hoga.

### Tactic 4: Self-Generated Challenges

_(Ranniti 4: Self-Generated Challenges)_
Upar di gayi tactics simple jankariyon ke retrieval ke sath sabse behtar kaam karti hain, jaise facts ya broad ideas ke summaries jisse aap kisi kitab ya lecture mein takra sakte hain. Halanki, agar aap ek skill ki practice karne ki koshish kar rahe hain, na ki merely jankari yaad rakhne ki, toh ho sakta hai ki woh kaafi na hon. Ek programmer ke liye, yeh jaana kafi nahi hai ki ek algorithm ka matlab kya hai, balki use code mein likhne kabil hona chahiye. Is case mein, jaise hi aap apne passive material se guzarre hain, aap baad mein solve karne ke liye apne liye challenges create can sakte hain. Aap ek nayi technique se takra sakte hain aur phir ek actual example mein us technique ko demonstrate karne ke liye ek note nahi likh sakte. Aise challenges ki ek list create karna baad mein vyavahar (practice) mein us jankari par maharat haasil karne ke liye ek prompt ke roop mein kaam kar sakta hai aur un tools ki aapki library ko expand kar sakta hai jinhein aap actually apply karne kabil hain.

### Tactic 5: Closed-Book Learning

_(Ranniti 5: Closed-Book Learning)_
Lagbhag koi bhi learning activity retrieval ka ek opportunity ban sakti hai agar aap hints khojne ki ability ko cut off kar dete hain. Concept mapping, woh strategy jisne Karpicke aur Blunt ke experiments mein students ke liye khhasakar achha kaam nahi kiya, use apna concept map generate karte waqt kitab dekhne se khud ko rok kar kaafi behtar (beefed up) banaya ja sakta hai. Mujhe shak hai ki agar yeh original experiment mein kiya gaya hota, toh closed-book concept mapping ke is roop ka upyog karne wale students ne aakhirkar us test par nishchit roop se behtar kiya hota jo ek concept map create karne par nirbhar tha. Kisi bhi practice ko, chahe direct ho ya ek drill, cheezon ko look up karne ki ability se cut off kiya ja sakta hai. Apne aap ko srot (source) se consult karne se rok kar, jankari ek reference manual ke andar hone ke bajaye aapke head ke andar stored knowledge ban jaati hai.

## Revisiting Ramanujan

_(Ramanujan Par Phir Se Vichar)_

Ramanujan smart the, isme koi deny nahi kar sakta. Halanki, unke genius ko ultralearner ke tool kit ke do mukhya nishaniyon dwara asimit roop se madad mili thi: obsessive intensity aur retrieval practice. Jaise hi unhone subah se raat tak apni slate par kaam kiya, Carr ke theorems ki thode se likhi gayi list ko figure out karne ki koshish karna incredibly hard work tha. Lekin isne un desirable difficulties ko bhi create kiya jinhone unhein tools aur tricks ki ek badi dimaagi library build karne ki izazat di jo unke baad ke mathematical prayason mein unki madad karegi.

Retrieval ne Ramanujan ke mathematical parvarish mein ek important role nibhaya, lekin woh is tactic ka fayda uthane wale akele shakhs shayad hi hain. Mere samna aaye bade geniuses aur contemporary ultralearners ki lagbhag har ek biography mein, retrieval practice ke kisi form ka zikr kiya jata hai. Benjamin Franklin ne memory se essays ko dobara construct karke apni writing ki practice ki. Mary Somerville ne dimaag mein hi problems par kaam kiya jab raat mein padhne ke liye koi candle available nahi thi. Roger Craig ne answers dekhe bina trivia questions ka abhyas kiya. Retrieval genius create karne ke liye ek sufficient tool nahi hai, lekin yeh ek necessary tool ho sakti hai.

Sahi answer produce karne ki koshish karna bajaye merely use review karne ke, halanki, ek bade cycle ka sirf aadha hissa hai. Retrieval ko sach mein effective banane liye, yeh jaan'ne mein madad milti hai ki kya aapne apne mind se jo answer nikala (dredged up) tha woh sahi tha ya nahi. Theek jaise hum aksar ready hone tak khud par test lene se bachte hain kyunki ek test ke sath struggle karna uncomfortable hota hai, hum aksar apne skill level ke baare mein jankari maangne se tab tak bachte hain jab tak hamein lagta hai ki yeh favorable (pakshein) hogi. Us jankari ko effectively process karne kabil hona, isme majood message ko loud aur clear sunna, hamesha aasan nahi hota. Phir bhi yahi wajah hai ki yeh itna important hai. Yeh hamein ultralearning ke agle niyan tak le jata hai: **feedback (pratikriya)**.

---

# Chapter 9 — Principle 6: Feedback

### _(Niyam 6 — Feedback: Punches Se Mat Bacho)_

---

> _"Everybody has a plan until they get punched in the mouth."_
> _(Har kisi ke paas ek plan hota hai jab tak ki unke muh par ek mukka [punched] na pade.)_
> — Mike Tyson

---

Peeche ki ek tang (narrow) staircase se, Chris Rock stage par entry karte hain theek usi samay jab unka naam announce kiya ja raha hota hai. Sold-out shows aur HBO specials ke sath, Rock stand-up comedy ke duniya mein koi nau-sikhia (neophyte) nahi hain. Unki performances ek rock concert jaisi feel hoti hain. Ek energetic aur punctuated (vram-chinhon ke sath ruki hui) delivery ke sath, woh kisi joke ke mukhya phrase (key phrase) ko kisi song ke chorus ki tarah repeat karne ke liye jaane jaate hain, iska rhythm itna sateek (precise) hota hai ki aapko ehsaas hota hai jaise woh kisi bhi cheez ko funny banane kabil hain. Aur exactly yahi problem hai. Jab aap jo kuch bhi karte hain woh funny hota hai, toh aap kaise jaante hain ki actually kaun si cheez kisi joke ko achha banati hai?

Bhare hue concert halls aur khush (jubilant) bheed se door, Rock Greenwich Village, New York City mein _Comedy Cellar_ ke ek mamuli brick-backed stage par mic ki taraf chalte hain. Unke haath mein cards ke tukde (scraps) hain jinpar unhone phrases ke kuch hisse scratch down (scribbled) kiye hain, naye material par kaam karne ki ek aisi chaal jise unhone apne grandfather se seekha tha, jo ek cab driver the aur weekends par bhashan (preached) dete the. Apne signature aggressive style ke bajaye, woh peeche ki wall ke sahare slump (dheele hokar teka lena) ho jaate hain. Yeh unki laboratory hai, aur woh ek prayog ki sateekta (precision of an experiment) ke sath comedy perform karne ja rahe hain.

“Yeh utna achha nahi hone wala hai,” Rock bhoot-bhoot (warn) karte hain bheed ko, jo chote comedy stage par unki bina kisi announcement ke aane par hakke-bakke (stunned) hain. “In keematon par toh bilkul nahi,” woh add karte hain, mazaak karte hue “In keematon par, main abhi yahan se nikal sakta hoon!” Woh reviews ki kalpana (envisions) karte hain: “Chris baahar aaye aur woh chale gaye. Yeh achha tha! Unhone koi jokes nahi sunaye—lekin yeh achha tha!” Notes haath mein liye, Rock audience ko playfully warn karte hain ki yeh ek typical Chris Rock performance nahi hone wali hai. Iske bajaye, woh controlled conditions ke tehat naye material par kaam karna chahte hain. “Woh aapko aapke famous hone ke kaaran lagbhag chheh minutes denge,” woh explain karte hain. “. . . phir aap wapas shuruat par (square one) aa jaate hain.” Woh jaan'na chahte hain ki kya funny hai, jab woh funny banne ki koshish nahi kar rahe hote.

Rock ka method unique nahi hai. Comedy Cellar bade-naam wale drop-ins (bina bataye aane walon) ke liye famous hai: Dave Chappelle, Jon Stewart, aur Amy Schumer kuch aise hi comedians hain jinhone prime-time specials aur concert-scale ke bade muqablon (gigs) mein perform karne se pehle yahan choti bheed ke samne apne material ko test kiya tha. Kisi chote club mein perform kyun karna jab aap ek badi performance se aasaani se badi bheed aur hazaron dollars attract kar sakte hain? Kyun bina kisi announcement ke aana aur phir deliberately apni hi comedic abilities ko ausat se kam dikhana (undersell)? Jis cheez ko Rock aur in doosre famous comedians ne recognize kiya hai woh ultralearning ke chhathe niyan ka mahatva hai: **feedback**.

## The Power of Information

_(Jankari Ki Taqat)_

Feedback un sabse consistent (lagaatar bane rehne wale) aspects mein se ek hai jise ultralearners apni strategy mein use karte hain. Roger Craig dwara answer jaane bina Jeopardy! clues par khud par test lene ke simple feedback se lekar, Benny Lewis ke us naye bhasha ko bolne ke liye strangers tak pahunche ke uncomfortable feedback tak jise unhone gujre kal hi seekhna shuru kiya tha, feedback haasil karna mere samna aaye ultralearners ke sabse common tactics mein se ek tha. Jo cheez aksar ultralearning strategy ko mazeed conventional approaches se alag karti thi woh pradan kiye ja rahe feedback ki tatkalikta (immediacy), accuracy, aur tivrata (intensity) thi. Tristan de Montebello apne script ko saavdhani se prepare karne aur phir har ek-do mahine mein ek bhashan deliver karne ka normal raasta le sakte the, jaisa zyaada tar Toastmasters ke sath hota hai. Iske bajaye unhone seedhe dive kiya, per week kai baar bolte hue, apni performance par different perspectives ikhatha karne liye different clubs ke beech jump karte hue. Feedback mein is gehri dive karne uncomfortable thi, lekin is rapid immersion ne unhein us anxiety (chinta) ke prati bhi nish-chet (desensitized) kar diya jo onstage hone par paada ho sakti hai.

Feedback deliberate practice par research mein mukhya roop se feature karta hai, jo K. Anders Ericsson aur doosre psychologists dwara shuru ki gayi expertise (nipunata) haasil karne ki ek scientific theory hai. Apne studies mein, Ericsson ne paaya hai ki apni performance par immediate feedback haasil karne ki ability expert levels tak pahunchna mein ek essential ingredient (mukhya tatva) hai. No feedback, aur result aksar stagnation (sthirta) hota hai—samay ka ek lamba period jab aap kisi skill ka use karna jaari rakhte hain lekin isme bilkul behtar nahi hote. Kabhi-kabhi feedback ki kami ke nateejatan ghatt-ti hui abilities (declining abilities) bhi ho sakti hain. Kai medical practitioners mazeed experience ke sath badtar (worse) hote jaate hain kyunki medical school se unki ikhatha ki gayi knowledge fade (dhundhli) hone lagti hai aur unke diagnoses ki accuracy par woh rapid feedback nahi milta jo aam taur par future learning ko badhava (promote) deta hai.

## Can Feedback Backfire?

_(Kya Feedback Ulta Asar Kar Sakta Hai?)_

Feedback ka mahatva probably bahut zyaada hairan karne wala nahi hai; hum sab sahaj roop se (intuitively) sense karte hain ki hum jo sahi aur galat kar rahe hain uske baare mein jankari haasil karna learning ko kaise tez (accelerate) kar sakta hai. Mazeed interestingly, feedback par research dikhati hai ki mazeed hamesha behtar nahi hota. Crucially (Mukhya roop se), jo matter karta hai woh pradan kiye ja rahe feedback ka type hai.

Ek bade meta-analysis mein, Avraham Kluger aur Angelo DeNisi ne learning ke liye feedback pradan karne ke impact par saikdon studies ko dekha. Bhale hi feedback ka overall effect positive tha, yeh note karna important hai ki **38 percent se zyaada cases mein, feedback ka actually ek negative impact pada.**

Yeh ek confusing situation ki taraf le jata hai. Ek taraf, expert attainment (nipunata haasil karne) ke liye feedback essential hai, jaisa deliberate practice ke scientific studies dwara pradarshit kiya gaya hai. Feedback ultralearning projects mein bhi mukhya roop se feature karta hai, aur unke successful hone ki kalpana karna difficult hai agar unke feedback ke sources ko turned off kar diya gaya hota. Same samay par, evidences ka moolyankan feedback ke sarvabhumik roop se (universally) positive hone ki picture paint nahi karta. Explanation kya hai?

Kluger aur begging DeNisi tark karte hain ki badlav (discrepancy) pradan kiye jaane wale feedback ke type mein hai. Feedback tab achha kaam karta hai jab yeh useful jankari provide karta hai jo future learning ko guide kar sake. Agar feedback aapko batata hai ki aap kya galat kar rahe hain ya ise kaise fix karna hai, toh yeh ek prabhavshali tool (potent tool) ho sakta hai. Lekin feedback aksar backfire (ulta asar) karta hai jab yeh kisi insaan ke aham/ego (ego) par aimed hota hai. Praise (tareef), ek common type ka feedback jise teachers aksar use karte hain (aur students enjoy karte hain), aam taur par future learning ke liye nuksaandayak (harmful) hota hai. Jab feedback ek individual ke roop mein aapke moolyankan (evaluations) mein steer (mud-ta) karta hai (e.g., “Aap bahut smart hain!” ya “Aap lazy hain”), toh iska aam taur par learning par ek negative impact padta hai.

Mazeed, useful jankari shamil karne wale feedback ko bhi learning ke liye ek motivator aur tool ke roop mein correctly process karne ki zarurat hoti hai. Researchers ne note kiya ki feedback ka negative impact dikhane wali kuch studies isliye huin kyunki subjects ne khud feedback ka constructively (rachnatmak roop se) upyog na karne ka chunaav kiya. Unhone shayad feedback ko reject kar diya, un standards ko kam kar diya jinqi woh apne aap se umeed karte hain, ya learning task ko poori tarah se chhod (given up) diya. Researchers note karte hain ki feedback kaun de raha hai yeh matter kar sakta hai, kyunki ek peer (saathi) ya teacher se aane wale feedback ke paas mere apni abilities ko behtar banane ki jankari se pare important social dynamics hote hain.

Mujhe is research ke baare mein do cheezein interesting lagti hain.

- **Pehle, yeh saaf hai ki bhale hi informative feedback beneficial hai, yeh backfire kar sakta hai** agar ise inappropriately process kiya jaye ya agar yeh useful jankari provide karne mein fail ho jaye. Iska matlab hai ki jab feedback dhoondh rahe hon, toh ultralearner ko do possibilities ke liye saavdhaan (on guard) rehne ki zarurat hai. Pehli yeh hai ki us feedback (dono positive aur negative) par overreact karna jo koi vishisht jankari (specific information) offer nahi karta jo improvement ki taraf le jaye. Ultralearners ko is baare mein sensitive hone ki zarurat hai ki kaun sa feedback actually useful hai aur baki sab ko tune out (ignore) kar dena chahiye. Yahi wajah hai ki, bhale hi mere samna aaye saare ultralearners ne feedback ka upyog kiya, unhone har ek possible feedback ke piece par action nahi liya. Eric Barone ne, for instance, apne game ke early drafts par har ek comment aur critique par dhayan nahi diya. Kai cases mein unhone unhein ignore kar diya, jab feedback unke vision ke sath conflict (takraav) mein tha.
- **Doosre, jab ise galat tareeqe se apply kiya jata hai, toh feedback ka motivation par ek negative impact pad sakta hai.** Na keval bahut zyaada negative feedback aapki motivation ko kam kar sakta hai, balki bahut zyaada positive feedback bhi aisa kar sakta hai. Ultralearners ko dono chintao ko balance karna chahiye, learning ke apne majooda stage ke liye feedback ke sahi level par push karte hue. Bhale hi hum sab karrwi aur gair-sahayak aalochna (harsh and unhelpful criticism) ko jaante hain (aur sahaj roop se isse bachte hain), research Rock ki us positive feedback ko nazarandaz (disregarding) karne ki strategy ka bhi samarthan karti hai jise unka celebrity status automatically generate karta hai.

Is research ke baare mein doosra interesting point yeh hai ki yeh explain karta hai ki feedback-seeking prayas (feedback-seeking efforts) aksar kam use kyun kiye jaate hain aur is tarah ultralearners ke liye tulnatmak advantage (comparative advantage) ka ek prabhavshali srot bane rehte hain. Feedback uncomfortable hota hai. Yeh karrwa (harsh) aur nirashajanak (discouraging) ho sakta hai, aur yeh hamesha achha feel nahi karwata. Jokes deliver karne ke liye kisi comedy club mein stage par khade hona stand-up comedy mein behtar banne ke sabse behtar tareeqon mein se ek hai. Lekin yeh act khud dravna (terrifying) ho sakta hai, kyunki ek awkward silence gehra kaat-ti (cuts deep) hai. Similarly, kisi nayi bhasha mein immediately bolna painful ho sakta hai, kyunki communicate karne ki aapki ability ka ehsaas us samay se tezi se neeche girta (goes down precipitously) hai jab aap apni native tongue (matribhasha) ka use karte hain.

Feedback ka darr aksar feedback ka khud experience karne ke mukable mazeed uncomfortable feel hota hai. Nateejatan, yeh apne aap mein utna negative feedback nahi hai jo progress ko badhit (impede) kar sakta hai balki aalochna (criticism) sunne ka darr hai jo hamein band (shut down) karne ka kaaran banta hai. Kabhi-kabhi sabse behtar action bas sabse hardest environment mein directly dive kar jana hai, kyunki bhale hi feedback shuruat mein bahut zyaada negative ho, yeh aapke project ko get started karne ke darr ko kam kar sakta hai aur agar yeh sahayak hone ke liye bahut zyaada karrwa sabit ho toh aapko baad mein adjust karne ki izazat de sakta hai.

In saare acts ke liye aatmavishwas, dradhta (resolve), aur persistence ki zarurat hoti hai, yahi wajah hai ki kai self-directed learning prayas us aakramak feedback (aggressive feedback) ko dhoondhne ko ignore karte hain jo mazeed tezi se results generate kar sakta hai. Srot (source) par jaane, directly feedback lene, aur tezi se seekhne ke liye us jankari ka use karne ke bajaye, log aksar punches se bachne (dodge the punches) aur learning ke ek potentially vishal srot se bachne ka chunaav karte hain. Ultralearners skills jaldi acquire karte hain kyunki woh aggressive feedback dhoondhte hain jab doosre aishi practice ka vikalp chunte hain jisme kamzor tarah ka feedback shamil ho ya bilkul feedback na ho.

## What Kind of Feedback Do You Need?

_(Aapko Kis Tarah Ke Feedback Ki Zarurat Hai?)_

Feedback learning projects ke different types ke liye kai different forms mein dikhta hai. Stand-up comedy mein behtar hona aur computer programs likhna seekhna feedback ke bahut zyaada different types ko shamil karte hain. Higher math seekhna aur bhashayein seekhna feedback ka different tareeqon se use karne wale hain. Behtar feedback dhoondhne ke opportunities is par depend karte hue badlenge (vary) ki aap kya seekhne ki koshish kar rahe hain.

Aapke learning project ke liye aapko exactly kis feedback ki zarurat hai ise bayan karne ke bajaye, mujhe lagta hai ki feedback ke different types par vichar karna important hai, sath hi is baat par bhi ki har ek ka use aur vikas (cultivated) kaise kiya ja sakta hai. Yeh jaan kar ki aap kis tarah ka feedback haasil kar rahe hain, aap sure kar sakte hain ki iska sabse behtar upyog karein, sath hi iski simaon (limitations) ko bhi recognize karein. In particular, main feedback ke teen types par vichar karna chahta hoon: **outcome feedback, informational feedback, aur corrective feedback.**

### Outcome Feedback: Are You Doing It Wrong?

_(Outcome Feedback: Kya Aap Ise Galat Kar Rhe Hain?)_
Feedback ka pehla type, aur sabse kam granular (mota-mota), outcome (parinaam) feedback hai. Yeh aapko is baare mein kuch batata hai ki aap overall kitna achha kar rahe hain lekin is baare mein koi ideas offer nahi karta ki aap kya behtar ya badtar kar rahe hain. Is tarah ka feedback ek grade ke roop mein aa sakta hai—pass/fail, A, B, or C—ya yeh aapke dwara same samay par liye ja rahe kai decisions ke ek kul feedback (aggregate feedback) ke roop mein aa sakta hai.

Tristan de Montebello ko ek speech ke baad mila applause (ya unhone jo sannaata [crickets] suna) outcome feedback ka ek example hai. Yeh unhein bata sakta tha ki woh behtar ho rahe hain ya badtar, lekin yeh sach mein nahi bata sakta tha ki kyun ya ise kaise fix karna hai. Har ek entrepreneur is tarah ke feedback ka experience karta hai jab ek naya product market mein hit karta hai. Yeh hairatangez roop se achha bik sakta hai ya behad kharab, lekin woh feedback bulk (ek dher) mein aata hai, jise directly product ke various aspects mein toda (decomposable) nahi ja sakta. Kya product ki cost bahut zyaada thi? Kya marketing message saaf nahi تھا? Kya packaging unappealing (na-pasand) thi? Customer reviews aur comments clues provide kar sakte hain, lekin ultimately kisi bhi naye product ki success ya failure factors ka ek complex bundle hoti hai.

Is type ka feedback haasil karna aksar sabse aasan hota hai, aur research dikhati hai ki bhale hi is feedback ko haasil karna, jisme aapko kya behtar banana hai is baare mein ek vishisht message (specific message) ki kami hoti hai, sahayak ho sakta hai. Ek study mein, visual acuity (drishti-teezta) shamil karne wale ek task ke liye feedback ne learning ko kabil (facilitated) banaya, bhale hi ise un blocks mein deliver kiya gaya tha jo is baare mein koi arthpurna jankari haasil karne ke liye bahut zyaada bade the ki kaun se responses sahi the aur kaun se galat.

Kai projects jinmein poori tarah se feedback ki kami hoti hai, unhein is bade paimane ke feedback (broad-scale feedback) ko haasil karne ke liye aasaani se badla ja sakta hai. Eric Barone ne, for instance, apne game par kaam publish karne aur early drafts se feedback maangne (solicit) ke liye ek development blog provide kiya. Yeh unhein is baare mein detailed jankari provide nahi kar sakta tha ki exactly kya behtar banana hai aur badalna hai, lekin unka simply ek aise environment mein immersed hona jo feedback provide karta tha, sahayak tha.

Outcome feedback kuch different mechanisms ke zariye aap kaise seekhte hain ise behtar bana sakta hai.

- Ek aapke goal ke khilaf ek motivational benchmark provide karke hai. Agar aapka goal feedback ki ek khhas quality tak pahunchna hai, toh yeh feedback aapko aapki progress par updates de sakta hai.
- Doosra yeh hai ki yeh aapko aapke dwara try kiye ja rahe different methods ke gun-dosh (relative merits) dikha sakta hai. Jab aap rapidly progress kar rahe hote hain, toh aap un learning methods aur approaches se chipak sakte hain. Jab progress stall (ruk) jaati hai, toh aap dekh sakte hain ki aap apne majooda approach mein kya badal sakte hain.

Bhale hi outcome feedback complete nahi hota, yeh aksar available akela type hota hai aur tab bhi aapki learning rate par ek potent impact daal sakta hai.

### Informational Feedback: What Are You Doing Wrong?

_(Informational Feedback: Aap Kya Galat Kar Rhe Hain?)_
Agla type informational feedback hai. Yeh feedback aapko batata hai ki aap kya galat kar rahe hain, lekin yeh zaroori nahi ki aapko bataye ki ise fix kaise karna hai. Kisi native speaker ke sath ek foreign bhasha bolna jo aapke sath bhasha share nahi karta, informational feedback mein ek exercise hai. Kisi word ka galat use karne par us insaan ki confused stare (ghoorthi hui nazar) aapko yeh nahi batayegi ki sahi word kaun sa hai, lekin yeh aapko batayegi ki aap ise galat kar rahe hain.
