Examples: “Main beginners ke liye Python programming par ek kitab padhne aur uski exercises ko complete karne ja raha hoon” ya “Main italki.com ke zariye online tutoring se Spanish seekhne ja raha hoon” ya “Main sketches banakar drawing ki practice karne ja raha hoon.” Kuch subjects mein, sthir materials (static materials) nirdharit karenge ki aap kaise aage badhenge. Doosron mein, woh aapki practice ko back up karne ke liye sahayak honge. Kisi bhi case mein, aapke shuru karne se pehle unhein identify, kharida, udhaar liya, ya unmein enroll kiya jana chahiye.
3. **Ek manak (benchmark) ki doosron ne is skill ya subject ko successfully kaise seekha hai.** Lagbhag kisi bhi popular skill ke paas online forums hote hain jahan jinhone pehle us skill ko seekha hai woh apne approaches share kar sakte hain. Aapko un cheezon ko identify karna chahiye jinhein us skill ko seekhne wale doosre logon ne ise seekhne ke liye kiya hai. Iska matlab yeh nahi hai ki aapko exactly unke kadamon par chalne ki zarurat hai, lekin yeh aapko kisi important cheez ko poori tarah se miss karne se rokega. Chapter 4 mein majood Expert Interview Method ispar follow up karne ke liye ek achha method provide karta hai.
4. **Direct practice gatividhiyan (direct practice activities).** Aap jo bhi skill aur subject seekh rahe hain, aakhirkar iska use kahin na kahin kiya jayega, bhale hi yeh kisi doosri cheez ko seekhne ke liye iska use karne jitna simple ho. Is baare mein sochna ki aap skill ka use kaise kar sakte hain, aapko jitna jaldi possible ho iska abhyas karne ke opportunities dhoondhna shuru karne kabil bana sakta hai. Agar direct practice impossible hai, toh aapko nevertheless practice ke un opportunities ko identify karna chahiye jo skill ka use karne ke dimaagi requirements (mental requirements) ki nakal (mimic) karte hon.
5. **Backup materials aur drills.** Jin mukhya materials aur methods ka aap use kar rahe honge, unke alava, un sambhavit drills aur backup materials ko dekhna ek achha idea hai jinhein aap use karna chahenge. Backup materials aam taur par tab acche hote hain jab aap recognize karte hain ki koi khhas tool ya materials ka set useful ho sakta hai lekin aap shuruat mein bojh (overwhelmed) tale nahi dabna chahte.

## Step 2: Schedule Your Time

_(Step 2: Apne Samay Ko Schedule Karein)_

Aapke ultralearning project ko safal hone ke liye ek tivra, full-time prayas (intensive, full-time endeavor) hone ki zarurat nahi hai. Halanki, isme kuch samay ke investment ki zarurat hogi, aur baad mein samay dhoondhne ki simplemente umeed karne ke bajaye pehle se yeh taye karna behtar hai ki aap learning ke liye kitna samay devot karne ke liye taiyar hain.

Pehle se apna schedule plan karne ke do acche kaaran hain. Pehla yeh hai ki is tareeqe se aap doosri cheezon se pehle apne calendar par ise set karke anjaane mein (subconsciously) apne project ko prathmikta (prioritize) dete hain. Doosra yeh hai ki learning aksar frustrating hoti hai aur Facebook, Twitter, ya Netflix par click kar jana lagbhag hamesha kahin zyaada aasan hota hai. Agar aap seekhne ke liye samay alag nahi rakhte hain, toh aisa karne ke liye motivation ko summon up karna kahin zyaada hard hoga.

Pehla faisala jo aapko karna chahiye woh yeh hai ki aap kitna samay commit karne ja rahe hain. Yeh aksar aapke schedule dwara nirdharit (dictated) hota hai. Aapke paas employment mein ek gap ho sakta hai jo intensive learning ki izazat deta hai, lekin kevel ek mahine ke liye. Alternatively, aapke paas ek full schedule ho sakta hai jo aapko kuch naya seekhne ke liye per week sirf kuch ghante devot karne ki izazat deta hai. Aap jo bhi samay commit kar sakein, pehle se ispar faisla karein.

Doosra faisala jo aapko karne ki zarurat hai woh yeh hai ki aap kab seekhne ja rahe hain. Sunday ko kuch ghanton ke dauran? Ek ghante pehle jaag kar aur kaam se pehle samay nikaal kar? Evening mein? Lunch breaks ke dauran? Ek baar phir, sabse behtar cheez wahi karna hai jise aapke schedule ke aadhar par sabse aasan banaya ja sake. Main jab bhi aap kar sakein tab learning ko fit karne ki koshish karne ke bajaye ek consistent schedule set karne ka suggestion deta hoon jo har week same ho. Consistency achhi habits ko badhava deti hai, jisse study karne ke liye required effort kam ho jaati hai. Agar aapke paas bilkul koi choice nahi hai, toh ek tadharth schedule (ad hoc schedule) na hone se behtar hai, lekin ise sustain karne ke liye mazeed discipline ki zarurat hogi.

Agar aapke paas apne schedule mein kuch lachilapan (flexibility) hai, toh aap ise optimize karna chahenge. Chote, spaced samay ke tukde memory ke liye crammed chunks ke mukable kahin zyaada behtar hote hain. Halanki, khhas tarah ke tasks, jaise writing aur programming, ke paas ek lamba warm-up samay hota hai jo lambe bina-badha wale samay ke tukdon (uninterrupted time chunks) se benefit le sakta hai. Aapke liye kya sabse behtar hai yeh dhoondhne ka sabse behtar tarika abhyas karna hai; agar aap paate hain ki warm up hone mein lamba samay lagta hai, toh apne schedule mein lambe spaces ka vikalp chunein. Agar aap paate hain ki aap shuru karne ke kuch minutes ke andar kaam par lag sakte hain, toh spread out kiye gaye chote samay ke tukde long-term retention ke liye sahayak honge.

Teesra faisala jo aapko karne ki zarurat hai woh aapke project ke samay ki length hai. Main aam taur par lambe commitments ke mukable chote commitments ko prefer karta hoon kyunki unke sath tike rehna (stick with) aasan hota hai. Ek intensive project jo ek mahine tak chalta hai usme life se ya aapqi motivation badalane aur kam hone (waning) se bhatkaav ke kam potential opportunities hote hain. Agar aapke paas koi bada goal hai jise aap accomplish karna chahte hain jise ek chote time frame mein nahi kiya ja sakta, toh main ise har ek kuch mahino ke multiple smaller goals mein todne ka suggestion deta hoon.

Finally, is saari jankari ko lein aur ise apne calendar mein dalen. Project par kaam ke saare ghante pehle se schedule karne ke important logistical aur dimaagi fayde (psychological benefits) hote hain. Logistically, yeh aapko vacations, kaam, ya family events ke kaaran apne schedule mein sambhavit conflicts ko spot karne mein madad karega. Psychologically, yeh aapko desk ke drawer mein tuke kiye gaye paper ke piece par likhe hone ke mukable apne shuruati plan ko behtar yaad rakhne aur uspar act karne mein madad karega. Kahin zyaada, schedule karne ka act project karne ke prati aapki gombhirta (seriousness) ko pradarshit karta hai.

Maine MIT Challenge shuru karne se pehle apne kaalpnik study schedule (hypothetical studying schedule) ko likhne ko saaf yaad rakh sakta hoon. Isne mujhe subah 7 aam baje utha kar study par laga diya aur shaam 6 pm baje tak kaam par rakkha, lunch ke liye sirf ek chote break ke sath. Bhale hi mera actual schedule, vyavahar (practice) mein, shayad hi kabhi us ideal tak pahuncha (yahan tak ki apne sabse intensive shuruati dino mein bhi, maine lagbhag kabhi lagataar eleven hours kaam nahi kiya), schedule likhne ke mere act ne mujhe aage ke project ke liye psychologically prepare karne mein madad ki. Agar aap apne calendar mein samay dalne ke liye taiyar nahi hain, toh aap study karne mein samay lagane ke liye lagbhag nishchit roop se taiyar nahi hain. Agar aap is stage par dol rahe hain (waffling), toh yeh ek achha sign hai ki aapka dil shuruat karne ke liye sahi jagah par nahi hai.

Ek bonus step ke roop mein, un logon ke liye jo cheh mahine ya usse zyaada ke lambe projects par badh rahe hain, main strongly apne schedule ka ek **pilot week (shuruati hafta)** karne ka suggestion deta hoon. Yeh simple hai: iske liye commit karne se pehle apne schedule ko ek week ke liye test karein. Yeh aapko is baare mein firsthand knowledge dega ki yeh kitna difficult hoga aur ati-aatmavishwas (overconfidence) ko rokega. Agar aap pehle week ke baad hi burned out feel karte hain, toh aapko adjustments karne ki zarurat ho sakti hai. Apne plan par wapas jaane aur ise apni life mein mazeed behtar fit baithane ke liye isme badlav karne (retooling) mein koi sharm nahi hai. Is tarah ka adjustment karna beech raaste mein chhod dene se kahin zyaada behtar hai kyunki aapka plan shuruat se hi asafal hone ki kismat (doomed) lekar paada hua था.

## Step 3: Execute Your Plan

_(Step 3: Apne Plan Par Amal Karein)_

Aapne jis bhi plan se shuru kiya ho, ab ise karne ka samay hai. Koi bhi plan perfect nahi hota, aur aap realize kar sakte hain ki aap learning ke liye jo kar rahe hain woh ideal se bhatak (departs) raha hai, jaisa ki ultralearning niyamon dwara establish kiya gaya hai. Aap notice kar sakte hain ki aapka plan retrieval practice ke bajaye passive reading par bahut zyaada nirbhar karta hai. Aap dekh sakte hain ki aap jis tareeqe se practice kar rahe hain woh us jagah se ek ghumavdar detour (winding detour) hai jahan aap actually iska use karna chahenge. Aap aisa feel kar sakte hain jaise aap cheezein bhool rahe hain ya unhein bina sach mein samjhe memorize kar rahe hain. Yeh theek hai. Kuch cases mein, aap learning ka perfect approach rakhne kabil nahi honge kyunki aisa karne ke liye resources exist nahi karte. Halanki, is baare mein sensitive banna ki aap kaise seekh rahe hain aur yeh niyamon ke sath kaise align nahi hai, un badlavon ko feel karne ka ek achha tarika hai jinhein aap ise behtar banane liye kar sakte hain.

Yahan apne aap se poochne ke liye kuch sawaal diye gaye hain yeh determine karne ke liye ki kya aap ideal se phisal (slipping) rahe hain:

1. **METALEARNING.** Kya maine is subject ya skill ko seekhne ke samanya tareeqon par research ki hai? Kya maine safal learners ka interview liya hai yeh dekhne ke liye ki woh kin resources aur salah ki recommend kar sakte hain? Kya maine apna project prepare karne mein kul samay ka lagbhag 10 percent spent kiya hai?
2. **FOCUS.** Jab main seekhne mein samay spent karta hoon, toh kya main focused hota hoon, ya main multitasking aur distracted hota hoon? Kya main learning sessions ko skip kar raha hoon ya procrastinate kar raha hoon? Jab main ek session shuru karta hoon, toh ek acche pravah (flow) mein aane mein kitna samay lagta hai? Mera mind bhatakna shuru hone se pehle main us focus ko kab tak sustain kar sakta hoon? Meri attention kitni teez hai? Kya ise intensity ke liye mazeed concentrated hona chahiye ya creativity ke liye mazeed diffuse (bikhra hua)?
3. **DIRECTNESS.** Kya main skill ko usi tareeqe se seekh raha hoon jaise main aakhirkar iska use karunga? Agar nahi, toh meri practice se kaun si dimaagi processes missing hain jo real environment mein exist karti hain? Main kitab/class/video se seekhi jankari ko real life mein transfer karne ka abhyas kaise kar sakta hoon?
4. **DRILL.** Kya main apni performance ke sabse kamzor points par focus karne mein samay spent ka rha hoon? Kaun sa begh-nirdharit karne wala kadam (rate-limiting step) hai jo mujhe peeche khinch raha hai? Kya aisa feel hota hai jaise meri learning slow ho rahi hai aur maharat haasil karne ke liye skill ke bahut saare components hain? If so, main ek complex skill ko chote, mazeed prabandhit karne yogya (manageable) ghaatakon mein kaam karne ke liye kaise split kar sakta hoon?
5. **RETRIEVAL.** Kya main apna zyaada tar samay padhne aur review karne mein spent kar raha hoon, ya main problems solve kar raha hoon aur apne notes ko dekhe bina memory se cheezon ko recall kar raha hoon? Kya mere paas khud par test lene ka koi tarika hai, ya main bas assume kar leta hoon ki mujhe yaad rahega? Kya main successfully explain kar sakta hoon ki maine kal, pichle hafte, ya ek saal pehle kya seekha tha? Main kaise jaanta hoon ki main kar sakta hoon?
6. **FEEDBACK.** Kya mujhe shuruat mein hi apni performance ke baare mein honest feedback mil raha hai, ya main punches se bachne aur aalochna se bachne ki koshish kar raha hoon? Kya main jaanta hoon ki main kya achhi tarah seekh raha hoon aur kya nahi? Kya main feedback ka correctly use kar raha hoon, ya main noisy data par overreact kar raha hoon?
7. **RETENTION.** Kya mere paas seekhi ja rahi cheez ko long term yaad rakhne ke liye ek plan jagah par hai? Kya main jankari ke apne exposure ko space de raha hoon taaki yeh mazeed lamba tike? Kya main factual jankari ko un procedures mein badal raha hoon jinhein main retain karunga? Kya main skill ke sabse critical aspects ko overlearning kar raha hoon?
8. **INTUITION.** Kya main jin cheezon ko seekh raha hoon unhein gehrai se samajhta hoon, ya main bas memorize kar raha hoon? Kya main jin ideas aur procedures ko study kar raha hoon unhein kisi aur ko sikha (teach) sakta hoon? Kya mere liye yeh saaf hai ki main jo seekh raha hoon woh sach kyun hai, ya yeh sab manmaani (arbitrary) aur unrelated lagta hai?
9. **EXPERIMENTATION.** Kya main apne majooda resources aur techniques ke sath stuck (atakh) ja raha hoon? Kya mujhe apne goal tak pahunchna ke liye baahar nikalne aur naye approaches try karne ki zarurat hai? Main basics par maharat haasil karne se pare kaise ja sakta hoon aur creative tareeqe se problems solve karne aur aishi cheezein karne ke liye ek unique style kaise create kar sakta hoon jinhein doosron ne pehle explore nahi kiya hai?

Ek sath yeh principles directions ke roop mein kaam karte hain, destinations ke roop mein nahi. Har case mein, dekhein ki aap currently apne materials ke beech se kaise progress kar rahe hain, aur dekhein ki aap kya different kar sakte hain. Kya aapko resources switch karne ki zarurat hai? Kya aapko unhi same resources se chipke rehne ki zarurat hai lekin ek different tarah ki practice par mazeed samay spent karna chahiye? Kya aapko feedback, directness, ya immersion ke liye naye environments dhoondhne chahiye? Yeh saare baareek adjustments (subtle adjustments) hain jinhein aap raaste mein kar sakte hain.

## Step 4: Review Your Results

_(Step 4: Apne Nateejon Ka Moolyankan Karein)_

Aapka project khatam hone ke baad (ya agar aap aakhirkar kisi kaaran se ise pause par dal dete hain), aapko iska vishleshan karne mein thoda samay spent karna chahiye. Kya sahi gaya? Kya galat gaya? Agli baar unhi same mistakes ko karne se bachne ke liye aapko kya karna chahiye?

Aapke saare projects successful nahi honge. Mere paas aise ultralearning projects rahe hain jinhe lekar maine achha feel kiya. Mere paas doosre rahe hain jinhone us tarah kaam nahi kiya jiski maine umeed ki थी. Bhale hi tendency willpower aur motivation ko dosh dene ki hoti hai, bahut zyaada baar projects ke sath problems unke kalpana (conception) se dhoondhi ja sakti hain. Maine apne trip ke baad, per week five hours invest karke apni Korean ko behtar banane ke liye samarpit ek project par kaam kiya. Yeh utna successful nahi raha jitni maine umeed ki thi kyunki maine shuruat se hi (from the get-go) immersive, direct practice par focus karne mein paryapt samay invest nahi kiya. Iske bajaye, mera study method textbook exercises par bahut zyaada nirbhar tha, jo boring the aur real world mein bahut zyaada transfer nahi hue. Agar maine is baare mein thoda mazeed socha hota, toh maine beech raaste mein pivot karne ki koshish karne ke bajaye, jab main pehle se hi kuch motivation kho raha था, practice karne ke opportunities dhoondhne mein pehle se ek ya do hafte spent kiye hote.

Yeh struggle pradarshit karta hai ki niyamon par maharat haasil karna ek poori life ki process hai. Bhashon ko seekhne ke kai experiences hone ke baad bhi, aur kya achha kaam karta hai yeh jaan'ne ke baad bhi, main ek kam effective approach mein slip ho gaya kyunki maine apne project ko adequately plan nahi kiya gya tha. Doosre cases mein ek project shayad us tarah kaam na kare jiski aapne umeed ki thi, lekin woh lesson tab bhi keemti hoga. Maine ek book list se jaakar cognitive science ko mazeed gehrai se seekhne ke ek project se shuruat ki thi. Aakhirkar, halanki, us project ka ek bada hissa is book ke liye research karne ki desire mein badal (morphed) gaya, jisne mujhe bahut saari science ke sath sampark mein laya, jo ab ise apply karne ke ek mazeed direct tareeqe ke outlet ke sath combined hai.

Bhale hi aapke successful projects hon, unka vishleshan karna keemti hai. Woh aksar aapko aapki failures se zyaada batate hain kyunki jin kaaranon se ek successful project safal hua woh wahi elements hain jinhein aap future ke liye retain aur replicate karna chahte hain. Ultralearning ke sath, jaisa ki saari swa-shiksha ke sath hota hai, goal merely ek single skill ya subject seekhna nahi hai balki aapqi overall learning process ko tez aur badhana (hone and enhance) hai. Agle project ke liye har ek successful project ko refine aur behtar banaya ja sakta hai.

## Step 5: Choose to Maintain or Master What You’ve Learned

_(Step 5: Jo Aapne Seekha Hai Ise Maintain Ya Master Karne Ka Chunaav Karein)_

Apni skill seekhne aur apne prayason ka vishleshan karne ke baad, aapko ek choice karni hai. Aap skill ke sath kya karna chahte hain? Kisi plan ke jagah par na hone se, zyaada tar jankari aakhirkar decay (kshay) ho jaati hai. Ise ultralearning ke niyamon ko follow karke thoda kam (alleviated) kiya ja sakta hai. Halanki, saari knowledge kisi bhi form ke hastakshep (intervention) ke bina decay ho jaati hai, isliye is baare mein choice karne ka sabse behtar samay ki aap ise kaise handle karne ja rahe hain kisi cheez ko seekhne ke theek baad hota hai.

### Option 1: Maintenance

_(Vikalp 1: Rakh-Rakhav / Maintenance)_
Pehla option skill ko sustain karne ke liye paryapt practice mein invest karna hai lekin ise ek naye level par le jaane ke kisi concrete goal ke bina. Yeh aksar niyamit abhyas ki ek habit set up karke accomplish kiya ja sakta hai, bhale hi yeh ek minimal ho. Jaisa ki retention par chapter mein zikr kiya gaya hai, "The Year Without English" project ke baad mujhe jo chintao mein se ek thi woh yeh thi ki itne chhote period ke dauran itni intensively bhashon ko seekhna na keval tezi se seekhne balki tezi se bhoolne (rapid forgetting) ki taraf le ja sakta hai. Nateejatan, maine trip khatam hone ke baad practice jaari rakhne ka prayas kiya, pehle saal mein har bhasha par week mein thirty minutes spent kiye aur uske baad ke saal mein har bhasha par month mein thirty minutes spent kiye.

Ek aur option skill ko apni life mein integrate karne ki koshish karna hai. Is tareeqe se main apne programming skills maintain karta hoon, jahan main un work tasks ko handle karne ke liye Python scripts likhta hoon jo otherwise bhaari-bhkam ya annoying hote. Is tarah ki practice mazeed sporadic (kabhi-kabar) hoti hai, lekin yeh ensure karti hai ki main ise itna jaari rakkhoon ki yeh usable rahe. Is tarah ka lightweight usage us gehre math aur algorithms se bahut door hai jise maine apne MIT coursework se seekha tha, lekin agar main baad ke samay mein kisi bade project par badhna chahta hoon toh door mein ek kadam (keep a foot in the door) rakhne ke liye kafi hai.

Bhoolna, jaisa ki Hermann Ebbinghaus dwara ek sau saal se zyaada samay pehle discover kiya gya tha, ek ghaatank roop se ghatt-ti hui curve (exponentially decaying curve) ke sath girta hai. Uska matlab hai ki jo memories mazeed lambe samay tak retain rehti hain unke bhoolay jaane ki sambhavna kam aur kam hoti jaati hai jab aap baad ki date par follow up karte hain. Yeh pattern suggest karta hai ki maintenance practice bhi ek ghatt-ti hui rate (decaying rate) par gir sakti hai, taaki aapne jo jankari acquire ki hai uska bada hissa preserved rahe. Iska matlab hai ki aap mazeed serious practice ki habit se shuruat kar sakte hain lekin aapka project khatam hone ke ek ya do saal baad ispar spent kiye jaane wale samay ko kam kar sakte hain tab bhi zyaada tar benefit paane ke liye, jaisa maine padhi gayi bhashon ke sath kiya.

### Option 2: Relearning

_(Vikalp 2: Dobara Seekhna / Relearning)_
Bhoolna ideal nahi hai, lekin kai skills ke liye baad mein skill ko relearn karne ki costs ise lagaatar teez (continuously sharp) rakhne ki costs se choti hoti hain. Iske ek-do kaaran hain. Pehle, aapne usse zyaada seekha ho sakta hai jitni aapko actually zarurat hai, isliye agar us knowledge ka kuch hissa use na hone ke kaaran selectively decay hota hai, toh yeh automatically aapke dwara acquire ki gayi kam important knowledge hone wali hai. Maine bahut saare MIT subjects study kiye jinhein mujhe nahi lagta ki main kabhi dobara use karunga, halanki unke gist (saar) ko samajhna baad mein handy aa sakta hai. Isliye, modal logic mein theorems prove karne ki apni ability ko, for example, up to date rakhne ki kevel simant keemat (marginal value) hai. Modal logic kya hai aur main ise kahan apply kar sakta hoon yeh jaan'na in case main aishi koi cheez seekhna chahta hoon jise iski zarurat ho, probably kafi hai.

Relearning aam taur par pehli-baar seekhne (first-time learning) se aasan hota hai. Bhale hi tests par performance drastically drop hoti hai, knowledge poori tarah se bhooli jaane ke bajaye lagbhag inaccessible hoti hai. Iska matlab hai ki ek refresher course ya practice series karna iske zyaada tar hisse ko us samay ke ek hisse (fraction) mein reactivate karne ke liye kafi ho sakta hai jitna ise shuruat mein seekhne mein laga tha. Yeh un subjects ke liye optimal strategy ho sakti hai jinhein aapko kam frequently use karne ki zarurat hai aur jinke liye unhein use karne ki situations bina kisi warning ke saamne nahi aayengi. Aksar, yeh recognize karna ki jankari ka ek khhas kshetra (domain of knowledge) kisi particular problem type ke liye sahayak hai, problem solve karne ke details se zyaada important hota hai, chunki baad wale ko relearn kiya ja sakta hai lekin pehle wale ko bhoolna aapko un problems ko solve karne se cut off kar dega.

### Option 3: Mastery

_(Vikalp 3: Maharat / Mastery)_
Teesra option, beshak, aapne jo skill seekhi hai usme mazeed gehrai se dive karna (dive deeper) hai. Yeh ek mazeed lighter pace par continued practice ke zariye ya ek aur ultralearning project ke sath follow up karke kiya ja sakta hai. Ek common pattern jo maine apni khud ki learning mein notice kiya hai woh yeh hai ki ek shuruati project ek bade territory aur kuch basics ko cover karne ka hota hai aur learning ke naye avenues ko expose karta hai jo pehle chhupay gaye the. Aap us domain ke andar ek subtopic ya skill ki branch ko identify kar sakte hain jise aap pehle seekh rahe the jise aap follow up karna chahte hain. Otherwise, aap ek jagah seekhi gayi skill ko ek naye domain par transfer karne ka faisala kar sakte hain. China se lautne ke baad mere goals mein se ek Chinese ko behtar padhna seekhna tha, jo wahan travel karne ke dauran mera sirf ek incidental (prasangik/goun) goal raha tha.

Maharat (Mastery) ek lamba raasta hai jo ek single project se kaafi pare tak phaila hua hai. Kabhi-kabhi aap apne shuruati prayas mein jin barriers ko overcome karte hain woh aakhirkar maharat tak pahunchna ke liye ikhatha karne ki ek slow process (slow process of accumulation) ke liye raasta saaf karne ke liye kafi hote hain. Kai domains mein, shuruat karna kaafi frustrating hota hai, isliye bina ek nirdharit matra mein effort ke abhyas karna difficult hota hai. Us threshold tak pahunchna ke baad, halanki, process jankariyon ke vishal daires (swaths of knowledge) ko ikhatha karne mein switch ho jaati hai aur isliye ek mazeed patient pace par aage badh sakti hai. Doosri taraf, kuch projects stuck ho jayenge, aur aapko unlearn karne mein samay spent karna hoga aur aage badhne ke liye apni niraashaon ke beech se phir push karna hoga. Is tarah ke projects aakhirkar maharat tak pahunchna ke liye ultralearning ke sateek aur aggressive methods se mazeed benefit lete hain.

## Alternatives to Ultralearning: Low-Intensity Habits and Formal Instruction

_(Ultralearning Ke Vikalp: Low-Intensity Habits Aur Formal Instruction)_

Is book ke start mein, maine point out kiya tha ki ultralearning ek strategy hai. Ek strategy hone ka matlab implies hai ki yeh khhas problems ko solve karne ke liye achhi hai. Diye gaye abhyas ke thoda unusual hone par, main book ka samay is strategy par focus karte hue bitana chahta tha, bajaye iske ki un saare possible tareeqon ka ek diffuse description dene ki koshish karoon jisse aap effectively seekh sakte hain. Halanki, ab jab maine aisa kar liya hai, mujhe lagta hai ki do doosri strategies par touch karna keemti hai jo different contexts mein, ultralearning ke sath kaam kar saqtii hain.

Mere samna aaye ultralearners mein se koi bhi har tarah ki learning ke liye same tareeqe se learning ko approach nahi karta. Benny Lewis, for example, bhashon ke liye intensive learning projects zoor karte hain, lekin unhone apni zyaada tar bhashayein un countries mein baar-baar visit karne ke dauran seekhi hain jahan woh boli jaati hain, un bhashon mein mazeed gehrai se khodte hue jinhein unhone pehle intense bursts mein establish kiya tha. Roger Craig ne Jeopardy! mein jeetne ke liye aggressively seekha zoor tha, lekin jab game show par unka aana imminent (nikat) nahi tha tab unhone trivia ke mazeed aaramdayak haasil karne (leisurely acquisition) mein engage kiya.

Ek ultralearner hone ka matlab implies nahi hai ki koi jo kuch bhi seekhta hai use sabse zyaada aggressive aur dramatic fashion mein hi kiya jana chahiye. Main briefly ultralearning ke do mukhya alternative strategies par vichar karna chahta hoon yeh dekhne liye ki woh lifelong learning ke ek bade picture mein kaise fit baithti hain.

### Alternative Strategy 1: Low-Intensity Habits

_(Alternative Strategy 1: Low-Intensity Habits)_
Low-intensity habits tab achha kaam karti hain jab learning mein engage hona sahaj (spontaneous) ho, aapka niraasha ka level (frustration level) kam ho, aur learning automatically rewarding ho. In cases mein, jab learning ke barriers kaafi kam hote hain, aapko bas itna karne ki zarurat hai ki aap wahan majood hon (show up). Kisi fancy project, principles, ya effort ki zarurat nahi hoti. Ek baar jab aap kisi bhasha mein conversational level tak pahunch jaate hain, for instance, toh ek aise country mein travel karna aur rehna aksar kaafi aasan hota hai jahan yeh boli jaati hai, ek lambe samay ke dauran mazeed se mazeed vocabulary aur knowledge ikhatha (accumulating) karte hue. Similarly, ek baar jab aap programming mein itne achhe ho jaate hain ki iska use apne kaam ke liye kar sakein, toh kaam khud hi aapko ek niyamit raftaar par nayi cheezein seekhne par push karega. Agar aapne kisi subject ke basics par maharat haasil kar li hai taaki aap is baare mein mazeed dense kitabhayein padh sakein, toh us topic par kitabhayein padhna mukhya roop se samay lagane (putting in time) ka mamla hai, na ki chalaak learning strategies develop karne ka.

Beshak, habits ka ek spectrum hota hai, zero-effort, spontaneous engagement se lekar ultralearning ke high-effort, rapid skill acquisition tak. Zyaada tar habits kahin beech mein hoti hain, jisme thodi si effort ki zarurat hoti hai lekin shayad ek ultralearning project ki poore paimane ki intensity (full-scale intensity) ki nahi. Aapne apne khud ke spreadsheet macros create karne ke liye kaafi Excel seekha ho sakta hai, lekin aapko hamesha iska use karne ke opportunities ya samay nahi milta, isliye aapko practice karne ke liye apne aap ko thoda push karne ki zarurat hoti hai. Aapne public speaking achhi tarah seekhi ho sakti hai, lekin stage par jaane mein abhi bhi thoda kaleja (guts) lagta hai. Yeh faisala ki kya agla step long-term habits set up karna hai ya ek concentrated ultralearning project create karna hai, aksar poori tarah se saaf nahi hota aur yeh ek kade-aur-teez rule (hard-and-fast rule) ke bajaye aapqi personality aur life constraints par mazeed depend ho sakta hai.

Habits tab sabse behtar kaam karti hain jab learning ka act mukhya roop se ikhatha karne (process of accumulation) ki ek process ho, naye skills aur knowledge add karte hue. Ultralearning aur mazeed deliberate prayas tab ke liye behtar sui-suited hain jab kisi field mein improvement ke liye gair-effective behaviours ya skills ko unlearn karne ki zarurat hoti hai. Kisi foreign bhasha mein apni vocabulary badhana aksar accumulation ki ek slow process hoti hai; aap aise words seekh rahe hote hain jinhein aap pehle nahi jaante gratitude the. Doosri taraf, apni pronunciation ko behtar banana unlearning ka ek act hai. Aap apne aap ko different muscular movements ka use karne ke liye train kar rahe hain jo aapke liye natural nahi hain. Ultralearning un kshetron ke liye bhi behtar hoti hai jahan learning ke paas bade niraasha ke barriers (frustration barriers) aur dimaagi obstacles hote hain jo kisi bhi form ke abhyas ko aasaani se establish hone wali aadat ke roop mein ek bahut bada prayas (too great an effort) bana dete hain.

Poori book ke dauran, humne us trade-off ko explore kiya hai jo is baare mein hota hai ki learning ke liye kya effective hai aur kya aasan aur enjoyable hai. Kabhi-kabhi jo sabse zyaada fun hota hai woh bahut zyaada effective nahi hota, aur jo effective hota hai woh aasan nahi hota. Yeh trade-off aapko learning ke mazeed aasan, mazeed enjoyable forms ka vikalp chun'ne par push kar sakta hai jo kuch kushalata (effectiveness) ka balidan dete hain. Halanki, apne personal experience mein, maine notice kiya hai ki enjoyment aam taur par cheezon mein achha hone (being good at things) se aata hai. Ek baar jab aap kisi skill mein competent feel karte hain, toh yeh bahut zyaada fun hona shuru ho jata hai. Isliye, bhale hi short term mein dono ke beech ek khinchtan exist kar sakti hai, main socha hoon ki aggressive ultralearning projects ko pursue karna aksar learning ko mazeed enjoy karne ka kahin zyaada pakka raasta hai, kyunki aapke ek aise level tak pahunchna ki mazeed sambhavna hoti hai jahan learning automatically fun ban jaati hai.

### Alternative Strategy 2: Formal, Structured Education

_(Alternative Strategy 2: Formal, Structured Education)_
Is book ke shuruat mein, maine explain kiya tha ki ultralearning self-directed hai, halanki zaroori nahi ki tanhaa ho. Self-directed hona is baare mein hai ki decisions kaun le raha hai, is baare mein nahi ki kya doosre log involve hain ya nahi. Isliye, kisi school ya university ke andar ultralearning ko pursue karne mein koi virodhabhas nahi hai. Jin skills ko aap acquire karna chahte hain unhein seekhne ka yeh sabse behtar tareeqa ho sakta hai. Bas ise kisi bhi doosre resource ki tarah treat karein.

Us badlav (distinction) ke bavajood, mujhe lagta hai ki un doosre kaaranon ke baare mein baat karna keemti hai jinki wajah se aap ultralearning ke bajaye formal education ko pursue karna chahenge. Sabse saaf credentials (yogyata praman) haasil karna hai. Agar aapke chune gaye kaam ke liye unki zarurat hai ya unki recommend ki jaati hai, toh unhein acquire karne ke liye aapko apni learning ke liye balidan dene par santusht hone ki zarurat ho sakti hai. Is book ka message yeh nahi hai ki aapko apne dum par seekhne ke liye school chhod (drop out) dena chahiye balki yeh hai ki aapko apni khud ki learning par control lena chahiye, chahe woh kahin bhi ho.

Formal education ko pursue karne ka ek aur kaaran yeh hai ki yeh ek learning environment create karti hai jo beneficial ho sakta hai. Bhale hi school ke kai aspects niraashaon se indirect aur ineffective hote hain, doosre kahin zyaada behtar perform karte hain. Design aur art schools aksar apprenticeships ki tarah function karte hain. Kuch programs team projects ke liye allow karte hain jinhein apne dum par shuru karna difficult hota hai. Finally, academia ke postgraduate levels aise communities create karte hain jahan immersion possible hai, taaki aap na keval un ideas ko acquire karte hain jinhein books aur papers mein likha gaya hai balki unhein bhi jinhein unki fields ke experts ke beech indirectly communicate kiya jata hai. Ultralearning un opportunities ka koi rejection nahi hai, aur agar mujhe yeh tark dete hue galat padha jaye (misread) ki woh exist nahi karte ya unhein ek tanhaa learning prayas se replace karna behtar hai, toh mujhe niraasha (disappointed) hogi. Cultivate karne ke liye sahi mindset kisi bhi slower ya standardized cheez ka rejection nahi hai balki yeh recognition hai ki kisi bhi cheez ko seekhne ki possibilities unke pehle dikhne ke mukable kahin zyaada vyapak (considerably broader) hain.

## Lifelong Learning

_(Ajeevan Shiksha / Lifelong Learning)_

Ultralearning ka goal aapke liye available opportunities ko expand karna hai, unhein narrow (tang) karna nahi. Yeh learning ke liye naye avenues create karna hai aur sideline par timidity se wait karne ke bajaye unhein aggressively pursue karne ke liye apne aap ko push karna hai. Yeh koi aisa method nahi hone wala hai jo har kisi ke liye suitable ho, lekin un logon ke liye jo iska use karne ke liye inspired feel karte hain, main umeed karta hoon ki yeh ek shuruat pradan karega.

---

# Chapter 14 — An Unconventional Education

### _(Ek Gair-Paramparagat Shiksha)_

---

> _"Give me a dozen healthy infants, well-formed, and my own specified world to bring them up in and I’ll guarantee to take any one at random and train him to become any type of specialist I might select—doctor, lawyer, artist, merchant-chief and, yes, even beggar-man and thief."_
> _(Mujhe ek doze swasth, su-gathit [well-formed] infants dein, aur unhein bada karne ke liye mera ek nirdharit world dein, aur main guarantee deta hoon ki main randomly kisi ko bhi chun kar use kisi bhi tarah ka specialist banane ke liye train kar sakta hoon—doctor, lawyer, artist, merchant-chief aur, haan, yahan tak ki bhikhari aur chor bhi.)_
> — Psychologist John Watson

---

Judit Polgár ko vyapak roop se abhi tak ki sabse behtar female chess player maana jata hai. Saat saal ki umra mein, unhone apni aankhon par patti baandh kar (blindfolded) ek chess master ke khilaf apna pehla game jeeta. Baarah saal ki umra mein, unhein Fédération Internationale des Échecs (FIDE) (World Chess Federation) dwara duniya ke saare chess players mein fifty-fifth rank rakkhi gayi thi. Fifteen tak, woh Bobby Fischer ke pichle record ko ek mahine se harakar abhi tak ki sabse youngest-ever grand master ban gayi thin. Apne peak par, Polgár duniya mein eighth rank par thin aur unhone World Chess Championship mein compete kiya, aisa karne wali woh akeli aurat thin.

Chess ek aisa game hai jispar adult mardoon ka dabdaba hai. Is tarah ek young girl ka compete karna unke competitors ke beech jigyasa aur purvagraha (prejudice) dono ko jagane wala tha. Grand master Edmar Mednis ne, young Polgár ka samna karte waqt, note kiya ki woh us young prodigy (vilakshanta/adbhut pratibha) ke khilaf apna best khelne ke liye bahut saavdhaan the, yeh note karte hue ki “Grandmasters 10-year-old girls se haarna pasand nahi karte, kyunki phir hum saare akhbaaron ke front page par aa jaate hain.” Unke kuch competitors ne Polgár ke khel ke saaf genius ko celebrates kiya. Grand master Nigel Short ka kehna tha ki Polgár history ke “teen ya char bade chess prodigies mein se ek” ho sakti hain. Ek purane world champion, Mikhail Tal ne suggest kiya jab Polgár abhi baarah ki thin ki woh aakhirkar world champion ke liye ek davedar (contender) ho sakti hain.

Garry Kasparov kam convinced the. Purane world champion ko kai logon dwara abhi tak ka sabse behtar chess player maana gya hai. Woh IBM ke _Deep Blue_ chess computer ke khilaf apne muqablon ke liye sabse famous hain, 1996 mein machine ke khilaf jeete aur 1997 mein haar gaye, jo ek aise game mein machine ke dabdaba (machine dominance) ke badlav (transition) ko mark karta hai jise aitihasik roop se insani creativity aur intelligence ke sabse oonche pradarshano (highest expressions) mein se ek maana jata tha. Kasparov young Polgár ke chances ke baare mein kam utsaahit the. “Uske paas fantastic chess talent hai, lekin woh hai toh aakhirkar ek aurat. Yeh sab feminine psyche (stree-mansikta) ki apurnataon (imperfections) par aakar rukta hai. Koi aurat ek lambi ladai barkarar nahi rakh sakti.”

Woh aam purvagraha (casual prejudice) unke pehle match ke dauran ek poore roop se vistarit vivad (full-blown controversy) mein phat pada. Polgár, jo tab sirf seventeen ki thin, Linares, Spain mein ek tournament mein khelte hue, us chess legend aur purane world champion ke samne baithin. Bhale hi chess ko aksar coldly rational (bina bhavna ke tarkshastri) ke roop mein dekha jata hai, kyunki dono players final outcome tak pahunchna ke liye sateekta (precision) ke sath moves calculate karte hain, dabdaba rakhne wale Russian ke samne baithne ke dimaagi asar (psychological effect) ko ausat se kam nahi dikhaya (understated) ja sakta. Us adbhut tension ko dekhte hue, yeh lagbhag avishwasniya tha khi Kasparov ne, move thirty-four par, apne knight ko rakkha aur, piece se apni fingers ko briefly uthane ke baad, apna mind badal diya aur ise ek behtar square par move kar diya. Polgár stun (hairan) thin. Chess ke rules ke mutabik, ek baar jab ek player kisi piece ko chhoona band kar deta hai, toh move ho jaati hai; koi badlav allowed nahi hota. Adhe avishwas mein, unhone referee ki taraf glance (dekha), yeh expect karte hue ki woh sanket dega ki Kasparov ne cheated (dhoka) kiya hai. Phir bhi referee ne us grand master ko chunauti nahi di. Us move se ladkhadati hui, Polgár game haar gayi.

Yeh poochne par ki unhone illegal move ko khud chunauti kyun nahi di, Polgár ne explain kiya, “Main World Champion ke sath khel rahi thi aur aise important event mein apne pehle invitation ke dauran na-khushi (unpleasantness) paada nahi karna chahti thi. Mujhe is baat ka darr bhi tha ki agar meri shikayat ko kharij (overruled) kar diya gaya toh jab hum samay ke tanav (time pressure) mein honge toh clock par mujhe penalize (dandit) kiya jayega.” Phir bhi, game khatam hone ke baad, woh kroodh se bhari thin. Unhone baad mein hotel ke bar mein Kasparov ka samna kiya, demand karte hue, “Aap mere sath aisa kaise kar sakte hain?” “Usne publicly mujhpar cheating ka aarop lagaya,” Kasparov ne aarop ke khilaf apna defense karte hue kaha. “Main socha hoon ki uski umra ki girl ko kuch achhe shishtachar (good manners) sikhaye jaane chahiye.” Un dono ke dobara baat karne mein saalon lag gaye, lekin jahan Kasparov pehle se hi chess duniya mein well-established the, Polgár ne abhi shuruat hi ki thi.

Polgár singular (anokhi) hain, na keval mardoon ke dabdaba wale game mein apne hunar ke liye balki is baare mein bhi ki unhone khelna kaise seekha. Doosre famous players, jaise Bobby Fischer, jinhone sahaj roop se game ke liye ek dhun (obsession) viksit ki, ke ulat Polgár ka chess genius koi accident nahi tha. Iske bajaye, yeh genius bacchon ko bada karne ke ek mard ke mission se shuru hua tha.

## The Chess Prodigy's Education

_(Vilakshan Pratibha Ki Shiksha)_

Judit dwara us legendary grand master ka samna karne se saalon pehle, chess mein unke tezi se oonchaiyon par pahunche (meteoric rise) ya unke pehle game se bhi pehle, unke father, László Polgár ne ek faisala kiya tha: woh ek genius bada karne ja rahe hain. College mein intelligence ka adhyayan karte waqt, unhone bache ya ek wife hone se bhi pehle apne project par vichar (contemplating) karna shuru kar diya تھا. “Ek genius paada nahi hota balki shikshit aur trained kiya jata hai,” unka manna tha. “Jab maine geniuses ke stories ko dekha,” unhone baad mein remark kiya, “mujhe same cheez mili. . . . Un sabne ek young age mein shuru kiya aur intensively study kiya.”

Lekin pehle, unhein apne is shikshashastra prayog (pedagogical experiment) ke liye ek partner dhoodhna tha. Unhein yeh Klára mein mili, jo ek Ukrainian foreign-language teacher thin. Normal love letters se bahut door, unhone pehle unhein ek email (correspondence) bheja jisme unhone genius bacchon ko bada karne ke apne idea ko explain kiya. Unke prastav (proposal) par sahmat hone ke baad, dono mile aur Soviet Union mein shaadi kar li, isse pehle ki unke native Hungary wapas move karein. Together couple ke teen bache hue, Zsuzsa, Zsófia, aur Judit. Bhale hi Judit aakhirkar sabse zyaada intensely competitive aur famous banin, teenon world-class chess players banin, jisme Zsuzsa bhi ek grand master banin aur Zsófia international master ke status tak pahunchin.

Ek tang apartment mein mamuli roop se (modestly) rehte hue, László aur unki wife ne genius bacchon ko bada karne ke apne project ke liye apna poora samay devot karne ka faisla kiya. Unki strategy ladkiyon ki shiksha jaldi shuru karne ki thi, teen saal ki umra mein, aur cheh saal se baad kisi single domain mein visheshtata (specialization) par badhne ki thi. Woh ladkiyon ko us subject se slowly introduce karke shuruat karenge, chote bursts mein, aur ise khel (play) mein badal denge taaki woh active roop se practice karna chahein bajaye iske ki aisa karne ke liye majboor (coerced) feel karein. Us strategy ne, halanki, koi topic nirdharit nahi kiya tha. László aur Klára ne apni daughters ke liye foreign bhashon se lekar mathematics tak kai different possible study topics par vichar kiya. Aakhirkar unhone chess par faisla kiya, kyunki yeh nishpaksh (objective) tha aur isme progress ko measure karna aasan tha. Isme koi shakk nahi ki un saalon mein socialist deshoon mein intellectually roop se chess ke dabdaba (preeminence) ne khel par focus karne ke unke faisala ko mazeed wajan (weight) diya.

Chess par zor dene ke bavajood, László ka vishwas nahi tha ki is tarah ki specialization unqi ladkiyon ki vyapak shiksha (broader education) ke balidan par aani chahiye. Teenon ne foreign bhashayein seekhin (Zsuzsa, sabse badi, ne aath seekhin), sath hi mathematics, table tennis, swimming, aur doosre subjects. Teeno ladkiyon ke sath chess par focus karne ka faisala ek practical kaaran se kiya gaya tha: dono parents ko resources aur samay dono mein jo intense devotion rakhne ki zarurat hogi, use dekhte hue apne prayas ko teen different disciplines par phailana unke budget ya schedule ke bardaasht se zyaada hota.

Zsuzsa shuru karne wali pehli thin. Unhone char saal ki umra mein khelna shuru kiya. Cheh mahine baad, woh apne father ke sath Budapest ke dhuen se bhare chess clubs mein ja rahi thin, elderly mardoon ke khilaf khel rahi thin—aur jeet rahi thin. Jab tak Judit ki baari aayi, woh pehle se hi apna training shuru karne ke liye motivated thin. Zsuzsa aur Zsófia ek chote room mein chess khelti thin jise László ne game ke liye devot kiya تھا, aur woh baahar chhootna nahi chahti thin.

Jald hi teeno ladkiyan ek team thin, kaafi bade, aam taur par male players ke khilaf compete karne ke liye travel karti thin. Unke sanjha mission (shared mission) ne ek aise game ko khelne mein irshya (jealousy) ke bajaye sauhard (camaraderie) create kiya jo aksar unke unusual status ke khilaf push karta tha. Hungarian Chess Federation ki policy auraton ke liye kevel auraton ke chess events mein compete karne ki thi. Halanki, László is idea ke sakht khilaf the. “Auraten dimaagi gatividhiyon ke kshetron (fields of intellectual activities) mein mardoon ke samroop results haasil karne kabil hain,” unhone feel kiya. “Chess dimaagi gatividhi ka ek roop hai, isliye yeh chess par apply hota hai. Accordingly (Iske mutabik), hum is mamle mein kisi bhi tarah ke bhed-bhav (discrimination) ko reject karte hain.” Bhed-bhav ne pehle hi Zsuzsa ko fifteen ki umra mein grand master ka title haasil karne se rok diya tha. Sabse chhoti hone ke naate, jab tak Judit in barriers ke paas pahunchin, unki badi sisters ne pehle se hi unhein thoda tod diya tha, jisse unhein kevel auraton ke tournaments mein compete karne se parhez karne ki izazat mili.

Bhale hi unki shiksha same thi aur teenon chess mein impressive heights tak pahunchin, ladkiyon ka hunar ek jaise nahi tha. Zsófia teenon mein sabse kamzor thin; international master ke impressive grade tak pahunchne ke bavajood, unhone baad mein art aur apni family par focus karne ke liye chess se retire hone ka faisla kiya. Zsuzsa ne ek chhoti umra se chess mein thoda kam specialize kiya tha, aath bhashayein seekhin, jise unke father admit karte hain ki unke maximum chess potential tak pahunchne se unka dhayan bhatka (distracted) diya ho sakta hai. Judit ne shuruat mazeed slowly ki, Zsuzsa ke mutabik, lekin unke paas sabse strong work ethic thi, woh chess ke sath is darje tak “obsessed” thin jo unke family ke hisab se bhi unusual tha.

## Rematch with Kasparov

_(Kasparov Ke Sath Dobara Muqabla)_

Kasparov dwara apni vivadit defeat ke aath saal baad, Judit ke paas us legendary grand master ka samna karne ka ek aur opportunity tha. Moscow mein 2002 ke _Russia Versus the Rest of the World_ match mein, Judit ne rapid chess ke ek game mein Kasparov ka samna kiya, jisme har player ke liye sirf twenty-five minutes aavantit the. Judit ne _Ruy Lopez_, ya Spanish game khela, jiska naam sixteenth-century ke Spanish bishop aur chess strategist ke naam par rakkha gya hai. Yeh chess mein sabse common openings mein se ek ka use karta hai, second aur third moves par knight aur bishop ko acche squares par baahar move karte hue. Kasparov ne _Berlin Defense_ ke sath counter kiya, board par ek doosra knight move karte hue jabki unhone apne opponent ke bishop dwara paada kiye gaye sambhavit danger ko ignore kiya; yeh ek mazboot counter hone ke roop mein jaana jata tha, jo aksar draws (barabari) ki taraf le jata tha. Kasparov koi chances nahi le rahe the.

Exchanged pieces ke ek jhonke ke baad, dono positions kaafi paas thin. Judit ne, white ke roop mein, apne king ko safety mein castle kar liya था. Kasparov ne, black ke roop mein, same safety ka opportunity khone mein light-square aur dark-square bishop dono ka joda retain rakkha tha, ek powerful combination jo aksar kisi game ko jeetne mein nirnayak (decisive) ho sakta hai. Judit ne calmly aige push kiya, Kasparov ke bishops mein se ek ko corner karte hue aur unke advantage ko neutralize karte hue. Slowly lekin surely, unki moves unki position ko behtar banati rahin jabki Kasparov ki tezi se sandehjanak (questionable) dikhne lagi. Aakhirkar, midgame ke dauran Judit dwara ikhatha kiye gaye chote sthaniye advantages (positional advantages) jeetne ki threat de rahe the. Do pawns neeche aur checkmate ke mandraate khatron (looming threats) ka samna karte hue, Kasparov ne isteefa (resigned/haar maan li) de diya.

Apni defeat ke baad, Kasparov ne Judit ki ability aur indeed game ke sabse highest levels par mardoon ke khilaf compete karne wali auraton ke idea ke apne pehle ke moolyankan (assessment) ko badal (revised) diya. “Polgárs ne dikhaya ki unki yogyata (aptitude) ki koi janmjaat seemayein (inherent limitations) nahi hain—ek aisa idea jise kai male players ne tab tak sweekar karne se mana kar diya jab tak ki unhein ponytail wali ek twelve-year-old ladki dwara un-ceremoniously kuchtal (crushed) nahi diya gya.”

## The Aftermath of an Experiment

_(Ek Prayog Ke Parinaam)_

László Polgár ka yeh conviction (draddh vishwas) ki woh kisi bhi swasth bache ko ek genius mein badal sakte hain, ek is tarah ka daava hai jo unhein ek paagal (crackpot) jaisa dikhata agar woh actually successful na hue hote. Nevertheless, ek saavdhaan reader note karein ga ki, jahan tak projects ki baat hai, László ke project mein dheron holes hain jo ise scientific purity ka ek model banne se rokte hain. Shuruat karne ke liye koi control group nahi tha. Teeno Polgár sisters ne same shiksha receive ki. Wahan koi fourth sister nahi thi jo normal tareeqe se school gayi ho aur László ki special training se chhook gayi ho. Koi randomization nahi tha. László ne apne unusual system mein bada karne ke liye kisi random bache ko adopt nahi kiya balki apne khud ke bacchon ko padhaya. Iska matlab yeh bhi hai ki genetics ke influence ko ignore nahi kiya ja sakta. Teeno bacchon ki success acquired talents ke bajaye vanshanugrat (hereditary) ke kaaran ho sakti hai. Wahan koi blinding bhi nahi thi. Saare Polgárs jaante the ki woh kisi special cheez ka hissa hain, ek unique mission jo unhein doosre families se alag karta tha. Isliye, nature aur nurture ke beech chal rahi behes mein, Polgár sisters ki success is role ka sanket (suggestive) de sakti hai jo gair-paramparagat shiksha (unorthodox education) play kar sakti hai, lekin yeh nirdharit (definitive) hone se bahut door hai.

Ek poori tarah se scientific experiment ke roop mein iski failures ke bavajood, Polgárs ka kaam nishchit roop se us baat ki ek window hai ki kya possible ho sakta hai. Teeno ladkiyon ne chess mein vishal results haasil kiye. Bhale hi hum nishchitta se nahi jaan sakte, yeh likely lagta hai ki woh kisi bhi doosri domains ke number mein bhi succeed ho sakti thin. Similarly, bhale hi László ke methods strange the, aisa nahi lagta ki ladkiyon ne suffer kiya, chahe unki vyapak shiksha mein ho ya unke bhavnatmak kalyan (emotional well-being) mein. Woh self-confident aur happy thin aur badi hokar apne khud ke loving families ke sath successful, emotionally stable adults banin. Yeh poochne par ki kya unke is ajeeb shikshashastra methods ne unqi ladkiyon se ek normal childhood chheen (robbed) liya tha, László ne iske ulta tark diya, ki yeh ek normal, ausat darje ki shiksha (mediocre education) hai jo aksar na-khushi (unhappiness) ki taraf le jaanti hai. Interviewer Endre Farkas ne, jinhone Polgár ke sath unqi book _Raise a Genius!_ par kaam kiya tha, poocha, “Kya unhein bahut narrow roop se shikshit kiya gya hai, ek nishchint childhood se vanchit (deprived) karke? Main Polgárs ka moolyankan karne kabil raha. . . . Koi saaf dekh sakta hai ki woh happy hain.”

## Educating Ultralearners?

_(Ultralearners Ko Shikshit Karna?)_

Is book ke liye research karne se pehle, mere samna aaye saare ultralearners ambitious self-starters the. Main convinced tha ki ultralearning ek aishi cheez thi jo individual ke liye bada potential rakhti thi. Halanki, khud learners dwara required intensity aur commitment ke kaaran, main skeptical tha ki ultralearning ka poore educational system par koi direct prabhav (direct implications) padega. Bache pehle se hi kashtdayak study sthitiyon (onerous studying conditions) ke khilaf struggle karte hain, aur mujhe aisa laga ki study ki intensity badhane se sirf unka stress aur anxiety hi badhegi.

Psychologists un goals ke beech ek bada farq recognize karte hain jinhein log intrinsically pursue karte hain, apne khud ke interests, decisions, aur targets ke aadhar par, aur un goals ke beech jinhein woh extrinsically pursue karte hain, dabdaba rakhne wale parents, punishing curricula, ya demanding employers dwara push kiye jaane par. Baad wala type, kyunki unke mutabik dhalne (conforming) ka motivation mukhya roop se baahri social pressures se aata hai, bahut zyaada kasht (misery) ka kaaran banta hai. Depression, anxiety, aur yahan tak ki suicide ke kisse un environments mein distressingly common hain jahan standardized tests par perform karne ke pressure ko ek uncomfortable darje tak ratcheted up (badhaya) jata hai. Ultralearning, kyunki yeh ek self-driven quest (khoj) hai, koi externally thopsi gayi obligation (baahri zimmedari) nahi, isko is tareeqe se hone ki zarurat nahi hai. Halanki, iski nature ke hi kaaran, mere liye yeh aspasht tha ki kya yeh koi aishi cheez thi jise sikhaya ja sakta hai.

Polgár sisters ek unusual case hain, phir, kyunki bhale hi unhein ek bahut hi early age se train kiya gya tha aur unhone incredibly hard work kiya, woh pressure se psychologically harmed hui nahi dikhtin. Ek stereotypical “tiger” parent ke ulat, unke parents ne khel (play) aur positive feedback ke zariye unki unusual specialization ko encourage kiya, authority aur punishment ke zariye nahi. Polgár sisters saari adulthood mein competitive level par chess khelna jaatri rakkha. Chess ke liye dhun (obsession), isliye, saaf taur par ek foster (viksit) ki gayi cheez thi, na ki thopsi gayi cheez. Same samay par, experiment mein unka participation poori tarah se voluntary (swachhik) nahi tha. László ne bacchon ke is program ke liye consent (sahamati) dene ya na dene ke jaan'ne se pehle hi geniuses ko bada karne ke apne goal ka sapna dekh liya tha, isliye yeh aisa case nahi tha jahan har daughter ne apne liye discover kiya ho ki woh khud ko chess practice ke ek intense regimen ke liye devot karna chahti hai. Polgár project ke us feature ne mujhe sabse zyaada interested kiya, kyunki aisa laga jaise László aur Klára ne us normal expectation mein ek loophole (kamzoori/rasta) dhoondh liya tha ki doosron ko intensively study karne par push karne se nishchit roop se misery paada hoti hai.

## How to Raise an Ultralearner

_(Ek Ultralearner Ko Kaise Bada Karein)_

László Polgár ne ek book likhi jiska title tha _Raise a Genius!_, shiksha ke apne gair-paramparagat approach ko document karte hue. Book mein, unhone kisi bhi normal, healthy bache ko ek genius mein badalna ke liye apni strategy ko outline kiya, bhasharte ki parents un extremes par jaane ke liye taiyar hon jinhein unhone aur unki wife ne is task ke liye dedicate kiya tha.

- **Pehla step jaldi shuru karna hai (start early).** Bache ki shiksha teen saal se baad shuru nahi honi chahiye, aur specialization cheh saal se baad shuru nahi honi chahiye. Bhale hi hamare age badhne par learning kitni zyaada harder ho jaati hai iska exact vistar aspasht hai, music aur bhashon jaise fields se evidences hain ki bacchon ke brains younger hone par mazeed plastic aur flexible hote hain. László ne is idea ko extreme tak liya, early-childhood education ke liye typical maane jaane wale se kahin mazeed early training ko encourage karte hue.
- **Doosra step specialize karna hai.** Bhale hi Polgár sisters ne bhashayein, mathematics, sports, aur doosre subjects seekhe, unka focus hamesha chess par tha. László ne note kiya ki “4-5 saal se shuru karke woh din mein 5 ya 6 ghante chess khelti thin.” Woh specialization geniuses ko bada karne ki unqi strategy mein do roles rakhti hui lagti hai. Pehla yeh hai ki isne us kaalpnik flexibility ka fayda uthaya jo younger bacchon ke paas naye subjects ko aasaani se seekhne ke liye hoti hai. Doosra yeh hai ki kisi single subject mein specialize karke, bache ek kahin zyaada young age mein proficiency tak pahunch sakte the. Chess mein bade aur mazeed experienced opponents ke khilaf jeetne ne unke confidence aur competitive spirit ko build kiya, taaki woh apne aap ko behtar banane liye active roop se mazeed practice karna chahein. Agar ladkiyon ne apni intellectual appetites ko bahut zyaada wide phhaila diya hota, toh woh us self-confidence ko viksit nahi kar patin jo intense practice ki taraf le jata hai.
- **Teesra step practice ko play (khel) mein badalna tha.** Chess, ek game hone ke naate, naturally play ke liye sui-suited hai. Halanki, László ladkiyon ke samne saarre subjects ko play ke forms ke roop mein introduce karne par insisted the. Jab ladkiyan game khelte waqt bhatak (distracted) jaatin ya uth kar chaaron taraf ghoomne (wander around) lagtin, toh unhein punishes nahi kiya jata tha balki jab woh ek solution dhoondh rahi hotin toh unhein apne minds ko bhatakne dene ke liye encourage kiya jata tha. Game ko fun aur light rakhna, khhasakar jab bache young the, drive aur self-confidence develop karne ke liye ek mukhya stepping-stone (papadan) tha jo baad mein mazeed serious prayason ko support karega. Halanki, yeh dimaag mein rakhna important hai jaisa László ne insisted kiya ki “play kaam ka ulta nahi hai” aur “ek bache ko kaam se alag play ki zarurat nahi hoti, balki arthpurna action (meaningful action) ki zarurat hoti hai,” yeh add karte hue ki “learning unhein ek sterile (banjh/fuzool) game ke mukable mazeed enjoyment pradan karti hai.” Play aur work Polgárs ke learning ke approach mein combined the, unke beech koi rigid boundary nahi thi.
- **Chautha, László positive reinforcement create karne ke liye saavdhaan the** taaki chess ko ek frustrating ke bajaye ek pleasant experience banaya ja sake. “Failure, suffering, aur darr achievement (uplabdhi) ko kam karte hain. Kai lagataar failures ke baad, ek nuksaandayak badhit karne wala complex (damaging inhibitory complex) bhi create ho sakta hai,” unhone explain kiya. Behaviorists se shuru karte hue, psychologists yeh detail se jaante hain ki ek positive experience hona, jaise game jeetna, un behaviours ko repeat karne ki ek desire create kar sakta hai jo us experience tak le gaye. Negative experiences, haarna, confused banna, ya ek stronger opponent ke khilaf frustration ka experience karne se lekar ek aise opponent ka samna karna jo bahut zyaada aasan ho aur player se ek impressive victory anjam dene ke santoosh ko chheen le, utsah (enthusiasm) ko kam karte hain. László ne saavdhani se shuruat mein hi positive feedback ke cycles ko establish kiya. Shuruat mein, jab woh abhi bhi ladkiyon se ek stronger player the, toh woh apne khel ko is tareeqe se adjust karte the ki unhein challenge toh mile lekin woh samay ke ek paryapt hisse (enough of the time) mein jeet sakein taaki game unhein enjoyable lage. “Hamein sure karna chahiye ki hum bache ke khilaf hamesha na jeetein; hamein unhein kabhi-kabhi jeetne dena chahiye taaki woh feel karein ki woh bhi sochne kabil hain,” unhone likha, yeh add karte hue ki “Shuruat mein sabse important interest jagana (awake interest) hai. . . . Hamein bache ko usse pyaar karwana chahiye jo woh karte hain—is darje tak ki woh ise lagbhag obsessively karein.”
- **Finally, László learning ko majboor karne (coercing) ke poori tarah khilaf the.** Self-discipline, motivation, aur commitment, unhone feel kiya, ladkiyon ke andar se hi aani chahiye. Unhone explain kiya, “One thing is certain: koi kabhi bhi coercion (majboori) ke zariye serious pedagogical results haasil nahi kar sakta, khhasakar ek high level par.” Unhone yeh bhi feel kiya ki “sabse important educational tasks mein se ek swa-shiksha (self-education) sikhana hai.” Unqi daughters ke liye unqi process ka yeh final step khhasakar important tha, kyunki unhone jaldi hi apne father ki ability ko piche chhod (outpaced) diya. Agar unhein khud ko sikhane aur apni learning ko adjust karne ki apni khud ki abilities develop karne liye encourage na kiya gaya hota, toh woh decent chess players ban saktin thin lekin nishchhit roop se grand masters nahi.

In basic niyamon ke alava, László aur Klára ne apni daughters ki advancement ke liye har ek opportunity provide karne mein khud ko intensively devot kiya, do lakh se zyaada muqablon (matches) ka ek database taiyar (cultivating) kiya, har ek chess textbook kharidi jise woh dhoondh sakte the, aur apni daughters ke liye chess tutors ko recruit kiya. Ladkiyon ke paas game par study karne aur improve karne ke opportunities ki koi kami nahi thi. Polgár ka ghar, jiski walls par chess positions ke diagrams tange the, is ancient game ke abhyas ko samarpit ek mandir (temple) ban gaya. László aur Klára ke liye, apne bacchon ko bada karna ek full-time job se zyaada tha kyunki unhone resources assemble karke aur unhein ghar par padha kar (schooling them at home) ladkiyon ke talents ko foster kiya.

## Ultralearning Principles in Action

_(Ultralearning Ke Niyam Kaam Mein)_

Genius bacchon ko bada karne ke Polgár ke niyamon ke alava, maine yeh interesting paaya ki ultralearning ke saare principles jinpar maine abhi tak discuss kiya hai woh unke learning ke approach mein present the.

### 1. Metalearning

Polgár ne apna poora samay is baat ko samajhne mein devot kiya ki log chess kaise seekhte hain aur kin conditions mein unki daughters thrive (fale-phoole) karengi. Unhone chess positions, strategies, aur games ke lists ka ek vishal library create kiya, jo vyapak internet se pehle ke dino mein koi chhota carnama nahi tha. Unhone ladkiyon ko game mein coach karne ke liye ek plan bhi bayan kiya jab woh abhi bahut young thin, unhein pehle board par squares ke naam sikhana shuru karke aur baad mein yeh jaanna ki pieces kaise move hote the. Us slow progression ne ladkiyon ko unqi doosri dimaagi kshamtayon (cognitive abilities) ke viksit hone se pehle hi game pick karne ki izazat di.

### 2. Focus

László “monotony (neerasata) ko handle karne ki ability, interest barkarar rakhne ki kabhiliyat aur persistent attention (lagaatar dhayan)” ko mukhya traits ke roop mein maante the jinhein unhone apni daughters mein instill karne ka maqsad rakkha tha. Ladkiyon ne pachas, nau, aur aath saal ki umra mein, respectively, twenty-four-hour chess marathons mein do baar part liya, us samay ke period mein sau matches complete karne ki zarurat hone par. Chess sirf brilliance ke flickers (chamako) ka game nahi hai balki endurance (sahan-shakti) aur stamina ka game hai. Training focus László ke system ka unqi daughters liye ek bada hissa tha, kyunki unhone unhein problem par apna mind focus karne aur bhatakne na dene ke liye encourage kiya.

### 3. Directness

László apni daughters ko mardoon ke sath games ke liye tab le gaye jab woh sirf char saal ki thin, unhein yeh dikhaate hue ki game un opponents ke khilaf kaise khela jana tha jo sach mein ek challenge offer karenge. Ladkiyon ne chess ke dheron games khele, jinhone unqi abilities ka backbone banaya. Usne unhein na keval game achhi tarah khelna seekhne ki balki samay ke tanav (time pressure) aur bade, mazeed intimidating opponents ke khilaf khelne ke dimaagi asurakshaon (psychological insecurities) se deal karne ki bhi izazat di. Casual games ke liye bhi chess timers ka use karke, ladkiyon ne ek aise environment mein practice ki jo un tournaments se mazeed closely match karta tha jiska woh samna karengi.

### 4. Drill

László ne game par study karne ke approaches ko badla, apni daughters ko pehle squares ke naam, phir mukhya pieces ke movements ko memorize karne se shuru karwaya. Ghar ki walls par tange chess puzzles ladkiyon ke homework ban gaye, kyunki unhein different tactical positions ko solve karna tha aur creative solutions ke sath aana tha. Blitz (tez chess) aur blindfolded games ne ladkiyon ko mazeed tezi se sochne aur mentally game ko simulate karne mein behtar banne kabil banaya.

### 5. Retrieval

Retrieval ke liye, László ne explain kiya, “Hamein unhein har cheez nahi batani chahiye; hamein bache se kuch bolwane (say something) ki koshish karni chahiye!” Jise unhone chess ke liye “Socratic method” ke roop mein describe kiya, unqi ladkiyon ko aise sawaal pesh karna jinka unhein javab dena hoga bajaye iske ki unhein pehle se solved solution yaad rakhne ke liye kahein, woh unqi memory aur samajh ke vistar ko encourage karne ke liye sahi method ka use kar rahe the. Blindfolded games ne, ek baar phir, ladkiyon ki strategy ka ek powerful component banaya. Board ko dekhe bina practice karke, isne unhein apne head mein positions ko follow karne ki ability cultivate karne par majboor kiya, jo na keval long term mukhya chess patterns ko retain karne ke liye useful tha balki board par un moves ko simulate karne ke hunar ko behtar banane liye bhi jo ek opponent khel sakta hai.

### 6. Feedback

László ne real opponents ke sath kaafi khel ko encourage kiya lekin “sui-suited partners, jinke paas aam taur par ek jaise khelne ki ability ho” ko select karne mein saavdhaan the. Interestingly, feedback yahan saavdhani se controlled tha, na keval ladkiyon ko paryapt challenge provide karne ke liye (aisa challenge face karne ke liye mardoon ke tournaments mein khelne par Polgárs ka zor iska ek example tha) balki jab unki abilities abhi nascent (shuruati) thin tab bahut bade challenge se bachne ke liye bhi. Shuruat mein positive feedback cultivate karna important tha, aur László game ke flow ko adjust karne ke liye hamesha ready the taaki yeh sure kiya ja sake ki yeh ek aise level par ho jo mazeed khel ko stimulate (prerit) kare.

### 7. Retention

László ne ladkiyon ko memory se chess patterns recall karne par focus kiya aur khel ki speed badhai taaki unke khel ke elements mazeed automatic ban sakein aur bhoolay jaane ke prati kam su-grahya (less susceptible) hon. Chess successfully khelne mein chess patterns ko memorize karna ek bada hissa hai, aur isme spaced practice aur blitz aur blindfolded games jaise specialized drills dono se madad mili.

### 8. Intuition

Feynman Technique ki nakal (mirroring) karte hue, László ne apni ladkiyon ko chess ke baare mein articles likhne ke liye encourage kiya, yeh explain karte hue ki, “Agar koi ek article likhta hai, toh woh bina kisi goal ke, akele sochne ya is baare mein kisi se bolne ke mukable kisi mamle par mazeed gehrai se vichar (considers a matter more deeply) karta hai.” Ladkiyon ko problems ke creative solutions ke sath aane ke liye bhi encourage kiya gya tha. Play, na keval chess ek game hone ke sense mein balki ek unconstructed, bina-goal wali activity ke sense mein bhi, teaching strategy ka hissa tha. Interesting solutions ke sath aana aur ladkiyon ko tricks aur naye insights ke baare mein sochne ki chunauti dena unhein usse baahar explore karne kabil banata tha jo purane nateejon (past results) ko memorize karke offer kiya ja sakta tha.

### 9. Experimentation

Jaise-jaise Polgár sisters chess ability mein apne father se aage nikal (eclipsed) gayin, game par maharat haasil karna jaari rakhne ka unka prerna (impetus) tezi se unke andar se hi aana tha. Har ek ladki ko apna khud ka unique style aur approach cultivate karna tha. Judit ne tricks aur tactics par focus karne ka chunaav kiya, yeh likhte hue ki “opening preparation us samay bilkul bhi important nahi thi. Yeh ek kaaran ho sakta hai kyunki, aaj bhi, mera sabse strong area middlegame bana hua hai.” Ladkiyon ke badalte hue chunaav dikhate hain ki chess, kisi bhi creative skill ki tarah, na keval patterns par ek maharat ko shamil karta hai balki vishal range ki possibilities ke andar kin skills aur styles ko cultivate karna hai is baare mein choices ko bhi.

Finally, Polgárs ne ultralearning ke idea ko iske sabse vyapak roop mein embody kiya, László ke is tark ke sath ki, “Mere opinion mein, hamein har field mein intensive learning ke idea ko phhailana (disseminate) chahiye.” Polgárs ki success usi pattern ko follow karti hai jaisa mere dwara mile zyaada tar ultralearners ke sath hai: **learning ke mukhya niyamon ko follow karne wali aakramak, utsaahit swa-shiksha (aggressive, enthusiastic self-education).**

## Fostering Ultralearning in the Home, School, and Workplace

_(Ghar, School, Aur Workplace Mein Ultralearning Ko Badhava Dena)_

Aap ek parent ya educator ke roop mein ya kisi organization mein ultralearning ko kaise foster (badhava) kar sakte hain? Kya doosron ko unke apne design ke difficult learning projects se aatmavishwas ke sath nipatne mein madad karna possible hai? Kya aap students ko na keval wahi material sikha sakte hain jise unhein study karne ki zarurat hai balki unhein apne dum par seekhna kaise hai yeh bhi, taaki woh classroom ke baahar self-sufficient (atmanirbhar) honge? Kya aap apni organization ke individuals ko mazeed aakramak roop se seekhne, unqi competency ke gaps ko fill karne aur unke full potential ko haasil karne ke liye lead kar sakte hain? Yeh saare dilchasp sawaal hain jinke hamare paas abhi tak nirdharit (definitive) javab nahi hain.

Learning par scientific sahitya (literature) ko padhne aur ultralearners ke stories ko follow karne mein, main na keval is baat se struck hua ki learning ke baare mein pehle se kitna kuch jaana ja chuka hai balki is baat se bhi ki kitne saare open questions exist karte hain jinke liye researchers aur autodidacts abhi bhi parikalpanayen (hypotheses) laga rahe hain. Ek baar jab aap social environment ko bhi introduce kar dete hain toh complications ghaatank roop se expand hoti hain. Ab yeh simply individual cognition (dimaag) ka sawaal nahi rehta balki emotions, culture, aur relationships ka sanket hota hai jo learning ko complex aur unexpected tareeqon se influence karna shuru karte hain.

Is perspective se, isliye, main saavdhani se ghar par, school mein, ya workplace mein ek aise environment ko support karne ke liye kuch starting points suggest karna chahta hoon jo ultralearning ko support karega. Yeh suggestions rules nahi hain, lekin unhein doosron ko ultralearning spirit ko capture karne kabil banane ke starting points ke roop mein dekha ja sakta hai.

### Suggestion 1: Create an Inspiring Goal

_(Suggestion 1: Ek Inspiring Goal Create Karein)_
Isse bhi behtar, logon ko apne khud ke learning goals design karne ki izazat dein jo unhein inspire karein. Ultralearning ki process mein inspiration ek essential starting point hai. Kisi insaan ke liye seekhne ke liye required energy aur self-discipline ko summon up karne ke liye kuch bahut hi compelling (mazboot) hona chahiye. Kabhi-kabhi career opportunities lane wale ek naye skill ka vaada hota hai. Coding boot camps, jo high-paying programming jobs ke badle mein saamne aaye hain, students ko ek brutal pace par push karte hain, kabhi-kabhi per week eighty hours ke paas pahunchete hue. Goal, halanki, is investment ko sahi thehrane ke liye kafi compelling hota hai: kuch hafton ke course ke dauran ek kade program (rigorous program) ko complete karein, aur aap Silicon Valley aur doosri jagahon par high-salaried tech jobs ki lader (seedhi) par upar chadh sakte hain. Process intense hai, lekin motive compelling hai.

Doosre cases mein, ultralearning ke liye motivation ek intrinsic interest se aati hai jo badh (amplified) jaati hai. Meri apni MIT Challenge is ehsaas se shuru hui thi ki maine school mein computer science na padh kar kuch miss kar diya tha. Normally, yeh computer science seekhne ke kisi bade, structured prayas ki taraf nahi le jata. Yeh tabhi tha jab ek chhote samay ke period mein poori degree karne ka idea, us research ke sath jisne mujhe yeh sochne par majboor kiya ki yeh possible ho sakta hai, meri shuruati interest ko ek passionate commitment mein badal (passionate commitment) diya.

Roger Craig, apne Jeopardy! carnamo ke sath, hamesha trivia competitions mein interested the. Yeh tabhi tha jab unhone recognize kiya ki us famous television show par aane ka ek chance ho sakta hai tab unka interest ek dhun (obsession) ban gaya. Eric Barone ne apne bachpan ke video game ke pyaar ko liya aur ise ek behtar version create karne ke prayas mein expand kiya. Ultralearning ke liye logon ke natural interests ko dhoondhne ka matlab un chingariyon (sparks) ko encourage karna hai jo pehle se exist karti hain, bajaye mere un topics ko unpar thopsne ke jinhein aap feel karte hain ki sabse zyaada beneficial honge. Ek baar jab log ek ultralearning project ka structure dekh lete hain, toh woh apne liye khud sochna shuru kar sakte hain ki unke liye kaam karne ke liye sabse zyaada interesting, exciting, aur useful kya hoga. Tristan de Montebello ne ultralearning ke concept se shuruat ki thi aur baad mein iske chaaron taraf ek public speaking project taiyar kiya.

### Suggestion 2: Be Careful with Competition

_(Suggestion 2: Competition Ke Sath Saavdhaan Rahein)_
Polgárs ka example saaf sanket deta hai ki early self-confidence ek utsah create kar sakta hai jo lagaatar investment ki taraf le jata hai. Aapko aisa feel karne ki zarurat nahi hai ki aap kisi cheez mein achhe hain taaki seekhne mein energy invest kar sakein. Akhirkar, kisi cheez mein achha banna hi learning hai. Halanki, aapko yeh feel karne ki zarurat hai ki aap isme achhe **ho sakte hain**. Log apni aparyaptata ke moolyankano (perceptions of inadequacy) ko ek apari-vartaneeya kismat (immutable destinies) banane ki taraf jhukte hain: “Main math mein achha nahi hoon,” “Main stick figures ke alava kuch draw nahi sakta,” “Mere paas language gene nahi hai.” Bhale hi janmjaat ability (innate ability) mein real differences exist karte hain, taaki yeh kathan (pronouncements) poori tarah se false na hon, woh ek important factor ko ignore karne ki taraf jhukte hain: **motivation**.

Jab aap apne aap ko kisi cheez mein achha hone ke potential se vanchit dekhte hain ya vishwas karte hain ki aap hamesha baaki sab se peeche rahenge chahe aap kitni hi hard work kyun na karein, toh yeh aapise hard work karne ki motivation chheen leta hai. Is tarah, bhale hi hum sab ke beech ability mein differences hain, unhein aksar us bhavnatmak daire (affective dimension) dwara mazeed badhaya (exacerbated) ja sakta hai jise woh is baare mein create karte hain ki hum learning ke baare mein kaise feel karte hain. Feel karein jaise aap kisi cheez ko karne mein lousy (ghatiya) hain, aur aapise badlav karne ki motivation chheen jaati hai.

Aap jis reference group (sandarbh samooh) se apni comparison karte hain uska ek powerful influence ho sakta hai. Mujhe yeh interesting lagta hai ki kai, lekin saare nahi, ultralearners ne aise projects ka maqsad rakkha jo itne unusual the ki unki ek normal reference group se comparison karna hard tha. De Montebello ki public speaking competition ne nishchit roop se unhein bade public speakers ke khilaf khada kiya. Yeh heenta ki bhavna (feeling of inferiority) create kar sakta tha, sivaye iske ki de Montebello apne calendar par kisi bhi perceived deficits ko itne kam pehle ke experience ke sath itne ambitious project ko try karne se paada hone ke roop mein explain kar sakte the. Agar aisa hota ki ek individual ultralearning project ke bajaye, unhein exactly same pehle ke experience wale ek dozen doosre competitors ke khilaf khada kiya gaya hota, toh woh iske bajaye kisi bhi perceived aparyaptata ko tarkshastri roop se (rationalized) apne simply kafi achha na hone ke roop mein bayan kar sakte the.

Yeh suggest karta hai ki project ki competitiveness dono tareeqon se kaat-ti (cuts both ways) hai: Jab aapke paas ek natural talent hota hai aur is tarah aap aasaani se identifiable reference group ke mukable bahut zyaada behtar perform karte hain, toh aapke paas tivrata ke sath practice karne aur seekhne ki mazeed motivation hogi. Halanki, if you come up short (agar aap peeche reh jaate hain), toh yeh practice karne ki motivation chheen sakta hai. Polgárs ne competition ka use apne advantage ke liye kiya. Kyunki ladkiyon ki training asadharn roop se young shuru hui thi, unhein hamesha precocious ke roop mein dekha jata tha aur competitive environment ne unqi motivation ko badhava diya. Agar unhone der se shuru kiya hota ya unhein kisi aise school mein rakkha gaya hota jahan unke star performers hone ki guarantee na hoti, toh unqi motivation sapped (kam) ho sakti थी.

Mere liye, reference group se implicit comparison se aane wale aise motivational asar ek dohre approach (twofold approach) ko apnaane ka suggestion dete hain.

- Agar koi aisa insaan jisme aap ek ultralearning spirit ko encourage karna chahte hain uske paas ek natural aptitude hai, toh competition probably achha hai. Doosron ke sath direct comparison mein apne aap ko achha karte hue dekhna mazeed improvement ke prati ek commitment ko encourage kar sakta hai.
- Kisi aise insaan ke liye jo ya toh moderate ability ka hai ya doosre logon se peeche hai, jaise kisi aise domain mein ek skill seekhna jisme uske paas koi experience nahi hai, ya jo life mein thoda baad mein ek nayi skill seekhna shuru kar raha hai, aapko project ko unique banane ka prayas karna chahiye. Yeh us insaan ko doosron ke sath competition ke kaaran nahi balki apne pichle self se comparison karke apni progress ko frame karne ke liye encourage karega.

Kabhi-kabhi ek project shuruat mein unique ho sakta hai, is tarah প্রতিকूल comparison (unfavorable comparison) ki karrwi roshni se bacha hua (sheltered), aur ek baar confidence establish hone ke baad ek mazeed competitive environment mein move kar sakta hai. For example, aap ek aisa game create karke programming seekhna shuru kar sakte hain jiska doosron se comparison karna hard ho lekin jaise hi aap mazeed competent feel karna shuru karein toh coding competitions mein enter karein.

### Suggestion 3: Make Learning a Priority

_(Suggestion 3: Learning Ko Ek Priority Banayein)_
School se baahar, learning ko aam taur par ek job karne ke ek by-product ke roop mein dekha jata hai, mukhya goal ke roop mein nahi. Bhale hi organizations khhas taur par ongoing training aur education ke liye lip service (sirf lafzon mein dikhava) deti hain, yeh aam taur par workshops ya seminars ke roop mein hota hai jisme koi nishkriya roop se baithta hai isse pehle ki haath mein majood asli kaam par wapas jayein. Ultralearning, direct, intensive practice ko encourage karke, ek tarah ke fusion project (mishrit project) ka opportunity provide karti hai—ek aisa project jo real objectives ko accomplish karta hai lekin kuch naya sikhane ke liye bhi design kiya gya hai.

Kisi project ko assign karne ka normal protocol kaam ke liye sabse behtar insaan ko dhoondhna aur unhein task dena hai. Ek learning-driven approach iske bajaye yeh suggestion dega ki jo log abhi tak task karne kabil nahi hain unhein project assign kiya jaye. Ek ultralearning-driven work environment employees ke apne samay ka ek bada hissa un projects par spend karne par consist ho sakta hai jo unqi competency levels ke andar ya paas hain lekin apne samay ka ek vishisht hissa (specific fraction) un projects par kaam karne ke liye devot karna jo unqi majooda abilities se ek udaan (leap) upar hain. Bhale hi yeh poori tarah se hypothetical hai, main is approach ke do faydo ki kalpana karta hoon.

- Pehle, yeh ek organization ke andar learning ka ek aisa culture create karega jahan log hamesha un problems ko solve karne ki koshish karne ke liye taiyar rehte hain jinhein woh abhi tak solve karna nahi jaante, bajaye iske ki kisi aur se answer pehle se hi jaan'ne ki umeed karein.
- Doosre, yeh logon ko challenges dekar talent zahir (reveal) karne mein madad karega jahan tak woh uth sakein. Agar mentorship ke opportunities aur difficult projects managers dwara sirf ek mauqe (whim) par assign kiye jaate hain, toh woh nishchit roop se un kai logon ko miss kar denge jinke paas difficult positions mein succeed hone ki ability ho sakti hai lekin unhein aisa karne ka opportunity kabhi nahi diya jata.

Sabse highest levels par, ek ultralearning-driven culture learning ko un kshetron mein jaane ki bhi izazat deta hai jahan shayad kisi aur ke paas koi khhas skill na ho. Bhale hi skill ke established levels ke beech jana important hai, yeh tab hota hai jab koi aisa karna seekhta hai jo koi aur nahi kar sakta tab learning truly keemti ban jaati hai.

## Conclusion

_(Upsamhaar / Conclusion)_

Kai mayno mein, is book ko likhna khud ek ultralearning project raha hai. Bhale hi ek book ke liye research karne wala writer mushkil se hi unique hota hai, saare ultralearning projects ko karne wale insaan ke liye matter karne ke liye unka one of a kind hone ki zarurat nahi hoti. Ghar par mere den mein printed journal articles ke hazaron pages se bhari binders ke dher (stacks) rakkhe hain. Meri bookshelf par ab is sawaal ke chhote tukdon par ki log kaise seekhte hain, daso gudh, out-of-print monographs (shodh-prabandh) hain. Different researchers ke sath calls ke recordings ne mujhe realize karne mein madad ki ki “Kya feedback sahayak hai?” aur “Log kyun bhoolte hain?” jaise simple sawaalon mein bhi kitna baareek farq (nuance) majood hai. Maine famous intellectuals, entrepreneurs, aur scientists ke dheron biographies ke beech se nikalne (poured over) ka prayas kiya taaki is baare mein ek samajh tak pahunch sakoon ki unhone learning ko kaise approach kiya.

Kai mayno mein, is book ko likhne ki process iske subject ka ek reflection thi—ultralearning ke baare mein ek book likhne ke liye ek ultralearning project. Bhale hi mujhe learning ke subject mein ek strong interest tha aur maine pehle textbooks, articles, aur biographies browse ki thin, yeh is structured project ko shuru karne ke baad hi tha jab maine sach mein gehrai se khodna (dig deep) shuru kiya.

Research se pare, yeh book mere liye ek writer ke roop mein ek challenge thi. Mera writing experience blogging se aata hai, kitabhayein likhne (authoring books) se nahi. Ek kitab mein sahi tone strike karna hard hai, aur yeh ek blog mein rozmarra ke casual missives (sandesho) se kaafi different hai.
