Main shuruat se hi jaanta tha ki main sirf apne khud ke experiences ko dohrane ke bajaye doosron ke stories aur unke carnamo ko share karna chahta hoon. Woh shuruat mein kaafi challenging tha. Zyaada tar biographies aur published stories learning methods par focus nahi karti hain. Jab learning story ka central theme hoti hai tab bhi, zyaada tar biographers talent ke aadar (awe of talent) mein santusht rehte hain, bajaye iske ki is vishisht details mein khodein ki ek insaan ne ek khhas cheez kaise ki. Mere research prayason mein aksar ek pach-sau pages ki biography ko is baare mein un kuch paragraphs ke liye chhan'na (scouring) shamil hota tha jisme guzarre hue samay mein learning methods ke concrete details ka zikr kiya gya ho. Bhale hi isne challenges create kiye, isne mujhe ek writer ke roop mein naye skills develop karne par bhi majboor kiya. Mujhe apni research aur writing skills ko un tareeqon se behtar banana tha jise blog articles likhne ke ek dashak se zyaada samay ne kabhi nahi kiya tha. Yahan tak ki kitab ke style ne mere liye ek skill-challenging project create kiya. Main ise aap par, reader par, chhodta hoon judge karne ke liye ki kya main successful tha.

Ultralearning ke baare mein ek book likhne ke is metaproject ne kuch important ideas ko bhi pradarshit kiya hai. Ek ke liye, bhale hi maine apni writing ability aur cognitive science ke knowledge aur famous learning carnamo ke stories mein vishal improvements kiye hain, abhi bhi seekhne ke liye kahin zyaada baki hai. Science mein gehrai se khodte hue, koi papers, theories, ideas, aur experiments ke pahad (mountain of papers) ke top par khde hokar jaldi se chakkar (vertigo) ka ek ehsaas viksit kar sakta hai, jo saare learning ke topic se loosely connected hain. Similarly, har ek biography jo maine padhi, uske liye aishi saikdon thin jinhein main nahi padh saka. Mere samna aaye har ek ultralearning story ke liye, aishi daso aur thin jinka meri searches ne khulasa nahi kiya. Yeh claim karna ek gehri galti (profound error) hai ki learning agyanata (ignorance) ko samajh se replace karne ke baare mein hai. Knowledge expand hoti hai, lekin agyanata bhi waisa hi karti hai, kyunki kisi subject ki ek behtar samajh ke sath un saare sawaalon ke liye ek bada aadar (greater appreciation) bhi aata hai jo unanswered reh jaate hain.

Iske samne, kisi ke paas same samay par confidence aur gehri namrata (deep humility) honi chahiye. Is belief ke bina ki kisi ke apne knowledge aur skill mein progress possible hai, koi ise generate karne ke liye required project haath mein nahi le sakta. Is tarah ke confidence ko outsiders dwara ghamand (arrogance) samajhne ki galti ki ja sakti hai, kyunki aisa lag sakta hai ki kisi cheez ko jaldi aur intensively seekhne ka prayas kisi tareeqe se ek kathan hai ki subject mamuli hai ya, kisi cheez ko seekh kar, kisi ne sab kuch seekh liya hai. Iske bajaye, is confidence ko gehri namrata (deep humility) ke sath pair hona chahiye. Maine jo bhi project haath mein liya hai, isko shamil karte hue, iske complete hone par mere vichar yeh nahi the ki main khatam kar chuka hoon balki sudden is baare mein aware hona tha ki main kitna mazeed aage ja sakta tha.

Mera MIT Challenge shuru karne se pehle, maine kalpana ki thi ki computer science ke concepts ke undergraduate degree ke barabar hisse ko cover karna kafi hoga. Mere khatam karne ke baad, main dekh sakta tha ki kaise har ek topic jise maine seekha tha use poori tarah se samajhne ke liye ek doctorate ke barabar ki research ya saalon beete coding mein multiply kiya ja sakta tha. Mera bhashon ko ek aise level tak seekhne ka experience jahan main conversations hold kar sakoon ne mujhe realize karwaya ki kitne mazeed words, expressions, sanskriti ke baareek farq (nuances of culture), aur difficult communication situations explore karne ke liye baki chhote the. Kisi project ko complete karna, isliye, aam taur par learning khatam hone ke ehsaas ke sath nahi hota balki possibility ke ehsaas ke create hone ke sath hota hai jaise hi kisi ki aankhein un saari cheezon par khulti hain jinhein seekhna baki hai.

Learning ka yahi aspect hai jise main sabse zyaada interesting paata hoon. Life mein kai prayason ke paas ek tarah ka santripti point (saturation point) hota hai, jiske baad kisi cheez ke liye mazeed tarasna (longing) aakhirkar kam ho jata hai jaise-jaise aap iska mazeed hissa paate hain. Ek bhookha insaan sirf itna hi khana kha sakta hai. Ek akela insaan sirf itni hi saath-sangat (companionship) rakh sakta hai. Jigyasa (Curiosity) is tareeqe se kaam nahi karti. **Koi jitna zyaada seekhta hai, mazeed seekhne ki tivra ichha (craving) utni hi badi hoti jaati hai.** Koi jitna behtar hota jata hai, koi utna hi mazeed recognize karta hai ki koi kitna mazeed behtar ban sakta hai. Agar aap is book ko padhna khatam karte hain aur apna khud ka project try karne liye encourage hue hain, toh yeh meri sabse badi umeed hogi—yeh nahi ki aap apne project mein successful hon balki yeh ki aapka ending ek shuruat (beginning) ho. Ki duniya mein majood un saari possibly jaan'ne yogya cheezon mein ek choti si darar (small crack) khol kar, aap jhank sakein aur paa sakein ki wahan usse kahin mazeed, kahin zyaada hai jitna aapne kabhi kalpana ki thi.

---

# Appendix — Further Notes on My Ultralearning Projects

### _(Parishisht — Mere Ultralearning Projects Par Mazeed Notes)_

---

## The MIT Challenge

_(MIT Challenge)_

> **GOAL (Lakshya):** MIT ke computer science ke undergraduate paathyakram (curriculum) mein padhai jaane wali jankari ko seekhna, unke freely pradan kiye gaye materials aur used textbooks ka upyog karte hue.
> **METHOD (Tareeqa):** Saare final exams ko pass karne ka maqsad rakhna (50 percent se upar score karna, jab tak ki doosri jankari pradan na ki gayi ho) aur programming projects ko complete karna.
> **TIMEFRAME (Samay-sima):** October 2011 se September 2012

### Notes and Discussion _(Notes Aur Charcha)_

Yeh note karna important hai ki maine jo aakhirkar complete kiya woh MIT ki degree ki nakal (facsimile) nahi tha. Bhale hi maine, jab bhi possible ho, cover kiye gaye overall curriculum aur moolyankan ki tivrata (intensity of evaluation) ko benchmark karne ka prayas kiya, phir bhi is baat se zaroori badlav (necessary departures) the ki ek actual MIT student ne same material ke beech se kaise progress ki hoti.

Poore curriculum ke level par badlav the. MIT ke OpenCourseWare ne us samay humanities ke liye aise options offer nahi kiye jinhein main khud grade kar sakoon, isliye maine unhein economics ke classes ke sath badal (swapped) diya. Lab-heavy classes jin ke liye mere paas equipment tak access nahi tha, unki jagah pencil-and-paper theory classes ko rakkha gya jinhein main kar sakta tha. MIT students se ek thesis project karne ki umeed ki jaati thi. Maine apne baarah mahine ke study period ke dauran aisa nahi kiya, lekin fun ke liye maine ek aisa computer program zaroor create kiya jo kisi ko computer opponent ke khilaf Scrabble khelne kabil banata hai, mere project ke officially conclude hone ke theek baad. Programming projects ka moolyankan karte waqt, maine unhein simply ek safalata ke roop mein gina agar woh kaam karte the aur desired functions perform karte the ya accompanied testing suites ko complete karne kabil the.

Final exams ke liye, mera default benchmark kam se kam 50 percent haasil karna tha. Maine jab bhi possible ho official grading rubric ko follow kiya. Jab wahan gaps the (jaise multistep problems par arithmetic ya algebraic errors ke liye points kaise deduct kiye jayein), maine apne faisale (judgment) ka use kiya. Baad ke stage ne kuch sambhavit paksh-paat (potential bias) ko introduce kiya, isliye maine challenge complete karne ke kai saal baad wapas jaane aur sabse strict possible grading scheme ka use karke apne saare exams ko reevaluate karne ka faisla kiya (kisi multipart question par koi bhi galti poore question ko zero points ke barabar bana degi; aage ke questions par apply kiya gaya koi bhi galat result un questions ko bhi zero points ke barabar bana dega). Nateejah yeh raha ki tees classes mein se chheh jinhein maine ek “pass” ke roop mein record kiya tha, unhein is stricter schema ke tehat “fail” gina jata. Mera vishwas nahi hai ki yeh moolyankan sahi hai, isliye main un exams ko pass karne ke apne original moolyankan par tike rehta (stand by) hoon, lekin yeh dikhane ke liye point out karne layak hai ki mere subjective decisions ka kitna bada impact pada. Kuch classes ke paas koi final exams nahi the, isliye un cases mein moolyankan assignments ya midterm exams par defaulted ho gya. Assignments complete karna kisi class ko complete karne ke liye ek requirement nahi tha, halanki learning process ke hisse ke roop mein maine aakhirkar unmein se kai ko kiya.

Challenge par mazeed jankari ke liye, jaise course lists, use kiye gaye materials aur mere exams ke scans, aap challenge homepage par visit kar sakte hain: [www.scotthyoung.com/blog/mit-challenge/](https://www.google.com/search?q=http://www.scotthyoung.com/blog/mit-challenge/).

---

## The Year Without English

_(English Ke Bina Ek Saal)_

> **GOAL (Lakshya):** Spanish, Portuguese, Mandarin Chinese, aur Korean seekhna.
> **METHOD (Tareeqa):** Poore saal English bolne se bachna, jabki Spain, Brazil, China, aur South Korea (mota-mota teen-teen mahine har ek) ka travel karna. Maine yeh project Vatsal Jaiswal ke sath kiya (jinka chapter chheh mein bhi zikr hai).
> **TIMEFRAME (Samay-sima):** September 2013 se August 2014

### Notes and Discussion _(Notes Aur Charcha)_

Har bhasha mein pahunche gaye kushalata ke level (level of proficiency) ko matra mein naapna (quantifying) ek pechida kaam hai. Ek dohra risk (dual risk) hai, dono badha-chadhakar batane (exaggeration) ka—perfect level of fluency ka sanket dena jabki yeh probably ek aishi process hai jisme dashakon ke immersion ki zarurat hoti hai—aur ausat se kam dikhane (downplaying) ka bhi. Trip ke baad maine jis ek insaan se baat ki, usne poocha ki kya main “kisi taxi driver ko directions de sakta hoon” bhale hi is task ke liye sirf kuch ghante ki practice ki zarurat hoti hai, mahino ki nahi. Toh un difficulties ko dimaag mein rakh kar, main us level ka anuman (estimate) lagane ki koshish karunga jahan tak hum pahunche:

- **SPANISH:** Yahan mera vishwas hai ki mere dost aur main dono teen mahine baad lagbhag ek **B2 level** tak pahunch gaye, bhashan seekhne ke liye Benny Lewis ke manak (standard for fluency) ko poora karte hue (bhale hi nishchit roop se har kisi ke manak ko nahi). Us level par, hamein Spanish mein kisi bhi topic par ghanton socializing karne mein bahut kam difficulty hui, halanki nishchit roop se hamara accent, grammar aur mazeed formal bolne ki abilities ek native speaker ke level par nahi thin.
- **PORTUGUESE:** Hum Spanish ke mukable Portuguese mein kamzor the, halanki bahut zyaada nahi. Dono bhashayein ek common base share karti hain, isliye Spanish ke mukable seekhne ke liye bahut kam tha. Hum dost bana sakte the aur socializing kar sakte the, lekin utni bina kisi mehnat ke (effortlessly) nahi.
- **MANDARIN CHINESE:** Yeh hamari abilities mein pehla bada bhatkaav (divergence) tha. Main sach mein Chinese seekhna chahta tha aur khud ko familiar karne ke liye hamare trip se pehle flash cards par kuch samay spent kiya tha. Mera dost kam interested tha aur usne mazeed struggle kiya. Ant mein, maine **HSK 4 exam** (Chinese proficiency ko naapne wale cheh-level ke exams ki shrankhla mein chautha) likha aur pass kiya aur main kahunga ki meri Mandarin decent thi, halanki advanced topics par mazeed limited thi, jahan vocabulary English se poori tarah se different hai. Mera dost ek lower-intermediate level tak pahuncha, comfortably bolne aur tones ka use karne kabil hote hue lekin kam vocabulary ke sath.
- **KOREAN:** Is bhasha mein hum dono ek lower-intermediate level tak pahunche, conversations karne aur daily life mein gujara karne kabil hote hue, lekin topics ki ek mazeed restricted range par. Iska ek hissa Korean bhasha ki difficulty thi, lekin ek bada hissa simply yeh tha ki chunki yeh lagataar chauthi nayi bhasha thi, hum burned out (thak) rahe the.

Bhale hi hamara maqsad har country mein pahunchne ke baad apni zyaada tar learning karne ka tha, humne har ek ke liye pehle se thoda purv-taiyari (prior preparation) zoor ki thi. Yeh mukhya roop se Pimsleur audio tapes sunna aur kuch flash cards karna tha. In general humne per bhasha lagbhag twenty-five se fifty hours spent kiye, halanki maine pahuncheetne se pehle Chinese par mazeed (lagbhag ek sau ghante) spent kiye the.

Interested log hamare project ke baare mein mazeed dekh sakte hain (jisme un videos ko shamil kiya gaya hai jinhein humne har country mein apni progress dikhaane ke liye ek sath rakkha tha), humne seekhne ke liye kya use kiya sath hi ek unscripted interview yeh dikhaane ke liye ki mota-mota hum project homepage par har bhasha mein kis level tak pahunche: [www.scotthyoung.com/blog/the-year-without-english/](https://www.google.com/search?q=http://www.scotthyoung.com/blog/the-year-without-english/).

---

## Portrait Drawing Challenge

_(Portrait Drawing Challenge)_

> **GOAL (Lakshya):** Chehroon ko realistically draw karne ki apni ability ko behtar banana.
> **METHOD (Tareeqa):** Rapid feedback, tarah-tarah ki kitabhon aur courses se techniques.
> **TIMEFRAME (Samay-sima):** July 2016

### Notes and Discussion _(Notes Aur Charcha)_

Yeh ek chhota project tha, jisme ek mahina laga aur kul mila kar ek sau ghante ki practice (one hundred hours of practice) hui. Quick sketches draw karne aur semitransparent reference photos ke upar unhein rakh kar (overlaying) unki comparison karne ki strategy ke alava, mujhe _Drawing on the Right Side of the Brain_ kitab se, aur Vitruvian Studio ki _Portrait Drawing_ class se bhi bada fayda (benefit) mila.

Maine apne dwara kiye gaye har ek drawing, sketch, aur self-portrait ko upload kiya hai, sath hi project homepage par is baare mein mazeed detailed discussion ke sath ki maine seekhne ke liye kya use kiya: [www.scotthyoung.com/blog/myprojects/portrait-challenge/](https://www.google.com/search?q=http://www.scotthyoung.com/blog/myprojects/portrait-challenge/).

_(Aage Ke Challenges)_

Is book ko likhne ke samay, upar diye gaye teen challenges mere mukhya public ultralearning projects hain. Halanki, main hamesha nayi cheezein seekhta rehta hoon, isliye jaise-jaise main mazeed public challenges karunga, main unhein yahan post karunga: [www.scotthyoung.com/blog/my-projects/](https://www.google.com/search?q=http://www.scotthyoung.com/blog/my-projects/).

## Chapter IV: Principle 1—Metalearning: First Draw a Map

_(Chapter IV: Niyam 1 — Metalearning: Pehle Ek Map Banayein)_

1. **“Kuti paoka djalou”:** Linguistic Society of America, “‘Monolingual Fieldwork Demonstration’—Daniel Everett,” filmed July 2013, YouTube video, 1:16:27, posted September 2013, [https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=sYpWp7g7XWU](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=sYpWp7g7XWU).
2. **What makes this feat particularly impressive:** Demonstration ko English ka use karke kharab karne se bachne ke liye, ek aishi bhasha jisse doosra speaker shayad familiar ho sakta tha, Everett ne apne saare shuruati sawaal (queries) Pirahã bhasha mein phrase karne ka chunaav kiya, jo Brazil ke Amazon jungle mein sirf ek door-daas ke logon (remote people) dwara boli jaati hai.
3. **Over the last thirty years:** Is bhasha ki vilakshanta (unusualness) ne linguistics mein thoda sa vivad (controversy) paada kiya hai, jisme Pirahã ke grammar ke baare mein Dan Everett ke daavon ko bhashayi kattarata (linguistic orthodoxy) par hamle ke roop mein mukhya stage par rakkha gya hai.
4. **To see why metalearning is so:** Jacqueline Thomas, “The Role Played by Metalinguistic Awareness in Second and Third Language Learning,” _Journal of Multilingual and Multicultural Development_ 9, no. 3 (1988): 235–46, [https://www.tandfonline.com/doi/abs/10.1080/01434632.1988.9994334](https://www.tandfonline.com/doi/abs/10.1080/01434632.1988.9994334).
5. **Determine if learning:** Ise is matlab mein mat lein ki main sochta hoon ki grad school be-buniyaad (useless) hai. Important cheez yeh taye karna hai ki kya yeh sach mein aapke liye matter karegii, is baat par depend karte hui ki aap kaun si job chahte hain, aapke adhyayan ka subject kya hai, aur sanstha (institution) kya hai. Mera point yeh nahi hai ki grad school samay ki barbaadi hai balki yeh hai ki jab itne zyaada samay aur cost wala faisala karna ho, toh behtar hoga ki aap apni research pehle karein!
6. **For example, one common recommendation:** Victor Mair, “How to Learn Chinese and Japanese,” _Language Log_, February 17, 2014, [http://languagelog.ldc.upenn.edu/nll/?p=10554](https://www.google.com/search?q=http://languagelog.ldc.upenn.edu/nll/%3Fp%3D10554).
7. **The literature on self-directed learning:** George E. Spear and Donald W. Mocker, “The Organizing Circumstance: Environmental Determinants in Self-Directed Learning,” _Adult Education Quarterly_ 35, no. 1 (March 1, 1984): 1–10, [https://journals.sagepub.com/doi/abs/10.1177/0001848184035001001?journalCode=aeqb](https://journals.sagepub.com/doi/abs/10.1177/0001848184035001001?journalCode=aeqb).
8. **That led me to do:** “Portrait Drawing—The Complete Online Course,” Vitruvian Studio, [https://vitruvianstudio.com/course/portrait-drawing/](https://vitruvianstudio.com/course/portrait-drawing/).
